

5. `src/stores/appStore.ts` (Zustand Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';

export type SourceType = 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';

interface AppState {
  activeSource: SourceType;
  setActiveSource: (source: SourceType) => void;
}

export const useAppStore = create<AppState>((set) => ({
  activeSource: 'storage',
  setActiveSource: (source) => set({ activeSource: source }),
}));

// Custom selector hooks for better performance
export const useActiveSource = () => useAppStore((state) => state.activeSource);
export const useSetActiveSource = () => useAppStore((state) => state.setActiveSource);
```

6. `src/components/ui/button.tsx` (ShadCN Button)

```typescript
import * as React from "react"
import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const buttonVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: "bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90",
        destructive:
          "bg-destructive text-white hover:bg-destructive/90 focus-visible:ring-destructive/20 dark:focus-visible:ring-destructive/40 dark:bg-destructive/60",
        outline:
          "border bg-background shadow-xs hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:bg-input/30 dark:border-input dark:hover:bg-input/50",
        secondary:
          "bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
        ghost:
          "hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50",
        link: "text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline",
      },
      size: {
        default: "h-9 px-4 py-2 has-[>svg]:px-3",
        sm: "h-8 rounded-md gap-1.5 px-3 has-[>svg]:px-2.5",
        lg: "h-10 rounded-md px-6 has-[>svg]:px-4",
        icon: "size-9",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
      size: "default",
    },
  }
)

function Button({
  className,
  variant,
  size,
  asChild = false,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<"button"> &
  VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> & {
    asChild?: boolean
  }) {
  const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button"

  return (
    <Comp
      data-slot="button"
      className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

export { Button, buttonVariants }
```

7. `src/lib/utils.ts`

```typescript
import { clsx, type ClassValue } from "clsx"
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge"

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs))
}
```

8. `src/components/LeftPanel.tsx`

```typescript
import { HardDrive, FolderGit, Github, Terminal } from 'lucide-react';
import { useAppStore, SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';

const buttons: { id: SourceType; label: string; icon: React.ElementType }[] = [
  { id: 'storage', label: 'Storage', icon: HardDrive },
  { id: 'drive', label: 'Drive', icon: FolderGit },
  { id: 'github', label: 'GitHub', icon: Github },
  { id: 'terminal', label: 'Terminal', icon: Terminal },
];

export function LeftPanel() {
  const { activeSource, setActiveSource } = useAppStore();

  return (
    <div className="w-full md:w-[320px] bg-card border-r border-border flex flex-col">
      <div className="p-4 border-b border-border">
        <h1 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground">App Navigator</h1>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Select a source</p>
      </div>
      
      <nav className="flex-1 p-3 space-y-2">
        {buttons.map((button) => {
          const Icon = button.icon;
          const isActive = activeSource === button.id;
          
          return (
            <button
              key={button.id}
              onClick={() => setActiveSource(button.id)}
              className={`
                w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium
                transition-all duration-200 ease-in-out
                ${isActive 
                  ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground scale-[1.02] shadow-md' 
                  : 'bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground'
                }
              `}
            >
              <Icon className="w-5 h-5" />
              <span>{button.label}</span>
              {isActive && (
                <div className="ml-auto w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-primary-foreground animate-pulse" />
              )}
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </nav>
      
      <div className="p-4 border-t border-border">
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center">
          Active: <span className="font-medium text-foreground capitalize">{activeSource}</span>
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { 
  HardDrive, 
  FolderGit, 
  Github, 
  Terminal,
  FileText,
  Folder,
  Database
} from 'lucide-react';

const placeholderContent: Record<string, { title: string; items: string[]; icon: React.ElementType }> = {
  storage: {
    title: 'Storage Overview',
    icon: Database,

export function RightPanel() {

  return (

              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-primary" />
                <span className="text-foreground font-mono text-sm">{item}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        <div className="mt-8 p-4 rounded-lg bg-muted/50 border border-border">
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center">
            This is placeholder content for the <span className="font-medium text-foreground capitalize">{activeSource}</span> panel.
            <br />
            Replace with actual functionality as needed.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

📝 Full Implementation

1. `src/types/filesystem.ts` (Type Definitions)

```typescript
// File System Access API Types
// Abstraction layer for easy backend swap later

export interface FileSystemEntry {
  name: string;
  kind: 'file' | 'directory';
  size: number;
  lastModified: Date;
  handle: FileSystemFileHandle | FileSystemDirectoryHandle;
}

export interface FileSystemFileEntry extends FileSystemEntry {
  kind: 'file';
  handle: FileSystemFileHandle;
}

export interface FileSystemDirectoryEntry extends FileSystemEntry {
  kind: 'directory';
  handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle;
}

export type ViewMode = 'grid' | 'list';
export type SortBy = 'name-asc' | 'name-desc' | 'date' | 'size';

// Backend interface - swap with Node.js implementation later
export interface IFileSystemBackend {
  pickDirectory(): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null>;
  readDirectory(handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle): Promise<FileSystemEntry[]>;
  createDirectory(parentHandle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle, name: string): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle>;
  getFileSize(handle: FileSystemFileHandle): Promise<number>;
  getFileDate(handle: FileSystemFileHandle): Promise<Date>;
}

// Fake mount points for browser (root level)
export interface MountPoint {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  icon: string;
  handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null;
  isFake: boolean;
}
```

2. `src/lib/fileSystemBackend.ts` (Backend Implementation)

```typescript
import { 
  FileSystemEntry, 
  FileSystemFileEntry, 
  FileSystemDirectoryEntry,
  IFileSystemBackend 
} from '@/types/filesystem';

// Browser File System Access API Backend
// Can be swapped with Node.js backend later
export class BrowserFileSystemBackend implements IFileSystemBackend {
  
  async pickDirectory(): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null> {
    try {
      // @ts-ignore - File System Access API
      const handle = await window.showDirectoryPicker({ mode: 'readwrite' });
      return handle;
    } catch (err) {
      if ((err as Error).name === 'AbortError') {
        return null;
      }
      throw err;
    }
  }

  async readDirectory(handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle): Promise<FileSystemEntry[]> {
    const entries: FileSystemEntry[] = [];
    
    // @ts-ignore - File System Access API
    for await (const [name, entryHandle] of handle.entries()) {
      const entry: FileSystemEntry = {
        name,
        kind: entryHandle.kind,
        size: 0,
        lastModified: new Date(),
        handle: entryHandle,
      };

      if (entryHandle.kind === 'file') {
        try {
          const file = await (entryHandle as FileSystemFileHandle).getFile();
          entry.size = file.size;
          entry.lastModified = new Date(file.lastModified);
        } catch (e) {
          // File might be inaccessible
        }
      }

      entries.push(entry);
    }

    return entries;
  }

  async createDirectory(
    parentHandle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle, 
    name: string
  ): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle> {
    // @ts-ignore - File System Access API
    const newHandle = await parentHandle.getDirectoryHandle(name, { create: true });
    return newHandle;
  }

  async getFileSize(handle: FileSystemFileHandle): Promise<number> {
    const file = await handle.getFile();
    return file.size;
  }

  async getFileDate(handle: FileSystemFileHandle): Promise<Date> {
    const file = await handle.getFile();
    return new Date(file.lastModified);
  }
}

// Singleton instance
export const fileSystemBackend = new BrowserFileSystemBackend();
```

3. `src/stores/fileSystemStore.ts` (Zustand Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { 
  FileSystemEntry, 
  FileSystemDirectoryEntry,
  ViewMode, 
  SortBy,
  MountPoint 
} from '@/types/filesystem';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';

interface NavigationHistory {
  handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle;
  name: string;
}

interface FileSystemState {
  // Current state
  currentPath: string;
  currentHandle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null;
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  viewMode: ViewMode;
  sortBy: SortBy;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  
  // History for back navigation
  history: NavigationHistory[];
  
  // Mount points (fake root)
  mountPoints: MountPoint[];
  
  // Actions
  setViewMode: (mode: ViewMode) => void;
  setSortBy: (sort: SortBy) => void;
  pickDirectory: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateTo: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateToRoot: () => void;
  refreshCurrent: () => Promise<void>;
  createFolder: (name: string) => Promise<void>;
  initMountPoints: () => void;
  selectMountPoint: (mountId: string) => Promise<void>;
  
  // Computed
  getSortedEntries: () => FileSystemEntry[];
}

const createFakeMountPoints = (): MountPoint[] => [
  {
    id: 'internal',
    name: 'Internal Storage',
    icon: 'hard-drive',
    handle: null,
    isFake: true,
  },
  {
    id: 'sd-card',
    name: 'SD Card',
    icon: 'sd-card',
    handle: null,
    isFake: true,
  },
];

export const useFileSystemStore = create<FileSystemState>((set, get) => ({
  currentPath: '/',
  currentHandle: null,
  entries: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  history: [],
  mountPoints: createFakeMountPoints(),

  setViewMode: (mode) => set({ viewMode: mode }),
  
  setSortBy: (sort) => set({ sortBy: sort }),

  pickDirectory: async () => {
    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    try {
      const handle = await fileSystemBackend.pickDirectory();
      if (handle) {
        const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(handle);
        set({ 
          currentHandle: handle,
          currentPath: `/${handle.name}`,
          entries,
          history: [],
          isLoading: false 
        });
      } else {
        set({ isLoading: false });
      }
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  navigateTo: async (entry) => {
    const { currentHandle, history, currentPath } = get();
    if (!currentHandle || entry.kind !== 'directory') return;

    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    try {
      const newEntries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(entry.handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle);
      set({
        currentHandle: entry.handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle,
        currentPath: `${currentPath}/${entry.name}`,
        entries: newEntries,
        history: [...history, { handle: currentHandle, name: currentPath.split('/').pop() || 'root' }],
        isLoading: false,
      });
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  navigateBack: async () => {
    const { history } = get();
    if (history.length === 0) {
      get().navigateToRoot();
      return;
    }

    const previous = history[history.length - 1];
    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    
    try {
      const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(previous.handle);
      set({
        currentHandle: previous.handle,
        currentPath: history.length === 1 ? '/' : `/${previous.name}`,
        entries,
        history: history.slice(0, -1),
        isLoading: false,
      });
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  navigateToRoot: () => {
    set({
      currentPath: '/',
      currentHandle: null,
      entries: [],
      history: [],
    });
  },

  refreshCurrent: async () => {
    const { currentHandle } = get();
    if (!currentHandle) return;

    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    try {
      const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(currentHandle);
      set({ entries, isLoading: false });
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  createFolder: async (name) => {
    const { currentHandle } = get();
    if (!currentHandle) return;

    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    try {
      await fileSystemBackend.createDirectory(currentHandle, name);
      await get().refreshCurrent();
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  initMountPoints: () => {
    set({ mountPoints: createFakeMountPoints() });
  },

  selectMountPoint: async (mountId) => {
    const { mountPoints } = get();
    const mount = mountPoints.find(m => m.id === mountId);
    
    if (!mount) return;
    
    // If mount has no handle yet, open picker
    if (!mount.handle) {
      const handle = await fileSystemBackend.pickDirectory();
      if (handle) {
        // Update mount point with handle
        const updatedMounts = mountPoints.map(m => 
          m.id === mountId ? { ...m, handle, isFake: false } : m
        );
        const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(handle);
        set({
          mountPoints: updatedMounts,
          currentHandle: handle,
          currentPath: `/${mount.name}`,
          entries,
          history: [],
        });
      }
    } else {
      // Use existing handle
      const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(mount.handle);
      set({
        currentHandle: mount.handle,
        currentPath: `/${mount.name}`,
        entries,
        history: [],
      });
    }
  },

  getSortedEntries: () => {
    const { entries, sortBy } = get();
    const sorted = [...entries];
    
    switch (sortBy) {
      case 'name-asc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
      case 'name-desc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
      case 'date':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.lastModified.getTime() - a.lastModified.getTime());
      case 'size':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.size - a.size);
      default:
        return sorted;
    }
  },
}));

// Selectors
export const useCurrentPath = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.currentPath);
export const useCurrentHandle = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.currentHandle);
export const useEntries = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.getSortedEntries());
export const useViewMode = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.viewMode);
export const useSortBy = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.sortBy);
export const useIsLoading = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.isLoading);
export const useHistory = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.history);
export const useMountPoints = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.mountPoints);
```

4. `src/components/ui/toggle.tsx` (ShadCN Toggle)

```typescript
import * as React from "react"
import * as TogglePrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-toggle"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const toggleVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-md text-sm font-medium hover:bg-muted hover:text-muted-foreground disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 data-[state=on]:bg-accent data-[state=on]:text-accent-foreground [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&_svg]:shrink-0 transition-all outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:ring-offset-2",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: "bg-transparent",
        outline:
          "border border-input bg-transparent shadow-sm hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground",
      },
      size: {
        default: "h-9 px-3 min-w-9",
        sm: "h-8 px-2 min-w-8",
        lg: "h-10 px-3 min-w-10",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
      size: "default",
    },
  }
)

function Toggle({
  className,
  variant,
  size,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof TogglePrimitive.Root> &
  VariantProps<typeof toggleVariants>) {
  return (
    <TogglePrimitive.Root
      data-slot="toggle"
      className={cn(toggleVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

export { Toggle, toggleVariants }
```

```typescript
        "focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px]",

      )}
```

7. `src/components/FileManager/Toolbar.tsx`

```typescript
import { 
  Grid3X3, 
  List, 
  ArrowLeft, 
  FolderPlus, 
  RefreshCw,
  HardDrive,
  ChevronDown,
  ArrowUpDown
} from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Toggle } from '@/components/ui/toggle';
import {
  DropdownMenu,
  DropdownMenuContent,
  DropdownMenuItem,
  DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import { ViewMode, SortBy } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { useFileSystemStore, useCurrentPath, useHistory, useIsLoading } from '@/stores/fileSystemStore';

interface ToolbarProps {
  viewMode: ViewMode;
  onViewModeChange: (mode: ViewMode) => void;
  sortBy: SortBy;
  onSortChange: (sort: SortBy) => void;
  onCreateFolder: () => void;
}

export function Toolbar({ 
  viewMode, 
  onViewModeChange, 
  sortBy, 
  onSortChange,
  onCreateFolder 
}: ToolbarProps) {
  const navigateBack = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.navigateBack);
  const refreshCurrent = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.refreshCurrent);
  const currentPath = useCurrentPath();
  const history = useHistory();
  const isLoading = useIsLoading();

  const sortLabels: Record<SortBy, string> = {
    'name-asc': 'Name (A-Z)',
    'name-desc': 'Name (Z-A)',
    'date': 'Date Modified',
    'size': 'Size',
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border bg-card">
      {/* Left: Navigation */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="icon"
          onClick={navigateBack}
          disabled={history.length === 0 && currentPath === '/'}
          className="h-9 w-9"
        >
          <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>
        
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 ml-2">
          <HardDrive className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
          <span className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">
            {currentPath === '/' ? 'Root' : currentPath}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Right: Actions */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        {/* Refresh */}
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="icon"
          onClick={refreshCurrent}
          disabled={isLoading}
          className="h-9 w-9"
        >
          <RefreshCw className={`h-4 w-4 ${isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
        </Button>

        {/* Create Folder */}
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          onClick={onCreateFolder}
          className="gap-2"
        >
          <FolderPlus className="h-4 w-4" />
          <span className="hidden sm:inline">New Folder</span>
        </Button>

        {/* Sort Dropdown */}
        <DropdownMenu>
          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
            <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="gap-2">
              <ArrowUpDown className="h-4 w-4" />
              <span className="hidden sm:inline">{sortLabels[sortBy]}</span>
              <ChevronDown className="h-3 w-3" />
            </Button>
          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
          <DropdownMenuContent align="end">
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-asc')}>
              Name (A-Z)
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-desc')}>
              Name (Z-A)
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('date')}>
              Date Modified
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('size')}>
              Size
            </DropdownMenuItem>
          </DropdownMenuContent>
        </DropdownMenu>

        {/* View Mode Toggle */}
        <div className="flex items-center border rounded-md">
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'grid'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('grid')}
            className="rounded-none rounded-l-md"
            aria-label="Grid view"
          >
            <Grid3X3 className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Toggle>
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'list'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('list')}
            className="rounded-none rounded-r-md"
            aria-label="List view"
          >
            <List className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Toggle>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

8. `src/components/FileManager/FileGrid.tsx`

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, Folder, FolderOpen } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { useFileSystemStore } from '@/stores/fileSystemStore';

interface FileGridProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

export function FileGrid({ entries }: FileGridProps) {
  const navigateTo = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.navigateTo);

  const handleEntryClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      navigateTo(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 md:grid-cols-4 lg:grid-cols-5 xl:grid-cols-6 gap-4 p-4">
      {entries.map((entry) => (
        <button
          key={entry.name}
          onClick={() => handleEntryClick(entry)}
          className="group flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent hover:border-accent transition-all duration-200 text-left"
        >
          <div className="mb-3 text-primary group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform">
            {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
              <FolderOpen className="w-12 h-12" />
            ) : (
              <File className="w-12 h-12" />
            )}
          </div>
          
          <div className="w-full text-center">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={entry.name}>
              {entry.name}
            </p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
              {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : 'Folder'}
            </p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
            </p>
          </div>
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

9. `src/components/FileManager/FileList.tsx`

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, Folder } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { useFileSystemStore } from '@/stores/fileSystemStore';

interface FileListProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

export function FileList({ entries }: FileListProps) {
  const navigateTo = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.navigateTo);

  const handleEntryClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      navigateTo(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-4 px-4 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground bg-muted/50">
        <div className="col-span-6">Name</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Size</div>
        <div className="col-span-4">Modified</div>
      </div>

      {/* Entries */}
      {entries.map((entry) => (
        <button
          key={entry.name}
          onClick={() => handleEntryClick(entry)}
          className="w-full grid grid-cols-12 gap-4 px-4 py-3 text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left items-center group"
        >
          <div className="col-span-6 flex items-center gap-3">
            {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
              <Folder className="w-5 h-5 text-primary group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform" />
            ) : (
              <File className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground" />
            )}
            <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={entry.name}>
              {entry.name}
            </span>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-2 text-muted-foreground">
            {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : '-'}
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-4 text-muted-foreground">
            {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
          </div>
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

10. `src/components/FileManager/CreateFolderDialog.tsx`

```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { useFileSystemStore } from '@/stores/fileSystemStore';

interface CreateFolderDialogProps {
  open: boolean;
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
}

export function CreateFolderDialog({ open, onOpenChange }: CreateFolderDialogProps) {
  const [folderName, setFolderName] = useState('');
  const [isCreating, setIsCreating] = useState(false);
  const createFolder = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.createFolder);

  const handleCreate = async () => {
    if (!folderName.trim()) return;
    
    setIsCreating(true);
    await createFolder(folderName.trim());
    setIsCreating(false);
    setFolderName('');
    onOpenChange(false);
  };

  const handleCancel = () => {
    setFolderName('');
    onOpenChange(false);
  };

  return (
    <Dialog open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
      <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle>Create New Folder</DialogTitle>
          <DialogDescription>
            Enter a name for the new folder in the current directory.
          </DialogDescription>
        </DialogHeader>
        
        <div className="py-4">
          <Input
            placeholder="Folder name"
            value={folderName}
            onChange={(e) => setFolderName(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={(e) => {
              if (e.key === 'Enter') handleCreate();
              if (e.key === 'Escape') handleCancel();
            }}
            autoFocus
          />
        </div>

        <DialogFooter>
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={handleCancel}>
            Cancel
          </Button>
          <Button 
            onClick={handleCreate} 
            disabled={!folderName.trim() || isCreating}
          >
            {isCreating ? 'Creating...' : 'Create'}
          </Button>
        </DialogFooter>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { HardDrive, SdCard } from 'lucide-react';
import { useFileSystemStore, useMountPoints } from '@/stores/fileSystemStore';

const iconMap: Record<string, React.ElementType> = {

  'sd-card': SdCard,

export function MountPointsView() {

  const selectMountPoint = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.selectMountPoint);

    <div className="p-6">
      <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground mb-4">Storage Locations</h2>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
        {mountPoints.map((mount) => {
          const Icon = iconMap[mount.icon] || HardDrive;
          
          return (
            <button
              key={mount.id}
              onClick={() => selectMountPoint(mount.id)}
              className="flex items-center gap-4 p-6 rounded-xl border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent hover:border-accent transition-all duration-200 text-left group"
            >
              <div className="p-3 rounded-lg bg-primary/10 text-primary group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform">
                <Icon className="w-8 h-8" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <h3 className="font-semibold text-foreground">{mount.name}</h3>
                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                  {mount.isFake ? 'Click to mount' : 'Mounted'}
                </p>
              </div>
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </div>
      
      <div className="mt-8 p-4 rounded-lg bg-muted/50 border border-border">
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center">
          Select a storage location to browse files.
          <br />
          This uses the File System Access API (Chrome only).
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

12. `src/components/FileManager/index.tsx` (Main Component)

```typescript
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Toolbar } from './Toolbar';
import { FileGrid } from './FileGrid';
import { FileList } from './FileList';
import { CreateFolderDialog } from './CreateFolderDialog';
import { MountPointsView } from './MountPointsView';
import { useFileSystemStore, useEntries, useViewMode, useSortBy, useCurrentHandle } from '@/stores/fileSystemStore';
import { ViewMode, SortBy } from '@/types/filesystem';

export function FileManager() {
  const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  
  const entries = useEntries();
  const viewMode = useViewMode();
  const sortBy = useSortBy();
  const currentHandle = useCurrentHandle();
  const setViewMode = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.setViewMode);
  const setSortBy = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.setSortBy);
  const initMountPoints = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.initMountPoints);

  useEffect(() => {
    initMountPoints();
  }, [initMountPoints]);

  const handleViewModeChange = (mode: ViewMode) => {
    setViewMode(mode);
  };

  const handleSortChange = (sort: SortBy) => {
    setSortBy(sort);
  };

  // If no directory is selected, show mount points
  if (!currentHandle) {
    return (
      <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
        <MountPointsView />
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <Toolbar
        viewMode={viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={handleViewModeChange}
        sortBy={sortBy}
        onSortChange={handleSortChange}
        onCreateFolder={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}
      />
      
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {entries.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p className="text-lg font-medium">Empty folder</p>
            <p className="text-sm">Create a new folder to get started</p>
          </div>
        ) : viewMode === 'grid' ? (
          <FileGrid entries={entries} />
        ) : (
          <FileList entries={entries} />
        )}
      </div>

      <CreateFolderDialog 
        open={createDialogOpen} 
        onOpenChange={setCreateDialogOpen} 
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { useAppStore } from '@/stores/appStore';
import { FileManager } from './FileManager';
import { 
  HardDrive, 
  FolderGit, 
  Github, 
  Terminal,
  FileText,
  Database
} from 'lucide-react';

const placeholderContent: Record<string, { title: string; icon: React.ElementType; component?: React.ReactNode }> = {
  storage: {
    title: 'File Manager',
    icon: Database,
    component: <FileManager />,
  },
  drive: {
    title: 'Drive Files',
    icon: FolderGit,
  },
  github: {
    title: 'GitHub Repositories',
    icon: Github,
  },
  terminal: {
    title: 'Terminal Sessions',
    icon: Terminal,
  },
};

function PlaceholderContent({ source }: { source: string }) {
  const content = placeholderContent[source];
  const Icon = content.icon;

  return (
    <div className="flex-1 bg-background p-6 overflow-auto">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
          <div className="p-3 rounded-xl bg-primary/10 text-primary">
            <Icon className="w-8 h-8" />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground">{content.title}</h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground">Placeholder for {source} content</p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="p-8 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card">
          <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center">
            This feature is not yet implemented.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function RightPanel() {
  const activeSource = useAppStore((state) => state.activeSource);
  const content = placeholderContent[activeSource];

  // If storage is selected, show FileManager
  if (activeSource === 'storage' && content.component) {
    return (
      <div className="flex-1 h-screen overflow-hidden">
        {content.component}
      </div>
    );
  }

  return <PlaceholderContent source={activeSource} />;
}
```

---

🚀 How to Use

1. Click "Storage" in the left panel
2. Select a mount point (Internal Storage or SD Card)
3. Choose a directory from your computer (Chrome will show picker)
4. Browse files:
   - Click folders to navigate inside
   - Use Back button to go up
   - Toggle Grid/List view
   - Sort by name, date, or size
5. Create folders with the "+ New Folder" button

1. `src/types/panel.ts` (Panel Types)

```typescript
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';
import { SortBy, ViewMode } from './filesystem';

export interface PanelState {
  id: string;
  source: SourceType;
  // Storage-specific state
  path: string;
  handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null;
  history: { handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle; name: string }[];
  viewMode: ViewMode;
  sortBy: SortBy;
  // Account/GitHub-specific state (for future)
  accountId: string | null;
  // UI state
  width: number; // in pixels
  isMinimized: boolean;
  isMaximized: boolean;
}

export interface PanelLayout {
  panels: PanelState[];
  activePanelId: string | null;
}

export const DEFAULT_PANEL_WIDTH = 400;
export const MIN_PANEL_WIDTH = 200;
export const MAX_PANEL_WIDTH = 800;
export const MAX_PANELS = 4;

export const createDefaultPanel = (id: string, index: number): PanelState => ({
  id,
  source: index === 0 ? 'storage' : 'drive',
  path: '/',
  handle: null,
  history: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  accountId: null,
  width: DEFAULT_PANEL_WIDTH,
  isMinimized: false,
  isMaximized: false,
});
```

2. `src/stores/panelStore.ts` (Zustand + Immer Panel Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { 
  PanelState, 
  PanelLayout, 
  createDefaultPanel,
  MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
  MAX_PANELS 
} from '@/types/panel';
import { SourceType } from './appStore';
import { ViewMode, SortBy } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';

interface PanelStore extends PanelLayout {
  // Actions
  addPanel: () => void;
  removePanel: (id: string) => void;
  setActivePanel: (id: string) => void;
  
  // Panel-specific actions
  setPanelSource: (id: string, source: SourceType) => void;
  setPanelPath: (id: string, path: string) => void;
  setPanelHandle: (id: string, handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null) => void;
  navigatePanelForward: (id: string, handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle, name: string) => void;
  navigatePanelBack: (id: string) => void;
  setPanelViewMode: (id: string, mode: ViewMode) => void;
  setPanelSortBy: (id: string, sort: SortBy) => void;
  setPanelWidth: (id: string, width: number) => void;
  togglePanelMinimize: (id: string) => void;
  
  // Storage operations
  pickDirectoryForPanel: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  refreshPanelDirectory: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  
  // Getters
  getPanel: (id: string) => PanelState | undefined;
  getPanelEntries: (id: string) => Promise<FileSystemEntry[]>;
}

import { FileSystemEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';

export const usePanelStore = create<PanelStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    panels: [
      createDefaultPanel('panel-1', 0),
      createDefaultPanel('panel-2', 1),
    ],
    activePanelId: 'panel-1',

    addPanel: () => {
      const { panels } = get();
      if (panels.length >= MAX_PANELS) return;
      
      const newId = `panel-${panels.length + 1}`;
      set((state) => {
        state.panels.push(createDefaultPanel(newId, panels.length));
        state.activePanelId = newId;
      });
    },

    removePanel: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.panels = state.panels.filter((p) => p.id !== id);
        if (state.activePanelId === id) {
          state.activePanelId = state.panels[0]?.id || null;
        }
      });
    },

    setActivePanel: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.activePanelId = id;
      });
    },

    setPanelSource: (id, source) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) {
          panel.source = source;
          // Reset path-specific state when source changes
          panel.path = '/';
          panel.handle = null;
          panel.history = [];
        }
      });
    },

    setPanelPath: (id, path) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.path = path;
      });
    },

    setPanelHandle: (id, handle) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.handle = handle;
      });
    },

    navigatePanelForward: (id, handle, name) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel && panel.handle) {
          panel.history.push({ handle: panel.handle, name: panel.path.split('/').pop() || 'root' });
          panel.handle = handle;
          panel.path = `${panel.path}/${name}`.replace('//', '/');
        }
      });
    },

    navigatePanelBack: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel && panel.history.length > 0) {
          const previous = panel.history.pop()!;
          panel.handle = previous.handle;
          panel.path = panel.history.length === 0 ? '/' : `/${previous.name}`;
        }
      });
    },

    setPanelViewMode: (id, mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setPanelSortBy: (id, sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    setPanelWidth: (id, width) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) {
          panel.width = Math.max(MIN_PANEL_WIDTH, width);
        }
      });
    },

    togglePanelMinimize: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.isMinimized = !panel.isMinimized;
      });
    },

    pickDirectoryForPanel: async (id) => {
      const handle = await fileSystemBackend.pickDirectory();
      if (handle) {
        set((state) => {
          const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
          if (panel) {
            panel.handle = handle;
            panel.path = `/${handle.name}`;
            panel.history = [];
          }
        });
      }
    },

    refreshPanelDirectory: async (id) => {
      // Trigger re-render by updating a timestamp or similar
      // Actual refresh happens in component via useEffect
    },

    getPanel: (id) => {
      return get().panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
    },

    getPanelEntries: async (id) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(id);
      if (!panel?.handle) return [];
      return fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const usePanels = () => usePanelStore((s) => s.panels);
export const useActivePanelId = () => usePanelStore((s) => s.activePanelId);
export const usePanel = (id: string) => usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(id));
export const usePanelCount = () => usePanelStore((s) => s.panels.length);
```

3. `src/hooks/useResizable.ts` (Resize Hook)

```typescript
import { useState, useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';

interface UseResizableOptions {
  initialWidth: number;
  minWidth: number;
  onResize: (width: number) => void;
}

export function useResizable({ initialWidth, minWidth, onResize }: UseResizableOptions) {
  const [isResizing, setIsResizing] = useState(false);
  const [currentWidth, setCurrentWidth] = useState(initialWidth);
  const startXRef = useRef(0);
  const startWidthRef = useRef(initialWidth);

  const startResize = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsResizing(true);
    startXRef.current = e.clientX;
    startWidthRef.current = currentWidth;
  }, [currentWidth]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isResizing) return;
      
      const delta = e.clientX - startXRef.current;
      const newWidth = Math.max(minWidth, startWidthRef.current + delta);
      setCurrentWidth(newWidth);
      onResize(newWidth);
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsResizing(false);
    };

    if (isResizing) {
      document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      document.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
      document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
    }

    return () => {
      document.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      document.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      document.body.style.cursor = '';
      document.body.style.userSelect = '';
    };
  }, [isResizing, minWidth, onResize]);

  return {
    width: currentWidth,
    isResizing,
    startResize,
  };
}
```

4. `src/components/Panel/PanelHeader.tsx`

```typescript
import { X, Minus, Square, HardDrive, FolderGit, Github, Terminal } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';

const sourceConfig: Record<SourceType, { icon: React.ElementType; label: string; color: string }> = {
  storage: { icon: HardDrive, label: 'Storage', color: 'text-blue-500' },
  drive: { icon: FolderGit, label: 'Drive', color: 'text-green-500' },
  github: { icon: Github, label: 'GitHub', color: 'text-purple-500' },
  terminal: { icon: Terminal, label: 'Terminal', color: 'text-orange-500' },
};

interface PanelHeaderProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  isActive: boolean;
  onActivate: () => void;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export function PanelHeader({ panel, isActive, onActivate, onClose }: PanelHeaderProps) {
  const setPanelSource = usePanelStore((s) => s.setPanelSource);
  const toggleMinimize = usePanelStore((s) => s.togglePanelMinimize);

  const handleSourceChange = (source: SourceType) => {
    setPanelSource(panel.id, source);
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'flex flex-col border-b border-border bg-card transition-colors',
        isActive && 'bg-accent/30'
      )}
      onClick={onActivate}
    >
      {/* Top bar with window controls */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-2 py-1">
        <span className="text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">
          {panel.id}
        </span>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            className="h-6 w-6"
            onClick={(e) => {
              e.stopPropagation();
              toggleMinimize(panel.id);
            }}
          >
            <Minus className="h-3 w-3" />
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            className="h-6 w-6 hover:bg-destructive hover:text-destructive-foreground"
            onClick={(e) => {
              e.stopPropagation();
              onClose();
            }}
          >
            <X className="h-3 w-3" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Source selector buttons */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 p-2">
        {(Object.keys(sourceConfig) as SourceType[]).map((source) => {
          const config = sourceConfig[source];
          const Icon = config.icon;
          const isSelected = panel.source === source;

          return (
            <button
              key={source}
              onClick={(e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                handleSourceChange(source);
              }}
              className={cn(
                'flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2.5 py-1.5 rounded-md text-xs font-medium transition-all duration-200',
                isSelected
                  ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground scale-105 shadow-sm'
                  : 'bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground'
              )}
            >
              <Icon className={cn('h-3.5 w-3.5', isSelected ? '' : config.color)} />
              <span className="hidden sm:inline">{config.label}</span>
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {/* Path breadcrumb */}
      <div className="px-3 pb-2">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
          <span className="font-medium">{sourceConfig[panel.source].label}</span>
          {panel.path !== '/' && (
            <>
              <span>/</span>
              <span className="truncate">{panel.path}</span>
            </>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

5. `src/components/Panel/PanelContent.tsx`

```typescript
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { FileSystemEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';
import { StoragePanel } from './StoragePanel';
import { PlaceholderPanel } from './PlaceholderPanel';

interface PanelContentProps {
  panel: PanelState;
}

export function PanelContent({ panel }: PanelContentProps) {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState<FileSystemEntry[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const refreshPanelDirectory = usePanelStore((s) => s.refreshPanelDirectory);

  // Load entries when handle changes
  useEffect(() => {
    if (panel.source === 'storage' && panel.handle) {
      setIsLoading(true);
      fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle)
        .then(setEntries)
        .finally(() => setIsLoading(false));
    }
  }, [panel.handle, panel.source, panel.id]);

  // Refresh handler
  const handleRefresh = async () => {
    if (!panel.handle) return;
    setIsLoading(true);
    const newEntries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
    setEntries(newEntries);
    setIsLoading(false);
  };

  switch (panel.source) {
    case 'storage':
      return (
        <StoragePanel
          panel={panel}
          entries={entries}
          isLoading={isLoading}
          onRefresh={handleRefresh}
        />
      );
    case 'drive':
    case 'github':
    case 'terminal':
      return <PlaceholderPanel panel={panel} source={panel.source} />;
    default:
      return null;
  }
}
```

6. `src/components/Panel/StoragePanel.tsx`

```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Toolbar } from '../FileManager/Toolbar';
import { FileGrid } from '../FileManager/FileGrid';
import { FileList } from '../FileManager/FileList';
import { CreateFolderDialog } from '../FileManager/CreateFolderDialog';
import { MountPointsView } from '../FileManager/MountPointsView';
import { HardDrive, SdCard } from 'lucide-react';

interface StoragePanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  isLoading: boolean;
  onRefresh: () => void;
}

const mountPoints = [
  { id: 'internal', name: 'Internal Storage', icon: HardDrive },
  { id: 'sd-card', name: 'SD Card', icon: SdCard },
];

export function StoragePanel({ panel, entries, isLoading, onRefresh }: StoragePanelProps) {
  const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const {
    setPanelViewMode,
    setPanelSortBy,
    navigatePanelForward,
    navigatePanelBack,
    pickDirectoryForPanel,
  } = usePanelStore();

  const handleNavigateTo = (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => {
    navigatePanelForward(panel.id, entry.handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle, entry.name);
  };

  const handlePickDirectory = async () => {
    await pickDirectoryForPanel(panel.id);
  };

  const getSortedEntries = (): FileSystemEntry[] => {
    const sorted = [...entries];
    switch (panel.sortBy) {
      case 'name-asc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
      case 'name-desc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
      case 'date':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.lastModified.getTime() - a.lastModified.getTime());
      case 'size':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.size - a.size);
      default:
        return sorted;
    }
  };

  // If no directory selected, show mount points
  if (!panel.handle) {
    return (
      <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
        <div className="p-4 border-b border-border">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">Select Storage</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
          {mountPoints.map((mount) => {
            const Icon = mount.icon;
            return (
              <button
                key={mount.id}
                onClick={handlePickDirectory}
                className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent transition-all text-left"
              >
                <div className="p-2 rounded-lg bg-primary/10 text-primary">
                  <Icon className="w-6 h-6" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="font-medium text-foreground">{mount.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Click to browse</p>
                </div>
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <Toolbar
        viewMode={panel.viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={(mode) => setPanelViewMode(panel.id, mode)}
        sortBy={panel.sortBy}
        onSortChange={(sort) => setPanelSortBy(panel.id, sort)}
        onCreateFolder={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}
        onNavigateBack={() => navigatePanelBack(panel.id)}
        onRefresh={onRefresh}
        canGoBack={panel.history.length > 0}
        isLoading={isLoading}
        currentPath={panel.path}
      />

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {entries.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p className="text-sm">Empty folder</p>
            <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="mt-2" onClick={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}>
              Create folder
            </Button>
          </div>
        ) : panel.viewMode === 'grid' ? (
          <FileGrid entries={getSortedEntries()} onNavigate={handleNavigateTo} />
        ) : (
          <FileList entries={getSortedEntries()} onNavigate={handleNavigateTo} />
        )}
      </div>

      <CreateFolderDialog
        open={createDialogOpen}
        onOpenChange={setCreateFolderOpen}
        panelId={panel.id}
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

7. `src/components/Panel/PlaceholderPanel.tsx`

```typescript
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';
import { HardDrive, FolderGit, Github, Terminal } from 'lucide-react';

const sourceIcons: Record<SourceType, React.ElementType> = {
  storage: HardDrive,
  drive: FolderGit,
  github: Github,
  terminal: Terminal,
};

const sourceLabels: Record<SourceType, string> = {
  storage: 'Storage',
  drive: 'Google Drive',
  github: 'GitHub',
  terminal: 'Terminal',
};

interface PlaceholderPanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  source: SourceType;
}

export function PlaceholderPanel({ panel, source }: PlaceholderPanelProps) {
  const Icon = sourceIcons[source];
  const label = sourceLabels[source];

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 text-center">
      <div className="p-4 rounded-xl bg-primary/10 text-primary mb-4">
        <Icon className="w-12 h-12" />
      </div>
      <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground mb-2">{label}</h3>
      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground max-w-xs">
        This {label} panel is independent from other panels.
        <br />
        Source: <span className="font-medium capitalize">{panel.source}</span>
      </p>
      <div className="mt-4 p-3 rounded-lg bg-muted text-xs text-muted-foreground">
        Panel ID: {panel.id}
        <br />
        Path: {panel.path}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

8. `src/components/Panel/ResizablePanel.tsx`

```typescript
import { useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { useResizable } from '@/hooks/useResizable';
import { PanelHeader } from './PanelHeader';
import { PanelContent } from './PanelContent';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { MIN_PANEL_WIDTH } from '@/types/panel';

interface ResizablePanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  isActive: boolean;
  isLast: boolean;
  onActivate: () => void;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export function ResizablePanel({ 
  panel, 
  isActive, 
  isLast,
  onActivate, 
  onClose 
}: ResizablePanelProps) {
  const setPanelWidth = usePanelStore((s) => s.setPanelWidth);
  
  const { width, isResizing, startResize } = useResizable({
    initialWidth: panel.width,
    minWidth: MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
    onResize: (newWidth) => setPanelWidth(panel.id, newWidth),
  });

  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'flex flex-col h-full relative border-r border-border last:border-r-0',
        isActive && 'ring-1 ring-primary/20',
        isResizing && 'select-none'
      )}
      style={{ 
        width: panel.isMinimized ? 60 : width,
        minWidth: panel.isMinimized ? 60 : MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
        flexShrink: 0,
      }}
    >
      <PanelHeader
        panel={panel}
        isActive={isActive}
        onActivate={onActivate}
        onClose={onClose}
      />
      
      {!panel.isMinimized && (
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
          <PanelContent panel={panel} />
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Resize handle */}
      {!isLast && !panel.isMinimized && (
        <div
          className={cn(
            'absolute right-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-1 cursor-col-resize z-10',
            'hover:bg-primary/50 transition-colors',
            isResizing && 'bg-primary'
          )}
          onMouseDown={startResize}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

9. `src/components/PanelContainer.tsx` (Main Container)

```typescript
import { Plus } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { usePanelStore, usePanels, useActivePanelId, usePanelCount } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { ResizablePanel } from './Panel/ResizablePanel';
import { MAX_PANELS } from '@/types/panel';

export function PanelContainer() {
  const panels = usePanels();
  const activePanelId = useActivePanelId();
  const panelCount = usePanelCount();
  const { addPanel, removePanel, setActivePanel } = usePanelStore();

  const canAddPanel = panelCount < MAX_PANELS;

  return (
    <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden bg-background">
      {/* Top bar with Add Panel button */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b border-border bg-card">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">
            Panels: {panelCount}/{MAX_PANELS}
          </span>
        </div>
        
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          onClick={addPanel}
          disabled={!canAddPanel}
          className="gap-2"
        >
          <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
          Add Panel
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* Panels container */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-x-auto overflow-y-hidden">
        {panels.map((panel, index) => (
          <ResizablePanel
            key={panel.id}
            panel={panel}
            isActive={panel.id === activePanelId}
            isLast={index === panels.length - 1}
            onActivate={() => setActivePanel(panel.id)}
            onClose={() => removePanel(panel.id)}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

11. `src/components/FileManager/FileGrid.tsx` (Updated with onNavigate)

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, FolderOpen } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';

interface FileGridProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  onNavigate: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => void;
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

export function FileGrid({ entries, onNavigate }: FileGridProps) {
  const handleClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      onNavigate(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-3 p-3">
      {entries.map((entry) => (
        <button
          key={entry.name}
          onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}
          className="group flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent transition-all text-left"
        >
          <div className="mb-2 text-primary group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform">
            {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
              <FolderOpen className="w-10 h-10" />
            ) : (
              <File className="w-10 h-10" />
            )}
          </div>
          
          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate w-full text-center" title={entry.name}>
            {entry.name}
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
            {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : 'Folder'}
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
          </p>
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, Folder } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';

interface FileListProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  onNavigate: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => void;
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

export function FileList({ entries, onNavigate }: FileListProps) {
  const handleClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      onNavigate(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground bg-muted/50">
        <div className="col-span-6">Name</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Size</div>
        <div className="col-span-4">Modified</div>
      </div>

      {entries.map((entry) => (
        <button
          key={entry.name}
          onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}
          className="w-full grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left items-center"
        >
          <div className="col-span-6 flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
            {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
              <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
            ) : (
              <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
            )}
            <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={entry.name}>
              {entry.name}
            </span>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-2 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
            {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : '-'}
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-4 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
            {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
          </div>
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

13. `src/components/FileManager/CreateFolderDialog.tsx` (Updated with panelId)

```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';

interface CreateFolderDialogProps {
  open: boolean;
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
  panelId: string;
}

export function CreateFolderDialog({ open, onOpenChange, panelId }: CreateFolderDialogProps) {
  const [folderName, setFolderName] = useState('');
  const [isCreating, setIsCreating] = useState(false);
  const panel = usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(panelId));

  const handleCreate = async () => {
    if (!folderName.trim() || !panel?.handle) return;
    
    setIsCreating(true);
    try {
      await fileSystemBackend.createDirectory(panel.handle, folderName.trim());
      // Refresh will happen via parent component
      onOpenChange(false);
      setFolderName('');
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Failed to create folder:', err);
    } finally {
      setIsCreating(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <Dialog open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
      <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle>Create New Folder</DialogTitle>
          <DialogDescription>
            Enter a name for the new folder.
          </DialogDescription>
        </DialogHeader>
        
        <div className="py-4">
          <Input
            placeholder="Folder name"
            value={folderName}
            onChange={(e) => setFolderName(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={(e) => {
              if (e.key === 'Enter') handleCreate();
            }}
            autoFocus
          />
        </div>

        <DialogFooter>
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}>
            Cancel
          </Button>
          <Button 
            onClick={handleCreate} 
            disabled={!folderName.trim() || isCreating}
          >
            {isCreating ? 'Creating...' : 'Create'}
          </Button>
        </DialogFooter>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```
