1. `src/types/drive.ts` (Drive Types)

```typescript
export interface GoogleAccount {
  id: string; // Gmail address
  name: string; // User's display name
  picture?: string;
  accessToken: string;
  refreshToken?: string;
  expiresAt: number; // Timestamp
}

export interface DriveFile {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  mimeType: string;
  modifiedTime: string;
  size?: string;
  thumbnailLink?: string;
  iconLink?: string;
  webViewLink?: string;
  parents?: string[];
}

export interface DriveFolder {
  id: string;
  name: string;
}

export type DriveViewMode = 'grid' | 'list';
export type DriveSortBy = 'name-asc' | 'name-desc' | 'modifiedTime' | 'size';

export interface DrivePanelState {
  accounts: GoogleAccount[];
  activeAccountId: string | null;
  currentFolderId: string; // 'root' for root
  currentPath: DriveFolder[]; // Breadcrumb stack
  files: DriveFile[];
  viewMode: DriveViewMode;
  sortBy: DriveSortBy;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
}
```

2. `src/lib/googleDriveApi.ts` (Drive API Client)

```typescript
import { GoogleAccount, DriveFile, DriveFolder } from '@/types/drive';

const DISCOVERY_DOC = 'https://www.googleapis.com/discovery/v1/apis/drive/v3/rest';
const SCOPES = 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.readonly https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.file';

class GoogleDriveApi {
  private gapiInited = false;
  private gsiInited = false;
  private tokenClient: any = null;

  async initialize(gapi: any, tokenClient: any): Promise<void> {
    this.tokenClient = tokenClient;
    this.gsiInited = true;
    this.gapiInited = true;
  }

  async listFiles(account: GoogleAccount, folderId: string = 'root'): Promise<DriveFile[]> {
    const response = await fetch(
      `https://www.googleapis.com/drive/v3/files?q='${folderId}'+in+parents+and+trashed=false&fields=files(id,name,mimeType,modifiedTime,size,thumbnailLink,iconLink,webViewLink,parents)&orderBy=name&pageSize=100`,
      {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${account.accessToken}`,
        },
      }
    );

    if (!response.ok) {
      if (response.status === 401) {
        throw new Error('Token expired');
      }
      throw new Error(`Drive API error: ${response.status}`);
    }

    const data = await response.json();
    return data.files || [];
  }

  async getFileInfo(account: GoogleAccount, fileId: string): Promise<DriveFile> {
    const response = await fetch(
      `https://www.googleapis.com/drive/v3/files/${fileId}?fields=id,name,mimeType,modifiedTime,size,thumbnailLink,iconLink,webViewLink,parents`,
      {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${account.accessToken}`,
        },
      }
    );

    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to get file info: ${response.status}`);
    }

    return response.json();
  }

  isFolder(file: DriveFile): boolean {
    return file.mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder';
  }

  formatFileSize(size?: string): string {
    if (!size) return '-';
    const bytes = parseInt(size, 10);
    if (isNaN(bytes)) return '-';
    
    const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
    let unitIndex = 0;
    let sizeNum = bytes;
    
    while (sizeNum >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
      sizeNum /= 1024;
      unitIndex++;
    }
    
    return `${sizeNum.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
  }

  formatDate(dateString: string): string {
    const date = new Date(dateString);
    return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
      month: 'short',
      day: 'numeric',
      year: 'numeric',
    });
  }

  getGmailUsername(email: string): string {
    return email.split('@')[0];
  }
}

export const driveApi = new GoogleDriveApi();
```

3. `src/stores/driveStore.ts` (Drive Panel Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { 
  GoogleAccount, 
  DriveFile, 
  DriveFolder,
  DriveViewMode,
  DriveSortBy,
  DrivePanelState 
} from '@/types/drive';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';

interface DriveStore extends DrivePanelState {
  // Actions
  addAccount: (account: GoogleAccount) => void;
  removeAccount: (id: string) => void;
  setActiveAccount: (id: string | null) => void;
  setCurrentFolder: (folderId: string, folderName?: string) => Promise<void>;
  navigateToFolder: (file: DriveFile) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateToRoot: () => void;
  setViewMode: (mode: DriveViewMode) => void;
  setSortBy: (sort: DriveSortBy) => void;
  refreshCurrent: () => Promise<void>;
  logout: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getActiveAccount: () => GoogleAccount | undefined;
  getSortedFiles: () => DriveFile[];
  getCurrentFolderName: () => string;
}

const createInitialState = (): DrivePanelState => ({
  accounts: [],
  activeAccountId: null,
  currentFolderId: 'root',
  currentPath: [],
  files: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
});

export const useDriveStore = create<DriveStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    ...createInitialState(),

    addAccount: (account) => {
      set((state) => {
        // Check if account already exists
        const existingIndex = state.accounts.findIndex(a => a.id === account.id);
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
          // Update existing account with new token
          state.accounts[existingIndex] = account;
        } else {
          state.accounts.push(account);
        }
        // Set as active if no active account
        if (!state.activeAccountId) {
          state.activeAccountId = account.id;
        }
      });
      // Load root files for new account
      get().setCurrentFolder('root', 'My Drive');
    },

    removeAccount: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.accounts = state.accounts.filter(a => a.id !== id);
        if (state.activeAccountId === id) {
          state.activeAccountId = state.accounts[0]?.id || null;
        }
      });
    },

    setActiveAccount: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.activeAccountId = id;
        state.currentFolderId = 'root';
        state.currentPath = [];
        state.files = [];
      });
      if (id) {
        get().setCurrentFolder('root', 'My Drive');
      }
    },

    setCurrentFolder: async (folderId, folderName) => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId) return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        const files = await driveApi.listFiles(account, folderId);
        set((state) => {
          state.currentFolderId = folderId;
          state.files = files;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateToFolder: async (file) => {
      if (!driveApi.isFolder(file)) return;
      
      const { currentPath } = get();
      
      set((state) => {
        state.currentPath.push({ id: state.currentFolderId, name: state.currentPath.length === 0 ? 'My Drive' : file.name });
      });
      
      await get().setCurrentFolder(file.id, file.name);
    },

    navigateBack: async () => {
      const { currentPath } = get();
      if (currentPath.length === 0) return;

      const parent = currentPath[currentPath.length - 1];
      set((state) => {
        state.currentPath.pop();
      });
      
      await get().setCurrentFolder(parent.id, parent.name);
    },

    navigateToRoot: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.currentFolderId = 'root';
        state.currentPath = [];
      });
      get().setCurrentFolder('root', 'My Drive');
    },

    setViewMode: (mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setSortBy: (sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    refreshCurrent: async () => {
      const { currentFolderId } = get();
      await get().setCurrentFolder(currentFolderId);
    },

    logout: () => {
      set(createInitialState());
    },

    getActiveAccount: () => {
      const { accounts, activeAccountId } = get();
      return accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
    },

    getSortedFiles: () => {
      const { files, sortBy } = get();
      const sorted = [...files];
      
      switch (sortBy) {
        case 'name-asc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
        case 'name-desc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
        case 'modifiedTime':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.modifiedTime).getTime() - new Date(a.modifiedTime).getTime());
        case 'size':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => {
            const sizeA = parseInt(a.size || '0', 10);
            const sizeB = parseInt(b.size || '0', 10);
            return sizeB - sizeA;
          });
        default:
          return sorted;
      }
    },

    getCurrentFolderName: () => {
      const { currentPath, currentFolderId } = get();
      if (currentFolderId === 'root') return 'My Drive';
      const current = currentPath[currentPath.length - 1];
      return current?.name || 'My Drive';
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useDriveAccounts = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.accounts);
export const useDriveActiveAccount = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.getActiveAccount());
export const useDriveFiles = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.getSortedFiles());
export const useDriveViewMode = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.viewMode);
export const useDriveSortBy = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.sortBy);
export const useDriveCurrentPath = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.currentPath);
export const useDriveIsLoading = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.isLoading);
export const useDriveError = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.error);
```

4. `src/components/GoogleDrive/GoogleDriveProvider.tsx` (OAuth Provider)

```typescript
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { GoogleOAuthProvider, useGoogleLogin } from '@react-oauth/google';
import { useDriveStore } from '@/stores/driveStore';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';

const CLIENT_ID = import.meta.env.VITE_GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID || '';

interface GoogleDriveProviderProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export function GoogleDriveProvider({ children }: GoogleDriveProviderProps) {
  return (
    <GoogleOAuthProvider clientId={CLIENT_ID}>
      {children}
    </GoogleOAuthProvider>
  );
}

// Hook for Google Login
export function useGoogleDriveAuth() {
  const addAccount = useDriveStore((s) => s.addAccount);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  const login = useGoogleLogin({
    onSuccess: async (tokenResponse) => {
      setIsLoading(true);
      try {
        // Fetch user info
        const userInfoResponse = await fetch(
          'https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v3/userinfo',
          {
            headers: {
              Authorization: `Bearer ${tokenResponse.access_token}`,
            },
          }
        );
        
        if (!userInfoResponse.ok) {
          throw new Error('Failed to fetch user info');
        }

        const userInfo = await userInfoResponse.json();

        const account = {
          id: userInfo.email,
          name: userInfo.name,
          picture: userInfo.picture,
          accessToken: tokenResponse.access_token,
          expiresAt: Date.now() + (tokenResponse.expires_in || 3600) * 1000,
        };

        addAccount(account);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Login error:', err);
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    },
    onError: (error) => {
      console.error('Login Failed:', error);
    },
    scope: 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.readonly https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.file',
  });

  return { login, isLoading };
}
```

5. `src/components/GoogleDrive/AccountSelector.tsx`

```typescript
import { Plus, X, User } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useDriveStore, useDriveAccounts, useDriveActiveAccount } from '@/stores/driveStore';
import { useGoogleDriveAuth } from './GoogleDriveProvider';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';

export function AccountSelector() {
  const accounts = useDriveAccounts();
  const activeAccount = useDriveActiveAccount();
  const setActiveAccount = useDriveStore((s) => s.setActiveAccount);
  const removeAccount = useDriveStore((s) => s.removeAccount);
  const { login, isLoading } = useGoogleDriveAuth();

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <div className="p-4 border-b border-border">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground">Google Drive</h2>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          {accounts.length === 0 
            ? 'Connect your Google account to access Drive'
            : `${accounts.length} account${accounts.length > 1 ? 's' : ''} connected`
          }
        </p>
      </div>

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4">
        {accounts.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full space-y-4">
            <div className="p-4 rounded-full bg-primary/10">
              <User className="w-12 h-12 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center">
              No accounts connected
            </p>
            <Button onClick={() => login()} disabled={isLoading}>
              {isLoading ? 'Connecting...' : 'Connect Google Account'}
            </Button>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {accounts.map((account) => {
              const isActive = activeAccount?.id === account.id;
              const username = driveApi.getGmailUsername(account.id);
              
              return (
                <button
                  key={account.id}
                  onClick={() => setActiveAccount(account.id)}
                  className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg border transition-all text-left ${
                    isActive 
                      ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5' 
                      : 'border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent'
                  }`}
                >
                  {account.picture ? (
                    <img 
                      src={account.picture} 
                      alt={account.name}
                      className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full"
                    />
                  ) : (
                    <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                      <User className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
                    </div>
                  )}
                  
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="font-medium text-foreground truncate">
                      {username}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
                      {account.name}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-8 w-8 shrink-0"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      removeAccount(account.id);
                    }}
                  >
                    <X className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Add Account Button */}
      {accounts.length > 0 && (
        <div className="p-4 border-t border-border">
          <Button 
            variant="outline" 
            className="w-full gap-2"
            onClick={() => login()}
            disabled={isLoading}
          >
            <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
            Add Account
          </Button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { 
  Grid3X3, 
  List, 
  ArrowLeft, 
  RefreshCw,
  ArrowUpDown,
  ChevronDown,
  LogOut
} from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Toggle } from '@/components/ui/toggle';
import {
  DropdownMenu,
  DropdownMenuContent,
  DropdownMenuItem,
  DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import { DriveViewMode, DriveSortBy } from '@/types/drive';
import { useDriveStore, useDriveCurrentPath, useDriveIsLoading, useDriveActiveAccount } from '@/stores/driveStore';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';

interface DriveToolbarProps {
  viewMode: DriveViewMode;
  onViewModeChange: (mode: DriveViewMode) => void;
  sortBy: DriveSortBy;
  onSortChange: (sort: DriveSortBy) => void;
  onNavigateBack: () => void;

  onLogout: () => void;

const sortLabels: Record<DriveSortBy, string> = {
  'name-asc': 'Name (A-Z)',
  'name-desc': 'Name (Z-A)',
  'modifiedTime': 'Date Modified',
  'size': 'Size',
};

export function DriveToolbar({
  viewMode,
  onViewModeChange,
  sortBy,
  onSortChange,
  onNavigateBack,
  onRefresh,
  onLogout,
  currentFolderName,
}: DriveToolbarProps) {

  const isLoading = useDriveIsLoading();

          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Right: Actions */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">

            {driveApi.getGmailUsername(activeAccount.id)}

              Size

      </div>

  );
```

7. `src/components/GoogleDrive/DriveFileGrid.tsx`

```typescript
import { Folder, FileText, Image, FileSpreadsheet, FileCode, MoreHorizontal } from 'lucide-react';
import { DriveFile } from '@/types/drive';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface DriveFileGridProps {
  files: DriveFile[];
  onFolderClick: (file: DriveFile) => void;
  onFileClick?: (file: DriveFile) => void;
}

function getFileIcon(mimeType: string) {
  if (mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder') {
    return Folder;
  }
  if (mimeType.startsWith('image/')) {
    return Image;
  }
  if (mimeType.includes('spreadsheet') || mimeType.includes('excel')) {
    return FileSpreadsheet;
  }
  if (mimeType.includes('document') || mimeType.includes('word')) {
    return FileText;
  }
  if (mimeType.includes('code') || mimeType.includes('json') || mimeType.includes('javascript')) {
    return FileCode;
  }
  return FileText;
}

export function DriveFileGrid({ files, onFolderClick, onFileClick }: DriveFileGridProps) {
  const handleClick = (file: DriveFile) => {
    if (driveApi.isFolder(file)) {
      onFolderClick(file);
    } else if (onFileClick) {
      onFileClick(file);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-3 p-3">
      {files.map((file) => {
        const Icon = getFileIcon(file.mimeType);
        const isFolder = driveApi.isFolder(file);
        
        return (
          <button
            key={file.id}
            onClick={() => handleClick(file)}
            className={cn(
              "group flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent transition-all text-left",
              isFolder && "hover:border-primary/50"
            )}
          >
            {/* Thumbnail or Icon */}
            <div className="mb-3 relative">
              {file.thumbnailLink && !isFolder ? (
                <img 
                  src={file.thumbnailLink} 
                  alt={file.name}
                  className="w-20 h-20 object-cover rounded-lg"
                />
              ) : (
                <div className={cn(
                  "p-4 rounded-lg",
                  isFolder ? "bg-primary/10 text-primary" : "bg-muted text-muted-foreground"
                )}>
                  <Icon className="w-10 h-10" />
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
            
            {/* File Info */}
            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate w-full text-center" title={file.name}>
              {file.name}
            </p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
              {isFolder ? 'Folder' : driveApi.formatFileSize(file.size)}
            </p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              {driveApi.formatDate(file.modifiedTime)}
            </p>
          </button>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}
```

8. `src/components/GoogleDrive/DriveFileList.tsx`

```typescript
import { Folder, FileText, Image, FileSpreadsheet, FileCode, ExternalLink } from 'lucide-react';
import { DriveFile } from '@/types/drive';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

interface DriveFileListProps {
  files: DriveFile[];
  onFolderClick: (file: DriveFile) => void;
  onFileClick?: (file: DriveFile) => void;
}

function getFileIcon(mimeType: string) {
  if (mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder') {
    return Folder;
  }
  if (mimeType.startsWith('image/')) {
    return Image;
  }
  if (mimeType.includes('spreadsheet') || mimeType.includes('excel')) {
    return FileSpreadsheet;
  }
  if (mimeType.includes('document') || mimeType.includes('word')) {
    return FileText;
  }
  if (mimeType.includes('code') || mimeType.includes('json')) {
    return FileCode;
  }
  return FileText;
}

export function DriveFileList({ files, onFolderClick, onFileClick }: DriveFileListProps) {
  const handleClick = (file: DriveFile) => {
    if (driveApi.isFolder(file)) {
      onFolderClick(file);
    } else if (onFileClick) {
      onFileClick(file);
    }
  };

  const handleOpenFile = (e: React.MouseEvent, file: DriveFile) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    if (file.webViewLink) {
      window.open(file.webViewLink, '_blank');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground bg-muted/50">
        <div className="col-span-6">Name</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Size</div>
        <div className="col-span-3">Modified</div>
        <div className="col-span-1"></div>
      </div>

      {/* Files */}
      {files.map((file) => {
        const Icon = getFileIcon(file.mimeType);
        const isFolder = driveApi.isFolder(file);
        
        return (
          <button
            key={file.id}
            onClick={() => handleClick(file)}
            className="w-full grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left items-center group"
          >
            <div className="col-span-6 flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
              <Icon className={cn(
                "w-4 h-4 shrink-0",
                isFolder ? "text-primary" : "text-muted-foreground"
              )} />
              <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={file.name}>
                {file.name}
              </span>
            </div>
            
            <div className="col-span-2 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
              {isFolder ? '-' : driveApi.formatFileSize(file.size)}
            </div>
            
            <div className="col-span-3 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
              {driveApi.formatDate(file.modifiedTime)}
            </div>

            <div className="col-span-1 flex justify-end">
              {!isFolder && file.webViewLink && (
                <Button
                  variant="ghost"
                  size="icon"
                  className="h-6 w-6 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100"
                  onClick={(e) => handleOpenFile(e, file)}
                >
                  <ExternalLink className="h-3 w-3" />
                </Button>
              )}
            </div>
          </button>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}
```

9. `src/components/GoogleDrive/DrivePanel.tsx` (Main Drive Panel)

```typescript
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { AccountSelector } from './AccountSelector';
import { DriveToolbar } from './DriveToolbar';
import { DriveFileGrid } from './DriveFileGrid';
import { DriveFileList } from './DriveFileList';
import { useDriveStore, useDriveFiles, useDriveViewMode, useDriveSortBy, useDriveActiveAccount, useDriveError } from '@/stores/driveStore';
import { DriveFile } from '@/types/drive';
import { GoogleDriveProvider } from './GoogleDriveProvider';

function DrivePanelContent() {
  const files = useDriveFiles();
  const viewMode = useDriveViewMode();
  const sortBy = useDriveSortBy();
  const activeAccount = useDriveActiveAccount();
  const error = useDriveError();
  
  const {
    setViewMode,
    setSortBy,
    navigateToFolder,
    navigateBack,
    refreshCurrent,
    navigateToRoot,
    setActiveAccount,
  } = useDriveStore();

  const currentFolderName = useDriveStore((s) => s.getCurrentFolderName());

  // Refresh when account changes
  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeAccount) {
      navigateToRoot();
    }
  }, [activeAccount?.id]);

  const handleFolderClick = (file: DriveFile) => {
    navigateToFolder(file);
  };

  const handleFileClick = (file: DriveFile) => {
    if (file.webViewLink) {
      window.open(file.webViewLink, '_blank');
    }
  };

  const handleBackToAccounts = () => {
    setActiveAccount(null);
  };

  // Show account selector if no active account
  if (!activeAccount) {
    return <AccountSelector />;
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <DriveToolbar
        viewMode={viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={setViewMode}
        sortBy={sortBy}
        onSortChange={setSortBy}
        onNavigateBack={navigateBack}
        onRefresh={refreshCurrent}
        onLogout={handleBackToAccounts}
        currentFolderName={currentFolderName}
      />

      {error && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-destructive/10 text-destructive text-sm text-center">
          {error}
          <button 
            onClick={refreshCurrent}
            className="ml-2 underline hover:no-underline"
          >
            Retry
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {files.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p className="text-sm">Empty folder</p>
          </div>
        ) : viewMode === 'grid' ? (
          <DriveFileGrid 
            files={files} 
            onFolderClick={handleFolderClick}
            onFileClick={handleFileClick}
          />
        ) : (
          <DriveFileList 
            files={files} 
            onFolderClick={handleFolderClick}
            onFileClick={handleFileClick}
          />
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Add Account Button - Bottom Center */}
      <div className="p-3 border-t border-border flex justify-center">
        <button
          onClick={handleBackToAccounts}
          className="text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors"
        >
          Switch Account
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function DrivePanel() {
  return (
    <GoogleDriveProvider>
      <DrivePanelContent />
    </GoogleDriveProvider>
  );
}
```

10. `src/components/Panel/PanelContent.tsx` (Updated with Drive)

```typescript
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { FileSystemEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';
import { StoragePanel } from './StoragePanel';
import { PlaceholderPanel } from './PlaceholderPanel';
import { DrivePanel } from '../GoogleDrive/DrivePanel';

interface PanelContentProps {
  panel: PanelState;
}

export function PanelContent({ panel }: PanelContentProps) {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState<FileSystemEntry[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const refreshPanelDirectory = usePanelStore((s) => s.refreshPanelDirectory);

  // Load entries when handle changes (for storage)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (panel.source === 'storage' && panel.handle) {
      setIsLoading(true);
      fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle)
        .then(setEntries)
        .finally(() => setIsLoading(false));
    }
  }, [panel.handle, panel.source, panel.id]);

  // Refresh handler
  const handleRefresh = async () => {
    if (!panel.handle) return;
    setIsLoading(true);
    const newEntries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
    setEntries(newEntries);
    setIsLoading(false);
  };

  switch (panel.source) {
    case 'storage':
      return (
        <StoragePanel
          panel={panel}
          entries={entries}
          isLoading={isLoading}
          onRefresh={handleRefresh}
        />
      );
    case 'drive':
      return <DrivePanel />;
    case 'github':
    case 'terminal':
      return <PlaceholderPanel panel={panel} source={panel.source} />;
    default:
      return null;
  }
}
```

11. `src/components/Panel/StoragePanel.tsx` (Updated - remove duplicate import)

```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { Toolbar } from '../FileManager/Toolbar';
import { FileGrid } from '../FileManager/FileGrid';
import { FileList } from '../FileManager/FileList';
import { CreateFolderDialog } from '../FileManager/CreateFolderDialog';
import { MountPointsView } from '../FileManager/MountPointsView';
import { HardDrive, SdCard } from 'lucide-react';

interface StoragePanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  isLoading: boolean;
  onRefresh: () => void;
}

const mountPoints = [
  { id: 'internal', name: 'Internal Storage', icon: HardDrive },
  { id: 'sd-card', name: 'SD Card', icon: SdCard },
];

export function StoragePanel({ panel, entries, isLoading, onRefresh }: StoragePanelProps) {
  const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const {
    setPanelViewMode,
    setPanelSortBy,
    navigatePanelForward,
    navigatePanelBack,
    pickDirectoryForPanel,
  } = usePanelStore();

  const handleNavigateTo = (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => {
    navigatePanelForward(panel.id, entry.handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle, entry.name);
  };

  const handlePickDirectory = async () => {
    await pickDirectoryForPanel(panel.id);
  };

  const getSortedEntries = (): FileSystemEntry[] => {
    const sorted = [...entries];
    switch (panel.sortBy) {
      case 'name-asc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
      case 'name-desc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
      case 'date':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.lastModified.getTime() - a.lastModified.getTime());
      case 'size':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.size - a.size);
      default:
        return sorted;
    }
  };

  // If no directory selected, show mount points
  if (!panel.handle) {
    return (
      <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
        <div className="p-4 border-b border-border">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">Select Storage</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
          {mountPoints.map((mount) => {
            const Icon = mount.icon;
            return (
              <button
                key={mount.id}
                onClick={handlePickDirectory}
                className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent transition-all text-left"
              >
                <div className="p-2 rounded-lg bg-primary/10 text-primary">
                  <Icon className="w-6 h-6" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="font-medium text-foreground">{mount.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Click to browse</p>
                </div>
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <Toolbar
        viewMode={panel.viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={(mode) => setPanelViewMode(panel.id, mode)}
        sortBy={panel.sortBy}
        onSortChange={(sort) => setPanelSortBy(panel.id, sort)}
        onCreateFolder={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}
        onNavigateBack={() => navigatePanelBack(panel.id)}
        onRefresh={onRefresh}
        canGoBack={panel.history.length > 0}
        isLoading={isLoading}
        currentPath={panel.path}
      />

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {entries.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p className="text-sm">Empty folder</p>
          </div>
        ) : panel.viewMode === 'grid' ? (
          <FileGrid entries={getSortedEntries()} onNavigate={handleNavigateTo} />
        ) : (
          <FileList entries={getSortedEntries()} onNavigate={handleNavigateTo} />
        )}
      </div>

      <CreateFolderDialog
        open={createDialogOpen}
        onOpenChange={setCreateDialogOpen}
        panelId={panel.id}
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

1. `src/types/github.ts` (GitHub Types)

```typescript
export interface GitHubAccount {
  id: string; // Username
  token: string; // Encrypted PAT
  avatarUrl?: string;
  permissions: GitHubPermission;
  addedAt: number;
}

export type GitHubPermission = 'read' | 'triage' | 'write' | 'admin';

export interface GitHubRepository {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  full_name: string;
  description: string | null;
  updated_at: string;
  pushed_at: string;
  stargazers_count: number;
  language: string | null;
  private: boolean;
  html_url: string;
  default_branch: string;
}

export interface GitHubContent {
  name: string;
  path: string;
  type: 'file' | 'dir' | 'symlink' | 'submodule';
  size: number;
  html_url: string;
  download_url: string | null;
  content?: string; // Base64 encoded for files
  encoding?: string;
}

export type GitHubViewMode = 'grid' | 'list';
export type GitHubSortBy = 'name-asc' | 'name-desc' | 'updated' | 'stars';

export interface GitHubPanelState {
  accounts: GitHubAccount[];
  activeAccountId: string | null;
  currentRepository: string | null;
  currentPath: string; // Empty string for root
  pathHistory: string[]; // For back navigation
  repositories: GitHubRepository[];
  contents: GitHubContent[];
  viewMode: GitHubViewMode;
  sortBy: GitHubSortBy;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  fileContent: string | null;
  fileName: string | null;
}
```

2. `src/lib/githubStorage.ts` (Encrypted IndexedDB Storage)

```typescript
import { openDB, DBSchema, IDBPDatabase } from 'idb';
import { GitHubAccount } from '@/types/github';
import CryptoJS from 'crypto-js';

const DB_NAME = 'github-accounts-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;
const STORE_NAME = 'accounts';

// Encryption key - in production, use a more secure method
const ENCRYPTION_KEY = import.meta.env.VITE_GITHUB_ENCRYPTION_KEY || 'your-secure-key-here';

interface GitHubDBSchema extends DBSchema {
  accounts: {
    key: string;
    value: {
      id: string;
      encryptedData: string;
      addedAt: number;
    };
  };
}

class GitHubStorage {
  private db: IDBPDatabase<GitHubDBSchema> | null = null;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.db = await openDB<GitHubDBSchema>(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
      upgrade(db) {
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE_NAME)) {
          db.createObjectStore(STORE_NAME, { keyPath: 'id' });
        }
      },
    });
  }

  private encrypt(data: string): string {
    return CryptoJS.AES.encrypt(data, ENCRYPTION_KEY).toString();
  }

  private decrypt(encryptedData: string): string {
    const bytes = CryptoJS.AES.decrypt(encryptedData, ENCRYPTION_KEY);
    return bytes.toString(CryptoJS.enc.Utf8);
  }

  async saveAccount(account: GitHubAccount): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.db) await this.init();

    const dataToEncrypt = JSON.stringify({
      token: account.token,
      avatarUrl: account.avatarUrl,
      permissions: account.permissions,
    });

    await this.db!.put(STORE_NAME, {
      id: account.id,
      encryptedData: this.encrypt(dataToEncrypt),
      addedAt: account.addedAt,
    });
  }

  async getAllAccounts(): Promise<GitHubAccount[]> {
    if (!this.db) await this.init();

    const allData = await this.db!.getAll(STORE_NAME);
    
    return allData.map((item) => {
      try {
        const decrypted = JSON.parse(this.decrypt(item.encryptedData));
        return {
          id: item.id,
          token: decrypted.token,
          avatarUrl: decrypted.avatarUrl,
          permissions: decrypted.permissions,
          addedAt: item.addedAt,
        };
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('Failed to decrypt account:', item.id);
        return null;
      }
    }).filter((acc): acc is GitHubAccount => acc !== null);
  }

  async deleteAccount(username: string): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.db) await this.init();
    await this.db!.delete(STORE_NAME, username);
  }

  async clearAll(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.db) await this.init();
    await this.db!.clear(STORE_NAME);
  }
}

export const githubStorage = new GitHubStorage();
```

3. `src/lib/githubApi.ts` (Octokit API Client)

```typescript
import { Octokit } from '@octokit/rest';
import { 
  GitHubAccount, 
  GitHubRepository, 
  GitHubContent,
  GitHubPermission 
} from '@/types/github';

class GitHubApi {
  private octokit: Octokit | null = null;
  private currentToken: string | null = null;

  async authenticate(token: string): Promise<{ username: string; avatarUrl?: string }> {
    this.octokit = new Octokit({ auth: token });
    this.currentToken = token;

    try {
      const { data } = await this.octokit.users.getAuthenticated();
      return {
        username: data.login,
        avatarUrl: data.avatar_url,
      };
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Invalid token or authentication failed');
    }
  }

  setToken(token: string): void {
    this.octokit = new Octokit({ auth: token });
    this.currentToken = token;
  }

  async listRepositories(username: string): Promise<GitHubRepository[]> {
    if (!this.octokit) throw new Error('Not authenticated');

    try {
      const { data } = await this.octokit.repos.listForUser({
        username,
        sort: 'updated',
        per_page: 100,
      });
      return data as GitHubRepository[];
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch repositories');
    }
  }

  async getRepositoryContents(
    owner: string,
    repo: string,
    path: string = ''
  ): Promise<GitHubContent[]> {
    if (!this.octokit) throw new Error('Not authenticated');

    try {
      const { data } = await this.octokit.repos.getContent({
        owner,
        repo,
        path,
      });

      // Handle single file vs directory
      if (!Array.isArray(data)) {
        return [data as GitHubContent];
      }

      return data as GitHubContent[];
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch repository contents');
    }
  }

  async getFileContent(
    owner: string,
    repo: string,
    path: string
  ): Promise<{ content: string; name: string; downloadUrl: string | null }> {
    if (!this.octokit) throw new Error('Not authenticated');

    try {
      const { data } = await this.octokit.repos.getContent({
        owner,
        repo,
        path,
      });

      if (Array.isArray(data)) {
        throw new Error('Path is a directory, not a file');
      }

      const fileData = data as GitHubContent;
      
      // Decode base64 content
      let decodedContent = '';
      if (fileData.content && fileData.encoding === 'base64') {
        decodedContent = atob(fileData.content.replace(/\n/g, ''));
      }

      return {
        content: decodedContent,
        name: fileData.name,
        downloadUrl: fileData.download_url,
      };
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch file content');
    }
  }

  async validateToken(token: string): Promise<boolean> {
    try {
      const tempOctokit = new Octokit({ auth: token });
      await tempOctokit.users.getAuthenticated();
      return true;
    } catch {
      return false;
    }
  }

  getPermissionLevel(scopes: string[]): GitHubPermission {
    // Determine permission based on token scopes
    if (scopes.includes('delete_repo') || scopes.includes('admin:org')) {
      return 'admin';
    }
    if (scopes.includes('repo')) {
      return 'write';
    }
    if (scopes.includes('write:discussion')) {
      return 'triage';
    }
    return 'read';
  }

  formatDate(dateString: string): string {
    const date = new Date(dateString);
    return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
      month: 'short',
      day: 'numeric',
      year: 'numeric',
    });
  }

  formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
    if (bytes === 0) return '-';
    const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
    let size = bytes;
    let unitIndex = 0;
    while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
      size /= 1024;
      unitIndex++;
    }
    return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
  }
}

export const githubApi = new GitHubApi();
```

4. `src/stores/githubStore.ts` (GitHub Panel Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { 
  GitHubAccount, 
  GitHubRepository, 
  GitHubContent,
  GitHubViewMode,
  GitHubSortBy,
  GitHubPanelState,
  GitHubPermission 
} from '@/types/github';
import { githubApi } from '@/lib/githubApi';
import { githubStorage } from '@/lib/githubStorage';

interface GitHubStore extends GitHubPanelState {
  // Actions
  loadAccounts: () => Promise<void>;
  addAccount: (username: string, token: string) => Promise<void>;
  removeAccount: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  setActiveAccount: (id: string | null) => void;
  loadRepositories: () => Promise<void>;
  selectRepository: (repo: GitHubRepository) => Promise<void>;
  navigateToPath: (path: string) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateToRoot: () => void;
  openFile: (file: GitHubContent) => Promise<void>;
  closeFile: () => void;
  setViewMode: (mode: GitHubViewMode) => void;
  setSortBy: (sort: GitHubSortBy) => void;
  refreshCurrent: () => Promise<void>;
  logout: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getActiveAccount: () => GitHubAccount | undefined;
  getSortedRepositories: () => GitHubRepository[];
  getSortedContents: () => GitHubContent[];
  getCurrentBreadcrumb: () => string[];
  canGoBack: () => boolean;
}

const createInitialState = (): GitHubPanelState => ({
  accounts: [],
  activeAccountId: null,
  currentRepository: null,
  currentPath: '',
  pathHistory: [],
  repositories: [],
  contents: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'updated',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  fileContent: null,
  fileName: null,
});

export const useGitHubStore = create<GitHubStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    ...createInitialState(),

    loadAccounts: async () => {
      const accounts = await githubStorage.getAllAccounts();
      set((state) => {
        state.accounts = accounts;
      });
    },

    addAccount: async (username, token) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        // Validate token and get user info
        const userInfo = await githubApi.authenticate(token);
        
        // Check if account already exists
        const existing = get().accounts.find(a => a.id === userInfo.username);
        if (existing) {
          throw new Error('Account already exists');
        }

        const account: GitHubAccount = {
          id: userInfo.username,
          token,
          avatarUrl: userInfo.avatarUrl,
          permissions: 'read', // Will be updated based on token scopes
          addedAt: Date.now(),
        };

        // Save to encrypted storage
        await githubStorage.saveAccount(account);

        set((state) => {
          state.accounts.push(account);
          state.activeAccountId = account.id;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });

        // Load repositories for new account
        await get().loadRepositories();
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
        throw err;
      }
    },

    removeAccount: async (id) => {
      await githubStorage.deleteAccount(id);
      set((state) => {
        state.accounts = state.accounts.filter(a => a.id !== id);
        if (state.activeAccountId === id) {
          state.activeAccountId = null;
          state.currentRepository = null;
          state.currentPath = '';
          state.pathHistory = [];
          state.repositories = [];
          state.contents = [];
        }
      });
    },

    setActiveAccount: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.activeAccountId = id;
        state.currentRepository = null;
        state.currentPath = '';
        state.pathHistory = [];
        state.contents = [];
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });
      
      if (id) {
        get().loadRepositories();
      }
    },

    loadRepositories: async () => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId) return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const repos = await githubApi.listRepositories(account.id);
        set((state) => {
          state.repositories = repos;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    selectRepository: async (repo) => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId) return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
        state.currentRepository = repo.name;
        state.currentPath = '';
        state.pathHistory = [];
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const contents = await githubApi.getRepositoryContents(account.id, repo.name, '');
        set((state) => {
          state.contents = contents;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateToPath: async (path) => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts, currentRepository, currentPath } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId || !currentRepository) return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
        state.pathHistory.push(currentPath);
        state.currentPath = path;
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const contents = await githubApi.getRepositoryContents(account.id, currentRepository, path);
        set((state) => {
          state.contents = contents;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateBack: async () => {
      const { pathHistory, activeAccountId, accounts, currentRepository } = get();
      if (pathHistory.length === 0 || !activeAccountId || !currentRepository) {
        // Go back to repository root
        set((state) => {
          state.currentPath = '';
          state.pathHistory = [];
          state.fileContent = null;
          state.fileName = null;
        });
        await get().refreshCurrent();
        return;
      }

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      const previousPath = pathHistory[pathHistory.length - 1];

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
        state.pathHistory.pop();
        state.currentPath = previousPath;
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const contents = await githubApi.getRepositoryContents(account.id, currentRepository, previousPath);
        set((state) => {
          state.contents = contents;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateToRoot: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.currentRepository = null;
        state.currentPath = '';
        state.pathHistory = [];
        state.contents = [];
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });
    },

    openFile: async (file) => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts, currentRepository } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId || !currentRepository || file.type !== 'file') return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const fileData = await githubApi.getFileContent(account.id, currentRepository, file.path);
        set((state) => {
          state.fileContent = fileData.content;
          state.fileName = fileData.name;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    closeFile: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });
    },

    setViewMode: (mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setSortBy: (sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    refreshCurrent: async () => {
      const { currentRepository, currentPath, activeAccountId, accounts } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId || !currentRepository) {
        await get().loadRepositories();
        return;
      }

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const contents = await githubApi.getRepositoryContents(account.id, currentRepository, currentPath);
        set((state) => {
          state.contents = contents;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    logout: () => {
      set(createInitialState());
    },

    getActiveAccount: () => {
      const { accounts, activeAccountId } = get();
      return accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
    },

    getSortedRepositories: () => {
      const { repositories, sortBy } = get();
      const sorted = [...repositories];
      
      switch (sortBy) {
        case 'name-asc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
        case 'name-desc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
        case 'updated':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.pushed_at).getTime() - new Date(a.pushed_at).getTime());
        case 'stars':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.stargazers_count - a.stargazers_count);
        default:
          return sorted;
      }
    },

    getSortedContents: () => {
      const { contents, sortBy } = get();
      const sorted = [...contents];
      
      // Always show folders first, then files
      const folders = sorted.filter(c => c.type === 'dir');
      const files = sorted.filter(c => c.type === 'file');
      
      const sortFn = (a: GitHubContent, b: GitHubContent) => {
        switch (sortBy) {
          case 'name-asc':
            return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
          case 'name-desc':
            return b.name.localeCompare(a.name);
          case 'size':
            return (b.size || 0) - (a.size || 0);
          default:
            return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
        }
      };
      
      return [...folders.sort(sortFn), ...files.sort(sortFn)];
    },

    getCurrentBreadcrumb: () => {
      const { currentPath } = get();
      if (!currentPath) return [];
      return currentPath.split('/').filter(Boolean);
    },

    canGoBack: () => {
      const { currentRepository, currentPath } = get();
      return !!currentRepository && (currentPath !== '' || true); // Can always go back to repo list
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useGitHubAccounts = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.accounts);
export const useGitHubActiveAccount = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.getActiveAccount());
export const useGitHubRepositories = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.getSortedRepositories());
export const useGitHubContents = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.getSortedContents());
export const useGitHubViewMode = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.viewMode);
export const useGitHubSortBy = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.sortBy);
export const useGitHubCurrentRepo = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.currentRepository);
export const useGitHubFileContent = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.fileContent);
export const useGitHubFileName = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.fileName);
export const useGitHubIsLoading = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.isLoading);
export const useGitHubError = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.error);
```

5. `src/components/GitHub/AddAccountDialog.tsx`

```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { useGitHubStore } from '@/stores/githubStore';
import { Eye, EyeOff, Github } from 'lucide-react';

interface AddAccountDialogProps {
  open: boolean;
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
}

export function AddAccountDialog({ open, onOpenChange }: AddAccountDialogProps) {
  const [username, setUsername] = useState('');
  const [token, setToken] = useState('');
  const [showToken, setShowToken] = useState(false);
  const [isVerifying, setIsVerifying] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  
  const addAccount = useGitHubStore((s) => s.addAccount);

  const handleSubmit = async () => {
    if (!username.trim() || !token.trim()) {
      setError('Please enter both username and token');
      return;
    }

    setIsVerifying(true);
    setError(null);

    try {
      await addAccount(username.trim(), token.trim());
      // Success - close dialog
      setUsername('');
      setToken('');
      onOpenChange(false);
    } catch (err) {
      setError((err as Error).message);
    } finally {
      setIsVerifying(false);
    }
  };

  const handleCancel = () => {
    setUsername('');
    setToken('');
    setError(null);
    onOpenChange(false);
  };

  return (
    <Dialog open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
      <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
        <DialogHeader>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Github className="w-6 h-6" />
            <DialogTitle>Connect GitHub Account</DialogTitle>
          </div>
          <DialogDescription>
            Enter your GitHub username and Personal Access Token.
            <a 
              href="https://github.com/settings/tokens" 
              target="_blank" 
              rel="noopener noreferrer"
              className="block mt-1 text-primary hover:underline"
            >
              Generate token here →
            </a>
          </DialogDescription>
        </DialogHeader>
        
        <div className="space-y-4 py-4">
          {error && (
            <div className="p-3 text-sm text-destructive bg-destructive/10 rounded-md">
              {error}
            </div>
          )}

          <div className="space-y-2">
            <Label htmlFor="username">GitHub Username</Label>
            <Input
              id="username"
              placeholder="e.g., octocat"
              value={username}
              onChange={(e) => setUsername(e.target.value)}
              onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSubmit()}
            />
          </div>

          <div className="space-y-2">
            <Label htmlFor="token">Personal Access Token</Label>
            <div className="relative">
              <Input
                id="token"
                type={showToken ? 'text' : 'password'}
                placeholder="ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxx"
                value={token}
                onChange={(e) => setToken(e.target.value)}
                onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSubmit()}
              />
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setShowToken(!showToken)}
                className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
              >
                {showToken ? <EyeOff className="w-4 h-4" /> : <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />}
              </button>
            </div>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              Token is stored locally and encrypted. Required scopes: repo, read:user
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <DialogFooter>
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={handleCancel}>
            Cancel
          </Button>
          <Button 
            onClick={handleSubmit} 
            disabled={isVerifying || !username.trim() || !token.trim()}
          >
            {isVerifying ? 'Verifying...' : 'Connect Account'}
          </Button>
        </DialogFooter>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```

6. `src/components/GitHub/AccountSelector.tsx`

```typescript
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { Plus, X, Github, Shield, ShieldCheck, ShieldAlert } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useGitHubStore, useGitHubAccounts, useGitHubActiveAccount } from '@/stores/githubStore';
import { AddAccountDialog } from './AddAccountDialog';
import { useState } from 'react';
import { GitHubPermission } from '@/types/github';

const permissionIcons: Record<GitHubPermission, React.ElementType> = {
  read: Shield,
  triage: ShieldCheck,
  write: ShieldAlert,
  admin: ShieldCheck,
};

const permissionLabels: Record<GitHubPermission, string> = {
  read: 'Read',
  triage: 'Triage',
  write: 'Write',
  admin: 'Admin',
};

export function AccountSelector() {
  const accounts = useGitHubAccounts();
  const activeAccount = useGitHubActiveAccount();
  const setActiveAccount = useGitHubStore((s) => s.setActiveAccount);
  const removeAccount = useGitHubStore((s) => s.removeAccount);
  const loadAccounts = useGitHubStore((s) => s.loadAccounts);
  const [addDialogOpen, setAddDialogOpen] = useState(false);

  // Load accounts on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    loadAccounts();
  }, [loadAccounts]);

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <div className="p-4 border-b border-border">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground flex items-center gap-2">
          <Github className="w-5 h-5" />
          GitHub
        </h2>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          {accounts.length === 0 
            ? 'Connect your GitHub account to access repositories'
            : `${accounts.length} account${accounts.length > 1 ? 's' : ''} connected`
          }
        </p>
      </div>

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4">
        {accounts.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full space-y-4">
            <div className="p-4 rounded-full bg-primary/10">
              <Github className="w-12 h-12 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center">
              No accounts connected
            </p>
            <Button onClick={() => setAddDialogOpen(true)}>
              Connect GitHub Account
            </Button>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {accounts.map((account) => {
              const isActive = activeAccount?.id === account.id;
              const PermissionIcon = permissionIcons[account.permissions];
              
              return (
                <button
                  key={account.id}
                  onClick={() => setActiveAccount(account.id)}
                  className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg border transition-all text-left ${
                    isActive 
                      ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5' 
                      : 'border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent'
                  }`}
                >
                  {account.avatarUrl ? (
                    <img 
                      src={account.avatarUrl} 
                      alt={account.id}
                      className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full"
                    />
                  ) : (
                    <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                      <Github className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
                    </div>
                  )}
                  
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="font-medium text-foreground truncate">
                      {account.id}
                    </p>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                      <PermissionIcon className="w-3 h-3" />
                      <span>{permissionLabels[account.permissions]}</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-8 w-8 shrink-0"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      removeAccount(account.id);
                    }}
                  >
                    <X className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Add Account Button */}
      {accounts.length > 0 && (
        <div className="p-4 border-t border-border">
          <Button 
            variant="outline" 
            className="w-full gap-2"
            onClick={() => setAddDialogOpen(true)}
          >
            <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
            Add Account
          </Button>
        </div>
      )}

      <AddAccountDialog 
        open={addDialogOpen} 
        onOpenChange={setAddDialogOpen} 
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { Star, GitFork, Lock, Globe, FolderGit } from 'lucide-react';
import { GitHubRepository } from '@/types/github';
import { githubApi } from '@/lib/githubApi';
import { useGitHubStore } from '@/stores/githubStore';

interface RepoListProps {
  repos: GitHubRepository[];
}

export function RepoList({ repos }: RepoListProps) {
  const selectRepository = useGitHubStore((s) => s.selectRepository);

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground bg-muted/50">
        <div className="col-span-6">Repository</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Language</div>
        <div className="col-span-3">Updated</div>
        <div className="col-span-1 text-right">★</div>
      </div>

      {repos.map((repo) => (
        <button
          key={repo.id}
          onClick={() => selectRepository(repo)}
          className="w-full grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-3 text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left items-start group"
        >
          <div className="col-span-6 min-w-0">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <FolderGit className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
              <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={repo.full_name}>
                {repo.name}
              </span>
              {repo.private ? (
                <Lock className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
              ) : (
                <Globe className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
              )}
            </div>
            {repo.description && (
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1 line-clamp-2">
                {repo.description}
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-2 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
            {repo.language || '-'}
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-3 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
            {githubApi.formatDate(repo.pushed_at)}
          </div>

          <div className="col-span-1 text-right text-xs font-medium">
            {repo.stargazers_count > 0 && (
              <span className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1">
                <Star className="w-3 h-3" />
                {repo.stargazers_count}
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

8. `src/components/GitHub/ContentList.tsx`

```typescript
import { 
  Folder, 
  FileText, 
  FileCode, 
  FileImage, 
  FileJson, 
  FileType, 
  Download,
  ChevronRight 
} from 'lucide-react';
import { GitHubContent } from '@/types/github';
import { githubApi } from '@/lib/githubApi';
import { useGitHubStore } from '@/stores/githubStore';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

interface ContentListProps {
  contents: GitHubContent[];
}

function getFileIcon(name: string, type: string) {
  if (type === 'dir') return Folder;
  
  const ext = name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
  
  switch (ext) {
    case 'js':
    case 'ts':
    case 'jsx':
    case 'tsx':
    case 'py':
    case 'java':
    case 'cpp':
    case 'c':
    case 'go':
    case 'rs':
      return FileCode;
    case 'json':
    case 'yaml':
    case 'yml':
      return FileJson;
    case 'png':
    case 'jpg':
    case 'jpeg':
    case 'gif':
    case 'svg':
    case 'webp':
      return FileImage;
    case 'md':
    case 'txt':
    case 'log':
      return FileText;
    default:
      return FileType;
  }
}

export function ContentList({ contents }: ContentListProps) {
  const navigateToPath = useGitHubStore((s) => s.navigateToPath);
  const openFile = useGitHubStore((s) => s.openFile);
  const currentRepo = useGitHubStore((s) => s.currentRepository);

  const handleClick = (item: GitHubContent) => {
    if (item.type === 'dir') {
      navigateToPath(item.path);
    } else {
      openFile(item);
    }
  };

  const handleDownload = (e: React.MouseEvent, item: GitHubContent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    if (item.download_url) {
      window.open(item.download_url, '_blank');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {/* Breadcrumb */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground bg-muted/50">
        <span className="font-medium text-foreground">{currentRepo}</span>
        {useGitHubStore((s) => s.getCurrentBreadcrumb()).map((part, i, arr) => (
          <span key={i} className="flex items-center gap-1">
            <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" />
            <span className={i === arr.length - 1 ? 'text-foreground' : ''}>{part}</span>
          </span>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Header */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">
        <div className="col-span-7">Name</div>
        <div className="col-span-3">Size</div>
        <div className="col-span-2"></div>
      </div>

      {contents.map((item) => {
        const Icon = getFileIcon(item.name, item.type);
        const isDir = item.type === 'dir';
        
        return (
          <button
            key={item.path}
            onClick={() => handleClick(item)}
            className="w-full grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left items-center group"
          >
            <div className="col-span-7 flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
              <Icon className={cn(
                "w-4 h-4 shrink-0",
                isDir ? "text-primary" : "text-muted-foreground"
              )} />
              <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={item.name}>
                {item.name}
              </span>
            </div>
            
            <div className="col-span-3 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
              {isDir ? '-' : githubApi.formatFileSize(item.size)}
            </div>

            <div className="col-span-2 flex justify-end">
              {!isDir && item.download_url && (
                <Button
                  variant="ghost"
                  size="icon"
                  className="h-6 w-6 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100"
                  onClick={(e) => handleDownload(e, item)}
                >
                  <Download className="h-3 w-3" />
                </Button>
              )}
            </div>
          </button>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}
```

9. `src/components/GitHub/FileViewer.tsx`

```typescript
import { X, Download, Copy, Check } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useGitHubStore } from '@/stores/githubStore';
import { useState } from 'react';

export function FileViewer() {
  const fileContent = useGitHubStore((s) => s.fileContent);
  const fileName = useGitHubStore((s) => s.fileName);
  const closeFile = useGitHubStore((s) => s.closeFile);
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);

  if (!fileContent || !fileName) return null;

  const handleCopy = async () => {
    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(fileContent);
    setCopied(true);
    setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2000);
  };

  // Determine language for syntax highlighting
  const ext = fileName.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
  const languageMap: Record<string, string> = {
    js: 'javascript',
    ts: 'typescript',
    jsx: 'jsx',
    tsx: 'tsx',
    py: 'python',
    java: 'java',
    cpp: 'cpp',
    c: 'c',
    go: 'go',
    rs: 'rust',
    html: 'html',
    css: 'css',
    json: 'json',
    md: 'markdown',
    yaml: 'yaml',
    yml: 'yaml',
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background border-l border-border">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border bg-card">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
          <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate">{fileName}</span>
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            ({fileContent.length.toLocaleString()} chars)
          </span>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            className="h-8 w-8"
            onClick={handleCopy}
            title="Copy content"
          >
            {copied ? <Check className="h-4 w-4 text-green-500" /> : <Copy className="h-4 w-4" />}
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            className="h-8 w-8"
            onClick={closeFile}
          >
            <X className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4">
        <pre className="text-sm font-mono text-foreground whitespace-pre-wrap break-all">
          {fileContent}
        </pre>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

10. `src/components/GitHub/GitHubToolbar.tsx`

```typescript
import { 
  Grid3X3, 
  List, 
  ArrowLeft, 
  RefreshCw,
  ArrowUpDown,
  Github,
  LogOut 
} from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Toggle } from '@/components/ui/toggle';
import {
  DropdownMenu,
  DropdownMenuContent,
  DropdownMenuItem,
  DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import { GitHubViewMode, GitHubSortBy } from '@/types/github';
import { useGitHubStore, useGitHubCurrentRepo, useGitHubIsLoading, useGitHubActiveAccount } from '@/stores/githubStore';

interface GitHubToolbarProps {
  viewMode: GitHubViewMode;
  onViewModeChange: (mode: GitHubViewMode) => void;
  sortBy: GitHubSortBy;
  onSortChange: (sort: GitHubSortBy) => void;
  onNavigateBack: () => void;
  onRefresh: () => void;
  onLogout: () => void;
  currentView: 'repos' | 'contents';
}

const sortLabels: Record<GitHubSortBy, string> = {
  'name-asc': 'Name (A-Z)',
  'name-desc': 'Name (Z-A)',
  'updated': 'Last Updated',
  'stars': 'Stars',
};

export function GitHubToolbar({
  viewMode,
  onViewModeChange,
  sortBy,
  onSortChange,
  onNavigateBack,
  onRefresh,
  onLogout,
  currentView,
}: GitHubToolbarProps) {
  const currentRepo = useGitHubCurrentRepo();
  const isLoading = useGitHubIsLoading();
  const activeAccount = useGitHubActiveAccount();
  const canGoBack = useGitHubStore((s) => s.canGoBack());

  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border bg-card">
      {/* Left: Navigation */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onNavigateBack}
          disabled={!canGoBack && currentView === 'repos'}
          className="h-8 w-8 shrink-0"
        >
          <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>

          <Github className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
          <span className="text-xs font-medium text-foreground truncate">
            {currentView === 'repos' 
              ? (activeAccount?.id || 'Repositories') 
              : (currentRepo || 'Repository')}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Right: Actions */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onRefresh}
          disabled={isLoading}
          className="h-8 w-8"

          <RefreshCw className={`h-4 w-4 ${isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />

          variant="ghost"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onLogout}
          className="h-8 w-8"
        >
          <LogOut className="h-4 w-4" />

          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-8 w-8">
              <ArrowUpDown className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
          <DropdownMenuContent align="end">
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-asc')}>
              Name (A-Z)
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-desc')}>
              Name (Z-A)
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('updated')}>
              Last Updated
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            {currentView === 'repos' && (
              <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('stars')}>
                Stars
              </DropdownMenuItem>
            )}
          </DropdownMenuContent>
        </DropdownMenu>

        <div className="flex items-center border rounded-md ml-1">
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'grid'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('grid')}
            className="h-8 w-8 rounded-none rounded-l-md data-[state=on]:bg-primary data-[state=on]:text-primary-foreground"
          >
            <Grid3X3 className="h-4 w-4" />
```
