11. `src/components/GitHub/GitHubPanel.tsx` (Main GitHub Panel)

```typescript
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { AccountSelector } from './AccountSelector';
import { GitHubToolbar } from './GitHubToolbar';
import { RepoList } from './RepoList';
import { ContentList } from './ContentList';
import { FileViewer } from './FileViewer';
import { useGitHubStore, useGitHubRepositories, useGitHubContents, useGitHubViewMode, useGitHubSortBy, useGitHubActiveAccount, useGitHubCurrentRepo, useGitHubFileContent, useGitHubError } from '@/stores/githubStore';

function GitHubPanelContent() {
  const repos = useGitHubRepositories();
  const contents = useGitHubContents();
  const viewMode = useGitHubViewMode();
  const sortBy = useGitHubSortBy();
  const activeAccount = useGitHubActiveAccount();
  const currentRepo = useGitHubCurrentRepo();
  const fileContent = useGitHubFileContent();
  const error = useGitHubError();
  
  const {
    setViewMode,
    setSortBy,
    navigateBack,
    refreshCurrent,
    navigateToRoot,
    setActiveAccount,
    loadAccounts,
  } = useGitHubStore();

  // Load accounts on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    loadAccounts();
  }, [loadAccounts]);

  const handleBackToAccounts = () => {
    setActiveAccount(null);
  };

  // Show account selector if no active account
  if (!activeAccount) {
    return <AccountSelector />;
  }

  const currentView = currentRepo ? 'contents' : 'repos';

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <GitHubToolbar
        viewMode={viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={setViewMode}
        sortBy={sortBy}
        onSortChange={setSortBy}
        onNavigateBack={navigateBack}
        onRefresh={refreshCurrent}
        onLogout={handleBackToAccounts}
        currentView={currentView}
      />

      {error && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-destructive/10 text-destructive text-sm text-center">
          {error}
          <button 
            onClick={refreshCurrent}
            className="ml-2 underline hover:no-underline"
          >
            Retry
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto flex">
        <div className={`flex-1 ${fileContent ? 'hidden md:block md:w-1/2' : 'w-full'}`}>
          {currentView === 'repos' ? (
            repos.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
                <p className="text-sm">No repositories found</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <RepoList repos={repos} />
            )
          ) : (
            contents.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
                <p className="text-sm">Empty folder</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <ContentList contents={contents} />
            )
          )}
        </div>

        {/* File Viewer - shows when file is selected */}
        {fileContent && (
          <div className="w-full md:w-1/2 h-full">
            <FileViewer />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function GitHubPanel() {
  return <GitHubPanelContent />;
}
```

12. `src/components/Panel/PanelContent.tsx` (Final Updated with GitHub)

```typescript
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { FileSystemEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';
import { StoragePanel } from './StoragePanel';
import { PlaceholderPanel } from './PlaceholderPanel';
import { DrivePanel } from '../GoogleDrive/DrivePanel';
import { GitHubPanel } from '../GitHub/GitHubPanel';

interface PanelContentProps {
  panel: PanelState;
}

export function PanelContent({ panel }: PanelContentProps) {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState<FileSystemEntry[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  // Load entries when handle changes (for storage)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (panel.source === 'storage' && panel.handle) {
      setIsLoading(true);
      fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle)
        .then(setEntries)
        .finally(() => setIsLoading(false));
    }
  }, [panel.handle, panel.source, panel.id]);

  const handleRefresh = async () => {
    if (!panel.handle) return;
    setIsLoading(true);
    const newEntries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
    setEntries(newEntries);
    setIsLoading(false);
  };

  switch (panel.source) {
    case 'storage':
      return (
        <StoragePanel
          panel={panel}
          entries={entries}
          isLoading={isLoading}
          onRefresh={handleRefresh}
        />
      );
    case 'drive':
      return <DrivePanel />;
    case 'github':
      return <GitHubPanel />;
    case 'terminal':
      return <PlaceholderPanel panel={panel} source={panel.source} />;
    default:
      return null;
  }
}
```

1. `src/types/terminal.ts` (Terminal Types)

```typescript
export interface TerminalFileSystemEntry {
  name: string;
  type: 'file' | 'directory' | 'symlink';
  size: number;
  lastModified: Date;
  permissions: string;
  path: string;
}

export interface TerminalDirectory extends TerminalFileSystemEntry {
  type: 'directory';
  children?: TerminalFileSystemEntry[];
}

export interface TerminalFile extends TerminalFileSystemEntry {
  type: 'file';
  content?: string;
}

export type TerminalViewMode = 'grid' | 'list' | 'tree';
export type TerminalSortBy = 'name-asc' | 'name-desc' | 'date' | 'size';

export interface TerminalPanelState {
  isInitialized: boolean;
  isBooting: boolean;
  bootProgress: number;
  currentPath: string;
  pathHistory: string[];
  entries: TerminalFileSystemEntry[];
  viewMode: TerminalViewMode;
  sortBy: TerminalSortBy;
  selectedFile: TerminalFile | null;
  error: string | null;
  webcontainerInstance: any | null; // WebContainer instance
}
```

2. `src/lib/webcontainerApi.ts` (WebContainer API Client)

```typescript
import { WebContainer } from '@webcontainer/api';
import { TerminalFileSystemEntry, TerminalDirectory, TerminalFile } from '@/types/terminal';

class WebContainerApi {
  private instance: WebContainer | null = null;
  private isBooting = false;

  async init(onProgress?: (progress: number) => void): Promise<WebContainer> {
    if (this.instance) return this.instance;
    if (this.isBooting) {
      // Wait for existing boot
      while (this.isBooting) {
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100));
      }
      return this.instance!;
    }

    this.isBooting = true;

    try {
      // Boot WebContainer with progress tracking
      this.instance = await WebContainer.boot({
        onProgress: (progress) => {
          onProgress?.(progress);
        },
      });

      this.isBooting = false;
      return this.instance;
    } catch (error) {
      this.isBooting = false;
      throw new Error(`Failed to boot WebContainer: ${(error as Error).message}`);
    }
  }

  getInstance(): WebContainer | null {
    return this.instance;
  }

  async readDirectory(path: string): Promise<TerminalFileSystemEntry[]> {
    if (!this.instance) throw new Error('WebContainer not initialized');

    try {
      // Use WebContainer's fs API to read directory
      const fs = this.instance.fs;
      const entries = await fs.readdir(path, { withFileTypes: true });

      const result: TerminalFileSystemEntry[] = [];

      for (const entry of entries) {
        const fullPath = `${path === '/' ? '' : path}/${entry.name}`;
        
        let type: 'file' | 'directory' | 'symlink' = 'file';
        if (entry.isDirectory()) type = 'directory';
        else if (entry.isSymbolicLink()) type = 'symlink';

        let size = 0;
        let lastModified = new Date();

        try {
          const stats = await fs.stat(fullPath);
          size = stats.size || 0;
          lastModified = new Date(stats.mtime || Date.now());
        } catch (e) {
          // Some entries might not have stats
        }

        result.push({
          name: entry.name,
          type,
          size,
          lastModified,
          permissions: this.formatPermissions(stats),
          path: fullPath,
        });
      }

      return result.sort((a, b) => {
        // Directories first, then files
        if (a.type === 'directory' && b.type !== 'directory') return -1;
        if (a.type !== 'directory' && b.type === 'directory') return 1;
        return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
      });
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to read directory: ${(error as Error).message}`);
    }
  }

  async readFile(path: string): Promise<string> {
    if (!this.instance) throw new Error('WebContainer not initialized');

    try {
      const fs = this.instance.fs;
      const content = await fs.readFile(path, 'utf-8');
      return content;
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to read file: ${(error as Error).message}`);
    }
  }

  async getFileStats(path: string): Promise<any> {
    if (!this.instance) throw new Error('WebContainer not initialized');

    try {
      const fs = this.instance.fs;
      return await fs.stat(path);
    } catch (error) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  formatPermissions(stats: any): string {
    if (!stats) return '---------';
    
    const mode = stats.mode || 0;
    const perms = [
      mode & 0o400 ? 'r' : '-',
      mode & 0o200 ? 'w' : '-',
      mode & 0o100 ? 'x' : '-',
      mode & 0o040 ? 'r' : '-',
      mode & 0o020 ? 'w' : '-',
      mode & 0o010 ? 'x' : '-',
      mode & 0o004 ? 'r' : '-',
      mode & 0o002 ? 'w' : '-',
      mode & 0o001 ? 'x' : '-',
    ];
    
    return perms.join('');
  }

  formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
    if (bytes === 0) return '-';
    const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
    let size = bytes;
    let unitIndex = 0;
    while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
      size /= 1024;
      unitIndex++;
    }
    return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
  }

  formatDate(date: Date): string {
    return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
      month: 'short',
      day: 'numeric',
      hour: '2-digit',
      minute: '2-digit',
    });
  }

  isReady(): boolean {
    return this.instance !== null && !this.isBooting;
  }

  async shutdown(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.instance) {
      // WebContainer doesn't have explicit shutdown, but we can clear reference
      this.instance = null;
      this.isBooting = false;
    }
  }
}

export const webcontainerApi = new WebContainerApi();
```

3. `src/stores/terminalStore.ts` (Terminal Panel Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { 
  TerminalFileSystemEntry, 
  TerminalFile,
  TerminalViewMode,
  TerminalSortBy,
  TerminalPanelState 
} from '@/types/terminal';
import { webcontainerApi } from '@/lib/webcontainerApi';

interface TerminalStore extends TerminalPanelState {
  // Actions
  initialize: () => Promise<void>;
  shutdown: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateTo: (path: string) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateToRoot: () => Promise<void>;
  selectFile: (file: TerminalFile | null) => Promise<void>;
  refreshCurrent: () => Promise<void>;
  setViewMode: (mode: TerminalViewMode) => void;
  setSortBy: (sort: TerminalSortBy) => void;
  
  // Getters
  getSortedEntries: () => TerminalFileSystemEntry[];
  getBreadcrumb: () => string[];
  canGoBack: () => boolean;
}

const createInitialState = (): TerminalPanelState => ({
  isInitialized: false,
  isBooting: false,
  bootProgress: 0,
  currentPath: '/',
  pathHistory: [],
  entries: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  selectedFile: null,
  error: null,
  webcontainerInstance: null,
});

export const useTerminalStore = create<TerminalStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    ...createInitialState(),

    initialize: async () => {
      const { isInitialized, isBooting } = get();
      if (isInitialized || isBooting) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isBooting = true;
        state.bootProgress = 0;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        const instance = await webcontainerApi.init((progress) => {
          set((state) => {
            state.bootProgress = Math.round(progress * 100);
          });
        });

        set((state) => {
          state.isInitialized = true;
          state.isBooting = false;
          state.bootProgress = 100;
          state.webcontainerInstance = instance;
        });

        // Load root directory
        await get().navigateTo('/');
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isBooting = false;
          state.bootProgress = 0;
        });
      }
    },

    shutdown: async () => {
      await webcontainerApi.shutdown();
      set(createInitialState());
    },

    navigateTo: async (path) => {
      const { currentPath, pathHistory } = get();
      
      set((state) => {
        state.isBooting = true;
        state.error = null;
        state.selectedFile = null;
      });

      try {
        const entries = await webcontainerApi.readDirectory(path);
        
        set((state) => {
          if (path !== currentPath) {
            state.pathHistory.push(currentPath);
          }
          state.currentPath = path;
          state.entries = entries;
          state.isBooting = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isBooting = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateBack: async () => {
      const { pathHistory } = get();
      if (pathHistory.length === 0) {
        await get().navigateToRoot();
        return;
      }

      const previousPath = pathHistory[pathHistory.length - 1];
      
      set((state) => {
        state.pathHistory.pop();
        state.selectedFile = null;
      });

      await get().navigateTo(previousPath);
    },

    navigateToRoot: async () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.pathHistory = [];
        state.selectedFile = null;
      });
      await get().navigateTo('/');
    },

    selectFile: async (file) => {
      if (!file) {
        set((state) => {
          state.selectedFile = null;
        });
        return;
      }

      if (file.type === 'directory') {
        await get().navigateTo(file.path);
      } else {
        // Read file content
        set((state) => {
          state.isBooting = true;
        });

        try {
          const content = await webcontainerApi.readFile(file.path);
          set((state) => {
            state.selectedFile = { ...file, content };
            state.isBooting = false;
          });
        } catch (err) {
          set((state) => {
            state.error = (err as Error).message;
            state.isBooting = false;
          });
        }
      }
    },

    refreshCurrent: async () => {
      const { currentPath } = get();
      await get().navigateTo(currentPath);
    },

    setViewMode: (mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setSortBy: (sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    getSortedEntries: () => {
      const { entries, sortBy } = get();
      const sorted = [...entries];
      
      switch (sortBy) {
        case 'name-asc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
        case 'name-desc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
        case 'date':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.lastModified.getTime() - a.lastModified.getTime());
        case 'size':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.size - a.size);
        default:
          return sorted;
      }
    },

    getBreadcrumb: () => {
      const { currentPath } = get();
      if (currentPath === '/') return ['root'];
      return ['root', ...currentPath.split('/').filter(Boolean)];
    },

    canGoBack: () => {
      const { pathHistory, currentPath } = get();
      return pathHistory.length > 0 || currentPath !== '/';
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useTerminalInitialized = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.isInitialized);
export const useTerminalBooting = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.isBooting);
export const useTerminalBootProgress = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.bootProgress);
export const useTerminalCurrentPath = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.currentPath);
export const useTerminalEntries = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.getSortedEntries());
export const useTerminalViewMode = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.viewMode);
export const useTerminalSortBy = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.sortBy);
export const useTerminalSelectedFile = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.selectedFile);
export const useTerminalError = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.error);
```

4. `src/components/Terminal/BootScreen.tsx`

```typescript
import { Terminal, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { useTerminalStore, useTerminalBootProgress, useTerminalError } from '@/stores/terminalStore';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';

export function BootScreen() {
  const initialize = useTerminalStore((s) => s.initialize);
  const isBooting = useTerminalStore((s) => s.isBooting);
  const progress = useTerminalBootProgress();
  const error = useTerminalError();

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-8 bg-background">
      <div className="max-w-md w-full space-y-6 text-center">
        <div className="p-4 rounded-full bg-primary/10 mx-auto w-fit">
          <Terminal className="w-12 h-12 text-primary" />
        </div>

        <div>
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">WebContainer Terminal</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-2">
            Initialize an in-browser Node.js environment to explore the file system.
          </p>
        </div>

        {error && (
          <div className="p-4 rounded-lg bg-destructive/10 text-destructive text-sm">
            <p className="font-medium">Failed to initialize</p>
            <p>{error}</p>
            <Button 
              variant="outline" 
              size="sm" 
              className="mt-2"
              onClick={() => initialize()}
            >
              Retry
            </Button>
          </div>
        )}

        {!error && (
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {isBooting ? (
              <>
                <Progress value={progress} className="w-full" />
                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                  Booting WebContainer... {progress}%
                </p>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                  <Loader2 className="w-3 h-3 animate-spin" />
                  <span>Downloading Node.js runtime</span>
                </div>
              </>
            ) : (
              <Button onClick={() => initialize()} className="w-full">
                Initialize Terminal
              </Button>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          Requires cross-origin isolation (COOP/COEP headers)
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

5. `src/components/Terminal/TerminalToolbar.tsx`

```typescript
import { 
  Grid3X3, 
  List, 
  TreePine,
  ArrowLeft, 
  RefreshCw,
  ArrowUpDown,
  Terminal,
  Power,
  FolderTree
} from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Toggle } from '@/components/ui/toggle';
import {
  DropdownMenu,
  DropdownMenuContent,
  DropdownMenuItem,
  DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import { TerminalViewMode, TerminalSortBy } from '@/types/terminal';
import { useTerminalStore, useTerminalCurrentPath, useTerminalBooting } from '@/stores/terminalStore';

interface TerminalToolbarProps {
  viewMode: TerminalViewMode;
  onViewModeChange: (mode: TerminalViewMode) => void;
  sortBy: TerminalSortBy;
  onSortChange: (sort: TerminalSortBy) => void;
  onNavigateBack: () => void;
  onRefresh: () => void;
  onShutdown: () => void;
}

const sortLabels: Record<TerminalSortBy, string> = {
  'name-asc': 'Name (A-Z)',
  'name-desc': 'Name (Z-A)',
  'date': 'Date Modified',
  'size': 'Size',
};

export function TerminalToolbar({
  viewMode,
  onViewModeChange,
  sortBy,
  onSortChange,
  onNavigateBack,
  onRefresh,
  onShutdown,
}: TerminalToolbarProps) {
  const currentPath = useTerminalCurrentPath();
  const isBooting = useTerminalBooting();
  const canGoBack = useTerminalStore((s) => s.canGoBack());
  const breadcrumb = useTerminalStore((s) => s.getBreadcrumb());

  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border bg-card">
      {/* Left: Navigation */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onNavigateBack}
          disabled={!canGoBack}
          className="h-8 w-8 shrink-0"
        >
          <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>
        
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 ml-2 min-w-0 overflow-hidden">
          <Terminal className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs font-medium text-foreground truncate">
            {breadcrumb.map((part, i) => (
              <span key={i} className="flex items-center gap-1">
                {i > 0 && <span className="text-muted-foreground">/</span>}
                <span className={i === breadcrumb.length - 1 ? 'text-foreground' : 'text-muted-foreground'}>
                  {part}
                </span>
              </span>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Right: Actions */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onRefresh}
          disabled={isBooting}
          className="h-8 w-8"
        >
          <RefreshCw className={`h-4 w-4 ${isBooting ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
        </Button>

        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onShutdown}
          className="h-8 w-8 text-destructive hover:text-destructive"
        >
          <Power className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>

        <DropdownMenu>
          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-8 w-8">
              <ArrowUpDown className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
          <DropdownMenuContent align="end">
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-asc')}>
              Name (A-Z)
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-desc')}>
              Name (Z-A)
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('date')}>
              Date Modified
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('size')}>
              Size
            </DropdownMenuItem>
          </DropdownMenuContent>
        </DropdownMenu>

        <div className="flex items-center border rounded-md ml-1">
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'list'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('list')}
            className="h-8 w-8 rounded-none rounded-l-md data-[state=on]:bg-primary data-[state=on]:text-primary-foreground"
          >
            <List className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Toggle>
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'grid'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('grid')}
            className="h-8 w-8 rounded-none data-[state=on]:bg-primary data-[state=on]:text-primary-foreground"
          >
            <Grid3X3 className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Toggle>
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'tree'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('tree')}
            className="h-8 w-8 rounded-none rounded-r-md data-[state=on]:bg-primary data-[state=on]:text-primary-foreground"
          >
            <FolderTree className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Toggle>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

6. `src/components/Terminal/FileList.tsx`

```typescript
import { 
  Folder, 
  FileText, 
  FileCode, 
  FileJson, 
  FileType, 
  Link,
  Lock
} from 'lucide-react';
import { TerminalFileSystemEntry, TerminalFile } from '@/types/terminal';
import { webcontainerApi } from '@/lib/webcontainerApi';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface FileListProps {
  entries: TerminalFileSystemEntry[];
  onEntryClick: (entry: TerminalFileSystemEntry) => void;
}

function getFileIcon(name: string, type: string) {
  if (type === 'directory') return Folder;
  if (type === 'symlink') return Link;
  
  const ext = name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
  
  switch (ext) {
    case 'js':
    case 'ts':
    case 'jsx':
    case 'tsx':
    case 'py':
    case 'java':
    case 'cpp':
    case 'c':
    case 'go':
    case 'rs':
      return FileCode;
    case 'json':
    case 'yaml':
    case 'yml':
      return FileJson;
    case 'md':
    case 'txt':
    case 'log':
      return FileText;
    default:
      return FileType;
  }
}

export function FileList({ entries, onEntryClick }: FileListProps) {
  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground bg-muted/50">
        <div className="col-span-5">Name</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Permissions</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Size</div>
        <div className="col-span-3">Modified</div>
      </div>

      {entries.map((entry) => {
        const Icon = getFileIcon(entry.name, entry.type);
        const isDir = entry.type === 'directory';
        const isSymlink = entry.type === 'symlink';
        
        return (
          <button
            key={entry.path}
            onClick={() => onEntryClick(entry)}
            className="w-full grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left items-center group"
          >
            <div className="col-span-5 flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
              <Icon className={cn(
                "w-4 h-4 shrink-0",
                isDir ? "text-primary" : isSymlink ? "text-orange-500" : "text-muted-foreground"
              )} />
              <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={entry.name}>
                {entry.name}
              </span>
              {isSymlink && <Link className="w-3 h-3 text-orange-500 shrink-0" />}
            </div>
            
            <div className="col-span-2 font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              {entry.permissions}
            </div>
            
            <div className="col-span-2 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
              {isDir ? '-' : webcontainerApi.formatFileSize(entry.size)}
            </div>

            <div className="col-span-3 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
              {webcontainerApi.formatDate(entry.lastModified)}
            </div>
          </button>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}
```

7. `src/components/Terminal/FileGrid.tsx`

```typescript
import { 
  Folder, 
  FileText, 
  FileCode, 
  FileJson, 
  FileType, 
  Link
} from 'lucide-react';
import { TerminalFileSystemEntry, TerminalFile } from '@/types/terminal';
import { webcontainerApi } from '@/lib/webcontainerApi';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface FileGridProps {
  entries: TerminalFileSystemEntry[];
  onEntryClick: (entry: TerminalFileSystemEntry) => void;
}

function getFileIcon(name: string, type: string) {
  if (type === 'directory') return Folder;
  if (type === 'symlink') return Link;
  
  const ext = name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
  
  switch (ext) {
    case 'js':
    case 'ts':
    case 'jsx':
    case 'tsx':
    case 'py':
    case 'java':
    case 'cpp':
    case 'c':
    case 'go':
    case 'rs':
      return FileCode;
    case 'json':
    case 'yaml':
    case 'yml':
      return FileJson;
    case 'md':
    case 'txt':
    case 'log':
      return FileText;
    default:
      return FileType;
  }
}

export function FileGrid({ entries, onEntryClick }: FileGridProps) {
  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-3 p-3">
      {entries.map((entry) => {
        const Icon = getFileIcon(entry.name, entry.type);
        const isDir = entry.type === 'directory';
        const isSymlink = entry.type === 'symlink';
        
        return (
          <button
            key={entry.path}
            onClick={() => onEntryClick(entry)}
            className={cn(
              "flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent transition-all text-left",
              isDir && "hover:border-primary/50"
            )}
          >
            <div className={cn(
              "mb-2 p-3 rounded-lg",
              isDir ? "bg-primary/10 text-primary" : 
              isSymlink ? "bg-orange-500/10 text-orange-500" : 
              "bg-muted text-muted-foreground"
            )}>
              <Icon className="w-8 h-8" />
            </div>
            
            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate w-full text-center" title={entry.name}>
              {entry.name}
            </p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
              {isDir ? 'Folder' : isSymlink ? 'Symlink' : webcontainerApi.formatFileSize(entry.size)}
            </p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-mono mt-1">
              {entry.permissions}
            </p>
          </button>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}
```

8. `src/components/Terminal/FileViewer.tsx`

```typescript
import { X, Download, Copy, Check, FileText } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useTerminalStore } from '@/stores/terminalStore';
import { useState } from 'react';

export function FileViewer() {
  const selectedFile = useTerminalStore((s) => s.selectedFile);
  const selectFile = useTerminalStore((s) => s.selectFile);
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);

  if (!selectedFile) return null;

  const handleCopy = async () => {
    if (!selectedFile.content) return;
    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(selectedFile.content);
    setCopied(true);
    setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2000);
  };

  const handleDownload = () => {
    if (!selectedFile.content) return;
    const blob = new Blob([selectedFile.content], { type: 'text/plain' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = selectedFile.name;
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  };

  // Determine language for display
  const ext = selectedFile.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
  const languageMap: Record<string, string> = {
    js: 'JavaScript',
    ts: 'TypeScript',
    jsx: 'JSX',
    tsx: 'TSX',
    py: 'Python',
    java: 'Java',
    cpp: 'C++',
    c: 'C',
    go: 'Go',
    rs: 'Rust',
    html: 'HTML',
    css: 'CSS',
    json: 'JSON',
    md: 'Markdown',
    yaml: 'YAML',
    yml: 'YAML',
    sh: 'Shell',
    bash: 'Bash',
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background border-l border-border">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border bg-card">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
          <FileText className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
          <div className="min-w-0">
            <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate block">{selectedFile.name}</span>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              {languageMap[ext || ''] || 'Plain Text'} • {selectedFile.content?.length.toLocaleString()} chars
            </span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            className="h-8 w-8"
            onClick={handleCopy}
            title="Copy content"
          >
            {copied ? <Check className="h-4 w-4 text-green-500" /> : <Copy className="h-4 w-4" />}
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            className="h-8 w-8"
            onClick={handleDownload}
            title="Download file"
          >
            <Download className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            className="h-8 w-8"
            onClick={() => selectFile(null)}
          >
            <X className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4">
        {selectedFile.content ? (
          <pre className="text-sm font-mono text-foreground whitespace-pre-wrap break-all">
            {selectedFile.content}
          </pre>
        ) : (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p>Binary file - cannot display content</p>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

9. `src/components/Terminal/TerminalPanel.tsx` (Main Terminal Panel)

```typescript
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { BootScreen } from './BootScreen';
import { TerminalToolbar } from './TerminalToolbar';
import { FileList } from './FileList';
import { FileGrid } from './FileGrid';
import { FileViewer } from './FileViewer';
import { useTerminalStore, useTerminalInitialized, useTerminalEntries, useTerminalViewMode, useTerminalSortBy, useTerminalSelectedFile, useTerminalError } from '@/stores/terminalStore';
import { TerminalFileSystemEntry, TerminalFile } from '@/types/terminal';

function TerminalPanelContent() {
  const isInitialized = useTerminalInitialized();
  const entries = useTerminalEntries();
  const viewMode = useTerminalViewMode();
  const sortBy = useTerminalSortBy();
  const selectedFile = useTerminalSelectedFile();
  const error = useTerminalError();
  
  const {
    setViewMode,
    setSortBy,
    navigateBack,
    navigateToRoot,
    refreshCurrent,
    selectFile,
    shutdown,
  } = useTerminalStore();

  // Initialize on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    // Auto-initialize if not already done
    // This can be disabled if manual init is preferred
  }, []);

  const handleEntryClick = (entry: TerminalFileSystemEntry) => {
    selectFile(entry as TerminalFile);
  };

  if (!isInitialized) {
    return <BootScreen />;
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <TerminalToolbar
        viewMode={viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={setViewMode}
        sortBy={sortBy}
        onSortChange={setSortBy}
        onNavigateBack={navigateBack}
        onRefresh={refreshCurrent}
        onShutdown={shutdown}
      />

      {error && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-destructive/10 text-destructive text-sm text-center">
          {error}
          <button 
            onClick={refreshCurrent}
            className="ml-2 underline hover:no-underline"
          >
            Retry
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto flex">
        <div className={`flex-1 ${selectedFile ? 'hidden md:block md:w-1/2' : 'w-full'}`}>
          {entries.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
              <p className="text-sm">Empty directory</p>
            </div>
          ) : viewMode === 'grid' ? (
            <FileGrid entries={entries} onEntryClick={handleEntryClick} />
          ) : (
            <FileList entries={entries} onEntryClick={handleEntryClick} />
          )}
        </div>

        {/* File Viewer */}
        {selectedFile && (
          <div className="w-full md:w-1/2 h-full">
            <FileViewer />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function TerminalPanel() {
  return <TerminalPanelContent />;
}
```

10. `src/components/Panel/PanelContent.tsx` (Final Updated with Terminal)

```typescript
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { FileSystemEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';
import { StoragePanel } from './StoragePanel';
import { PlaceholderPanel } from './PlaceholderPanel';
import { DrivePanel } from '../GoogleDrive/DrivePanel';
import { GitHubPanel } from '../GitHub/GitHubPanel';
import { TerminalPanel } from '../Terminal/TerminalPanel';

interface PanelContentProps {
  panel: PanelState;
}

export function PanelContent({ panel }: PanelContentProps) {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState<FileSystemEntry[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  // Load entries when handle changes (for storage)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (panel.source === 'storage' && panel.handle) {
      setIsLoading(true);
      fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle)
        .then(setEntries)
        .finally(() => setIsLoading(false));
    }
  }, [panel.handle, panel.source, panel.id]);

  const handleRefresh = async () => {
    if (!panel.handle) return;
    setIsLoading(true);
    const newEntries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
    setEntries(newEntries);
    setIsLoading(false);
  };

  switch (panel.source) {
    case 'storage':
      return (
        <StoragePanel
          panel={panel}
          entries={entries}
          isLoading={isLoading}
          onRefresh={handleRefresh}
        />
      );
    case 'drive':
      return <DrivePanel />;
    case 'github':
      return <GitHubPanel />;
    case 'terminal':
      return <TerminalPanel />;
    default:
      return null;
  }
}
```

```typescript
import path from "path"
import tailwindcss from "@tailwindcss/vite"
import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react"
import { defineConfig } from "vite"

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react(), tailwindcss()],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      "@": path.resolve(__dirname, "./src"),
    },
  },
  server: {
    headers: {
      // Required for WebContainer cross-origin isolation
      'Cross-Origin-Embedder-Policy': 'require-corp',
      'Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy': 'same-origin',
    },
  },
  optimizeDeps: {
    exclude: ['@webcontainer/api'],
  },
})
```

14. `src/components/Panel/PlaceholderPanel.tsx` (Updated - remove terminal from placeholder)

```typescript
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';
import { 
  HardDrive, 
  FolderGit, 
  Github, 
  Terminal,
  CheckCircle
} from 'lucide-react';

const sourceIcons: Record<SourceType, React.ElementType> = {
  storage: HardDrive,
  drive: FolderGit,
  github: Github,
  terminal: Terminal,
};

const sourceLabels: Record<SourceType, string> = {
  storage: 'Storage',
  drive: 'Google Drive',
  github: 'GitHub',
  terminal: 'Terminal',
};

interface PlaceholderPanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  source: SourceType;
}

export function PlaceholderPanel({ panel, source }: PlaceholderPanelProps) {
  const Icon = sourceIcons[source];
  const label = sourceLabels[source];

  // Terminal is now fully implemented, shouldn't show placeholder
  if (source === 'terminal') {
    return (
      <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 text-center">
        <CheckCircle className="w-12 h-12 text-green-500 mb-4" />
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground">Terminal Ready</h3>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          Click the Terminal button in the panel header to initialize WebContainer.
        </p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 text-center">
      <div className="p-4 rounded-xl bg-primary/10 text-primary mb-4">
        <Icon className="w-12 h-12" />
      </div>
      <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground mb-2">{label}</h3>
      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground max-w-xs">
        This {label} panel is independent from other panels.
        <br />
        Source: <span className="font-medium capitalize">{panel.source}</span>
      </p>
      <div className="mt-4 p-3 rounded-lg bg-muted text-xs text-muted-foreground">
        Panel ID: {panel.id}
        <br />
        Path: {panel.path}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

---

🔧 WebContainer Setup Notes

Cross-Origin Isolation Requirements

WebContainer requires cross-origin isolation for security. This is configured in:

1. vite.config.ts - Development server headers
2. index.html - Meta tags (fallback)

Important Notes:

1. SharedArrayBuffer: WebContainer uses SharedArrayBuffer which requires COOP/COEP
2. Browser Support: Chrome/Edge 92+, Firefox 103+ (with flags), Safari not supported
3. HTTPS Required: In production, must be served over HTTPS
4. CORS: All resources must be served with proper CORS headers

Troubleshooting:

If you see "SharedArrayBuffer is not defined" error:
- Check COOP/COEP headers are set correctly
- Use Chrome/Edge for best compatibility
- Check browser console for specific errors

📝 Full Implementation

1. `src/types/dragDrop.ts` (Drag Drop Types)

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry } from './filesystem';
import { DriveFile } from './drive';
import { GitHubContent } from './github';
import { TerminalFileSystemEntry } from './terminal';

export type SourceType = 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';

export type DragItem = 
  | { type: 'storage'; item: FileSystemEntry; panelId: string }
  | { type: 'drive'; item: DriveFile; panelId: string }
  | { type: 'github'; item: GitHubContent; panelId: string }
  | { type: 'terminal'; item: TerminalFileSystemEntry; panelId: string };

export interface SelectedItem {
  id: string;
  sourceType: SourceType;
  item: any;
  panelId: string;
}

export interface DragDropState {
  isDragging: boolean;
  isDragMode: boolean;
  selectedItems: SelectedItem[];
  dragSourcePanel: string | null;
  dragImagePosition: { x: number; y: number } | null;
  pendingOperation: 'copy' | 'move' | null;
  targetPanel: string | null;
  showConfirmDialog: boolean;
}

export interface DragDropActions {
  enterDragMode: (panelId: string) => void;
  exitDragMode: () => void;
  toggleSelection: (item: SelectedItem) => void;
  clearSelection: () => void;
  selectAll: (items: SelectedItem[]) => void;
  startDrag: (panelId: string, position: { x: number; y: number }) => void;
  endDrag: () => void;
  setDragImagePosition: (position: { x: number; y: number }) => void;
  setTargetPanel: (panelId: string | null) => void;
  showConfirm: (operation: 'copy' | 'move') => void;
  hideConfirm: () => void;
  confirmOperation: () => void;
  cancelOperation: () => void;
}
```

2. `src/stores/dragDropStore.ts` (Drag Drop Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { DragDropState, DragDropActions, SelectedItem } from '@/types/dragDrop';

interface DragDropStore extends DragDropState, DragDropActions {}

export const useDragDropStore = create<DragDropStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    isDragging: false,
    isDragMode: false,
    selectedItems: [],
    dragSourcePanel: null,
    dragImagePosition: null,
    pendingOperation: null,
    targetPanel: null,
    showConfirmDialog: false,

    // Actions
    enterDragMode: (panelId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragMode = true;
        state.dragSourcePanel = panelId;
        state.selectedItems = [];
      });
    },

    exitDragMode: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragMode = false;
        state.isDragging = false;
        state.selectedItems = [];
        state.dragSourcePanel = null;
        state.dragImagePosition = null;
        state.pendingOperation = null;
        state.targetPanel = null;
        state.showConfirmDialog = false;
      });
    },

    toggleSelection: (item) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existingIndex = state.selectedItems.findIndex(
          (i) => i.id === item.id && i.panelId === item.panelId
        );
        
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
          state.selectedItems.splice(existingIndex, 1);
        } else {
          state.selectedItems.push(item);
        }
      });
    },

    clearSelection: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedItems = [];
      });
    },

    selectAll: (items) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedItems = items;
      });
    },

    startDrag: (panelId, position) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragging = true;
        state.dragSourcePanel = panelId;
        state.dragImagePosition = position;
      });
    },

    endDrag: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragging = false;
        state.dragImagePosition = null;
      });
    },

    setDragImagePosition: (position) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.dragImagePosition = position;
      });
    },

    setTargetPanel: (panelId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.targetPanel = panelId;
      });
    },

    showConfirm: (operation) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.pendingOperation = operation;
        state.showConfirmDialog = true;
      });
    },

    hideConfirm: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.showConfirmDialog = false;
        state.pendingOperation = null;
      });
    },

    confirmOperation: () => {
      // This will be handled by the panel that receives the drop
      set((state) => {
        state.showConfirmDialog = false;
      });
    },

    cancelOperation: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragging = false;
        state.pendingOperation = null;
        state.targetPanel = null;
        state.showConfirmDialog = false;
        state.dragImagePosition = null;
      });
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useIsDragMode = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.isDragMode);
export const useIsDragging = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.isDragging);
export const useSelectedItems = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.selectedItems);
export const useDragSourcePanel = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.dragSourcePanel);
export const useDragImagePosition = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.dragImagePosition);
export const usePendingOperation = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.pendingOperation);
export const useTargetPanel = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.targetPanel);
export const useShowConfirmDialog = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.showConfirmDialog);
```

3. `src/components/DragDrop/DragDropProvider.tsx`

```typescript
import { DndProvider, useDrag, useDrop } from 'react-dnd';
import { HTML5Backend } from 'react-dnd-html5-backend';
import { TouchBackend } from 'react-dnd-touch-backend';
import { useEffect, useState, ReactNode } from 'react';
import { useDragDropStore, useIsDragging, useSelectedItems, useDragImagePosition } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';
import { DragOverlay } from './DragOverlay';
import { ConfirmDialog } from './ConfirmDialog';

interface DragDropProviderProps {
  children: ReactNode;
}

// Detect touch device
const isTouchDevice = () => {
  return 'ontouchstart' in window || navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0;
};

export function DragDropProvider({ children }: DragDropProviderProps) {
  const [backend, setBackend] = useState<any>(HTML5Backend);
  
  useEffect(() => {
    // Dynamically import touch backend if needed
    if (isTouchDevice()) {
      import('react-dnd-touch-backend').then((mod) => {
        setBackend(() => mod.TouchBackend);
      });
    }
  }, []);

  return (
    <DndProvider backend={backend} options={{ enableMouseEvents: true }}>
      {children}
      <DragOverlay />
      <ConfirmDialog />
    </DndProvider>
  );
}
```

4. `src/components/DragDrop/DragOverlay.tsx`

```typescript
import { useDragDropStore, useIsDragging, useSelectedItems, useDragImagePosition } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';
import { File, Folder, GripVertical, X, Copy, ArrowRightLeft } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

export function DragOverlay() {
  const isDragging = useIsDragging();
  const selectedItems = useSelectedItems();
  const position = useDragImagePosition();
  const cancelOperation = useDragDropStore((s) => s.cancelOperation);
  
  const [localPosition, setLocalPosition] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });

  useEffect(() => {
    if (position) {
      setLocalPosition(position);
    }
  }, [position]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (isDragging) {
        setLocalPosition({ x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY });
      }
    };

    const handleTouchMove = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      if (isDragging && e.touches[0]) {
        setLocalPosition({ x: e.touches[0].clientX, y: e.touches[0].clientY });
      }
    };

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove, { passive: false });
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove);
    };
  }, [isDragging]);

  if (!isDragging || selectedItems.length === 0) return null;

  return (
    <>
      {/* Floating drag handle */}
      <div
        className={cn(
          "fixed z-50 pointer-events-auto",
          "bg-primary text-primary-foreground",
          "rounded-full shadow-lg",
          "flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2",
          "transform -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2"
        )}
        style={{
          left: localPosition.x,
          top: localPosition.y - 60,
        }}
      >
        <GripVertical className="w-4 h-4" />
        <span className="text-sm font-medium">
          {selectedItems.length} item{selectedItems.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}
        </span>
        
        {/* Action buttons */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 ml-2 border-l border-primary-foreground/30 pl-2">
          <button
            onClick={(e) => {
              e.stopPropagation();
              useDragDropStore.getState().showConfirm('copy');
            }}
            className="p-1 hover:bg-primary-foreground/20 rounded"
            title="Copy"
          >
            <Copy className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={(e) => {
              e.stopPropagation();
              useDragDropStore.getState().showConfirm('move');
            }}
            className="p-1 hover:bg-primary-foreground/20 rounded"
            title="Move"
          >
            <ArrowRightLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={(e) => {
              e.stopPropagation();
              cancelOperation();
            }}
            className="p-1 hover:bg-destructive/20 rounded text-destructive-foreground"
            title="Cancel"
          >
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Drag preview cards */}
      <div
        className="fixed z-40 pointer-events-none opacity-80"
        style={{
          left: localPosition.x,
          top: localPosition.y,
          transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',
        }}
      >
        {selectedItems.slice(0, 3).map((item, index) => (
          <div
            key={item.id}
            className={cn(
              "bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-lg",
              "flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 mb-1",
              "w-48"
            )}
            style={{
              transform: `translate(${index * 4}px, ${index * 4}px)`,
              zIndex: 3 - index,
            }}
          >
            {item.sourceType === 'storage' || item.sourceType === 'terminal' ? (
              item.item.kind === 'directory' || item.item.type === 'directory' ? (
                <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
              ) : (
                <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
              )
            ) : item.sourceType === 'drive' ? (
              item.item.mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder' ? (
                <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
              ) : (
                <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
              )
            ) : (
              item.item.type === 'dir' ? (
                <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
              ) : (
                <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
              )
            )}
            <span className="text-sm truncate">{item.item.name}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
        
        {selectedItems.length > 3 && (
          <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center mt-1">
            +{selectedItems.length - 3} more
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </>
  );
}
```

5. `src/components/DragDrop/ConfirmDialog.tsx`

```typescript
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useDragDropStore, useShowConfirmDialog, usePendingOperation, useSelectedItems, useTargetPanel, useDragSourcePanel } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';
import { Copy, ArrowRightLeft, Folder, File } from 'lucide-react';

export function ConfirmDialog() {
  const showConfirm = useShowConfirmDialog();
  const pendingOperation = usePendingOperation();
  const selectedItems = useSelectedItems();
  const targetPanel = useTargetPanel();
  const sourcePanel = useDragSourcePanel();
  const hideConfirm = useDragDropStore((s) => s.hideConfirm);
  const confirmOperation = useDragDropStore((s) => s.confirmOperation);
  const cancelOperation = useDragDropStore((s) => s.cancelOperation);

  const handleConfirm = () => {
    confirmOperation();
    // The actual operation will be handled by the drop target
    hideConfirm();
  };

  const handleCancel = () => {
    cancelOperation();
    hideConfirm();
  };

  if (!showConfirm || !pendingOperation) return null;

  const Icon = pendingOperation === 'copy' ? Copy : ArrowRightLeft;

  return (
    <Dialog open={showConfirm} onOpenChange={(open) => !open && handleCancel()}>
      <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
        <DialogHeader>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Icon className="w-6 h-6 text-primary" />
            <DialogTitle>
              {pendingOperation === 'copy' ? 'Copy Items' : 'Move Items'}
            </DialogTitle>
          </div>
          <DialogDescription>
            {pendingOperation === 'copy' 
              ? `Copy ${selectedItems.length} item(s) to target panel?`
              : `Move ${selectedItems.length} item(s) to target panel? Original items will be removed.`
            }
          </DialogDescription>
        </DialogHeader>

        <div className="py-4">
          <div className="space-y-2 max-h-48 overflow-auto">
            {selectedItems.map((item) => (
              <div 
                key={item.id} 
                className="flex items-center gap-2 p-2 rounded bg-muted text-sm"
              >
                {item.item.kind === 'directory' || item.item.type === 'directory' || item.item.mimeType?.includes('folder') ? (
                  <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
                ) : (
                  <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
                )}
                <span className="truncate">{item.item.name}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
          
          <div className="mt-4 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            <p>From: Panel {sourcePanel}</p>
            <p>To: Panel {targetPanel || 'Unknown'}</p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <DialogFooter>
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={handleCancel}>
            Cancel
          </Button>
          <Button 
            onClick={handleConfirm}
            variant={pendingOperation === 'move' ? 'destructive' : 'default'}
          >
            {pendingOperation === 'copy' ? 'Copy' : 'Move'}
          </Button>
        </DialogFooter>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```

6. `src/components/DragDrop/useDragDrop.ts` (Hook for items)

```typescript
import { useDrag, useDrop } from 'react-dnd';
import { useCallback, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { useDragDropStore, useIsDragMode, useSelectedItems } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';
import { SelectedItem, SourceType } from '@/types/dragDrop';

interface UseDragDropOptions {
  item: any;
  id: string;
  sourceType: SourceType;
  panelId: string;
  onDrop?: (items: SelectedItem[], operation: 'copy' | 'move') => void;
}

export function useDragDrop({ item, id, sourceType, panelId, onDrop }: UseDragDropOptions) {
  const isDragMode = useIsDragMode();
  const selectedItems = useSelectedItems();
  const dragDropStore = useDragDropStore();
  
  const [isSelected, setIsSelected] = useState(false);
  const [isPressed, setIsPressed] = useState(false);
  const longPressTimer = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);
  const touchStartPos = useRef<{ x: number; y: number } | null>(null);

  // Check if this item is selected
  const isItemSelected = selectedItems.some(
    (si) => si.id === id && si.panelId === panelId
  );

  // Toggle selection
  const toggleSelection = useCallback(() => {
    const selectedItem: SelectedItem = {
      id,
      sourceType,
      item,
      panelId,
    };
    dragDropStore.toggleSelection(selectedItem);
  }, [id, sourceType, item, panelId, dragDropStore]);

  // Long press / touch handlers
  const handleTouchStart = useCallback((e: React.TouchEvent) => {
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    touchStartPos.current = { x: touch.clientX, y: touch.clientY };
    setIsPressed(true);
    
    // Start long press timer
    longPressTimer.current = setTimeout(() => {
      if (!isDragMode) {
        dragDropStore.enterDragMode(panelId);
        toggleSelection();
      }
    }, 500); // 500ms long press
  }, [isDragMode, panelId, dragDropStore, toggleSelection]);

  const handleTouchMove = useCallback((e: React.TouchEvent) => {
    if (!touchStartPos.current) return;
    
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    const deltaX = Math.abs(touch.clientX - touchStartPos.current.x);
    const deltaY = Math.abs(touch.clientY - touchStartPos.current.y);
    
    // Cancel long press if moved too much
    if (deltaX > 10 || deltaY > 10) {
      if (longPressTimer.current) {
        clearTimeout(longPressTimer.current);
        longPressTimer.current = null;
      }
      setIsPressed(false);
    }
    
    // Update drag position if in drag mode
    if (isDragMode && dragDropStore.isDragging) {
      dragDropStore.setDragImagePosition({ x: touch.clientX, y: touch.clientY });
    }
  }, [isDragMode, dragDropStore]);

  const handleTouchEnd = useCallback((e: React.TouchEvent) => {
    if (longPressTimer.current) {
      clearTimeout(longPressTimer.current);
      longPressTimer.current = null;
    }
    setIsPressed(false);
    touchStartPos.current = null;
    
    // If in drag mode and not dragging yet, start drag
    if (isDragMode && !dragDropStore.isDragging && isItemSelected) {
      const touch = e.changedTouches[0];
      dragDropStore.startDrag(panelId, { x: touch.clientX, y: touch.clientY });
    }
  }, [isDragMode, dragDropStore, isItemSelected, panelId]);

  // Mouse handlers for desktop
  const handleMouseDown = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    if (e.button !== 0) return; // Only left click
    
    if (isDragMode) {
      e.preventDefault();
      toggleSelection();
      
      if (!dragDropStore.isDragging && isItemSelected) {
        dragDropStore.startDrag(panelId, { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY });
      }
    }
  }, [isDragMode, dragDropStore, isItemSelected, panelId, toggleSelection]);

  // React DnD setup
  const [{ isDragging }, drag] = useDrag(() => ({
    type: sourceType,
    item: { id, sourceType, item, panelId },
    collect: (monitor) => ({
      isDragging: !!monitor.isDragging(),
    }),
    canDrag: isDragMode && isItemSelected,
  }), [isDragMode, isItemSelected, id, sourceType, item, panelId]);

  const [{ isOver, canDrop }, drop] = useDrop(() => ({
    accept: ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'],
    drop: (droppedItem: any, monitor) => {
      if (!monitor.didDrop()) {
        // Show confirm dialog
        dragDropStore.setTargetPanel(panelId);
        // The operation type will be set by the drag overlay buttons
      }
    },
    collect: (monitor) => ({
      isOver: !!monitor.isOver(),
      canDrop: !!monitor.canDrop(),
    }),
    canDrop: (droppedItem: any) => {
      // Don't drop on same panel
      return droppedItem.panelId !== panelId;
    },
  }), [panelId, dragDropStore]);

  // Combine refs
  const setRefs = useCallback((node: HTMLElement | null) => {
    drag(node);
    drop(node);
  }, [drag, drop]);

  return {
    setRef: setRefs,
    isSelected: isItemSelected,
    isDragging: isDragging || dragDropStore.isDragging,
    isOver,
    canDrop,
    isPressed,
    isDragMode,
    toggleSelection,
    handlers: {
      onTouchStart: handleTouchStart,
      onTouchMove: handleTouchMove,
      onTouchEnd: handleTouchEnd,
      onMouseDown: handleMouseDown,
    },
  };
}
```

7. `src/components/DragDrop/DragDropItem.tsx` (Wrapper Component)

```typescript
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { Check, GripVertical } from 'lucide-react';
import { useDragDrop } from './useDragDrop';
import { SourceType } from '@/types/dragDrop';

interface DragDropItemProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  item: any;
  id: string;
  sourceType: SourceType;
  panelId: string;
  className?: string;
  onDrop?: (items: any[], operation: 'copy' | 'move') => void;
}

export function DragDropItem({
  children,
  item,
  id,
  sourceType,
  panelId,
  className,
  onDrop,
}: DragDropItemProps) {
  const {
    setRef,
    isSelected,
    isDragging,
    isOver,
    canDrop,
    isPressed,
    isDragMode,
    toggleSelection,
    handlers,
  } = useDragDrop({ item, id, sourceType, panelId, onDrop });

  return (
    <div
      ref={setRef}
      className={cn(
        "relative transition-all",
        isSelected && "ring-2 ring-primary bg-primary/5",
        isDragging && "opacity-50",
        isOver && canDrop && "bg-accent/50 ring-2 ring-accent",
        isPressed && "scale-95",
        className
      )}
      {...handlers}
    >
      {/* Selection checkbox */}
      {isDragMode && (
        <div 
          className="absolute top-2 left-2 z-10"
          onClick={(e) => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            toggleSelection();
          }}
        >
          <div className={cn(
            "w-5 h-5 rounded border-2 flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer",
            isSelected 
              ? "bg-primary border-primary text-primary-foreground" 
              : "border-muted-foreground bg-background"
          )}>
            {isSelected && <Check className="w-3 h-3" />}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Drag handle indicator */}
      {isDragMode && isSelected && (
        <div className="absolute top-2 right-2 z-10 p-1 bg-primary/10 rounded cursor-move">
          <GripVertical className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
        </div>
      )}

      {children}
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { useDragDropStore, useIsDragMode, useSelectedItems } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';
import { X, Check, GripVertical } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export function DragModeIndicator() {
  const isDragMode = useIsDragMode();
  const selectedItems = useSelectedItems();
  const exitDragMode = useDragDropStore((s) => s.exitDragMode);
  const clearSelection = useDragDropStore((s) => s.clearSelection);
  const selectAll = useDragDropStore((s) => s.selectAll);

  if (!isDragMode) return null;

  return (
    <div className={cn(
      "fixed bottom-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-40",
      "bg-card border border-border shadow-lg rounded-full",
      "flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2"
    )}>
      <GripVertical className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />

        {selectedItems.length} selected
      </span>

      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 ml-2 border-l border-border pl-2">
        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="sm"
          className="h-7 text-xs"
          onClick={clearSelection}
        >
          Clear
        </Button>
        
        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="sm"
          className="h-7 text-xs text-destructive hover:text-destructive"
          onClick={exitDragMode}
        >
          <X className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />
          Cancel
        </Button>
      </div>

      {selectedItems.length > 0 && (
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 border-l border-border pl-2">
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            Drag to another panel
          </span>
        </div>

    </div>
```

9. `src/components/FileManager/FileGrid.tsx` (Updated with DragDrop)

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, FolderOpen } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { DragDropItem } from '../DragDrop/DragDropItem';

interface FileGridProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  onNavigate: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => void;
  panelId: string;
}

export function FileGrid({ entries, onNavigate, panelId }: FileGridProps) {
  const handleClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      onNavigate(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-3 p-3">
      {entries.map((entry) => (
        <DragDropItem
          key={entry.name}
          item={entry}
          id={entry.name}
          sourceType="storage"
          panelId={panelId}
          className="group flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent transition-all text-left"
        >
          <div 
            className="mb-2 text-primary group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform"
            onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}
          >
            {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
              <FolderOpen className="w-10 h-10" />
            ) : (
              <File className="w-10 h-10" />
            )}
          </div>
          
          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate w-full text-center" title={entry.name}>
            {entry.name}
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
            {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : 'Folder'}
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
          </p>
        </DragDropItem>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
```

```typescript
          key={entry.name}

          id={entry.name}
          sourceType="storage"

        >

            onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}
          >
            {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
              <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
            ) : (
              <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
            )}
            <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={entry.name}>
              {entry.name}
            </span>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-2 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
            {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : '-'}
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-4 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
            {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
          </div>
        </DragDropItem>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
```

11. `src/components/Panel/ResizablePanel.tsx` (Updated with Drop Target)

```typescript
import { useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useDrop } from 'react-dnd';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { useResizable } from '@/hooks/useResizable';
import { PanelHeader } from './PanelHeader';
import { PanelContent } from './PanelContent';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { MIN_PANEL_WIDTH } from '@/types/panel';
import { useDragDropStore, useIsDragging, usePendingOperation, useTargetPanel } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';

interface ResizablePanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  isActive: boolean;
  isLast: boolean;
  onActivate: () => void;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export function ResizablePanel({ 
  panel, 
  isActive, 
  isLast,
  onActivate, 
  onClose 
}: ResizablePanelProps) {
  const setPanelWidth = usePanelStore((s) => s.setPanelWidth);
  const isDraggingGlobal = useIsDragging();
  const pendingOperation = usePendingOperation();
  const targetPanel = useTargetPanel();
  const dragDropStore = useDragDropStore();
  
  const { width, isResizing, startResize } = useResizable({
    initialWidth: panel.width,
    minWidth: MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
    onResize: (newWidth) => setPanelWidth(panel.id, newWidth),
  });

  // Drop target for drag and drop
  const [{ isOver, canDrop }, drop] = useDrop(() => ({
    accept: ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'],
    drop: (item: any, monitor) => {
      if (!monitor.didDrop()) {
        dragDropStore.setTargetPanel(panel.id);
        // Don't complete here - wait for user to select copy/move from floating handle
      }
    },
    collect: (monitor) => ({
      isOver: !!monitor.isOver(),
      canDrop: !!monitor.canDrop(),
    }),
    canDrop: (item: any) => {
      return item.panelId !== panel.id;
    },
  }), [panel.id, dragDropStore]);

  // Handle drop completion when operation is confirmed
  const handleDropComplete = useCallback(() => {
    if (targetPanel === panel.id && pendingOperation) {
      // Execute the copy/move operation
      const selectedItems = dragDropStore.selectedItems;
      
      // TODO: Implement actual copy/move logic based on source and target types
      console.log(`${pendingOperation} ${selectedItems.length} items to panel ${panel.id}`);
      
      // Reset drag state
      dragDropStore.exitDragMode();
    }
  }, [targetPanel, pendingOperation, panel.id, dragDropStore]);

  // Watch for operation confirmation
  useRef(() => {
    if (!dragDropStore.showConfirmDialog && pendingOperation && targetPanel === panel.id) {
      handleDropComplete();
    }
  });

  return (
    <div
      ref={drop}
      className={cn(
        'flex flex-col h-full relative border-r border-border last:border-r-0',
        isActive && 'ring-1 ring-primary/20',
        isResizing && 'select-none',
        isOver && canDrop && 'bg-accent/20 ring-2 ring-accent ring-inset',
        isOver && !canDrop && 'bg-destructive/10'
      )}
      style={{ 
        width: panel.isMinimized ? 60 : width,
        minWidth: panel.isMinimized ? 60 : MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
        flexShrink: 0,
      }}
    >
      <PanelHeader
        panel={panel}
        isActive={isActive}
        onActivate={onActivate}
        onClose={onClose}
      />
      
      {!panel.isMinimized && (
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
          <PanelContent panel={panel} />
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Drop indicator */}
      {isOver && canDrop && (
        <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none bg-accent/10 z-50">
          <div className="bg-card border border-border shadow-lg rounded-lg px-4 py-2">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium">Drop here</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Select copy or move from handle</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Resize handle */}
      {!isLast && !panel.isMinimized && !isDraggingGlobal && (
        <div
          className={cn(
            'absolute right-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-1 cursor-col-resize z-10',
            'hover:bg-primary/50 transition-colors',
            isResizing && 'bg-primary'
          )}
          onMouseDown={startResize}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

14. `src/components/DragDrop/DropHandler.tsx` (Cross-panel operations)

```typescript
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { useDragDropStore, usePendingOperation, useTargetPanel, useSelectedItems, useDragSourcePanel } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';
import { githubApi } from '@/lib/githubApi';
import { webcontainerApi } from '@/lib/webcontainerApi';

// This component handles the actual copy/move operations when confirmed
export function DropHandler() {
  const showConfirm = useDragDropStore((s) => s.showConfirmDialog);
  const pendingOperation = usePendingOperation();
  const targetPanel = useTargetPanel();
  const sourcePanel = useDragSourcePanel();
  const selectedItems = useSelectedItems();

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!showConfirm && pendingOperation && targetPanel && sourcePanel) {
      executeOperation();
    }
  }, [showConfirm, pendingOperation, targetPanel, sourcePanel]);

  const executeOperation = async () => {
    const targetPanelState = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(targetPanel!);
    
    if (!targetPanelState) return;

    console.log(`Executing ${pendingOperation} from ${sourcePanel} to ${targetPanel}`);

    for (const item of selectedItems) {
      try {
        switch (targetPanelState.source) {
          case 'storage':
            await handleStorageDrop(item, pendingOperation!);
            break;
          case 'drive':
            // TODO: Implement Google Drive write operations
            console.log('Drive drop not yet implemented');
            break;
          case 'github':
            // GitHub requires commit operations - read-only for now
            console.log('GitHub is read-only');
            break;
          case 'terminal':
            await handleTerminalDrop(item, pendingOperation!);
            break;
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`Failed to ${pendingOperation} ${item.id}:`, error);
      }
    }

    // Reset drag state
    useDragDropStore.getState().exitDragMode();
  };

  const handleStorageDrop = async (item: any, operation: 'copy' | 'move') => {
    // TODO: Implement actual file system copy/move
    // This requires access to the source file handle and target directory handle
    console.log(`Storage ${operation}:`, item);
  };

  const handleTerminalDrop = async (item: any, operation: 'copy' | 'move') => {
    // TODO: Implement WebContainer FS operations
    console.log(`Terminal ${operation}:`, item);
  };

  return null; // This is a logic-only component
}
```
