1. `src/types/rename.ts` (Rename Types)

```typescript
export type FileExtension = string;

export interface ConversionRule {
  from: FileExtension[];
  to: FileExtension;
  engine: 'mammoth' | 'sharp' | 'ffmpeg' | 'jszip' | 'native';
  description: string;
}

export interface RenameState {
  renamingItem: {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    path: string;
    sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
    panelId: string;
  } | null;
  newName: string;
  isConverting: boolean;
  conversionProgress: number;
  conversionResult: {
    success: boolean;
    originalFile?: Blob;
    convertedFile?: Blob;
    message: string;
  } | null;
  showKeepReplaceDialog: boolean;
  pendingConversion: {
    originalName: string;
    newName: string;
    originalBlob: Blob;
    convertedBlob: Blob;
  } | null;
}

export interface ConversionEngine {
  name: string;
  isReady: boolean;
  init: () => Promise<void>;
  convert: (file: Blob, fromExt: string, toExt: string, onProgress?: (p: number) => void) => Promise<Blob>;
}

export const CONVERSION_RULES: ConversionRule[] = [
  // Document conversions
  { from: ['.docx', '.doc'], to: '.txt', engine: 'mammoth', description: 'Word to Text' },
  { from: ['.docx', '.doc'], to: '.html', engine: 'mammoth', description: 'Word to HTML' },
  
  // Image conversions (via Sharp WASM or canvas)
  { from: ['.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp', '.gif', '.bmp'], to: '.png', engine: 'sharp', description: 'To PNG' },
  { from: ['.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp', '.gif', '.bmp'], to: '.jpg', engine: 'sharp', description: 'To JPEG' },
  { from: ['.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp', '.gif', '.bmp'], to: '.webp', engine: 'sharp', description: 'To WebP' },
  
  // Video/Audio conversions (via FFmpeg WASM)
  { from: ['.mp4', '.avi', '.mov', '.mkv', '.webm'], to: '.mp4', engine: 'ffmpeg', description: 'To MP4' },
  { from: ['.mp4', '.avi', '.mov', '.mkv', '.webm'], to: '.webm', engine: 'ffmpeg', description: 'To WebM' },
  { from: ['.mp3', '.wav', '.aac', '.ogg', '.flac'], to: '.mp3', engine: 'ffmpeg', description: 'To MP3' },
  
  // Archive conversions
  { from: ['.folder'], to: '.zip', engine: 'jszip', description: 'Folder to ZIP' },
];
```

2. `src/lib/conversionEngines.ts` (Conversion Engines)

```typescript
import { ConversionEngine, CONVERSION_RULES } from '@/types/rename';
import { FFmpeg } from '@ffmpeg/ffmpeg';
import { fetchFile, toBlobURL } from '@ffmpeg/util';
import JSZip from 'jszip';
import mammoth from 'mammoth';
import { saveAs } from 'file-saver';

// FFmpeg WASM Engine
class FFmpegEngine implements ConversionEngine {
  name = 'ffmpeg';
  isReady = false;
  private ffmpeg: FFmpeg | null = null;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.isReady) return;
    
    this.ffmpeg = new FFmpeg();
    const baseURL = 'https://unpkg.com/@ffmpeg/core@0.12.6/dist/umd';
    
    await this.ffmpeg.load({
      coreURL: await toBlobURL(`${baseURL}/ffmpeg-core.js`, 'text/javascript'),
      wasmURL: await toBlobURL(`${baseURL}/ffmpeg-core.wasm`, 'application/wasm'),
    });
    
    this.isReady = true;
  }

  async convert(
    file: Blob, 
    fromExt: string, 
    toExt: string, 
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    if (!this.ffmpeg) throw new Error('FFmpeg not initialized');
    
    const inputName = `input${fromExt}`;
    const outputName = `output${toExt}`;
    
    // Write file to FFmpeg FS
    const fileData = await fetchFile(file);
    await this.ffmpeg.writeFile(inputName, fileData);
    
    // Run conversion
    const args = this.getConversionArgs(fromExt, toExt, inputName, outputName);
    
    this.ffmpeg.on('progress', ({ progress }) => {
      onProgress?.(Math.round(progress * 100));
    });
    
    await this.ffmpeg.exec(args);
    
    // Read output
    const data = await this.ffmpeg.readFile(outputName);
    const outputBlob = new Blob([data], { type: this.getMimeType(toExt) });
    
    // Cleanup
    await this.ffmpeg.deleteFile(inputName);
    await this.ffmpeg.deleteFile(outputName);
    
    return outputBlob;
  }

  private getConversionArgs(fromExt: string, toExt: string, input: string, output: string): string[] {
    // Video to video
    if (['.mp4', '.avi', '.mov', '.mkv', '.webm'].includes(fromExt)) {
      if (toExt === '.webm') return ['-i', input, '-c:v', 'libvpx-vp9', '-c:a', 'libopus', output];
      return ['-i', input, '-c:v', 'libx264', '-c:a', 'aac', output];
    }
    
    // Audio to audio
    if (['.mp3', '.wav', '.aac', '.ogg', '.flac'].includes(fromExt)) {
      if (toExt === '.mp3') return ['-i', input, '-c:a', 'libmp3lame', '-q:a', '2', output];
      return ['-i', input, output];
    }
    
    return ['-i', input, output];
  }

  private getMimeType(ext: string): string {
    const mimeTypes: Record<string, string> = {
      '.mp4': 'video/mp4',
      '.webm': 'video/webm',
      '.mp3': 'audio/mpeg',
      '.wav': 'audio/wav',
    };
    return mimeTypes[ext] || 'application/octet-stream';
  }
}

// Sharp-like Image Engine (using Canvas API for browser)
class CanvasImageEngine implements ConversionEngine {
  name = 'sharp';
  isReady = true;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.isReady = true;
  }

  async convert(
    file: Blob, 
    fromExt: string, 
    toExt: string, 
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const img = new Image();
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);
      
      img.onload = () => {
        const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
        canvas.width = img.width;
        canvas.height = img.height;
        
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        if (!ctx) {
          reject(new Error('Canvas not supported'));
          return;
        }
        
        // Handle transparency for PNG/WebP
        if (toExt === '.png' || toExt === '.webp') {
          ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        }
        
        ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        
        const mimeType = toExt === '.jpg' || toExt === '.jpeg' 
          ? 'image/jpeg' 
          : toExt === '.webp' 
            ? 'image/webp' 
            : 'image/png';
        
        canvas.toBlob((blob) => {
          if (blob) {
            resolve(blob);
          } else {
            reject(new Error('Canvas to Blob failed'));
          }
        }, mimeType, 0.9);
      };
      
      img.onerror = () => {
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        reject(new Error('Image load failed'));
      };
      
      img.src = url;
    });
  }
}

// Mammoth Document Engine
class MammothEngine implements ConversionEngine {
  name = 'mammoth';
  isReady = true;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.isReady = true;
  }

  async convert(
    file: Blob, 
    fromExt: string, 
    toExt: string, 
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
    
    let result: { value: string };
    
    if (toExt === '.html') {
      result = await mammoth.convertToHtml({ arrayBuffer });
    } else {
      result = await mammoth.extractRawText({ arrayBuffer });
    }
    
    const mimeType = toExt === '.html' ? 'text/html' : 'text/plain';
    return new Blob([result.value], { type: mimeType });
  }
}

// JSZip Archive Engine
class JSZipEngine implements ConversionEngine {
  name = 'jszip';
  isReady = true;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.isReady = true;
  }

  async convert(
    file: Blob, 
    fromExt: string, 
    toExt: string, 
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    // For folder to zip conversion
    // This requires the folder contents to be passed separately
    // For now, return empty zip as placeholder
    const zip = new JSZip();
    const content = await zip.generateAsync({ type: 'blob' });
    return content;
  }

  async compressFolder(
    files: { name: string; content: Blob | string }[],
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    const zip = new JSZip();
    
    files.forEach((file, index) => {
      zip.file(file.name, file.content);
      onProgress?.(Math.round((index / files.length) * 50));
    });
    
    const content = await zip.generateAsync(
      { type: 'blob' },
      (metadata) => {
        onProgress?.(50 + Math.round(metadata.percent / 2));
      }
    );
    
    return content;
  }
}

// Export engines
export const ffmpegEngine = new FFmpegEngine();
export const imageEngine = new CanvasImageEngine();
export const mammothEngine = new MammothEngine();
export const zipEngine = new JSZipEngine();

export function getEngineForConversion(fromExt: string, toExt: string): ConversionEngine | null {
  const rule = CONVERSION_RULES.find(r => 
    r.from.includes(fromExt.toLowerCase()) && r.to === toExt.toLowerCase()
  );
  
  if (!rule) return null;
  
  switch (rule.engine) {
    case 'ffmpeg': return ffmpegEngine;
    case 'sharp': return imageEngine;
    case 'mammoth': return mammothEngine;
    case 'jszip': return zipEngine;
    default: return null;
  }
}

export function needsConversion(oldName: string, newName: string): boolean {
  const oldExt = getExtension(oldName);
  const newExt = getExtension(newName);
  return oldExt !== newExt && getEngineForConversion(oldExt, newExt) !== null;
}

export function getExtension(filename: string): string {
  const ext = filename.slice(filename.lastIndexOf('.')).toLowerCase();
  return ext.includes('.') ? ext : '';
}
```

3. `src/stores/renameStore.ts` (Rename Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { RenameState } from '@/types/rename';
import { getEngineForConversion, needsConversion, getExtension } from '@/lib/conversionEngines';

interface RenameStore extends RenameState {
  // Actions
  startRename: (item: RenameState['renamingItem']) => void;
  updateNewName: (name: string) => void;
  cancelRename: () => void;
  confirmRename: () => Promise<void>;
  setConversionProgress: (progress: number) => void;
  showKeepReplaceDialog: (result: RenameState['pendingConversion']) => void;
  keepBoth: () => Promise<void>;
  replaceOriginal: () => Promise<void>;
  skipConversion: () => Promise<void>;
}

export const useRenameStore = create<RenameStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    renamingItem: null,
    newName: '',
    isConverting: false,
    conversionProgress: 0,
    conversionResult: null,
    showKeepReplaceDialog: false,
    pendingConversion: null,

    startRename: (item) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.renamingItem = item;
        state.newName = item.name;
        state.isConverting = false;
        state.conversionProgress = 0;
        state.conversionResult = null;
        state.showKeepReplaceDialog = false;
        state.pendingConversion = null;
      });
    },

    updateNewName: (name) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.newName = name;
      });
    },

    cancelRename: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.renamingItem = null;
        state.newName = '';
        state.isConverting = false;
        state.conversionProgress = 0;
        state.conversionResult = null;
        state.showKeepReplaceDialog = false;
        state.pendingConversion = null;
      });
    },

    confirmRename: async () => {
      const { renamingItem, newName } = get();
      if (!renamingItem) return;

      const oldExt = getExtension(renamingItem.name);
      const newExt = getExtension(newName);

      // Check if conversion needed
      if (oldExt !== newExt && needsConversion(renamingItem.name, newName)) {
        set((state) => {
          state.isConverting = true;
          state.conversionProgress = 0;
        });

        try {
          const engine = getEngineForConversion(oldExt, newExt);
          if (!engine) {
            throw new Error('Conversion not supported');
          }

          // Initialize engine if needed
          if (!engine.isReady) {
            await engine.init();
          }

          // Get original file blob
          const originalBlob = await getOriginalFileBlob(renamingItem);
          
          // Convert
          const convertedBlob = await engine.convert(
            originalBlob,
            oldExt,
            newExt,
            (progress) => {
              set((state) => {
                state.conversionProgress = progress;
              });
            }
          );

          // Show keep/replace dialog
          set((state) => {
            state.isConverting = false;
            state.pendingConversion = {
              originalName: renamingItem.name,
              newName,
              originalBlob,
              convertedBlob,
            };
            state.showKeepReplaceDialog = true;
          });

        } catch (error) {
          set((state) => {
            state.isConverting = false;
            state.conversionResult = {
              success: false,
              message: (error as Error).message,
            };
          });
        }
      } else {
        // Simple rename without conversion
        await performSimpleRename(renamingItem, newName);
        get().cancelRename();
      }
    },

    setConversionProgress: (progress) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.conversionProgress = progress;
      });
    },

    showKeepReplaceDialog: (result) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.pendingConversion = result;
        state.showKeepReplaceDialog = true;
      });
    },

    keepBoth: async () => {
      const { pendingConversion, renamingItem } = get();
      if (!pendingConversion || !renamingItem) return;

      // Save both files
      await saveFile(pendingConversion.originalBlob, pendingConversion.originalName, renamingItem);
      await saveFile(pendingConversion.convertedBlob, pendingConversion.newName, renamingItem);
      
      get().cancelRename();
    },

    replaceOriginal: async () => {
      const { pendingConversion, renamingItem } = get();
      if (!pendingConversion || !renamingItem) return;

      // Delete original and save converted
      await deleteFile(renamingItem);
      await saveFile(pendingConversion.convertedBlob, pendingConversion.newName, renamingItem);
      
      get().cancelRename();
    },

    skipConversion: async () => {
      const { renamingItem, newName } = get();
      if (!renamingItem) return;

      // Just rename without conversion
      await performSimpleRename(renamingItem, newName);
      get().cancelRename();
    },
  }))
);

// Helper functions
async function getOriginalFileBlob(item: any): Promise<Blob> {
  // Implementation depends on source type
  switch (item.sourceType) {
    case 'storage':
      // Use File System Access API
      if (item.handle) {
        const file = await item.handle.getFile();
        return file;
      }
      break;
    case 'drive':
      // Download from Google Drive
      // TODO: Implement Drive download
      break;
    case 'github':
      // Download from GitHub
      // TODO: Implement GitHub download
      break;
    case 'terminal':
      // Read from WebContainer
      // TODO: Implement WebContainer read
      break;
  }
  throw new Error('Cannot read file from source');
}

async function saveFile(blob: Blob, name: string, context: any): Promise<void> {
  // Implementation depends on source type
  console.log('Saving file:', name, 'Size:', blob.size);
  // TODO: Implement per-source save
}

async function deleteFile(item: any): Promise<void> {
  // Implementation depends on source type
  console.log('Deleting file:', item.name);
  // TODO: Implement per-source delete
}

async function performSimpleRename(item: any, newName: string): Promise<void> {

  // TODO: Implement per-source rename
}
```

4. `src/components/Rename/InlineRenameInput.tsx`

```typescript
import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { useRenameStore } from '@/stores/renameStore';
import { Loader2, AlertCircle, Check } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { getExtension, needsConversion } from '@/lib/conversionEngines';

interface InlineRenameInputProps {
  item: {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    path: string;
    sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
    panelId: string;
  };
  onComplete?: () => void;
  className?: string;
}

export function InlineRenameInput({ item, onComplete, className }: InlineRenameInputProps) {
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const [showExtensionWarning, setShowExtensionWarning] = useState(false);
  
  const {
    renamingItem,
    newName,
    isConverting,
    conversionProgress,
    updateNewName,
    cancelRename,
    confirmRename,
  } = useRenameStore();

  // Start rename mode for this item
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!renamingItem || renamingItem.id !== item.id) {
      useRenameStore.getState().startRename(item);
    }
  }, [item]);

  // Focus input on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    if (inputRef.current) {
      inputRef.current.focus();
      inputRef.current.select();
    }
  }, []);

  // Check for extension change
  useEffect(() => {
    const oldExt = getExtension(item.name);
    const newExt = getExtension(newName);
    setShowExtensionWarning(oldExt !== newExt && needsConversion(item.name, newName));
  }, [newName, item.name]);

  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter') {
      confirmRename();
    } else if (e.key === 'Escape') {
      cancelRename();
      onComplete?.();
    }
  };

  const handleBlur = () => {
    // Don't cancel immediately to allow clicking buttons
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (!useRenameStore.getState().showKeepReplaceDialog) {
        cancelRename();
        onComplete?.();
      }
    }, 200);
  };

  if (!renamingItem || renamingItem.id !== item.id) return null;

  return (
    <div className={cn("relative", className)}>
      <div className="relative flex items-center">
        <input
          ref={inputRef}
          type="text"
          value={newName}
          onChange={(e) => updateNewName(e.target.value)}
          onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
          onBlur={handleBlur}
          disabled={isConverting}
          className={cn(
            "w-full px-2 py-1 text-sm rounded border",
            "bg-background text-foreground",
            "focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary",
            isConverting && "opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed",
            showExtensionWarning && "border-orange-500 focus:border-orange-500 focus:ring-orange-500"
          )}
        />
        
        {isConverting && (
          <div className="absolute right-2 flex items-center gap-1">
            <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin text-primary" />
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{conversionProgress}%</span>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Extension change warning */}
      {showExtensionWarning && !isConverting && (
        <div className="absolute top-full left-0 mt-1 p-2 bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded text-xs text-orange-700 flex items-start gap-1 z-50">
          <AlertCircle className="w-3 h-3 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
          <div>
            <p className="font-medium">Format conversion required</p>
            <p>Press Enter to convert from {getExtension(item.name)} to {getExtension(newName)}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Conversion success indicator */}
      {useRenameStore.getState().conversionResult?.success && (
        <div className="absolute top-full left-0 mt-1 p-2 bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded text-xs text-green-700 flex items-center gap-1">
          <Check className="w-3 h-3" />
          Conversion complete
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

5. `src/components/Rename/KeepReplaceDialog.tsx`

```typescript
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useRenameStore } from '@/stores/renameStore';
import { File, Copy, Replace, SkipForward } from 'lucide-react';

export function KeepReplaceDialog() {
  const {
    showKeepReplaceDialog,
    pendingConversion,
    keepBoth,
    replaceOriginal,
    skipConversion,
    cancelRename,
  } = useRenameStore();

  if (!showKeepReplaceDialog || !pendingConversion) return null;

  const originalSize = (pendingConversion.originalBlob.size / 1024).toFixed(1);
  const convertedSize = (pendingConversion.convertedBlob.size / 1024).toFixed(1);

  return (
    <Dialog open={showKeepReplaceDialog} onOpenChange={(open) => !open && cancelRename()}>
      <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <File className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
            Conversion Complete
          </DialogTitle>
          <DialogDescription>
            Choose how to handle the converted file
          </DialogDescription>
        </DialogHeader>

        <div className="py-4 space-y-4">
          {/* File comparison */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-lg bg-muted">
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1">Original</p>
              <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{pendingConversion.originalName}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{originalSize} KB</p>
            </div>
            <div className="p-3 rounded-lg bg-primary/5 border border-primary/20">
              <p className="text-xs text-primary mb-1">Converted</p>
              <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{pendingConversion.newName}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{convertedSize} KB</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Options */}
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <Button
              variant="outline"
              className="w-full justify-start gap-2"
              onClick={keepBoth}
            >
              <Copy className="w-4 h-4" />
              <div className="text-left">
                <p className="font-medium">Keep Both</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Save original and converted file</p>
              </div>
            </Button>

            <Button
              variant="outline"
              className="w-full justify-start gap-2"
              onClick={replaceOriginal}
            >
              <Replace className="w-4 h-4" />
              <div className="text-left">
                <p className="font-medium">Replace Original</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Delete original, keep converted only</p>
              </div>
            </Button>

            <Button
              variant="ghost"
              className="w-full justify-start gap-2 text-muted-foreground"
              onClick={skipConversion}
            >
              <SkipForward className="w-4 h-4" />
              <div className="text-left">
                <p className="font-medium">Skip Conversion</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Just rename without converting</p>
              </div>
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <DialogFooter>
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={cancelRename}>
            Cancel
          </Button>
        </DialogFooter>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```

6. `src/components/FileManager/FileList.tsx` (Updated with Rename)

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, Folder, Pencil } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { DragDropItem } from '../DragDrop/DragDropItem';
import { InlineRenameInput } from '../Rename/InlineRenameInput';
import { useRenameStore } from '@/stores/renameStore';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface FileListProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  onNavigate: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => void;
  panelId: string;
}

export function FileList({ entries, onNavigate, panelId }: FileListProps) {
  const [renamingId, setRenamingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const renamingItem = useRenameStore((s) => s.renamingItem);

  const handleClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (renamingId) return; // Don't navigate while renaming
    
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      onNavigate(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  const startRename = (entry: FileSystemEntry, e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setRenamingId(entry.name);
  };

  const handleRenameComplete = () => {
    setRenamingId(null);
  };

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground bg-muted/50">
        <div className="col-span-6">Name</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Size</div>
        <div className="col-span-3">Modified</div>
        <div className="col-span-1"></div>
      </div>

      {entries.map((entry) => {
        const isRenaming = renamingId === entry.name;
        
        return (
          <DragDropItem
            key={entry.name}
            item={entry}
            id={entry.name}
            sourceType="storage"
            panelId={panelId}
            className="w-full grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left items-center group"
          >
            {isRenaming ? (
              <div className="col-span-12">
                <InlineRenameInput
                  item={{
                    id: entry.name,
                    name: entry.name,
                    path: entry.handle?.name || entry.name,
                    sourceType: 'storage',
                    panelId,
                    handle: entry.handle,
                  }}
                  onComplete={handleRenameComplete}
                />
              </div>
            ) : (
              <>
                <div 
                  className="col-span-6 flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0"
                  onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}
                >
                  {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
                    <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
                  ) : (
                    <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
                  )}
                  <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={entry.name}>
                    {entry.name}
                  </span>
                </div>
                
                <div className="col-span-2 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
                  {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : '-'}
                </div>
                
                <div className="col-span-3 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
                  {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
                </div>

                <div className="col-span-1 flex justify-end opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100">
                  <button
                    onClick={(e) => startRename(entry, e)}
                    className="p-1 hover:bg-accent rounded"
                  >
                    <Pencil className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
                  </button>
                </div>
              </>
            )}
          </DragDropItem>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
```

7. `src/components/FileManager/FileGrid.tsx` (Updated with Rename)

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, FolderOpen, Pencil } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { DragDropItem } from '../DragDrop/DragDropItem';
import { InlineRenameInput } from '../Rename/InlineRenameInput';
import { useRenameStore } from '@/stores/renameStore';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface FileGridProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  onNavigate: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => void;
  panelId: string;
}

export function FileGrid({ entries, onNavigate, panelId }: FileGridProps) {
  const [renamingId, setRenamingId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const handleClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (renamingId) return;
    
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      onNavigate(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  const startRename = (entry: FileSystemEntry, e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setRenamingId(entry.name);
  };

  const handleRenameComplete = () => {
    setRenamingId(null);
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-3 p-3">
      {entries.map((entry) => {
        const isRenaming = renamingId === entry.name;
        
        return (
          <DragDropItem
            key={entry.name}
            item={entry}
            id={entry.name}
            sourceType="storage"
            panelId={panelId}
            className="group flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent transition-all text-left relative"
          >
            {isRenaming ? (
              <div className="w-full">
                <InlineRenameInput
                  item={{
                    id: entry.name,
                    name: entry.name,
                    path: entry.handle?.name || entry.name,
                    sourceType: 'storage',
                    panelId,
                    handle: entry.handle,
                  }}
                  onComplete={handleRenameComplete}
                />
              </div>
            ) : (
              <>
                {/* Rename button */}
                <button
                  onClick={(e) => startRename(entry, e)}
                  className="absolute top-2 right-2 p-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 hover:bg-accent rounded transition-opacity"
                >
                  <Pencil className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
                </button>

                <div 
                  className="mb-2 text-primary group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform"
                  onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}
                >
                  {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
                    <FolderOpen className="w-10 h-10" />
                  ) : (
                    <File className="w-10 h-10" />
                  )}
                </div>
                
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate w-full text-center" title={entry.name}>
                  {entry.name}
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                  {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : 'Folder'}
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                  {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
                </p>
              </>
            )}
          </DragDropItem>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
```

9. `src/components/Rename/WebWorkerConverter.ts` (Web Worker for heavy conversions)

```typescript
// Web Worker for running conversions off main thread

const workerCode = `
self.onmessage = async (e) => {
  const { type, fileData, fromExt, toExt } = e.data;
  
  try {
    switch (type) {
      case 'ffmpeg':
        // FFmpeg operations would go here
        // Note: FFmpeg WASM can't easily run in worker due to SharedArrayBuffer
        self.postMessage({ type: 'progress', progress: 50 });
        break;
        
      case 'image':
        // Canvas-based image conversion
        const result = await convertImage(fileData, fromExt, toExt);
        self.postMessage({ type: 'complete', result });
        break;
        
      default:
        throw new Error('Unknown conversion type');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    self.postMessage({ type: 'error', error: error.message });
  }
};

async function convertImage(fileData: ArrayBuffer, fromExt: string, toExt: string): Promise<ArrayBuffer> {
  // Create blob from array buffer
  const blob = new Blob([fileData]);
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  
  try {
    const img = await loadImage(url);
    const canvas = new OffscreenCanvas(img.width, img.height);
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    
    if (!ctx) throw new Error('Canvas context not available');
    
    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    
    const mimeType = toExt === '.jpg' || toExt === '.jpeg' 
      ? 'image/jpeg' 
      : toExt === '.webp' 
        ? 'image/webp' 
        : 'image/png';
    
    const outputBlob = await canvas.convertToBlob({ type: mimeType, quality: 0.9 });
    return await outputBlob.arrayBuffer();
  } catch (error) {
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    throw error;
  }
}

function loadImage(url: string): Promise<ImageBitmap> {
  return fetch(url)
    .then(r => r.blob())
    .then(b => createImageBitmap(b));
}
`;

// Create worker from code string
export function createConverterWorker(): Worker {
  const blob = new Blob([workerCode], { type: 'application/javascript' });
  const workerUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  return new Worker(workerUrl);
}
```

1. `src/types/tree.ts` (Tree Types)

```typescript
export interface TreeNode {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: 'file' | 'directory' | 'symlink' | 'root';
  path: string;
  size: number;
  lastModified: Date;
  children?: TreeNode[];
  parent?: TreeNode;
  depth: number;
  properties: NodeProperties;
}

export interface NodeProperties {
  mountPath?: string;
  usedSpace?: number;
  freeSpace?: number;
  totalSpace?: number;
  fileSystemType?: string;
  label?: string;
  createdAt?: Date;
  modifiedAt?: Date;
  accessedAt?: Date;
  permissions?: string;
  owner?: string;
  group?: string;
  mimeType?: string;
  isHidden?: boolean;
  isReadOnly?: boolean;
  isSystem?: boolean;
  linkTarget?: string;
  checksum?: string;
  version?: string;
  tags?: string[];
}

export interface TreeViewState {
  isOpen: boolean;
  selectedNode: TreeNode | null;
  rootNode: TreeNode | null;
  expandedNodes: Set<string>;
  viewMode: 'hierarchy' | 'flat' | 'properties';
  searchQuery: string;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  exportFormat: 'txt' | 'pdf' | null;
}

export interface TreeStats {
  totalFiles: number;
  totalDirectories: number;
  totalSize: number;
  maxDepth: number;
  averageFileSize: number;
}
```

2. `src/stores/treeStore.ts` (Tree Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { TreeViewState, TreeNode, TreeStats, NodeProperties } from '@/types/tree';

interface TreeStore extends TreeViewState {
  // Actions
  openTree: (node: TreeNode) => void;
  closeTree: () => void;
  toggleNode: (nodeId: string) => void;
  expandAll: () => void;
  collapseAll: () => void;
  expandToNode: (nodeId: string) => void;
  setViewMode: (mode: TreeViewState['viewMode']) => void;
  setSearchQuery: (query: string) => void;
  updateNodeProperties: (nodeId: string, properties: Partial<NodeProperties>) => void;
  selectNode: (node: TreeNode) => void;
  calculateStats: () => TreeStats;
  exportToTxt: () => string;
  exportToPdf: () => Promise<Blob>;
  copyToClipboard: (type: 'properties' | 'tree' | 'both') => Promise<void>;
}

const createInitialState = (): TreeViewState => ({
  isOpen: false,
  selectedNode: null,
  rootNode: null,
  expandedNodes: new Set(),
  viewMode: 'hierarchy',
  searchQuery: '',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  exportFormat: null,
});

export const useTreeStore = create<TreeStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    ...createInitialState(),

    openTree: (node) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isOpen = true;
        state.selectedNode = node;
        state.rootNode = node;
        state.expandedNodes = new Set([node.id]);
      });
    },

    closeTree: () => {
      set(createInitialState());
    },

    toggleNode: (nodeId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.expandedNodes.has(nodeId)) {
          state.expandedNodes.delete(nodeId);
        } else {
          state.expandedNodes.add(nodeId);
        }
      });
    },

    expandAll: () => {
      const { rootNode } = get();
      if (!rootNode) return;

      const allIds = new Set<string>();
      const collectIds = (node: TreeNode) => {
        allIds.add(node.id);
        node.children?.forEach(collectIds);
      };
      collectIds(rootNode);

      set((state) => {
        state.expandedNodes = allIds;
      });
    },

    collapseAll: () => {
      const { rootNode } = get();
      if (!rootNode) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.expandedNodes = new Set([rootNode.id]);
      });
    },

    expandToNode: (nodeId) => {
      set((state) => {
        // Expand all parents of the target node
        let current = state.selectedNode;
        while (current?.parent) {
          state.expandedNodes.add(current.parent.id);
          current = current.parent;
        }
        state.expandedNodes.add(nodeId);
      });
    },

    setViewMode: (mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setSearchQuery: (query) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.searchQuery = query;
      });
    },

    updateNodeProperties: (nodeId, properties) => {
      set((state) => {
        const updateNode = (node: TreeNode): boolean => {
          if (node.id === nodeId) {
            node.properties = { ...node.properties, ...properties };
            return true;
          }
          return node.children?.some(updateNode) || false;
        };
        if (state.rootNode) updateNode(state.rootNode);
      });
    },

    selectNode: (node) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedNode = node;
      });
    },

    calculateStats: () => {
      const { rootNode } = get();
      if (!rootNode) {
        return {
          totalFiles: 0,
          totalDirectories: 0,
          totalSize: 0,
          maxDepth: 0,
          averageFileSize: 0,
        };
      }

      let totalFiles = 0;
      let totalDirectories = 0;
      let totalSize = 0;
      let maxDepth = 0;
      const fileSizes: number[] = [];

      const traverse = (node: TreeNode, depth: number) => {
        maxDepth = Math.max(maxDepth, depth);
        
        if (node.type === 'file') {
          totalFiles++;
          totalSize += node.size;
          fileSizes.push(node.size);
        } else if (node.type === 'directory') {
          totalDirectories++;
        }

        node.children?.forEach(child => traverse(child, depth + 1));
      };

      traverse(rootNode, 0);

      return {
        totalFiles,
        totalDirectories,
        totalSize,
        maxDepth,
        averageFileSize: fileSizes.length > 0 
          ? fileSizes.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / fileSizes.length 
          : 0,
      };
    },

    exportToTxt: () => {
      const { rootNode, selectedNode } = get();
      const targetNode = selectedNode || rootNode;
      if (!targetNode) return '';

      let output = '';
      output += `TREE STRUCTURE REPORT\n`;
      output += `=====================\n\n`;
      output += `Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}\n`;
      output += `Root: ${targetNode.name}\n`;
      output += `Path: ${targetNode.path}\n\n`;

      const buildTree = (node: TreeNode, prefix: string, isLast: boolean) => {
        const connector = isLast ? '└── ' : '├── ';
        const line = prefix + connector + node.name;
        output += line + '\n';

        if (node.children) {
          const newPrefix = prefix + (isLast ? '    ' : '│   ');
          node.children.forEach((child, index) => {
            buildTree(child, newPrefix, index === node.children!.length - 1);
          });
        }
      };

      if (targetNode.children) {
        targetNode.children.forEach((child, index) => {
          buildTree(child, '', index === targetNode.children!.length - 1);
        });
      }

      // Add properties section
      output += `\n\nPROPERTIES\n`;
      output += `==========\n`;
      output += formatProperties(targetNode.properties);

      return output;
    },

    exportToPdf: async () => {
      const { jsPDF } = await import('jspdf');
      const { rootNode, selectedNode } = get();
      const targetNode = selectedNode || rootNode;
      
      if (!targetNode) throw new Error('No node selected');

      const doc = new jsPDF();
      
      // Title
      doc.setFontSize(20);
      doc.text('Tree Structure Report', 14, 20);
      
      // Metadata
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.text(`Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`, 14, 30);
      doc.text(`Root: ${targetNode.name}`, 14, 36);
      doc.text(`Path: ${targetNode.path}`, 14, 42);

      // Tree table
      const tableData: string[][] = [];
      const buildTableData = (node: TreeNode, depth: number) => {
        const indent = '  '.repeat(depth);
        tableData.push([
          indent + node.name,
          node.type,
          formatBytes(node.size),
          node.lastModified.toLocaleDateString(),
        ]);

        node.children?.forEach(child => buildTableData(child, depth + 1));
      };

      if (targetNode.children) {
        targetNode.children.forEach(child => buildTableData(child, 0));
      }

      // @ts-ignore - jspdf-autotable
      doc.autoTable({
        startY: 50,
        head: [['Name', 'Type', 'Size', 'Modified']],
        body: tableData,
        styles: { fontSize: 8, cellPadding: 2 },
        headStyles: { fillColor: [66, 139, 202] },
      });

      // Properties section
      const finalY = (doc as any).lastAutoTable?.finalY || 50;
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.text('Properties', 14, finalY + 10);

      const props = formatPropertiesForPdf(targetNode.properties);
      // @ts-ignore
      doc.autoTable({
        startY: finalY + 15,
        body: props,
        styles: { fontSize: 8 },
      });

      return doc.output('blob');
    },

    copyToClipboard: async (type) => {
      const { exportToTxt, selectedNode, rootNode } = get();
      const targetNode = selectedNode || rootNode;
      if (!targetNode) return;

      let text = '';

      switch (type) {
        case 'properties':
          text = formatProperties(targetNode.properties);
          break;
        case 'tree':
          text = exportToTxt();
          break;
        case 'both':
          text = exportToTxt();
          break;
      }

      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    },
  }))
);

// Helper functions
function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

function formatProperties(props: NodeProperties): string {
  let output = '';
  if (props.mountPath) output += `Mount Path: ${props.mountPath}\n`;
  if (props.usedSpace !== undefined) output += `Used Space: ${formatBytes(props.usedSpace)}\n`;
  if (props.freeSpace !== undefined) output += `Free Space: ${formatBytes(props.freeSpace)}\n`;
  if (props.totalSpace !== undefined) output += `Total Space: ${formatBytes(props.totalSpace)}\n`;
  if (props.fileSystemType) output += `File System: ${props.fileSystemType}\n`;
  if (props.label) output += `Label: ${props.label}\n`;
  if (props.createdAt) output += `Created: ${props.createdAt.toLocaleString()}\n`;
  if (props.modifiedAt) output += `Modified: ${props.modifiedAt.toLocaleString()}\n`;
  if (props.accessedAt) output += `Accessed: ${props.accessedAt.toLocaleString()}\n`;
  if (props.permissions) output += `Permissions: ${props.permissions}\n`;
  if (props.owner) output += `Owner: ${props.owner}\n`;
  if (props.group) output += `Group: ${props.group}\n`;
  if (props.mimeType) output += `MIME Type: ${props.mimeType}\n`;
  if (props.isHidden !== undefined) output += `Hidden: ${props.isHidden}\n`;
  if (props.isReadOnly !== undefined) output += `Read Only: ${props.isReadOnly}\n`;
  if (props.isSystem !== undefined) output += `System: ${props.isSystem}\n`;
  if (props.linkTarget) output += `Link Target: ${props.linkTarget}\n`;
  if (props.checksum) output += `Checksum: ${props.checksum}\n`;
  if (props.version) output += `Version: ${props.version}\n`;
  if (props.tags?.length) output += `Tags: ${props.tags.join(', ')}\n`;
  return output;
}

function formatPropertiesForPdf(props: NodeProperties): string[][] {
  const result: string[][] = [];
  if (props.mountPath) result.push(['Mount Path', props.mountPath]);
  if (props.usedSpace !== undefined) result.push(['Used Space', formatBytes(props.usedSpace)]);
  if (props.freeSpace !== undefined) result.push(['Free Space', formatBytes(props.freeSpace)]);
  if (props.totalSpace !== undefined) result.push(['Total Space', formatBytes(props.totalSpace)]);
  if (props.fileSystemType) result.push(['File System', props.fileSystemType]);
  if (props.label) result.push(['Label', props.label]);
  if (props.createdAt) result.push(['Created', props.createdAt.toLocaleString()]);
  if (props.modifiedAt) result.push(['Modified', props.modifiedAt.toLocaleString()]);
  if (props.permissions) result.push(['Permissions', props.permissions]);
  if (props.owner) result.push(['Owner', props.owner]);
  return result;
}
```

3. `src/components/Tree/TreeViewModal.tsx` (Main Tree View Modal)

```typescript
import { X, TreePine, Copy, Download, FileText, FileCode, ChevronRight, ChevronDown, Search, ExpandAll, CollapseAll, Eye, EyeOff } from 'lucide-react';
import { useTreeStore, useTreeStats } from '@/stores/treeStore';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useState, useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';
import { TreeNode } from '@/types/tree';
import { saveAs } from 'file-saver';

export function TreeViewModal() {
  const { isOpen, closeTree, rootNode, selectedNode, expandedNodes, viewMode, searchQuery, toggleNode, expandAll, collapseAll, setViewMode, setSearchQuery, selectNode, exportToTxt, exportToPdf, copyToClipboard } = useTreeStore();
  
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<'tree' | 'properties' | 'stats'>('tree');
  const [isExporting, setIsExporting] = useState(false);

  if (!isOpen || !rootNode) return null;

  const handleExportTxt = async () => {
    const content = exportToTxt();
    const blob = new Blob([content], { type: 'text/plain;charset=utf-8' });
    saveAs(blob, `${selectedNode?.name || rootNode.name}_tree.txt`);
  };

  const handleExportPdf = async () => {
    setIsExporting(true);
    try {
      const blob = await exportToPdf();
      saveAs(blob, `${selectedNode?.name || rootNode.name}_tree.pdf`);
    } finally {
      setIsExporting(false);
    }
  };

  const handleCopy = async (type: 'properties' | 'tree' | 'both') => {
    await copyToClipboard(type);
    // Show toast notification
  };

  // Filter nodes based on search
  const filteredNodes = useMemo(() => {
    if (!searchQuery) return rootNode;
    
    const filterNode = (node: TreeNode): TreeNode | null => {
      const matches = node.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
      const filteredChildren = node.children?.map(filterNode).filter(Boolean) as TreeNode[];
      
      if (matches || (filteredChildren && filteredChildren.length > 0)) {
        return {
          ...node,
          children: filteredChildren,
        };
      }
      return null;
    };
    
    return filterNode(rootNode) || rootNode;
  }, [rootNode, searchQuery]);

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-5xl h-[85vh] bg-background rounded-lg shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border bg-card">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="p-2 rounded-lg bg-primary/10">
              <TreePine className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <div>
              <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground">
                {selectedNode?.name || rootNode.name}
              </h2>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate max-w-md">
                {selectedNode?.path || rootNode.path}
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            {/* View Tabs */}
            <div className="flex items-center border rounded-md mr-4">
              <button
                onClick={() => setActiveTab('tree')}
                className={cn(
                  "px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium transition-colors",
                  activeTab === 'tree' ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground" : "hover:bg-accent"
                )}
              >
                Tree
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setActiveTab('properties')}
                className={cn(
                  "px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium transition-colors",
                  activeTab === 'properties' ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground" : "hover:bg-accent"
                )}
              >
                Properties
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setActiveTab('stats')}
                className={cn(
                  "px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium transition-colors",
                  activeTab === 'stats' ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground" : "hover:bg-accent"
                )}
              >
                Stats
              </button>
            </div>

            {/* Copy Dropdown */}
            <div className="relative group">
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="gap-1">
                <Copy className="w-3 h-3" />
                Copy
              </Button>
              <div className="absolute right-0 top-full mt-1 w-40 bg-card border border-border rounded-md shadow-lg opacity-0 invisible group-hover:opacity-100 group-hover:visible transition-all z-50">
                <button onClick={() => handleCopy('properties')} className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm text-left hover:bg-accent">Properties</button>
                <button onClick={() => handleCopy('tree')} className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm text-left hover:bg-accent">Tree Structure</button>
                <button onClick={() => handleCopy('both')} className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm text-left hover:bg-accent">Both</button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Export Dropdown */}
            <div className="relative group">
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="gap-1">
                <Download className="w-3 h-3" />
                Export
              </Button>
              <div className="absolute right-0 top-full mt-1 w-40 bg-card border border-border rounded-md shadow-lg opacity-0 invisible group-hover:opacity-100 group-hover:visible transition-all z-50">
                <button onClick={handleExportTxt} className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm text-left hover:bg-accent flex items-center gap-2">
                  <FileText className="w-3 h-3" /> TXT
                </button>
                <button onClick={handleExportPdf} disabled={isExporting} className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm text-left hover:bg-accent flex items-center gap-2">
                  <FileCode className="w-3 h-3" /> PDF {isExporting && '...'}
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={closeTree}>
              <X className="w-4 h-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Content */}
        <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-hidden">
          {/* Left: Tree View */}
          <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col border-r border-border">
            {/* Toolbar */}
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 p-3 border-b border-border">
              <div className="relative flex-1">
                <Search className="absolute left-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
                <Input
                  placeholder="Search files..."
                  value={searchQuery}
                  onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                  className="pl-8"
                />
              </div>
              <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={expandAll} title="Expand All">
                <ExpandAll className="w-4 h-4" />
              </Button>
              <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={collapseAll} title="Collapse All">
                <CollapseAll className="w-4 h-4" />
              </Button>
            </div>

            {/* Tree Content */}
            <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4">
              {activeTab === 'tree' && (
                <TreeNodeView 
                  node={filteredNodes} 
                  depth={0}
                  onToggle={toggleNode}
                  onSelect={selectNode}
                  expandedNodes={expandedNodes}
                  selectedId={selectedNode?.id}
                />
              )}
              {activeTab === 'properties' && (
                <PropertiesView node={selectedNode || rootNode} onCopy={handleCopy} />
              )}
              {activeTab === 'stats' && (
                <StatsView />
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// Tree Node Component
function TreeNodeView({ 
  node, 
  depth, 
  onToggle, 
  onSelect, 
  expandedNodes,
  selectedId 
}: { 
  node: TreeNode; 
  depth: number; 
  onToggle: (id: string) => void;
  onSelect: (node: TreeNode) => void;
  expandedNodes: Set<string>;
  selectedId?: string;
}) {
  const hasChildren = node.children && node.children.length > 0;
  const isExpanded = expandedNodes.has(node.id);
  const isSelected = selectedId === node.id;

  return (
    <div>
      <div 
        className={cn(
          "flex items-center gap-1 py-1 px-2 rounded cursor-pointer hover:bg-accent group",
          isSelected && "bg-primary/10"
        )}
        style={{ paddingLeft: `${depth * 20 + 8}px` }}
        onClick={() => onSelect(node)}
      >
        {hasChildren ? (
          <button
            onClick={(e) => {
              e.stopPropagation();
              onToggle(node.id);
            }}
            className="p-0.5 hover:bg-accent rounded"
          >
            {isExpanded ? (
              <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
            ) : (
              <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
            )}
          </button>
        ) : (
          <span className="w-5" />
        )}
        
        <span className="text-sm truncate flex-1">{node.name}</span>
        
        <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100">
          {formatBytes(node.size)}
        </span>
      </div>
      
      {hasChildren && isExpanded && (
        <div>
          {node.children!.map((child) => (
            <TreeNodeView
              key={child.id}
              node={child}
              depth={depth + 1}
              onToggle={onToggle}
              onSelect={onSelect}
              expandedNodes={expandedNodes}
              selectedId={selectedId}
            />
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// Properties View Component
function PropertiesView({ node, onCopy }: { node: TreeNode; onCopy: (type: any) => void }) {
  const properties = [
    { label: 'Name', value: node.name, key: 'name' },
    { label: 'Type', value: node.type, key: 'type' },
    { label: 'Path', value: node.path, key: 'path' },
    { label: 'Size', value: formatBytes(node.size), key: 'size' },
    { label: 'Modified', value: node.lastModified.toLocaleString(), key: 'modified' },
    { label: 'Mount Path', value: node.properties.mountPath, key: 'mountPath' },
    { label: 'File System', value: node.properties.fileSystemType, key: 'fsType' },
    { label: 'Label', value: node.properties.label, key: 'label' },
    { label: 'Used Space', value: node.properties.usedSpace !== undefined ? formatBytes(node.properties.usedSpace) : undefined, key: 'used' },
    { label: 'Free Space', value: node.properties.freeSpace !== undefined ? formatBytes(node.properties.freeSpace) : undefined, key: 'free' },
    { label: 'Permissions', value: node.properties.permissions, key: 'perms' },
    { label: 'Owner', value: node.properties.owner, key: 'owner' },
    { label: 'MIME Type', value: node.properties.mimeType, key: 'mime' },
    { label: 'Hidden', value: node.properties.isHidden !== undefined ? String(node.properties.isHidden) : undefined, key: 'hidden' },
    { label: 'Read Only', value: node.properties.isReadOnly !== undefined ? String(node.properties.isReadOnly) : undefined, key: 'readonly' },
  ].filter(p => p.value !== undefined);

  const copyValue = async (value: string) => {
    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(value);
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <h3 className="font-medium">Properties</h3>
        <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => onCopy('properties')}>
          <Copy className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> Copy All
        </Button>
      </div>
      
      <div className="grid gap-2">
        {properties.map(({ label, value, key }) => (
          <div 
            key={key}
            className="flex items-center justify-between p-2 rounded hover:bg-accent group cursor-pointer"
            onClick={() => copyValue(String(value))}
          >
            <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{label}</span>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="text-sm font-medium text-right">{value}</span>
              <Copy className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100" />
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// Stats View Component
function StatsView() {
  const stats = useTreeStore((s) => s.calculateStats());

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <h3 className="font-medium">Statistics</h3>
      
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <div className="p-4 rounded-lg bg-card border border-border">
          <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{stats.totalFiles.toLocaleString()}</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Total Files</p>
        </div>
        
        <div className="p-4 rounded-lg bg-card border border-border">
          <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{stats.totalDirectories.toLocaleString()}</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Total Directories</p>
        </div>
        
        <div className="p-4 rounded-lg bg-card border border-border">
          <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{formatBytes(stats.totalSize)}</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Total Size</p>
        </div>
        
        <div className="p-4 rounded-lg bg-card border border-border">
          <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{stats.maxDepth}</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Max Depth</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div className="p-4 rounded-lg bg-muted">
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          Average File Size: <span className="font-medium text-foreground">{formatBytes(stats.averageFileSize)}</span>
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
```

4. `src/components/Tree/TreeIconButton.tsx` (Tree Icon for Items)

```typescript
import { TreePine } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useTreeStore } from '@/stores/treeStore';
import { TreeNode, NodeProperties } from '@/types/tree';

interface TreeIconButtonProps {
  item: any;
  sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
  panelId: string;
  className?: string;
}

export function TreeIconButton({ item, sourceType, panelId, className }: TreeIconButtonProps) {
  const openTree = useTreeStore((s) => s.openTree);

  const handleClick = async () => {
    // Build tree node from item
    const treeNode = await buildTreeNode(item, sourceType, panelId);
    openTree(treeNode);
  };

  return (
    <Button
      variant="ghost"
      size="icon"
      className={className}
      onClick={handleClick}
      title="View Tree Structure"
    >
      <TreePine className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
    </Button>
  );
}

async function buildTreeNode(
  item: any, 
  sourceType: string, 
  panelId: string
): Promise<TreeNode> {
  const baseNode: TreeNode = {
    id: item.id || item.name || String(Date.now()),
    name: item.name || 'Unknown',
    type: getNodeType(item, sourceType),
    path: item.path || item.name || '/',
    size: item.size || 0,
    lastModified: item.lastModified ? new Date(item.lastModified) : new Date(),
    depth: 0,
    properties: await buildProperties(item, sourceType),
  };

  // Build children if it's a directory
  if (baseNode.type === 'directory' && item.children) {
    baseNode.children = item.children.map((child: any, index: number) => ({
      ...buildTreeNode(child, sourceType, panelId),
      parent: baseNode,
      depth: 1,
    }));
  }

  return baseNode;
}

function getNodeType(item: any, sourceType: string): 'file' | 'directory' | 'symlink' | 'root' {
  if (sourceType === 'storage' || sourceType === 'terminal') {
    return item.kind === 'directory' ? 'directory' : 
           item.type === 'symlink' ? 'symlink' : 'file';
  }
  if (sourceType === 'drive') {
    return item.mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder' ? 'directory' : 'file';
  }
  if (sourceType === 'github') {
    return item.type === 'dir' ? 'directory' : 
           item.type === 'symlink' ? 'symlink' : 'file';
  }
  return 'file';
}

async function buildProperties(item: any, sourceType: string): Promise<NodeProperties> {
  const props: NodeProperties = {
    createdAt: item.createdAt ? new Date(item.createdAt) : undefined,
    modifiedAt: item.lastModified ? new Date(item.lastModified) : undefined,
    mimeType: item.mimeType,
    isHidden: item.name?.startsWith('.'),
    isReadOnly: item.permissions && !item.permissions.includes('w'),
  };

  // Add source-specific properties
  switch (sourceType) {
    case 'storage':
      props.permissions = item.permissions;
      props.mountPath = item.path;
      break;
    case 'drive':
      props.fileSystemType = 'Google Drive';
      props.label = 'Cloud Storage';
      break;
    case 'github':
      props.fileSystemType = 'Git Repository';
      props.owner = item.owner;
      props.version = item.sha;
      break;
    case 'terminal':
      props.fileSystemType = 'WebContainer FS';
      props.permissions = item.permissions;
      props.owner = 'root';
      props.group = 'root';
      break;
  }

  return props;
}
```

5. `src/components/FileManager/FileList.tsx` (Updated with Tree Icon)

```typescript
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, Folder, Pencil } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { DragDropItem } from '../DragDrop/DragDropItem';
import { InlineRenameInput } from '../Rename/InlineRenameInput';
import { TreeIconButton } from '../Tree/TreeIconButton';
import { useRenameStore } from '@/stores/renameStore';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface FileListProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  onNavigate: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => void;
  panelId: string;
}

export function FileList({ entries, onNavigate, panelId }: FileListProps) {
  const [renamingId, setRenamingId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const handleClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (renamingId) return;
    
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      onNavigate(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  const startRename = (entry: FileSystemEntry, e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setRenamingId(entry.name);
  };

  const handleRenameComplete = () => {
    setRenamingId(null);
  };

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground bg-muted/50">
        <div className="col-span-5">Name</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Size</div>
        <div className="col-span-3">Modified</div>
        <div className="col-span-2">Actions</div>
      </div>

      {entries.map((entry) => {
        const isRenaming = renamingId === entry.name;
        
        return (
          <DragDropItem
            key={entry.name}
            item={entry}
            id={entry.name}
            sourceType="storage"
            panelId={panelId}
            className="w-full grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left items-center group"
          >
            {isRenaming ? (
              <div className="col-span-12">
                <InlineRenameInput
                  item={{
                    id: entry.name,
                    name: entry.name,
                    path: entry.handle?.name || entry.name,
                    sourceType: 'storage',
                    panelId,
                    handle: entry.handle,
                  }}
                  onComplete={handleRenameComplete}
                />
              </div>
            ) : (
              <>
                <div 
                  className="col-span-5 flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0"
                  onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}
                >
                  {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
                    <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
                  ) : (
                    <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
                  )}
                  <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate" title={entry.name}>
                    {entry.name}
                  </span>
                </div>
                
                <div className="col-span-2 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
                  {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : '-'}
                </div>
                
                <div className="col-span-3 text-muted-foreground text-xs">
                  {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
                </div>

                <div className="col-span-2 flex items-center justify-end gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100">
                  <TreeIconButton
                    item={entry}
                    sourceType="storage"
                    panelId={panelId}
                    className="h-6 w-6"
                  />
                  <button
                    onClick={(e) => startRename(entry, e)}
                    className="p-1 hover:bg-accent rounded h-6 w-6 flex items-center justify-center"
                  >
                    <Pencil className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
                  </button>
                </div>
              </>
            )}
          </DragDropItem>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
```
