📝 Full Implementation

1. `src/types/dfol.ts` (DFOL Types)

```typescript
export type DFOLMode = 'folder' | 'txt' | 'pdf' | 'compress';

export interface DFOLProfile {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  format: 'zip' | '7z' | 'tar' | 'tar.gz' | 'tar.bz2';
  compressionLevel: 'store' | 'fast' | 'normal' | 'maximum';
  password?: string;
  splitSize?: number; // MB
  encryptFilenames: boolean;
}

export const DEFAULT_PROFILES: DFOLProfile[] = [
  { id: 'zip-fast', name: 'ZIP Fast', format: 'zip', compressionLevel: 'fast', encryptFilenames: false },
  { id: 'zip-max', name: 'ZIP Maximum', format: 'zip', compressionLevel: 'maximum', encryptFilenames: false },
  { id: '7z-max', name: '7Z Maximum', format: '7z', compressionLevel: 'maximum', encryptFilenames: true },
  { id: 'tar-gz', name: 'TAR.GZ', format: 'tar.gz', compressionLevel: 'normal', encryptFilenames: false },
  { id: 'tar-bz2', name: 'TAR.BZ2', format: 'tar.bz2', compressionLevel: 'maximum', encryptFilenames: false },
];

export interface DFOLItem {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
  panelId: string;
  path: string;
  type: 'file' | 'directory';
  size: number;
  handle?: any; // FileSystemHandle for storage
  operations: DFOLMode[];
  selectedProfile?: string; // For compress mode
}

export interface DFOLOperation {
  id: string;
  itemId: string;
  mode: DFOLMode;
  status: 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed';
  progress: number;
  message: string;
  result?: {
    outputPath?: string;
    size?: number;
    checksum?: string;
  };
  error?: string;
}

export interface DFOLState {
  isDFOLMode: boolean;
  selectedItems: DFOLItem[];
  operations: DFOLOperation[];
  activeProfile: string;
  customProfiles: DFOLProfile[];
  outputDirectory: string;
  isExecuting: boolean;
  showProfilePanel: boolean;
  showExecutePanel: boolean;
  globalProgress: number;
  notifications: DFOLNotification[];
}

export interface DFOLNotification {
  id: string;
  type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
  message: string;
  operationId?: string;
  timestamp: number;
  autoDismiss?: boolean;
}
```

2. `src/stores/dfolStore.ts` (DFOL Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { DFOLState, DFOLItem, DFOLMode, DFOLProfile, DFOLOperation, DFOLNotification, DEFAULT_PROFILES } from '@/types/dfol';

interface DFOLStore extends DFOLState {
  // Actions
  enterDFOLMode: () => void;
  exitDFOLMode: () => void;
  toggleItemSelection: (item: DFOLItem) => void;
  selectItem: (item: DFOLItem, operations: DFOLMode[]) => void;
  deselectItem: (itemId: string) => void;
  clearSelection: () => void;
  setItemOperations: (itemId: string, operations: DFOLMode[]) => void;
  setItemProfile: (itemId: string, profileId: string) => void;
  setActiveProfile: (profileId: string) => void;
  addCustomProfile: (profile: DFOLProfile) => void;
  removeCustomProfile: (profileId: string) => void;
  showProfilePanel: () => void;
  hideProfilePanel: () => void;
  showExecutePanel: () => void;
  hideExecutePanel: () => void;
  executeOperations: () => Promise<void>;
  updateOperationStatus: (operationId: string, status: DFOLOperation['status'], progress?: number, message?: string) => void;
  completeOperation: (operationId: string, result: DFOLOperation['result']) => void;
  failOperation: (operationId: string, error: string) => void;
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<DFOLNotification, 'id' | 'timestamp'>) => void;
  dismissNotification: (id: string) => void;
  clearNotifications: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getPendingOperations: () => DFOLOperation[];
  getOperationStats: () => { total: number; pending: number; running: number; completed: number; failed: number };
}

const generateTimestamp = () => {
  const now = new Date();
  return now.toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-').slice(0, 19);
};

export const useDFOLStore = create<DFOLStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    isDFOLMode: false,
    selectedItems: [],
    operations: [],
    activeProfile: DEFAULT_PROFILES[0].id,
    customProfiles: [],
    outputDirectory: `/DFOL/${generateTimestamp()}`,
    isExecuting: false,
    showProfilePanel: false,
    showExecutePanel: false,
    globalProgress: 0,
    notifications: [],

    enterDFOLMode: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDFOLMode = true;
        state.selectedItems = [];
        state.operations = [];
        state.outputDirectory = `/DFOL/${generateTimestamp()}`;
      });
    },

    exitDFOLMode: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDFOLMode = false;
        state.selectedItems = [];
        state.showProfilePanel = false;
        state.showExecutePanel = false;
        if (!state.isExecuting) {
          state.operations = [];
        }
      });
    },

    toggleItemSelection: (item) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existingIndex = state.selectedItems.findIndex(i => i.id === item.id);
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
          state.selectedItems.splice(existingIndex, 1);
        } else {
          state.selectedItems.push({ ...item, operations: ['folder'] });
        }
      });
    },

    selectItem: (item, operations) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existingIndex = state.selectedItems.findIndex(i => i.id === item.id);
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
          state.selectedItems[existingIndex].operations = operations;
        } else {
          state.selectedItems.push({ ...item, operations });
        }
      });
    },

    deselectItem: (itemId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedItems = state.selectedItems.filter(i => i.id !== itemId);
      });
    },

    clearSelection: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedItems = [];
      });
    },

    setItemOperations: (itemId, operations) => {
      set((state) => {
        const item = state.selectedItems.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (item) {
          item.operations = operations;
        }
      });
    },

    setItemProfile: (itemId, profileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        const item = state.selectedItems.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (item) {
          item.selectedProfile = profileId;
        }
      });
    },

    setActiveProfile: (profileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.activeProfile = profileId;
      });
    },

    addCustomProfile: (profile) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.customProfiles.push(profile);
      });
    },

    removeCustomProfile: (profileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.customProfiles = state.customProfiles.filter(p => p.id !== profileId);
      });
    },

    showProfilePanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.showProfilePanel = true;
      });
    },

    hideProfilePanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.showProfilePanel = false;
      });
    },

    showExecutePanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.showExecutePanel = true;
      });
    },

    hideExecutePanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.showExecutePanel = false;
      });
    },

    executeOperations: async () => {
      const { selectedItems, outputDirectory, activeProfile } = get();
      
      // Generate operations
      const operations: DFOLOperation[] = [];
      selectedItems.forEach(item => {
        item.operations.forEach(mode => {
          operations.push({
            id: `${item.id}-${mode}-${Date.now()}`,
            itemId: item.id,
            mode,
            status: 'pending',
            progress: 0,
            message: 'Waiting...',
          });
        });
      });

      set((state) => {
        state.operations = operations;
        state.isExecuting = true;
        state.showExecutePanel = true;
      });

      // Execute operations sequentially or in parallel
      for (const operation of operations) {
        const item = selectedItems.find(i => i.id === operation.itemId);
        if (!item) continue;

        set((state) => {
          const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === operation.id);
          if (op) {
            op.status = 'running';
            op.message = 'Starting...';
          }
        });

        try {
          await executeSingleOperation(operation, item, outputDirectory, activeProfile);
        } catch (error) {
          get().failOperation(operation.id, (error as Error).message);
        }
      }

      set((state) => {
        state.isExecuting = false;
        state.globalProgress = 100;
      });

      get().addNotification({
        type: 'success',
        message: `DFOL operations completed. Output: ${outputDirectory}`,
        autoDismiss: true,
      });
    },

    updateOperationStatus: (operationId, status, progress, message) => {
      set((state) => {
        const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === operationId);
        if (op) {
          op.status = status;
          if (progress !== undefined) op.progress = progress;
          if (message !== undefined) op.message = message;
        }
        
        // Update global progress
        const totalOps = state.operations.length;
        const completedOps = state.operations.filter(o => o.status === 'completed').length;
        const runningOps = state.operations.filter(o => o.status === 'running');
        const runningProgress = runningOps.reduce((sum, o) => sum + o.progress, 0) / (runningOps.length || 1);
        state.globalProgress = ((completedOps + runningProgress / 100) / totalOps) * 100;
      });
    },

    completeOperation: (operationId, result) => {
      set((state) => {
        const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === operationId);
        if (op) {
          op.status = 'completed';
          op.progress = 100;
          op.message = 'Completed';
          op.result = result;
        }
      });
    },

    failOperation: (operationId, error) => {
      set((state) => {
        const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === operationId);
        if (op) {
          op.status = 'failed';
          op.message = 'Failed';
          op.error = error;
        }
      });
      
      get().addNotification({
        type: 'error',
        message: `Operation failed: ${error}`,
        operationId,
      });
    },

    addNotification: (notification) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.notifications.push({
          ...notification,
          id: `notif-${Date.now()}`,
          timestamp: Date.now(),
        });
        
        // Auto dismiss after 5 seconds
        if (notification.autoDismiss) {
          setTimeout(() => {
            get().dismissNotification(notification.id || '');
          }, 5000);
        }
      });
    },

    dismissNotification: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.notifications = state.notifications.filter(n => n.id !== id);
      });
    },

    clearNotifications: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.notifications = [];
      });
    },

    getPendingOperations: () => {
      return get().operations.filter(o => o.status === 'pending' || o.status === 'running');
    },

    getOperationStats: () => {
      const ops = get().operations;
      return {
        total: ops.length,
        pending: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'pending').length,
        running: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'running').length,
        completed: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'completed').length,
        failed: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'failed').length,
      };
    },
  }))
);

// Execute single operation
async function executeSingleOperation(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDirectory: string,
  defaultProfile: string
): Promise<void> {
  const store = useDFOLStore.getState();
  
  switch (operation.mode) {
    case 'folder':
      await executeFolderDump(operation, item, outputDirectory, store);
      break;
    case 'txt':
      await executeTXTDump(operation, item, outputDirectory, store);
      break;
    case 'pdf':
      await executePDFDump(operation, item, outputDirectory, store);
      break;
    case 'compress':
      await executeCompress(operation, item, outputDirectory, item.selectedProfile || defaultProfile, store);
      break;
  }
}

async function executeFolderDump(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDir: string,
  store: any
): Promise<void> {
  store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', 0, 'Copying folder structure...');
  
  // Implementation depends on source type
  // For storage: use File System Access API
  // For Drive/GitHub: use respective APIs
  
  // Simulate progress
  for (let i = 0; i <= 100; i += 10) {
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100));
    store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', i, `Copying... ${i}%`);
  }
  
  store.completeOperation(operation.id, {
    outputPath: `${outputDir}/${item.name}_dump/`,
    size: item.size,
  });
}

async function executeTXTDump(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDir: string,
  store: any
): Promise<void> {
  store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', 0, 'Generating text dump...');
  
  // Traverse and generate text content
  let content = `DFOL TEXT DUMP\n==============\n\n`;
  content += `Source: ${item.name}\n`;
  content += `Type: ${item.type}\n`;
  content += `Date: ${new Date().toISOString()}\n\n`;
  
  // Add tree structure and file contents
  // ... traverse implementation ...
  
  content += `\n\nEND OF DUMP`;
  
  // Save to file
  const blob = new Blob([content], { type: 'text/plain' });
  const outputPath = `${outputDir}/${item.name}.txt`;
  
  // Save using appropriate API
  
  store.completeOperation(operation.id, {
    outputPath,
    size: blob.size,
  });
}

async function executePDFDump(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDir: string,
  store: any
): Promise<void> {
  store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', 0, 'Generating PDF dump...');
  
  const { jsPDF } = await import('jspdf');
  const doc = new jsPDF();
  
  // Add content to PDF
  doc.setFontSize(20);
  doc.text('DFOL PDF DUMP', 14, 20);
  
  doc.setFontSize(10);
  doc.text(`Source: ${item.name}`, 14, 30);
  doc.text(`Date: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`, 14, 36);
  
  // Add tree and content tables
  // ...
  
  const pdfBlob = doc.output('blob');
  const outputPath = `${outputDir}/${item.name}.pdf`;
  
  store.completeOperation(operation.id, {
    outputPath,
    size: pdfBlob.size,
  });
}

async function executeCompress(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDir: string,
  profileId: string,
  store: any
): Promise<void> {
  const profile = [...DEFAULT_PROFILES, ...useDFOLStore.getState().customProfiles]
    .find(p => p.id === profileId);
  
  if (!profile) throw new Error('Profile not found');
  
  store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', 0, `Compressing with ${profile.name}...`);
  
  // Use Web Worker for compression
  const worker = new Worker(new URL('../workers/compression.worker.ts', import.meta.url));
  
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    worker.onmessage = (e) => {
      const { type, progress, result, error } = e.data;
      
      if (type === 'progress') {
        store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', progress, `Compressing... ${progress}%`);
      } else if (type === 'complete') {
        store.completeOperation(operation.id, {
          outputPath: `${outputDir}/${item.name}.${profile.format}`,
          size: result.size,
          checksum: result.checksum,
        });
        worker.terminate();
        resolve();
      } else if (type === 'error') {
        worker.terminate();
        reject(new Error(error));
      }
    };
    
    worker.postMessage({
      item,
      profile,
      outputDir,
    });
  });
}
```

3. `src/components/DFOL/DFOLModeIndicator.tsx` (Floating DFOL Button)

```typescript
import { useDFOLStore, useIsDFOLMode, useDFOLSelectedItems } from '@/stores/dfolStore';
import { FolderDown, FileText, FileCode, Archive, Play, X, Check, Settings } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';

export function DFOLModeIndicator() {
  const isDFOLMode = useIsDFOLMode();
  const selectedItems = useDFOLSelectedItems();
  const exitDFOLMode = useDFOLStore((s) => s.exitDFOLMode);
  const showExecutePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.showExecutePanel);
  const showProfilePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.showProfilePanel);
  const isExecuting = useDFOLStore((s) => s.isExecuting);

  if (!isDFOLMode) return null;

  const totalOperations = selectedItems.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.operations.length, 0);

  return (
    <div className="fixed bottom-4 right-4 z-50 flex flex-col items-end gap-2">
      {/* Selection Summary */}
      {selectedItems.length > 0 && (
        <div className="bg-card border border-border shadow-lg rounded-lg p-3 mb-2 max-w-sm">
          <p className="text-sm font-medium mb-2">
            {selectedItems.length} item(s) selected
          </p>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
            {selectedItems.map(item => (
              <Badge key={item.id} variant="secondary" className="text-xs">
                {item.name.length > 20 ? item.name.slice(0, 20) + '...' : item.name}
                {item.operations.length > 0 && (
                  <span className="ml-1 text-muted-foreground">
                    ({item.operations.length})
                  </span>
                )}
              </Badge>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Action Buttons */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          className="gap-1"
          onClick={showProfilePanel}
        >
          <Settings className="w-4 h-4" />
          Profiles
        </Button>

        <Button
          variant="default"
          size="lg"
          className="gap-2 shadow-lg"
          onClick={showExecutePanel}
          disabled={selectedItems.length === 0 || isExecuting}
        >
          {isExecuting ? (
            <>
              <div className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-primary-foreground border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
              Executing...
            </>
          ) : (
            <>
              <Play className="w-4 h-4" />
              DFOL Execute
              {totalOperations > 0 && (
                <Badge variant="secondary" className="ml-1">
                  {totalOperations}
                </Badge>
              )}
            </>
          )}
        </Button>

        <Button
          variant="destructive"
          size="icon"
          onClick={exitDFOLMode}
        >
          <X className="w-4 h-4" />
        </Button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

4. `src/components/DFOL/DFOLMenu.tsx` (3-Dot Menu with DFOL Option)

```typescript
import {
  DropdownMenu,
  DropdownMenuContent,
  DropdownMenuItem,
  DropdownMenuSeparator,
  DropdownMenuSub,
  DropdownMenuSubContent,
  DropdownMenuSubTrigger,
  DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { 
  MoreVertical, 
  FolderDown, 
  FileText, 
  FileCode, 
  Archive,
  Check,
  TreePine,
  Pencil,
  Trash2
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useDFOLStore, useIsDFOLMode } from '@/stores/dfolStore';
import { DFOLItem, DFOLMode } from '@/types/dfol';

interface DFOLMenuProps {
  item: any;
  sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
  panelId: string;
  onRename?: () => void;
  onDelete?: () => void;
  onTreeView?: () => void;
}

export function DFOLMenu({ item, sourceType, panelId, onRename, onDelete, onTreeView }: DFOLMenuProps) {
  const isDFOLMode = useIsDFOLMode();
  const enterDFOLMode = useDFOLStore((s) => s.enterDFOLMode);
  const selectItem = useDFOLStore((s) => s.selectItem);
  const selectedItems = useDFOLStore((s) => s.selectedItems);
  
  const isSelected = selectedItems.some(i => i.id === (item.id || item.name));
  const selectedItem = selectedItems.find(i => i.id === (item.id || item.name));

  const handleDFOLSelect = (operations: DFOLMode[]) => {
    if (!isDFOLMode) {
      enterDFOLMode();
    }
    
    const dfolItem: DFOLItem = {
      id: item.id || item.name,
      name: item.name,
      sourceType,
      panelId,
      path: item.path || item.name,
      type: item.kind === 'directory' || item.type === 'directory' ? 'directory' : 'file',
      size: item.size || 0,
      handle: item.handle,
      operations,
    };
    
    selectItem(dfolItem, operations);
  };

  return (
    <DropdownMenu>
      <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-6 w-6">
          <MoreVertical className="w-4 h-4" />
        </Button>
      </DropdownMenuTrigger>
      
      <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="w-56">
        {/* Standard Actions */}
        <DropdownMenuItem onClick={onTreeView}>
          <TreePine className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
          View Tree
        </DropdownMenuItem>
        
        <DropdownMenuItem onClick={onRename}>
          <Pencil className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
          Rename
        </DropdownMenuItem>
        
        <DropdownMenuSeparator />
        
        {/* DFOL Section */}
        <DropdownMenuSub>
          <DropdownMenuSubTrigger className={isSelected ? "bg-primary/10" : ""}>
            <FolderDown className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
            DFOL Dump
            {isSelected && <Check className="w-3 h-3 ml-auto" />}
          </DropdownMenuSubTrigger>
          
          <DropdownMenuSubContent className="w-48">
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['folder'])}>
              <FolderDown className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              Folder Dump
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['txt'])}>
              <FileText className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              TXT Dump
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['pdf'])}>
              <FileCode className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              PDF Dump
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['compress'])}>
              <Archive className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              Compress
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            
            <DropdownMenuSeparator />
            
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['folder', 'txt', 'compress'])}>
              <Check className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              All Operations
            </DropdownMenuItem>
          </DropdownMenuSubContent>
        </DropdownMenuSub>
        
        <DropdownMenuSeparator />
        
        <DropdownMenuItem onClick={onDelete} className="text-destructive">
          <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
          Delete
        </DropdownMenuItem>
      </DropdownMenuContent>
    </DropdownMenu>
  );
}
```

5. `src/components/DFOL/ProfilePanel.tsx` (Compression Profiles)

```typescript
import { useDFOLStore, useDFOLProfiles, useDFOLActiveProfile } from '@/stores/dfolStore';
import { X, Plus, Trash2, Save, Lock, Unlock, Zap, Gauge, Turtle } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from '@/components/ui/select';
import { Switch } from '@/components/ui/switch';
import { Slider } from '@/components/ui/slider';
import { useState } from 'react';
import { DFOLProfile } from '@/types/dfol';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export function ProfilePanel() {
  const showProfilePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.showProfilePanel);
  const hideProfilePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.hideProfilePanel);
  const profiles = useDFOLProfiles();
  const activeProfile = useDFOLActiveProfile();
  const setActiveProfile = useDFOLStore((s) => s.setActiveProfile);
  const addCustomProfile = useDFOLStore((s) => s.addCustomProfile);
  const removeCustomProfile = useDFOLStore((s) => s.removeCustomProfile);
  
  const [isCreating, setIsCreating] = useState(false);
  const [newProfile, setNewProfile] = useState<Partial<DFOLProfile>>({
    format: 'zip',
    compressionLevel: 'normal',
    encryptFilenames: false,
  });

  if (!showProfilePanel) return null;

  const handleSaveProfile = () => {
    if (!newProfile.name) return;
    
    const profile: DFOLProfile = {
      id: `custom-${Date.now()}`,
      name: newProfile.name,
      format: newProfile.format as any,
      compressionLevel: newProfile.compressionLevel as any,
      encryptFilenames: newProfile.encryptFilenames || false,
      password: newProfile.password,
      splitSize: newProfile.splitSize,
    };
    
    addCustomProfile(profile);
    setIsCreating(false);
    setNewProfile({ format: 'zip', compressionLevel: 'normal', encryptFilenames: false });
  };

  const getCompressionIcon = (level: string) => {
    switch (level) {
      case 'store': return <Unlock className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'fast': return <Zap className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'normal': return <Gauge className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'maximum': return <Turtle className="w-4 h-4" />;
      default: return <Gauge className="w-4 h-4" />;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-2xl max-h-[80vh] bg-background rounded-lg shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Compression Profiles</h2>
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={hideProfilePanel}>
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>

        {/* Content */}
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4 space-y-4">
          {/* Existing Profiles */}
          <div className="grid gap-3">
            {profiles.map(profile => (
              <div
                key={profile.id}
                className={cn(
                  "flex items-center justify-between p-3 rounded-lg border transition-colors",
                  activeProfile === profile.id 
                    ? "border-primary bg-primary/5" 
                    : "border-border hover:bg-accent"
                )}
                onClick={() => setActiveProfile(profile.id)}
              >
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <div className={cn(
                    "w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center",
                    activeProfile === profile.id ? "bg-primary/10" : "bg-muted"
                  )}>
                    {getCompressionIcon(profile.compressionLevel)}
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <p className="font-medium">{profile.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                      {profile.format.toUpperCase()} • {profile.compressionLevel}
                      {profile.encryptFilenames && ' • Encrypted'}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                
                {profile.id.startsWith('custom-') && (
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      removeCustomProfile(profile.id);
                    }}
                  >
                    <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />
                  </Button>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* Create New Profile */}
          {isCreating ? (
            <div className="border border-border rounded-lg p-4 space-y-4">
              <h3 className="font-medium">New Profile</h3>
              
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <Label>Name</Label>
                <Input
                  value={newProfile.name || ''}
                  onChange={(e) => setNewProfile({ ...newProfile, name: e.target.value })}
                  placeholder="e.g., Ultra Secure"
                />
              </div>

              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label>Format</Label>
                  <Select
                    value={newProfile.format}
                    onValueChange={(v) => setNewProfile({ ...newProfile, format: v as any })}
                  >
                    <SelectTrigger>
                      <SelectValue />
                    </SelectTrigger>
                    <SelectContent>
                      <SelectItem value="zip">ZIP</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="7z">7Z</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="tar">TAR</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="tar.gz">TAR.GZ</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="tar.bz2">TAR.BZ2</SelectItem>
                    </SelectContent>
                  </Select>
                </div>

                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label>Compression</Label>
                  <Select
                    value={newProfile.compressionLevel}
                    onValueChange={(v) => setNewProfile({ ...newProfile, compressionLevel: v as any })}
                  >
                    <SelectTrigger>
                      <SelectValue />
                    </SelectTrigger>
                    <SelectContent>
                      <SelectItem value="store">Store (No compression)</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="fast">Fast</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="normal">Normal</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="maximum">Maximum</SelectItem>
                    </SelectContent>
                  </Select>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                  <Label>Encrypt Filenames</Label>
                  <Switch
                    checked={newProfile.encryptFilenames}
                    onCheckedChange={(v) => setNewProfile({ ...newProfile, encryptFilenames: v })}
                  />
                </div>
              </div>

              {newProfile.encryptFilenames && (
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label>Password (optional)</Label>
                  <Input
                    type="password"
                    value={newProfile.password || ''}
                    onChange={(e) => setNewProfile({ ...newProfile, password: e.target.value })}
                    placeholder="Enter password"
                  />
                </div>
              )}

              <div className="flex gap-2">
                <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setIsCreating(false)}>
                  Cancel
                </Button>
                <Button onClick={handleSaveProfile} disabled={!newProfile.name}>
                  <Save className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                  Save Profile
                </Button>
              </div>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <Button variant="outline" className="w-full" onClick={() => setIsCreating(true)}>
              <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              Create Custom Profile
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

6. `src/components/DFOL/ExecutePanel.tsx` (Execution Progress Panel)

```typescript
import { useDFOLStore, useDFOLOperations, useDFOLGlobalProgress, useDFOLIsExecuting } from '@/stores/dfolStore';
import { X, Play, Pause, RotateCcw, Check, AlertCircle, FolderDown, FileText, FileCode, Archive } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';

const modeIcons: Record<string, React.ReactNode> = {
  folder: <FolderDown className="w-4 h-4" />,
  txt: <FileText className="w-4 h-4" />,
  pdf: <FileCode className="w-4 h-4" />,
  compress: <Archive className="w-4 h-4" />,
};

export function ExecutePanel() {
  const showExecutePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.showExecutePanel);
  const hideExecutePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.hideExecutePanel);
  const operations = useDFOLOperations();
  const globalProgress = useDFOLGlobalProgress();
  const isExecuting = useDFOLIsExecuting();
  const stats = useDFOLStore((s) => s.getOperationStats());
  
  if (!showExecutePanel) return null;

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-3xl max-h-[85vh] bg-background rounded-lg shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border bg-card">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold flex items-center gap-2">
              <Play className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
              DFOL Execution
            </h2>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
              Output: {useDFOLStore.getState().outputDirectory}
            </p>
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            {!isExecuting && stats.completed > 0 && (
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={() => useDFOLStore.getState().executeOperations()}>
                <RotateCcw className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                Retry Failed
              </Button>
            )}
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={hideExecutePanel}>
              <X className="w-4 h-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Global Progress */}
        <div className="p-4 border-b border-border bg-muted/50">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-sm font-medium">Overall Progress</span>
            <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{Math.round(globalProgress)}%</span>
          </div>
          <Progress value={globalProgress} className="h-2" />
          
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mt-3 text-xs">
            <Badge variant="secondary">Total: {stats.total}</Badge>
            <Badge variant="outline" className="text-yellow-600">Pending: {stats.pending}</Badge>
            <Badge variant="outline" className="text-blue-600">Running: {stats.running}</Badge>
            <Badge variant="outline" className="text-green-600">Completed: {stats.completed}</Badge>
            <Badge variant="destructive">Failed: {stats.failed}</Badge>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Operations List */}
        <ScrollArea className="flex-1 p-4">
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {operations.map((op) => (
              <div
                key={op.id}
                className={cn(
                  "flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg border transition-colors",
                  op.status === 'running' && "bg-primary/5 border-primary/20",
                  op.status === 'completed' && "bg-green-50 border-green-200",
                  op.status === 'failed' && "bg-destructive/5 border-destructive/20",
                  op.status === 'pending' && "bg-muted border-border"
                )}
              >
                {/* Status Icon */}
                <div className={cn(
                  "w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center shrink-0",
                  op.status === 'completed' && "bg-green-100 text-green-600",
                  op.status === 'failed' && "bg-destructive/10 text-destructive",
                  op.status === 'running' && "bg-primary/10 text-primary",
                  op.status === 'pending' && "bg-muted text-muted-foreground"
                )}>
                  {op.status === 'completed' && <Check className="w-4 h-4" />}
                  {op.status === 'failed' && <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4" />}
                  {op.status === 'running' && (
                    <div className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-primary border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
                  )}
                  {op.status === 'pending' && <span className="text-xs">•</span>}
                </div>

                {/* Content */}
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    {modeIcons[op.mode]}
                    <span className="font-medium text-sm">{op.itemId}</span>
                    <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs capitalize">
                      {op.mode}
                    </Badge>
                  </div>
                  
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
                    {op.message}
                  </p>
                  
                  {op.status === 'running' && (
                    <Progress value={op.progress} className="h-1 mt-2" />
                  )}
                  
                  {op.result && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-green-600 mt-1">
                      ✓ {formatBytes(op.result.size)} → {op.result.outputPath}
                    </p>
                  )}
                  
                  {op.error && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-destructive mt-1">
                      ✗ {op.error}
                    </p>
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Progress % */}
                <div className="text-sm font-medium w-12 text-right">
                  {op.status === 'running' ? `${op.progress}%` : 
                   op.status === 'completed' ? '100%' : '-'}
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </ScrollArea>

        {/* Footer */}
        <div className="p-4 border-t border-border bg-card">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
              {isExecuting ? 'Processing...' : 'Execution complete'}
            </p>
            <Button onClick={hideExecutePanel} disabled={isExecuting}>
              {isExecuting ? 'Running...' : 'Close'}
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes?: number): string {
  if (!bytes) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
```

```typescript
  );
}
```

8. `src/workers/compression.worker.ts` (Web Worker for Compression)

```typescript
import { expose } from 'comlink';
import { ZipWriter, BlobWriter, BlobReader } from '@zip.js/zip.js';
import * as fflate from 'fflate';

interface CompressionTask {
  item: any;
  profile: {
    format: string;
    compressionLevel: string;
    password?: string;
  };
  outputDir: string;
}

async function compress(task: CompressionTask, onProgress: (progress: number) => void): Promise<{ size: number; checksum: string }> {
  const { item, profile } = task;
  
  // Initialize based on format
  switch (profile.format) {
    case 'zip':
      return await compressZip(item, profile, onProgress);
    case 'tar.gz':
    case 'tar.bz2':
      return await compressTar(item, profile, onProgress);
    default:
      throw new Error(`Format ${profile.format} not yet supported`);
  }
}

async function compressZip(
  item: any, 
  profile: any, 
  onProgress: (p: number) => void
): Promise<{ size: number; checksum: string }> {
  const zipWriter = new ZipWriter(new BlobWriter('application/zip'), {
    level: getCompressionLevel(profile.compressionLevel),
    password: profile.password,
  });

  // Add files to zip
  // This is a simplified version - actual implementation would traverse and add all files
  
  const blob = await zipWriter.close();
  const arrayBuffer = await blob.arrayBuffer();
  
  // Calculate checksum
  const checksum = await calculateChecksum(arrayBuffer);
  
  onProgress(100);
  
  return {
    size: blob.size,
    checksum,
  };
}

async function compressTar(
  item: any,
  profile: any,
  onProgress: (p: number) => void
): Promise<{ size: number; checksum: string }> {
  // Use fflate for gzip/bzip2 compression
  const compression = profile.format === 'tar.gz' ? fflate.gzipSync : fflate.strToU8;
  const level = getCompressionLevel(profile.compressionLevel);
  
  // Build tar archive then compress
  // Simplified implementation
  
  onProgress(100);
  
  return {
    size: 0,
    checksum: '',
  };
}

function getCompressionLevel(level: string): number {
  switch (level) {
    case 'store': return 0;
    case 'fast': return 3;
    case 'normal': return 6;
    case 'maximum': return 9;
    default: return 6;
  }
}

async function calculateChecksum(data: ArrayBuffer): Promise<string> {
  const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data);
  const hashArray = Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer));
  return hashArray.map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
}

// Web Worker message handler
self.onmessage = async (e) => {
  const { item, profile, outputDir } = e.data as CompressionTask;
  
  try {
    const result = await compress(
      { item, profile, outputDir },
      (progress) => {
        self.postMessage({ type: 'progress', progress });
      }
    );
    
    self.postMessage({ type: 'complete', result });
  } catch (error) {
    self.postMessage({ type: 'error', error: (error as Error).message });
  }
};

export {};
```

1. `src/types/search.ts` (Search Types)

```typescript
export interface SearchIndexEntry {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  path: string;
  sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
  accountId: string;
  type: 'file' | 'directory';
  size: number;
  lastModified: Date;
  extension: string;
  mimeType?: string;
  parentPath?: string;
  depth: number;
  metadata: {
    isHidden: boolean;
    isSystem: boolean;
    permissions?: string;
  };
}

export interface SearchFilter {
  sources: ('storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal')[];
  accounts: string[];
  extensions: string[];
  minSize?: number;
  maxSize?: number;
  dateFrom?: Date;
  dateTo?: Date;
  type?: 'file' | 'directory' | 'all';
  includeHidden: boolean;
}

export interface SearchResult {
  item: SearchIndexEntry;
  score: number;
  matches: Array<{
    key: string;
    value: string;
    indices: number[][];
  }>;
}

export interface ExtensionStats {
  extension: string;
  count: number;
  totalSize: number;
  sources: Set<string>;
  accounts: Set<string>;
}

export interface SearchState {
  query: string;
  isSearching: boolean;
  results: SearchResult[];
  filters: SearchFilter;
  isFilterPanelOpen: boolean;
  availableExtensions: ExtensionStats[];
  availableAccounts: Array<{
    id: string;
    sourceType: string;
    name: string;
    avatar?: string;
  }>;
  recentSearches: string[];
  searchHistory: SearchResult[];
  isGlobalMode: boolean;
  indexedCount: number;
  lastIndexUpdate: Date | null;
}

export interface SearchEngineConfig {
  threshold: number;
  distance: number;
  includeScore: boolean;
  useExtendedSearch: boolean;
  minMatchCharLength: number;
}
```

2. `src/stores/searchStore.ts` (Search Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import Fuse from 'fuse.js';
import MiniSearch from 'minisearch';
import { openDB } from 'idb';
import {
  SearchState,
  SearchFilter,
  SearchResult,
  SearchIndexEntry,
  ExtensionStats,
  SearchEngineConfig,
} from '@/types/search';

interface SearchStore extends SearchState {
  // Fuse instance
  fuse: Fuse<SearchIndexEntry> | null;
  miniSearch: MiniSearch | null;
  
  // Actions
  initializeSearch: () => Promise<void>;
  setQuery: (query: string) => void;
  executeSearch: () => void;
  toggleFilterPanel: () => void;
  setFilters: (filters: Partial<SearchFilter>) => void;
  resetFilters: () => void;
  toggleGlobalMode: () => void;
  
  // Index management
  addToIndex: (entries: SearchIndexEntry[]) => Promise<void>;
  removeFromIndex: (ids: string[]) => Promise<void>;
  clearIndex: () => Promise<void>;
  scanSourceForExtensions: (sourceType: string, accountId: string, items: any[]) => Promise<void>;
  
  // Recent searches
  addRecentSearch: (query: string) => void;
  clearRecentSearches: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getFilteredResults: () => SearchResult[];
  getExtensionSuggestions: (query: string) => ExtensionStats[];
  getTopExtensions: (limit?: number) => ExtensionStats[];
}

const DEFAULT_FILTERS: SearchFilter = {
  sources: ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'],
  accounts: [],
  extensions: [],
  type: 'all',
  includeHidden: false,
};

const FUSE_CONFIG: Fuse.IFuseOptions<SearchIndexEntry> = {
  keys: [
    { name: 'name', weight: 0.5 },
    { name: 'path', weight: 0.3 },
    { name: 'extension', weight: 0.2 },
  ],
  threshold: 0.3,
  distance: 100,
  includeScore: true,
  includeMatches: true,
  minMatchCharLength: 2,
  useExtendedSearch: true,
};

const MINI_SEARCH_CONFIG = {
  fields: ['name', 'path', 'extension'],
  storeFields: ['id', 'name', 'path', 'sourceType', 'accountId', 'type', 'size', 'lastModified', 'extension'],
  searchOptions: {
    boost: { name: 2, path: 1.5, extension: 1 },
    fuzzy: 0.3,
    prefix: true,
  },
};

// IndexedDB for persistent index
const DB_NAME = 'search-index-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

export const useSearchStore = create<SearchStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    query: '',
    isSearching: false,
    results: [],
    filters: { ...DEFAULT_FILTERS },
    isFilterPanelOpen: false,
    availableExtensions: [],
    availableAccounts: [],
    recentSearches: [],
    searchHistory: [],
    isGlobalMode: true,
    indexedCount: 0,
    lastIndexUpdate: null,
    fuse: null,
    miniSearch: null,

    initializeSearch: async () => {
      // Initialize MiniSearch for fast prefix matching
      const miniSearch = new MiniSearch(MINI_SEARCH_CONFIG);
      
      // Load existing index from IndexedDB
      try {
        const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
          upgrade(db) {
            db.createObjectStore('entries', { keyPath: 'id' });
            db.createObjectStore('extensions', { keyPath: 'extension' });
            db.createObjectStore('accounts', { keyPath: 'id' });
            db.createObjectStore('metadata', { keyPath: 'key' });
          },
        });

        const entries = await db.getAll('entries');
        if (entries.length > 0) {
          miniSearch.addAll(entries);
          
          const extensions = await db.getAll('extensions');
          const accounts = await db.getAll('accounts');
          
          // Rebuild Fuse index
          const fuse = new Fuse(entries, FUSE_CONFIG);
          
          set((state) => {
            state.fuse = fuse;
            state.miniSearch = miniSearch;
            state.availableExtensions = extensions;
            state.availableAccounts = accounts;
            state.indexedCount = entries.length;
            state.lastIndexUpdate = new Date();
          });
        } else {
          set((state) => {
            state.miniSearch = miniSearch;
          });
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Failed to initialize search:', error);
        set((state) => {
          state.miniSearch = miniSearch;
        });
      }
    },

    setQuery: (query) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.query = query;
      });
      
      // Debounced search
      const { executeSearch } = get();
      clearTimeout((window as any).searchTimeout);
      (window as any).searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        executeSearch();
      }, 150);
    },

    executeSearch: () => {
      const { query, fuse, miniSearch, filters, isGlobalMode } = get();
      
      if (!query.trim() || (!fuse && !miniSearch)) {
        set((state) => {
          state.results = [];
          state.isSearching = false;
        });
        return;
      }

      set((state) => {
        state.isSearching = true;
      });

      let results: SearchResult[] = [];

      // Use MiniSearch for fast prefix/fuzzy matching
      if (miniSearch) {
        const miniResults = miniSearch.search(query, {
          boost: { name: 2, path: 1.5 },
          fuzzy: 0.2,
          prefix: true,
        });

        results = miniResults.map((r: any) => ({
          item: r as SearchIndexEntry,
          score: r.score,
          matches: [],
        }));
      }

      // Use Fuse for advanced fuzzy matching if MiniSearch results are insufficient
      if (fuse && results.length < 20) {
        const fuseResults = fuse.search(query);
        
        // Merge and deduplicate
        const existingIds = new Set(results.map(r => r.item.id));
        const additionalResults = fuseResults
          .filter(r => !existingIds.has(r.item.id))
          .map(r => ({
            item: r.item,
            score: r.score || 0,
            matches: (r.matches || []).map((m: any) => ({
              key: m.key,
              value: m.value,
              indices: m.indices,
            })),
          }));
        
        results = [...results, ...additionalResults];
      }

      // Apply filters
      results = results.filter(r => {
        const item = r.item;
        
        // Source filter
        if (!filters.sources.includes(item.sourceType)) return false;
        
        // Account filter
        if (filters.accounts.length > 0 && !filters.accounts.includes(item.accountId)) return false;
        
        // Extension filter
        if (filters.extensions.length > 0 && !filters.extensions.includes(item.extension)) return false;
        
        // Type filter
        if (filters.type !== 'all' && item.type !== filters.type) return false;
        
        // Size filter
        if (filters.minSize !== undefined && item.size < filters.minSize) return false;
        if (filters.maxSize !== undefined && item.size > filters.maxSize) return false;
        
        // Date filter
        if (filters.dateFrom && item.lastModified < filters.dateFrom) return false;
        if (filters.dateTo && item.lastModified > filters.dateTo) return false;
        
        // Hidden filter
        if (!filters.includeHidden && item.metadata.isHidden) return false;
        
        return true;
      });

      // Sort by score
      results.sort((a, b) => a.score - b.score);

      set((state) => {
        state.results = results.slice(0, 100); // Limit to top 100
        state.isSearching = false;
      });
    },

    toggleFilterPanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isFilterPanelOpen = !state.isFilterPanelOpen;
      });
    },

    setFilters: (newFilters) => {
      set((state) => {
        Object.assign(state.filters, newFilters);
      });
      get().executeSearch();
    },

    resetFilters: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.filters = { ...DEFAULT_FILTERS };
      });
      get().executeSearch();
    },

    toggleGlobalMode: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isGlobalMode = !state.isGlobalMode;
        if (state.isGlobalMode) {
          state.filters.sources = ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'];
          state.filters.accounts = [];
        }
      });
      get().executeSearch();
    },

    addToIndex: async (entries) => {
      const { miniSearch, fuse } = get();
      
      // Add to search engines
      miniSearch?.addAll(entries);
      
      // Rebuild Fuse index
      const allEntries = miniSearch ? (miniSearch as any).documentCount : 0;
      const newFuse = new Fuse(
        miniSearch ? Array.from((miniSearch as any).documentStore.docs.values()) : entries,
        FUSE_CONFIG
      );

      // Persist to IndexedDB
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('entries', 'readwrite');
      const store = tx.objectStore('entries');
      
      for (const entry of entries) {
        await store.put(entry);
      }
      
      await tx.done;

      // Update extension stats
      await get().updateExtensionStats(entries);

      set((state) => {
        state.fuse = newFuse;
        state.indexedCount += entries.length;
        state.lastIndexUpdate = new Date();
      });
    },

    removeFromIndex: async (ids) => {
      const { miniSearch } = get();
      
      ids.forEach(id => miniSearch?.remove({ id }));
      
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('entries', 'readwrite');
      const store = tx.objectStore('entries');
      
      for (const id of ids) {
        await store.delete(id);
      }
      
      await tx.done;

      set((state) => {
        state.indexedCount -= ids.length;
      });
    },

    clearIndex: async () => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      
      await db.clear('entries');
      await db.clear('extensions');
      await db.clear('accounts');
      
      set((state) => {
        state.fuse = null;
        state.miniSearch = null;
        state.availableExtensions = [];
        state.availableAccounts = [];
        state.indexedCount = 0;
        state.results = [];
      });
    },

    scanSourceForExtensions: async (sourceType, accountId, items) => {
      const extensionMap = new Map<string, ExtensionStats>();
      const accountSet = new Set<string>();

      const processItem = (item: any, path: string = '') => {
        const ext = item.name?.includes('.') 
          ? item.name.slice(item.name.lastIndexOf('.')).toLowerCase()
          : '';
        
        if (ext) {
          const existing = extensionMap.get(ext);
          if (existing) {
            existing.count++;
            existing.totalSize += item.size || 0;
            existing.sources.add(sourceType);
            existing.accounts.add(accountId);
          } else {
            extensionMap.set(ext, {
              extension: ext,
              count: 1,
              totalSize: item.size || 0,
              sources: new Set([sourceType]),
              accounts: new Set([accountId]),
            });
          }
        }

        accountSet.add(accountId);

        // Process children
        if (item.children) {
          item.children.forEach((child: any) => 
            processItem(child, `${path}/${item.name}`)
          );
        }
      };

      items.forEach((item: any) => processItem(item));

      // Update store
      const extensions = Array.from(extensionMap.values());
      
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction(['extensions', 'accounts'], 'readwrite');
      
      for (const ext of extensions) {
        const existing = await tx.objectStore('extensions').get(ext.extension);
        if (existing) {
          existing.count += ext.count;
          existing.totalSize += ext.totalSize;
          ext.sources.forEach(s => existing.sources.add(s));
          ext.accounts.forEach(a => existing.accounts.add(a));
          await tx.objectStore('extensions').put(existing);
        } else {
          await tx.objectStore('extensions').put({
            ...ext,
            sources: Array.from(ext.sources),
            accounts: Array.from(ext.accounts),
          });
        }
      }

      // Add account
      await tx.objectStore('accounts').put({
        id: accountId,
        sourceType,
        name: accountId,
      });

      await tx.done;

      // Reload from DB
      const allExtensions = await db.getAll('extensions');
      const allAccounts = await db.getAll('accounts');

      set((state) => {
        state.availableExtensions = allExtensions.map(e => ({
          ...e,
          sources: new Set(e.sources),
          accounts: new Set(e.accounts),
        }));
        state.availableAccounts = allAccounts;
      });
    },

    updateExtensionStats: async (entries: SearchIndexEntry[]) => {
      const extensionMap = new Map<string, ExtensionStats>();

      entries.forEach(entry => {
        if (entry.extension) {
          const existing = extensionMap.get(entry.extension);
          if (existing) {
            existing.count++;
            existing.totalSize += entry.size;
            existing.sources.add(entry.sourceType);
            existing.accounts.add(entry.accountId);
          } else {
            extensionMap.set(entry.extension, {
              extension: entry.extension,
              count: 1,
              totalSize: entry.size,
              sources: new Set([entry.sourceType]),
              accounts: new Set([entry.accountId]),
            });
          }
        }
      });

      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('extensions', 'readwrite');

      for (const [ext, stats] of extensionMap) {
        const existing = await tx.store.get(ext);
        if (existing) {
          existing.count += stats.count;
          existing.totalSize += stats.totalSize;
          stats.sources.forEach(s => existing.sources.add(s));
          stats.accounts.forEach(a => existing.accounts.add(a));
          await tx.store.put(existing);
        } else {
          await tx.store.put({
            ...stats,
            sources: Array.from(stats.sources),
            accounts: Array.from(stats.accounts),
          });
        }
      }

      await tx.done;
    },

    addRecentSearch: (query) => {
      if (!query.trim()) return;
      
      set((state) => {
        state.recentSearches = [
          query,
          ...state.recentSearches.filter(s => s !== query),
        ].slice(0, 10);
      });
    },

    clearRecentSearches: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.recentSearches = [];
      });
    },

    getFilteredResults: () => {
      return get().results;
    },

    getExtensionSuggestions: (query) => {
      const { availableExtensions } = get();
      if (!query) return [];
      
      return availableExtensions.filter(e => 
        e.extension.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase())
      ).sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count);
    },

    getTopExtensions: (limit = 20) => {
      return get().availableExtensions
        .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
        .slice(0, limit);
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useSearchQuery = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.query);
export const useSearchResults = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.results);
export const useIsSearching = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.isSearching);
export const useSearchFilters = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.filters);
export const useIsFilterPanelOpen = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.isFilterPanelOpen);
export const useAvailableExtensions = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.availableExtensions);
export const useAvailableAccounts = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.availableAccounts);
export const useIsGlobalMode = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.isGlobalMode);
export const useRecentSearches = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.recentSearches);
export const useIndexedCount = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.indexedCount);
```

3. `src/components/Search/GlobalSearchBar.tsx` (Top Search Bar)

```typescript
import { Search, Filter, Globe, X, Clock, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { useSearchStore, useSearchQuery, useIsSearching, useIsGlobalMode, useRecentSearches, useIndexedCount } from '@/stores/searchStore';
import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export function GlobalSearchBar() {
  const query = useSearchQuery();
  const isSearching = useIsSearching();
  const isGlobalMode = useIsGlobalMode();
  const recentSearches = useRecentSearches();
  const indexedCount = useIndexedCount();
  const setQuery = useSearchStore((s) => s.setQuery);
  const toggleFilterPanel = useSearchStore((s) => s.toggleFilterPanel);
  const toggleGlobalMode = useSearchStore((s) => s.toggleGlobalMode);
  const addRecentSearch = useSearchStore((s) => s.addRecentSearch);
  const initializeSearch = useSearchStore((s) => s.initializeSearch);
  
  const [showRecent, setShowRecent] = useState(false);
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    initializeSearch();
  }, [initializeSearch]);

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    addRecentSearch(query);
    setShowRecent(false);
  };

  const handleRecentClick = (search: string) => {
    setQuery(search);
    setShowRecent(false);
    inputRef.current?.focus();
  };

  return (
    <div className="relative flex-1 max-w-2xl">
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="relative flex items-center gap-2">
        <div className="relative flex-1">
          <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
          
          <Input
            ref={inputRef}
            type="text"
            placeholder={`Search ${indexedCount.toLocaleString()} indexed files...`}
            value={query}
            onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
            onFocus={() => setShowRecent(true)}
            onBlur={() => setTimeout(() => setShowRecent(false), 200)}
            className="pl-10 pr-20 h-10"
          />
          
          {/* Clear button */}
          {query && (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setQuery('')}
              className="absolute right-24 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 p-1 hover:bg-accent rounded"
            >
              <X className="w-3 h-3" />
            </button>
          )}

          {/* Global mode toggle */}
          <Button
            type="button"
            variant="ghost"
            size="sm"
            onClick={toggleGlobalMode}
            className={cn(
              "absolute right-12 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-6 px-2",
              isGlobalMode && "text-primary bg-primary/10"
            )}
          >
            <Globe className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>

          {/* Filter button */}
          <Button
            type="button"
            variant="ghost"
            size="sm"
            onClick={toggleFilterPanel}
            className="absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-6 px-2"
          >
            <Filter className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>

          {/* Searching indicator */}
          {isSearching && (
            <Loader2 className="absolute right-32 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 animate-spin text-primary" />
          )}
        </div>
      </form>

      {/* Recent searches dropdown */}
      {showRecent && recentSearches.length > 0 && !query && (
        <div className="absolute top-full left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-lg z-50 py-2">
          <p className="px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-2">
            <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
            Recent Searches
          </p>
          {recentSearches.map((search, index) => (
            <button
              key={index}
              onClick={() => handleRecentClick(search)}
              className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm text-left hover:bg-accent flex items-center gap-2"
            >
              <Search className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
              {search}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Global mode badge */}
      {isGlobalMode && (
        <Badge variant="secondary" className="absolute -bottom-6 left-0 text-xs">
          <Globe className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />
          Global Search Active
        </Badge>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

4. `src/components/Search/FilterPanel.tsx` (Filter Overlay Panel)

```typescript
import { useSearchStore, useSearchFilters, useAvailableExtensions, useAvailableAccounts, useIsFilterPanelOpen } from '@/stores/searchStore';
import { X, HardDrive, Github, FolderGit, Terminal, File, Folder, Eye, EyeOff, Calendar, HardDriveIcon } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { Checkbox } from '@/components/ui/checkbox';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { Separator } from '@/components/ui/separator';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';

const sourceIcons = {
  storage: HardDrive,
  drive: FolderGit,
  github: Github,
  terminal: Terminal,
};

export function FilterPanel() {
  const isOpen = useIsFilterPanelOpen();
  const filters = useSearchFilters();
  const extensions = useAvailableExtensions();
  const accounts = useAvailableAccounts();
  const setFilters = useSearchStore((s) => s.setFilters);
  const resetFilters = useSearchStore((s) => s.resetFilters);
  const toggleFilterPanel = useSearchStore((s) => s.toggleFilterPanel);

  const [extensionSearch, setExtensionSearch] = useState('');

  const filteredExtensions = useMemo(() => {
    if (!extensionSearch) return extensions.slice(0, 50);
    return extensions
      .filter(e => e.extension.toLowerCase().includes(extensionSearch.toLowerCase()))
      .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count);
  }, [extensions, extensionSearch]);

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  const toggleSource = (source: string) => {
    const newSources = filters.sources.includes(source as any)
      ? filters.sources.filter(s => s !== source)
      : [...filters.sources, source as any];
    setFilters({ sources: newSources });
  };

  const toggleAccount = (accountId: string) => {
    const newAccounts = filters.accounts.includes(accountId)
      ? filters.accounts.filter(a => a !== accountId)
      : [...filters.accounts, accountId];
    setFilters({ accounts: newAccounts });
  };

  const toggleExtension = (ext: string) => {
    const newExtensions = filters.extensions.includes(ext)
      ? filters.extensions.filter(e => e !== ext)
      : [...filters.extensions, ext];
    setFilters({ extensions: newExtensions });
  };

  const activeFilterCount = 
    (filters.sources.length < 4 ? 1 : 0) +
    (filters.accounts.length > 0 ? 1 : 0) +
    (filters.extensions.length > 0 ? 1 : 0) +
    (filters.type !== 'all' ? 1 : 0) +
    (filters.includeHidden ? 1 : 0);

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-start justify-center pt-20 bg-black/30 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-4xl max-h-[80vh] bg-background rounded-lg shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Search Filters</h2>
            {activeFilterCount > 0 && (
              <Badge variant="secondary">{activeFilterCount} active</Badge>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={resetFilters}>
              Reset All
            </Button>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={toggleFilterPanel}>
              <X className="w-4 h-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Content */}
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden flex">
          {/* Left: Sources & Accounts */}
          <div className="w-1/3 border-r border-border p-4 space-y-6">
            {/* Sources */}
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-sm font-medium mb-3 flex items-center gap-2">
                <HardDriveIcon className="w-4 h-4" />
                Sources
              </h3>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                {(Object.keys(sourceIcons) as Array<keyof typeof sourceIcons>).map(source => {
                  const Icon = sourceIcons[source];
                  const isActive = filters.sources.includes(source);
                  
                  return (
                    <button
                      key={source}
                      onClick={() => toggleSource(source)}
                      className={cn(
                        "w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors",
                        isActive ? "bg-primary/10 text-primary" : "hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground"
                      )}
                    >
                      <Icon className="w-4 h-4" />
                      <span className="capitalize">{source}</span>
                      {isActive && <Badge variant="outline" className="ml-auto text-xs">On</Badge>}
                    </button>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </div>

            <Separator />

            {/* Accounts */}
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-sm font-medium mb-3">Accounts</h3>
              <ScrollArea className="h-48">
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  {accounts.map(account => {
                    const isActive = filters.accounts.includes(account.id);
                    
                    return (
                      <button
                        key={account.id}
                        onClick={() => toggleAccount(account.id)}
                        className={cn(
                          "w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors",
                          isActive ? "bg-primary/10 text-primary" : "hover:bg-accent"
                        )}
                      >
                        <div className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center text-xs">
                          {account.name.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
                        </div>
                        <span className="truncate">{account.name}</span>
                        {isActive && <Check className="w-3 h-3 ml-auto" />}
                      </button>
                    );
                  })}
                  
                  {accounts.length === 0 && (
                    <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-4">
                      No accounts connected
                    </p>
                  )}
                </div>
              </ScrollArea>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Middle: Extensions */}
          <div className="w-1/3 border-r border-border p-4">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium mb-3 flex items-center gap-2">
              <File className="w-4 h-4" />
              Extensions
              <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs">{extensions.length}</Badge>
            </h3>
            
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="Search extensions..."
              value={extensionSearch}
              onChange={(e) => setExtensionSearch(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full px-3 py-2 mb-3 text-sm border rounded-md bg-background"
            />

            <ScrollArea className="h-96">
              <div className="space-y-1">
                {filteredExtensions.map(ext => {
                  const isActive = filters.extensions.includes(ext.extension);
                  
                  return (
                    <button
                      key={ext.extension}
                      onClick={() => toggleExtension(ext.extension)}
                      className={cn(
                        "w-full flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors",
                        isActive ? "bg-primary/10 text-primary" : "hover:bg-accent"
                      )}
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <span className="font-mono text-xs bg-muted px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">
                          {ext.extension}
                        </span>
                        <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                          {ext.count.toLocaleString()}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      {isActive && <Check className="w-3 h-3" />}
                    </button>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </ScrollArea>
          </div>

          {/* Right: Type & Options */}
          <div className="w-1/3 p-4 space-y-6">
            {/* Type */}
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-sm font-medium mb-3 flex items-center gap-2">
                <Folder className="w-4 h-4" />
                Type
              </h3>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                {(['all', 'file', 'directory'] as const).map(type => (
                  <button
                    key={type}
                    onClick={() => setFilters({ type })}
                    className={cn(
                      "w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors capitalize",
                      filters.type === type ? "bg-primary/10 text-primary" : "hover:bg-accent"
                    )}
                  >
                    {type === 'all' && <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />}
                    {type === 'file' && <File className="w-4 h-4" />}
                    {type === 'directory' && <Folder className="w-4 h-4" />}
                    {type}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>

            <Separator />

            {/* Options */}
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-sm font-medium mb-3">Options</h3>
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                  <Checkbox
                    id="includeHidden"
                    checked={filters.includeHidden}
                    onCheckedChange={(checked) => 
                      setFilters({ includeHidden: checked as boolean })
                    }
                  />
                  <Label htmlFor="includeHidden" className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    {filters.includeHidden ? <Eye className="w-3 h-3" /> : <EyeOff className="w-3 h-3" />}
                    Include hidden files
                  </Label>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <Separator />

            {/* Selected filters summary */}
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-sm font-medium mb-2">Active Filters</h3>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                {filters.sources.length < 4 && filters.sources.map(s => (
                  <Badge key={s} variant="secondary" className="capitalize">
                    {s}
                  </Badge>
                ))}
                {filters.accounts.map(a => (
                  <Badge key={a} variant="secondary">
                    {a.split('@')[0]}
                  </Badge>
                ))}
                {filters.extensions.map(e => (
                  <Badge key={e} variant="secondary">
                    {e}
                  </Badge>
                ))}
                {filters.type !== 'all' && (
                  <Badge variant="secondary" className="capitalize">
                    {filters.type}s only
                  </Badge>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

5. `src/components/Search/SearchResultsOverlay.tsx` (Interactive Results)

```typescript
import { useSearchStore, useSearchResults, useSearchQuery } from '@/stores/searchStore';
import { HardDrive, Github, FolderGit, Terminal, File, Folder, X, ExternalLink, Pencil, Move, MoreVertical } from 'lucide-react';

export function SearchResultsOverlay() {
  const results = useSearchResults();
  const query = useSearchQuery();
  const setQuery = useSearchStore((s) => s.setQuery);
  
  const [selectedResult, setSelectedResult] = useState<string | null>(null);

  if (!query.trim() || results.length === 0) return null;

  const handleOpen = (result: any) => {
    // Open in appropriate panel
    console.log('Opening:', result.item.path);
  };

    // Trigger rename
    console.log('Renaming:', result.item.name);
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-full max-w-3xl max-h-[70vh] bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-2xl z-40 flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">

            for "{query}"
          </span>

      {/* Results */}

        <div className="divide-y divide-border">
          {results.map((result, index) => {
            const Icon = sourceIcons[result.item.sourceType];
            const isSelected = selectedResult === result.item.id;
            
            return (
              <div
                key={result.item.id}
                className={cn(
                  "group p-3 hover:bg-accent transition-colors cursor-pointer",
                  isSelected && "bg-accent"
                )}

                onDoubleClick={() => handleOpen(result)}
              >
                <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
                  {/* Icon */}
                  <div className={cn(
                    "w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0",
                    result.item.type === 'directory' ? "bg-primary/10" : "bg-muted"
                  )}>
                    {result.item.type === 'directory' ? (
                      <Folder className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
                    ) : (
                      <File className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground" />
                    )}
                  </div>

                  {/* Content */}
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      <Icon className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
                      <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground uppercase">
                        {result.item.sourceType}
                      </span>
                      <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">•</span>
                      <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
                        {result.item.accountId}
                      </span>

                      <HighlightMatches text={result.item.name} matches={result.matches} />
                    </p>
```
