```typescript
                      {result.item.path}
                    </p>

                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                      <span>{formatBytes(result.item.size)}</span>
                      <span>•</span>
                      <span>{new Date(result.item.lastModified).toLocaleDateString()}</span>
                      {result.item.extension && (
                        <>
                          <span>•</span>
                          <Badge variant="outline" className="text-[10px] px-1">
                            {result.item.extension}
                          </Badge>
                        </>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Actions */}
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
                    <Button
                      variant="ghost"
                      size="icon"
                      className="h-7 w-7"
                      onClick={(e) => {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        handleOpen(result);
                      }}
                    >
                      <ExternalLink className="w-4 h-4" />
                    </Button>
                    
                    <TreeIconButton
                      item={result.item}
                      sourceType={result.item.sourceType}
                      panelId="search"
                      className="h-7 w-7"
                    />
                    
                    <DFOLMenu
                      item={result.item}
                      sourceType={result.item.sourceType}
                      panelId="search"
                      onRename={() => handleRename(result)}
                      onDelete={() => {}}
                      onTreeView={() => {}}
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Match highlights */}
                {result.matches.length > 0 && result.matches[0].key !== 'name' && (
                  <div className="mt-2 pl-13 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                    <HighlightMatches 
                      text={result.matches[0].value} 
                      matches={[result.matches[0]]}
                      maxLength={100}
                    />
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </ScrollArea>

      {/* Footer */}
      <div className="p-2 border-t border-border bg-muted/50 text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center">
        Double-click to open • Use DFOL menu for batch operations
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function HighlightMatches({ 
  text, 
  matches, 
  maxLength = 50 
}: { 
  text: string; 
  matches: Array<{ key: string; value: string; indices: number[][] }>;
  maxLength?: number;
}) {
  if (!matches || matches.length === 0) {
    return <span>{text.length > maxLength ? text.slice(0, maxLength) + '...' : text}</span>;
  }

  // Get all indices from all matches
  const allIndices = matches.flatMap(m => m.indices);
  allIndices.sort((a, b) => a[0] - b[0]);

  // Merge overlapping indices
  const mergedIndices: number[][] = [];
  let current: number[] | null = null;
  
  for (const [start, end] of allIndices) {
    if (!current || start > current[1] + 1) {
      if (current) mergedIndices.push(current);
      current = [start, end];
    } else {
      current[1] = Math.max(current[1], end);
    }
  }
  if (current) mergedIndices.push(current);

  // Build highlighted text
  const parts: React.ReactNode[] = [];
  let lastEnd = 0;
  
  for (const [start, end] of mergedIndices) {
    if (start > lastEnd) {
      parts.push(
        <span key={`text-${lastEnd}`}>
          {text.slice(lastEnd, start)}
        </span>
      );
    }
    parts.push(
      <mark key={`mark-${start}`} className="bg-yellow-200 dark:bg-yellow-900 px-0.5 rounded">
        {text.slice(start, end + 1)}
      </mark>
    );
    lastEnd = end + 1;
  }
  
  if (lastEnd < text.length) {
    parts.push(
      <span key={`text-${lastEnd}`}>
        {text.slice(lastEnd, maxLength)}
      </span>
    );
  }

  return <>{parts}{text.length > maxLength && '...'}</>;
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
```

6. `src/workers/extensionScanner.worker.ts` (Extension Scanner Worker)

```typescript
import { expose } from 'comlink';

interface ScanResult {
  extensions: Map<string, { count: number; totalSize: number }>;
  totalFiles: number;
  totalSize: number;
}

class ExtensionScanner {
  async scan(items: any[]): Promise<ScanResult> {
    const extensions = new Map<string, { count: number; totalSize: number }>();
    let totalFiles = 0;
    let totalSize = 0;

    const processItem = (item: any) => {
      const ext = this.getExtension(item.name);
      
      if (item.type === 'file' || item.kind === 'file') {
        totalFiles++;
        totalSize += item.size || 0;

        if (ext) {
          const existing = extensions.get(ext);
          if (existing) {
            existing.count++;
            existing.totalSize += item.size || 0;
          } else {
            extensions.set(ext, {
              count: 1,
              totalSize: item.size || 0,
            });
          }
        }
      }

      // Recursively process children
      if (item.children) {
        item.children.forEach(processItem);
      }
    };

    items.forEach(processItem);

    return {
      extensions,
      totalFiles,
      totalSize,
    };
  }

  private getExtension(filename: string): string | null {
    if (!filename || !filename.includes('.')) return null;
    const ext = filename.slice(filename.lastIndexOf('.')).toLowerCase();
    return ext.length > 1 ? ext : null;
  }

  async incrementalScan(
    existingExtensions: Map<string, { count: number; totalSize: number }>,
    newItems: any[]
  ): Promise<ScanResult> {
    const result = await this.scan(newItems);
    
    // Merge with existing
    for (const [ext, stats] of result.extensions) {
      const existing = existingExtensions.get(ext);
      if (existing) {
        existing.count += stats.count;
        existing.totalSize += stats.totalSize;
      } else {
        existingExtensions.set(ext, stats);
      }
    }

    return {
      extensions: existingExtensions,
      totalFiles: result.totalFiles,
      totalSize: result.totalSize,
    };
  }
}

expose(ExtensionScanner);
```

```typescript
import { usePanelStore, usePanels, useActivePanelId } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { ResizablePanel } from './Panel/ResizablePanel';
import { GlobalSearchBar } from './Search/GlobalSearchBar';
import { FilterPanel } from './Search/FilterPanel';
import { SearchResultsOverlay } from './Search/SearchResultsOverlay';
import { Plus } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { MAX_PANELS } from '@/types/panel';

export function PanelContainer() {
  const panels = usePanels();
  const activePanelId = useActivePanelId();
  const { addPanel, removePanel, setActivePanel } = usePanelStore();

  const canAddPanel = panels.length < MAX_PANELS;

  return (
    <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden bg-background">
      {/* Top bar with search */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-4 px-4 py-2 border-b border-border bg-card">
        <GlobalSearchBar />
        
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          onClick={addPanel}
          disabled={!canAddPanel}
          className="shrink-0 gap-2"
        >
          <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
          Add Panel
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* Filter Panel */}
      <FilterPanel />

      {/* Search Results */}
      <SearchResultsOverlay />

      {/* Panels */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-x-auto overflow-y-hidden">
        {panels.map((panel, index) => (
          <ResizablePanel
            key={panel.id}
            panel={panel}
            isActive={panel.id === activePanelId}
            isLast={index === panels.length - 1}
            onActivate={() => setActivePanel(panel.id)}
            onClose={() => removePanel(panel.id)}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

1. `src/types/auth.ts` (Authority Types)

```typescript
export interface User {
  id: string;
  username: string;
  passwordHash: string; // SHA-256
  role: 'admin' | 'user';
  createdAt: Date;
  lastLogin?: Date;
  isActive: boolean;
}

export interface ActionPassword {
  action: 'delete' | 'format' | 'rename' | 'dfol';
  passwordHash: string;
  required: boolean;
}

export interface Session {
  id: string;
  userId: string;
  username: string;
  startTime: Date;
  endTime?: Date;
  logs: LogEntry[];
  ip?: string;
  userAgent?: string;
}

export interface LogEntry {
  id: string;
  timestamp: Date;
  level: 'info' | 'warn' | 'error' | 'debug';
  category: 'auth' | 'file' | 'system' | 'network' | 'ui';
  action: string;
  details: Record<string, any>;
  userId: string;
  sessionId: string;
  panelId?: string;
  sourceType?: string;
  duration?: number; // ms
}

export interface Notification {
  id: string;
  type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
  title: string;
  message: string;
  timestamp: Date;
  read: boolean;
  action?: {
    label: string;
    onClick: () => void;
  };
  expiresAt?: Date;
}

export interface TokenExpiry {
  provider: 'drive' | 'github';
  accountId: string;
  expiresAt: Date;
  warned: boolean;
}
```

2. `src/stores/authStore.ts` (Authority & Session Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import CryptoJS from 'crypto-js';
import { User, Session, ActionPassword, TokenExpiry } from '@/types/auth';
import { openDB } from 'idb';

const ADMIN_PASSWORD_HASH = '5e884898da28047151d0e56f8dc6292773603d0d6aabbdd62a11ef721d1542d8'; // "password"

interface AuthState {
  currentUser: User | null;
  currentSession: Session | null;
  isAuthenticated: boolean;
  users: User[];
  actionPasswords: ActionPassword[];
  tokenExpiries: TokenExpiry[];
  isAdminRoute: boolean;
}

interface AuthActions {
  // Auth
  login: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<boolean>;
  logout: () => Promise<void>;
  adminLogin: (password: string) => boolean;
  adminLogout: () => void;
  
  // Users
  createUser: (username: string, password: string, role?: 'admin' | 'user') => Promise<void>;
  updateUser: (userId: string, updates: Partial<User>) => Promise<void>;
  deleteUser: (userId: string) => Promise<void>;
  getUsers: () => User[];
  
  // Action passwords
  setActionPassword: (action: string, password: string, required: boolean) => void;
  verifyActionPassword: (action: string, password: string) => boolean;
  
  // Token expiry
  addTokenExpiry: (expiry: TokenExpiry) => void;
  removeTokenExpiry: (accountId: string) => void;
  checkTokenExpiries: () => TokenExpiry[];
  
  // Session
  getSessionLogs: () => LogEntry[];
  exportSession: () => Promise<Blob>;
  
  // Admin check
  checkIsAdmin: () => boolean;
}

const hashPassword = (password: string): string => {
  return CryptoJS.SHA256(password).toString();
};

const DB_NAME = 'auth-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

export const useAuthStore = create<AuthState & AuthActions>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    currentUser: null,
    currentSession: null,
    isAuthenticated: false,
    users: [],
    actionPasswords: [],
    tokenExpiries: [],
    isAdminRoute: false,

    // Auth
    login: async (username, password) => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const user = await db.get('users', username);
      
      if (!user || !user.isActive) return false;
      
      const passwordHash = hashPassword(password);
      if (user.passwordHash !== passwordHash) return false;
      
      // Create session
      const session: Session = {
        id: `session-${Date.now()}`,
        userId: user.id,
        username: user.username,
        startTime: new Date(),
        logs: [],
      };
      
      // Update last login
      user.lastLogin = new Date();
      await db.put('users', user);
      
      set((state) => {
        state.currentUser = user;
        state.currentSession = session;
        state.isAuthenticated = true;
      });
      
      return true;
    },

    logout: async () => {
      const { currentSession, currentUser } = get();
      
      if (currentSession && currentUser) {
        // Save session logs
        const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
        currentSession.endTime = new Date();
        await db.add('sessions', currentSession);
      }
      
      set((state) => {
        state.currentUser = null;
        state.currentSession = null;
        state.isAuthenticated = false;
      });
    },

    adminLogin: (password) => {
      const hash = hashPassword(password);
      if (hash === ADMIN_PASSWORD_HASH) {
        set((state) => {
          state.isAdminRoute = true;
        });
        return true;
      }
      return false;
    },

    adminLogout: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isAdminRoute = false;
      });
    },

    // Users
    createUser: async (username, password, role = 'user') => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      
      const existing = await db.get('users', username);
      if (existing) throw new Error('Username already exists');
      
      const user: User = {
        id: `user-${Date.now()}`,
        username,
        passwordHash: hashPassword(password),
        role,
        createdAt: new Date(),
        isActive: true,
      };
      
      await db.put('users', user);
      
      set((state) => {
        state.users.push(user);
      });
    },

    updateUser: async (userId, updates) => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('users', 'readwrite');
      const store = tx.objectStore('users');
      
      const users = await store.getAll();
      const user = users.find(u => u.id === userId);
      if (!user) throw new Error('User not found');
      
      Object.assign(user, updates);
      if (updates.password) {
        user.passwordHash = hashPassword(updates.password);
      }
      
      await store.put(user);
      await tx.done;
    },

    deleteUser: async (userId) => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('users', 'readwrite');
      const store = tx.objectStore('users');
      
      const users = await store.getAll();
      const user = users.find(u => u.id === userId);
      if (user) {
        user.isActive = false;
        await store.put(user);
      }
      
      await tx.done;
    },

    getUsers: () => {
      return get().users;
    },

    // Action passwords
    setActionPassword: (action, password, required) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existing = state.actionPasswords.find(p => p.action === action);
        if (existing) {
          existing.passwordHash = hashPassword(password);
          existing.required = required;
        } else {
          state.actionPasswords.push({
            action: action as any,
            passwordHash: hashPassword(password),
            required,
          });
        }
      });
    },

    verifyActionPassword: (action, password) => {
      const { actionPasswords } = get();
      const config = actionPasswords.find(p => p.action === action);
      
      if (!config || !config.required) return true;
      
      return config.passwordHash === hashPassword(password);
    },

    // Token expiry
    addTokenExpiry: (expiry) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existing = state.tokenExpiries.find(e => e.accountId === expiry.accountId);
        if (existing) {
          Object.assign(existing, expiry);
        } else {
          state.tokenExpiries.push(expiry);
        }
      });
    },

    removeTokenExpiry: (accountId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.tokenExpiries = state.tokenExpiries.filter(e => e.accountId !== accountId);
      });
    },

    checkTokenExpiries: () => {
      const now = new Date();
      const tenDaysFromNow = new Date(now.getTime() + 10 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
      
      return get().tokenExpiries.filter(e => {
        return e.expiresAt <= tenDaysFromNow && !e.warned;
      });
    },

    // Session
    getSessionLogs: () => {
      return get().currentSession?.logs || [];
    },

    exportSession: async () => {
      const { currentSession, currentUser } = get();
      if (!currentSession || !currentUser) throw new Error('No active session');
      
      const exportData = {
        session: currentSession,
        user: {
          id: currentUser.id,
          username: currentUser.username,
          role: currentUser.role,
        },
        exportedAt: new Date(),
      };
      
      return new Blob([JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
    },

    checkIsAdmin: () => {
      const { currentUser, isAdminRoute } = get();
      return isAdminRoute || currentUser?.role === 'admin';
    },
  }))
);

// Initialize DB
const initAuthDB = async () => {
  const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
    upgrade(db) {
      db.createObjectStore('users', { keyPath: 'username' });
      db.createObjectStore('sessions', { keyPath: 'id' });
      db.createObjectStore('logs', { keyPath: 'id' });
    },
  });
  
  // Create default admin if none exists
  const users = await db.getAll('users');
  if (users.length === 0) {
    await db.put('users', {
      id: 'admin-1',
      username: 'admin',
      passwordHash: ADMIN_PASSWORD_HASH,
      role: 'admin',
      createdAt: new Date(),
      isActive: true,
    });
  }
  
  return db;
};

initAuthDB();
```

3. `src/stores/logStore.ts` (Live Log Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { LogEntry, Notification } from '@/types/auth';
import { openDB } from 'idb';
import { useAuthStore } from './authStore';

interface LogState {
  logs: LogEntry[];
  notifications: Notification[];
  isLiveLogOpen: boolean;
  logLevel: 'debug' | 'info' | 'warn' | 'error';
  logCategories: string[];
  unreadCount: number;
}

interface LogActions {
  // Logging
  log: (entry: Omit<LogEntry, 'id' | 'timestamp' | 'userId' | 'sessionId'>) => void;
  logAction: (action: string, details: Record<string, any>, category?: LogEntry['category']) => void;
  
  // Live log
  toggleLiveLog: () => void;
  setLogLevel: (level: LogState['logLevel']) => void;
  toggleCategory: (category: string) => void;
  getFilteredLogs: () => LogEntry[];
  clearLogs: () => void;
  exportLogs: () => Promise<Blob>;
  
  // Notifications
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<Notification, 'id' | 'timestamp' | 'read'>) => void;
  markNotificationRead: (id: string) => void;
  markAllRead: () => void;
  dismissNotification: (id: string) => void;
  getUnreadCount: () => number;
  
  // Background processes
  startBackgroundChecks: () => void;
  stopBackgroundChecks: () => void;
}

const DB_NAME = 'logs-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

export const useLogStore = create<LogState & LogActions>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    logs: [],
    notifications: [],
    isLiveLogOpen: false,
    logLevel: 'info',
    logCategories: ['auth', 'file', 'system', 'network', 'ui'],
    unreadCount: 0,

    // Logging
    log: async (entry) => {
      const { currentUser, currentSession } = useAuthStore.getState();
      
      const fullEntry: LogEntry = {
        ...entry,
        id: `log-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`,
        timestamp: new Date(),
        userId: currentUser?.id || 'anonymous',
        sessionId: currentSession?.id || 'no-session',
      };
      
      // Add to current session
      if (currentSession) {
        currentSession.logs.push(fullEntry);
      }
      
      // Persist to IndexedDB
      try {
        const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
        await db.add('logs', fullEntry);
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('Failed to persist log:', e);
      }
      
      set((state) => {
        state.logs.push(fullEntry);
        
        // Keep only last 1000 logs in memory
        if (state.logs.length > 1000) {
          state.logs = state.logs.slice(-1000);
        }
      });
    },

    logAction: (action, details, category = 'ui') => {
      get().log({
        level: 'info',
        category,
        action,
        details,
      });
    },

    // Live log
    toggleLiveLog: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isLiveLogOpen = !state.isLiveLogOpen;
      });
    },

    setLogLevel: (level) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.logLevel = level;
      });
    },

    toggleCategory: (category) => {
      set((state) => {
        const exists = state.logCategories.includes(category);
        if (exists) {
          state.logCategories = state.logCategories.filter(c => c !== category);
        } else {
          state.logCategories.push(category);
        }
      });
    },

    getFilteredLogs: () => {
      const { logs, logLevel, logCategories } = get();
      
      const levelPriority = { debug: 0, info: 1, warn: 2, error: 3 };
      const minLevel = levelPriority[logLevel];
      
      return logs.filter(log => {
        const logPriority = levelPriority[log.level];
        return logPriority >= minLevel && logCategories.includes(log.category);
      }).slice(-500); // Last 500 matching logs
    },

    clearLogs: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.logs = [];
      });
    },

    exportLogs: async () => {
      const { currentUser } = useAuthStore.getState();
      const { logs } = get();
      
      const exportData = {
        exportedBy: currentUser?.username || 'unknown',
        exportedAt: new Date(),
        totalLogs: logs.length,
        logs: logs,
      };
      
      return new Blob([JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
    },

    // Notifications
    addNotification: (notification) => {
      const fullNotification: Notification = {
        ...notification,
        id: `notif-${Date.now()}`,
        timestamp: new Date(),
        read: false,
      };
      
      set((state) => {
        state.notifications.unshift(fullNotification);
        state.unreadCount++;
        
        // Keep only last 50 notifications
        if (state.notifications.length > 50) {
          state.notifications = state.notifications.slice(0, 50);
        }
      });
    },

    markNotificationRead: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        const notif = state.notifications.find(n => n.id === id);
        if (notif && !notif.read) {
          notif.read = true;
          state.unreadCount = Math.max(0, state.unreadCount - 1);
        }
      });
    },

    markAllRead: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.notifications.forEach(n => n.read = true);
        state.unreadCount = 0;
      });
    },

    dismissNotification: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        const index = state.notifications.findIndex(n => n.id === id);
        if (index >= 0) {
          const wasUnread = !state.notifications[index].read;
          state.notifications.splice(index, 1);
          if (wasUnread) {
            state.unreadCount = Math.max(0, state.unreadCount - 1);
          }
        }
      });
    },

    getUnreadCount: () => {
      return get().unreadCount;
    },

    // Background checks
    startBackgroundChecks: () => {
      // Token expiry check every day
      const checkInterval = setInterval(() => {
        const { checkTokenExpiries, tokenExpiries } = useAuthStore.getState();
        const { addNotification } = get();
        
        const expiring = checkTokenExpiries();
        
        expiring.forEach(expiry => {
          const daysLeft = Math.ceil((expiry.expiresAt.getTime() - Date.now()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
          
          addNotification({
            type: 'warning',
            title: 'Token Expiring Soon',
            message: `${expiry.provider} token for ${expiry.accountId} expires in ${daysLeft} days`,
            action: {
              label: 'Refresh',
              onClick: () => {
                // Trigger token refresh
                console.log('Refreshing token for', expiry.accountId);
              },
            },
          });
          
          // Mark as warned
          expiry.warned = true;
        });
      }, 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // Every 24 hours
      
      // Store interval for cleanup
      (window as any).backgroundCheckInterval = checkInterval;
    },

    stopBackgroundChecks: () => {
      if ((window as any).backgroundCheckInterval) {
        clearInterval((window as any).backgroundCheckInterval);
      }
    },
  }))
);

// Initialize log DB
const initLogDB = async () => {
  await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
    upgrade(db) {
      db.createObjectStore('logs', { keyPath: 'id' });
      db.createObjectStore('notifications', { keyPath: 'id' });
    },
  });
};

initLogDB();
```

4. `src/components/Notification/NotificationBell.tsx` (Notification Component)

```typescript
import { Bell, Check, AlertCircle, Info, X, Clock } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { useLogStore, useLogNotifications, useLogUnreadCount } from '@/stores/logStore';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

export function NotificationBell() {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const notifications = useLogNotifications();
  const unreadCount = useLogUnreadCount();
  const markNotificationRead = useLogStore((s) => s.markNotificationRead);
  const markAllRead = useLogStore((s) => s.markAllRead);
  const dismissNotification = useLogStore((s) => s.dismissNotification);

  // Auto-start background checks
  useEffect(() => {
    const { startBackgroundChecks } = useLogStore.getState();
    startBackgroundChecks();
    
    return () => {
      const { stopBackgroundChecks } = useLogStore.getState();
      stopBackgroundChecks();
    };
  }, []);

  const getIcon = (type: string) => {
    switch (type) {
      case 'success': return <Check className="w-4 h-4 text-green-500" />;
      case 'warning': return <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-yellow-500" />;
      case 'error': return <X className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />;
      default: return <Info className="w-4 h-4 text-blue-500" />;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="relative">
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        className="relative"
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
      >
        <Bell className="w-5 h-5" />
        {unreadCount > 0 && (
          <Badge 
            variant="destructive" 
            className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 h-5 w-5 flex items-center justify-center p-0 text-xs"
          >
            {unreadCount > 9 ? '9+' : unreadCount}
          </Badge>
        )}
      </Button>

      {isOpen && (
        <>
          <div 
            className="fixed inset-0 z-40" 
            onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
          />
          <div className="absolute right-0 top-full mt-2 w-96 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-xl z-50">
            {/* Header */}
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border">
              <h3 className="font-semibold">Notifications</h3>
              {unreadCount > 0 && (
                <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={markAllRead}>
                  Mark all read
                </Button>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Notifications */}
            <ScrollArea className="h-80">
              {notifications.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
                  <Bell className="w-8 h-8 mb-2 opacity-50" />
                  <p className="text-sm">No notifications</p>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="divide-y divide-border">
                  {notifications.map((notif) => (
                    <div
                      key={notif.id}
                      className={cn(
                        "p-3 hover:bg-accent transition-colors",
                        !notif.read && "bg-primary/5"
                      )}
                      onClick={() => markNotificationRead(notif.id)}
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
                        {getIcon(notif.type)}
                        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                          <p className="font-medium text-sm">{notif.title}</p>
                          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                            {notif.message}
                          </p>
                          
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2">
                            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1">
                              <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
                              {new Date(notif.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()}
                            </span>
                            
                            {notif.action && (
                              <Button
                                variant="outline"
                                size="sm"
                                className="h-6 text-xs"
                                onClick={(e) => {
                                  e.stopPropagation();
                                  notif.action?.onClick();
                                }}
                              >
                                {notif.action.label}
                              </Button>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        
                        <Button
                          variant="ghost"
                          size="icon"
                          className="h-6 w-6 shrink-0"
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            dismissNotification(notif.id);
                          }}
                        >
                          <X className="w-3 h-3" />
                        </Button>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </ScrollArea>
          </div>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

5. `src/components/Log/LiveLogPanel.tsx` (Live Log Panel)

```typescript
import { X, Settings, Download, Trash2, Filter, Terminal, Bug, Info, AlertTriangle, AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { Switch } from '@/components/ui/switch';
import { useLogStore, useLogFilteredLogs, useLogIsLiveLogOpen } from '@/stores/logStore';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { saveAs } from 'file-saver';

const levelIcons = {
  debug: <Bug className="w-3 h-3" />,
  info: <Info className="w-3 h-3" />,
  warn: <AlertTriangle className="w-3 h-3" />,
  error: <AlertCircle className="w-3 h-3" />,
};

const levelColors = {
  debug: 'text-muted-foreground',
  info: 'text-blue-500',
  warn: 'text-yellow-500',
  error: 'text-destructive',
};

const categoryColors = {
  auth: 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-800',
  file: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800',
  system: 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800',
  network: 'bg-orange-100 text-orange-800',
  ui: 'bg-pink-100 text-pink-800',
};

export function LiveLogPanel() {
  const isOpen = useLogIsLiveLogOpen();
  const logs = useLogFilteredLogs();
  const toggleLiveLog = useLogStore((s) => s.toggleLiveLog);
  const setLogLevel = useLogStore((s) => s.setLogLevel);
  const clearLogs = useLogStore((s) => s.clearLogs);
  const exportLogs = useLogStore((s) => s.exportLogs);
  const logLevel = useLogStore((s) => s.logLevel);
  const logCategories = useLogStore((s) => s.logCategories);
  const toggleCategory = useLogStore((s) => s.toggleCategory);

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  const handleExport = async () => {
    const blob = await exportLogs();
    saveAs(blob, `logs-${new Date().toISOString()}.json`);
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed bottom-4 left-4 right-4 h-80 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-2xl z-50 flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border bg-muted/50">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Terminal className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
          <h3 className="font-semibold">Live Log</h3>
          <Badge variant="outline">{logs.length} entries</Badge>
        </div>
        
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {/* Level filter */}
          <select
            value={logLevel}
            onChange={(e) => setLogLevel(e.target.value as any)}
            className="text-xs border rounded px-2 py-1 bg-background"
          >
            <option value="debug">Debug</option>
            <option value="info">Info</option>
            <option value="warn">Warn</option>
            <option value="error">Error</option>
          </select>

          {/* Category toggles */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
            {(['auth', 'file', 'system', 'network', 'ui'] as const).map(cat => (
              <button
                key={cat}
                onClick={() => toggleCategory(cat)}
                className={cn(
                  "px-2 py-1 text-xs rounded capitalize",
                  logCategories.includes(cat) ? categoryColors[cat] : "bg-muted text-muted-foreground"
                )}
              >
                {cat}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-8 w-8" onClick={handleExport}>
            <Download className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>
          
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-8 w-8" onClick={clearLogs}>
            <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>
          
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-8 w-8" onClick={toggleLiveLog}>
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Log entries */}
      <ScrollArea className="flex-1 p-2 font-mono text-xs">
        <div className="space-y-1">
          {logs.length === 0 ? (
            <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center py-8">No logs to display</p>
          ) : (
            logs.map((log) => (
              <div
                key={log.id}
                className="flex items-start gap-2 p-1.5 rounded hover:bg-accent/50"
              >
                <span className={cn("shrink-0", levelColors[log.level])}>
                  {levelIcons[log.level]}
                </span>
                
                <span className="text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
                  {new Date(log.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()}
                </span>
                
                <Badge 
                  variant="secondary" 
                  className={cn("shrink-0 text-[10px] px-1", categoryColors[log.category])}
                >
                  {log.category}
                </Badge>
                
                <span className="text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
                  [{log.userId.slice(0, 8)}]
                </span>
                
                <span className={cn("font-medium", levelColors[log.level])}>
                  {log.action}
                </span>
                
                {Object.keys(log.details).length > 0 && (
                  <span className="text-muted-foreground truncate">
                    {JSON.stringify(log.details)}
                  </span>
                )}
                
                {log.duration && (
                  <span className="text-muted-foreground ml-auto">
                    {log.duration}ms
                  </span>
                )}
              </div>
            ))
          )}
        </div>
      </ScrollArea>
    </div>
  );
}
```

6. `src/components/Admin/AdminPanel.tsx` (Admin Panel)

```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';
import { useAuthStore } from '@/stores/authStore';
import { User, ActionPassword } from '@/types/auth';
import { X, Plus, Trash2, Save, Shield, Key, Users, Activity } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Switch } from '@/components/ui/switch';
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from '@/components/ui/tabs';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export function AdminPanel() {
  const isAdminRoute = useAuthStore((s) => s.isAdminRoute);
  const adminLogin = useAuthStore((s) => s.adminLogin);
  const adminLogout = useAuthStore((s) => s.adminLogout);
  const users = useAuthStore((s) => s.users);
  const createUser = useAuthStore((s) => s.createUser);
  const updateUser = useAuthStore((s) => s.updateUser);
  const deleteUser = useAuthStore((s) => s.deleteUser);
  const setActionPassword = useAuthStore((s) => s.setActionPassword);

  const [adminPassword, setAdminPassword] = useState('');
  const [loginError, setLoginError] = useState('');
  
  const [newUser, setNewUser] = useState({ username: '', password: '', role: 'user' as const });
  const [editingUser, setEditingUser] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [actionPasswords, setActionPasswords] = useState({
    delete: { password: '', required: false },
    format: { password: '', required: false },
    rename: { password: '', required: false },
    dfol: { password: '', required: false },
  });

  if (!isAdminRoute) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background">
        <div className="w-full max-w-md p-6 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-lg">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-6">
            <Shield className="w-6 h-6 text-primary" />
            <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Admin Access</h1>
          </div>
          
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <div>
              <Label>Admin Password</Label>
              <Input
                type="password"
                value={adminPassword}
                onChange={(e) => setAdminPassword(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Enter admin password"
              />
            </div>
            
            {loginError && (
              <p className="text-sm text-destructive">{loginError}</p>
            )}
            
            <Button 
              className="w-full" 
              onClick={() => {
                if (adminLogin(adminPassword)) {
                  setLoginError('');
                } else {
                  setLoginError('Invalid password');
                }
              }}
            >
              Login
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const handleCreateUser = async () => {
    try {
      await createUser(newUser.username, newUser.password, newUser.role);
      setNewUser({ username: '', password: '', role: 'user' });
    } catch (error) {
      alert((error as Error).message);
    }
  };

  const handleSaveActionPasswords = () => {
    Object.entries(actionPasswords).forEach(([action, config]) => {
      if (config.password) {
        setActionPassword(action, config.password, config.required);
      }
    });
    alert('Action passwords saved');
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background p-6">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <Shield className="w-8 h-8 text-primary" />
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold">Admin Panel</h1>
          </div>
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={adminLogout}>
            <X className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
            Logout
          </Button>
        </div>

        <Tabs defaultValue="users">
          <TabsList className="mb-6">
            <TabsTrigger value="users" className="gap-2">
              <Users className="w-4 h-4" />
              Users
            </TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="security" className="gap-2">
              <Key className="w-4 h-4" />
              Security
            </TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="logs" className="gap-2">
              <Activity className="w-4 h-4" />
              System Logs
            </TabsTrigger>
          </TabsList>

          {/* Users Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="users" className="space-y-6">
            {/* Create User */}
            <div className="p-4 border border-border rounded-lg bg-card">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4">Create New User</h3>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                <div>
                  <Label>Username</Label>
                  <Input
                    value={newUser.username}
                    onChange={(e) => setNewUser({ ...newUser, username: e.target.value })}
                    placeholder="username"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <Label>Password</Label>
                  <Input
                    type="password"
                    value={newUser.password}
                    onChange={(e) => setNewUser({ ...newUser, password: e.target.value })}
                    placeholder="password"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <Label>Role</Label>
                  <select
                    value={newUser.role}
                    onChange={(e) => setNewUser({ ...newUser, role: e.target.value as any })}
                    className="w-full h-10 px-3 rounded-md border bg-background"
                  >
                    <option value="user">User</option>
                    <option value="admin">Admin</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
              </div>
              <Button className="mt-4" onClick={handleCreateUser}>
                <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                Create User
              </Button>
            </div>

            {/* User List */}
            <div className="border border-border rounded-lg bg-card">
              <table className="w-full">
                <thead className="bg-muted">
                  <tr>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm font-medium">Username</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm font-medium">Role</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm font-medium">Status</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm font-medium">Last Login</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-right text-sm font-medium">Actions</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody className="divide-y divide-border">
                  {users.map((user) => (
                    <tr key={user.id} className={cn(!user.isActive && "opacity-50")}>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">{user.username}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <Badge variant={user.role === 'admin' ? 'default' : 'secondary'}>
                          {user.role}
                        </Badge>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <Badge variant={user.isActive ? 'outline' : 'destructive'}>
                          {user.isActive ? 'Active' : 'Inactive'}
                        </Badge>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                        {user.lastLogin?.toLocaleString() || 'Never'}
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                        <Button
                          variant="ghost"
                          size="sm"
                          onClick={() => deleteUser(user.id)}
                        >
                          <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />
                        </Button>
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  ))}
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </div>
          </TabsContent>

          {/* Security Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="security" className="space-y-6">
            <div className="p-4 border border-border rounded-lg bg-card">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4">Action Passwords</h3>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4">
                Require additional passwords for sensitive operations
              </p>

              <div className="space-y-4">
                {(['delete', 'format', 'rename', 'dfol'] as const).map((action) => (
                  <div key={action} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border rounded-lg">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                      <Switch
                        checked={actionPasswords[action].required}
                        onCheckedChange={(checked) => 
                          setActionPasswords({
                            ...actionPasswords,
                            [action]: { ...actionPasswords[action], required: checked }
                          })
                        }
                      />
                      <span className="font-medium capitalize">{action}</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    {actionPasswords[action].required && (
                      <Input
                        type="password"
                        placeholder={`${action} password`}
                        value={actionPasswords[action].password}
                        onChange={(e) => 
                          setActionPasswords({
                            ...actionPasswords,
                            [action]: { ...actionPasswords[action], password: e.target.value }
                          })
                        }
                        className="w-48"
                      />
                    )}
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>

              <Button className="mt-4" onClick={handleSaveActionPasswords}>
                <Save className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                Save Security Settings
              </Button>
            </div>
          </TabsContent>

          {/* Logs Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="logs">
            <div className="p-4 border border-border rounded-lg bg-card">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4">System Logs</h3>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                View and export system-wide logs
              </p>
              {/* Log viewer implementation */}
            </div>
          </TabsContent>
        </Tabs>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

7. `src/components/Log/LogActionWrapper.tsx` (Action Logging Wrapper)

```typescript
import { useLogStore } from '@/stores/logStore';
import { useCallback } from 'react';

export function useLoggedAction() {
  const logAction = useLogStore((s) => s.logAction);

  const wrapAction = useCallback(<T extends (...args: any[]) => any>(
    actionName: string,
    fn: T,
    category?: Parameters<typeof logAction>[2]
  ): T => {
    return (async (...args: any[]) => {
      const startTime = performance.now();
      
      logAction(`${actionName}_start`, { args }, category);
      
      try {
        const result = await fn(...args);
        const duration = Math.round(performance.now() - startTime);
        
        logAction(`${actionName}_complete`, { 
          args, 
          result: typeof result === 'object' ? 'success' : result,
          duration 
        }, category);
        
        return result;
      } catch (error) {
        const duration = Math.round(performance.now() - startTime);
        
        logAction(`${actionName}_error`, { 
          args, 
          error: (error as Error).message,
          duration 
        }, category || 'system');
        
        throw error;
      }
    }) as T;
  }, [logAction]);

  return { wrapAction, logAction };
}

// Hook for component-level logging
export function useComponentLogger(componentName: string) {
  const logAction = useLogStore((s) => s.logAction);

  const logEvent = useCallback((event: string, details?: Record<string, any>) => {
    logAction(`${componentName}_${event}`, details || {}, 'ui');
  }, [logAction, componentName]);

  const logMount = useCallback(() => {
    logEvent('mount');
  }, [logEvent]);

  const logUnmount = useCallback(() => {
    logEvent('unmount');
  }, [logEvent]);

  const logClick = useCallback((element: string, details?: Record<string, any>) => {
    logEvent(`click_${element}`, details);
  }, [logEvent]);

  return { logEvent, logMount, logUnmount, logClick };
}
```

8. `src/App.tsx` (Final with Admin Route)

```typescript
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { MainApp } from './MainApp';
import { AdminPanel } from './components/Admin/AdminPanel';
import { NotificationBell } from './components/Notification/NotificationBell';
import { LiveLogPanel } from './components/Log/LiveLogPanel';
import { useLogStore } from './stores/logStore';

function App() {
  // Initialize logging
  useEffect(() => {
    const { logAction } = useLogStore.getState();
    
    // Log app start
    logAction('app_start', {
      userAgent: navigator.userAgent,
      platform: navigator.platform,
    }, 'system');

    // Setup global error handler
    window.onerror = (message, source, lineno, colno, error) => {
      logAction('uncaught_error', {
        message,
        source,
        lineno,
        colno,
        stack: error?.stack,
      }, 'system');
      return false;
    };

    // Setup unhandled promise rejection handler
    window.onunhandledrejection = (event) => {
      logAction('unhandled_rejection', {
        reason: event.reason?.toString(),
      }, 'system');
    };
  }, []);

  return (
    <BrowserRouter>
      <Routes>
        <Route path="/" element={<MainApp />} />
        <Route path="/admin" element={<AdminPanel />} />
        <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
      </Routes>
      
      {/* Global overlays */}
      <NotificationBell />
      <LiveLogPanel />
    </BrowserRouter>
  );
}

export default App;
```

1. `src/types/prompt.ts` (Prompt Manager Types)

```typescript
export interface PromptSession {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
  promptText: string;
  notes: PromptNote[];
  files: PromptFile[];
  folderStructure: PromptFolder;
  isCompleted: boolean;
  uploadResult?: {
    provider: 'drive' | 'github';
    folderPath: string;
    shareLink: string;
    rawLink?: string;
    uploadedAt: Date;
  };
}

export interface PromptNote {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  content: string;
  createdAt: Date;
  attachedToLink?: boolean;
}

export interface PromptFile {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  size: number;
  type: string;
  source: 'upload' | 'drag-drop' | 'reference';
  sourcePath?: string;
  sourcePanelId?: string;
  content?: Blob; // Only stored at end
  folderPath: string;
  isCompressed: boolean;
  compressionProfile?: string;
}

export interface PromptFolder {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  path: string;
  children: (PromptFolder | PromptFile)[];
  parent?: PromptFolder;
}

export interface PromptManagerState {
  sessions: PromptSession[];
  currentSession: PromptSession | null;
  isPromptManagerOpen: boolean;
  selectedUploadProvider: 'drive' | 'github';
  isUploading: boolean;
  uploadProgress: number;
}

export interface FileOperation {
  type: 'create' | 'rename' | 'delete' | 'move' | 'compress';
  targetId: string;
  params: Record<string, any>;
}
```

2. `src/stores/promptStore.ts` (Prompt Manager Store)

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';
import { PromptSession, PromptNote, PromptFile, PromptFolder, PromptManagerState } from '@/types/prompt';
import { openDB } from 'idb';

interface PromptStore extends PromptManagerState {
  // Session management
  createSession: (name: string) => PromptSession;
  loadSession: (id: string) => void;
  saveSession: () => Promise<void>;
  deleteSession: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  duplicateSession: (id: string) => PromptSession;
  renameSession: (id: string, newName: string) => void;
  
  // Prompt operations
  updatePromptText: (text: string) => void;
  
  // Note operations
  addNote: (title: string, content: string) => void;
  updateNote: (id: string, updates: Partial<PromptNote>) => void;
  deleteNote: (id: string) => void;
  toggleNoteAttachment: (id: string) => void;
  
  // File operations
  addFile: (file: Omit<PromptFile, 'id'>, folderPath?: string) => void;
  moveFile: (fileId: string, newFolderPath: string) => void;
  renameFile: (fileId: string, newName: string) => void;
  deleteFile: (fileId: string) => void;
  createFolder: (name: string, parentPath: string) => void;
  renameFolder: (folderId: string, newName: string) => void;
  deleteFolder: (folderId: string) => void;
  compressFile: (fileId: string, profileId: string) => void;
  
  // Drag-drop from main app
  addDragDropFile: (fileData: any, sourcePanelId: string) => void;
  
  // Upload
  completeAndUpload: () => Promise<{ shareLink: string }>;
  setUploadProvider: (provider: 'drive' | 'github') => void;
  
  // UI
  openPromptManager: () => void;
  closePromptManager: () => void;
  togglePromptManager: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getSessionFiles: () => PromptFile[];
  getFolderStructure: () => PromptFolder;
  getTotalSize: () => number;
  getAttachedNotes: () => PromptNote[];
}

const DB_NAME = 'prompt-manager-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

const createDefaultFolder = (): PromptFolder => ({
  id: 'root',
  name: 'root',
  path: '/',
  children: [],
});

const createEmptySession = (name: string): PromptSession => ({
  id: `session-${uuidv4()}`,
  name,
  createdAt: new Date(),
  updatedAt: new Date(),
  promptText: '',
  notes: [],
  files: [],
  folderStructure: createDefaultFolder(),
  isCompleted: false,
});

export const usePromptStore = create<PromptStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    sessions: [],
    currentSession: null,
    isPromptManagerOpen: false,
    selectedUploadProvider: 'drive',
    isUploading: false,
    uploadProgress: 0,

    // Session management
    createSession: (name) => {
      const session = createEmptySession(name);
      set((state) => {
        state.sessions.push(session);
        state.currentSession = session;
      });
      return session;
    },

    loadSession: (id) => {
      const session = get().sessions.find(s => s.id === id);
      if (session) {
        set((state) => {
          state.currentSession = session;
        });
      }
    },

    saveSession: async () => {
      const { currentSession } = get();
      if (!currentSession) return;

      currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();

      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      await db.put('sessions', currentSession);

      set((state) => {
        const index = state.sessions.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSession.id);
        if (index >= 0) {
          state.sessions[index] = currentSession;
        }
      });
    },

    deleteSession: async (id) => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      await db.delete('sessions', id);

      set((state) => {
        state.sessions = state.sessions.filter(s => s.id !== id);
        if (state.currentSession?.id === id) {
          state.currentSession = null;
        }
      });
    },

    duplicateSession: (id) => {
      const original = get().sessions.find(s => s.id === id);
      if (!original) throw new Error('Session not found');

      const copy: PromptSession = {
        ...original,
        id: `session-${uuidv4()}`,
        name: `${original.name} (Copy)`,
        createdAt: new Date(),
        updatedAt: new Date(),
        isCompleted: false,
        uploadResult: undefined,
      };

      set((state) => {
        state.sessions.push(copy);
      });

      return copy;
    },

    renameSession: (id, newName) => {
      set((state) => {
        const session = state.sessions.find(s => s.id === id);
        if (session) {
          session.name = newName;
          session.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    // Prompt operations
    updatePromptText: (text) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.promptText = text;
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    // Note operations
    addNote: (title, content) => {
      const note: PromptNote = {
        id: `note-${uuidv4()}`,
        title,
        content,
        createdAt: new Date(),
        attachedToLink: false,
      };

      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.notes.push(note);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    updateNote: (id, updates) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const note = state.currentSession.notes.find(n => n.id === id);
          if (note) {
            Object.assign(note, updates);
            state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
          }
        }
      });
    },

    deleteNote: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.notes = state.currentSession.notes.filter(n => n.id !== id);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    toggleNoteAttachment: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const note = state.currentSession.notes.find(n => n.id === id);
          if (note) {
            note.attachedToLink = !note.attachedToLink;
          }
        }
      });
    },

    // File operations
    addFile: (fileData, folderPath = '/') => {
      const file: PromptFile = {
        id: `file-${uuidv4()}`,
        ...fileData,
        folderPath,
      };

      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.files.push(file);
          addFileToFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, file, folderPath);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    moveFile: (fileId, newFolderPath) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const file = state.currentSession.files.find(f => f.id === fileId);
          if (file) {
            // Remove from old location
            removeFromFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, fileId);
            // Add to new location
            file.folderPath = newFolderPath;
            addFileToFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, file, newFolderPath);
            state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
          }
        }
      });
    },

    renameFile: (fileId, newName) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const file = state.currentSession.files.find(f => f.id === fileId);
          if (file) {
            file.name = newName;
            updateInFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, fileId, { name: newName });
            state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
          }
        }
      });
    },

    deleteFile: (fileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.files = state.currentSession.files.filter(f => f.id !== fileId);
          removeFromFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, fileId);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    createFolder: (name, parentPath) => {
      const folder: PromptFolder = {
        id: `folder-${uuidv4()}`,
        name,
        path: `${parentPath === '/' ? '' : parentPath}/${name}`,
        children: [],
      };

      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          addFolderToFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, folder, parentPath);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    renameFolder: (folderId, newName) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          updateFolderInFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, folderId, { name: newName });
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    deleteFolder: (folderId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          // Remove files in folder
          const folderPath = getFolderPath(state.currentSession.folderStructure, folderId);
          if (folderPath) {
            state.currentSession.files = state.currentSession.files.filter(f => !f.folderPath.startsWith(folderPath));
          }
          removeFolderFromFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, folderId);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    compressFile: (fileId, profileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const file = state.currentSession.files.find(f => f.id === fileId);
          if (file) {
            file.isCompressed = true;
            file.compressionProfile = profileId;
            state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
          }
        }
      });
    },

    // Drag-drop from main app
    addDragDropFile: (fileData, sourcePanelId) => {
      const file: PromptFile = {
        id: `file-${uuidv4()}`,
        name: fileData.name,
        size: fileData.size,
        type: fileData.type || 'application/octet-stream',
        source: 'drag-drop',
        sourcePath: fileData.path,
        sourcePanelId,
        folderPath: '/',
        isCompressed: false,
      };

      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.files.push(file);
          addFileToFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, file, '/');
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    // Upload
    completeAndUpload: async () => {
      const { currentSession, selectedUploadProvider } = get();
      if (!currentSession) throw new Error('No active session');

      set((state) => {
        state.isUploading = true;
        state.uploadProgress = 0;
      });

      try {
        // Generate upload structure
        const uploadData = await prepareUploadData(currentSession);
        
        // Upload to selected provider
        let result;
        if (selectedUploadProvider === 'drive') {
          result = await uploadToDrive(uploadData, currentSession.name, (progress) => {
            set((state) => { state.uploadProgress = progress; });
          });
        } else {
          result = await uploadToGitHub(uploadData, currentSession.name, (progress) => {
            set((state) => { state.uploadProgress = progress; });
          });
        }

        // Update session
        set((state) => {
          if (state.currentSession) {
            state.currentSession.isCompleted = true;
            state.currentSession.uploadResult = {
              provider: selectedUploadProvider,
              folderPath: result.folderPath,
              shareLink: result.shareLink,
              rawLink: result.rawLink,
              uploadedAt: new Date(),
            };
          }
          state.isUploading = false;
        });

        return { shareLink: result.shareLink };
      } catch (error) {
        set((state) => {
          state.isUploading = false;
        });
        throw error;
      }
    },

    setUploadProvider: (provider) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedUploadProvider = provider;
      });
    },

    // UI
    openPromptManager: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isPromptManagerOpen = true;
        if (!state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession = createEmptySession('Untitled Session');
          state.sessions.push(state.currentSession);
        }
      });
    },

    closePromptManager: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isPromptManagerOpen = false;
      });
    },

    togglePromptManager: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isPromptManagerOpen = !state.isPromptManagerOpen;
        if (state.isPromptManagerOpen && !state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession = createEmptySession('Untitled Session');
          state.sessions.push(state.currentSession);
        }
      });
    },

    // Getters
    getSessionFiles: () => get().currentSession?.files || [],
    getFolderStructure: () => get().currentSession?.folderStructure || createDefaultFolder(),
    getTotalSize: () => {
      return get().currentSession?.files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size, 0) || 0;
    },
    getAttachedNotes: () => {
      return get().currentSession?.notes.filter(n => n.attachedToLink) || [];
    },
  }))
);

// Helper functions for folder operations
function addFileToFolder(root: PromptFolder, file: PromptFile, path: string) {
  if (path === '/' || path === '') {
    root.children.push(file);
    return;
  }

  const parts = path.split('/').filter(Boolean);
  let current = root;

  for (const part of parts) {
    const folder = current.children.find(c => 'children' in c && c.name === part) as PromptFolder;
    if (folder) {
      current = folder;
    }
  }

  current.children.push(file);
}

function addFolderToFolder(root: PromptFolder, folder: PromptFolder, parentPath: string) {
  if (parentPath === '/' || parentPath === '') {
    root.children.push(folder);
    return;
  }

  const parts = parentPath.split('/').filter(Boolean);
  let current = root;

  for (const part of parts) {
    const found = current.children.find(c => 'children' in c && c.name === part) as PromptFolder;
    if (found) {
      current = found;
    }
  }

  current.children.push(folder);
}

function removeFromFolder(root: PromptFolder, fileId: string): boolean {
  const index = root.children.findIndex(c => !('children' in c) && c.id === fileId);
  if (index >= 0) {
    root.children.splice(index, 1);
    return true;
  }

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      if (removeFromFolder(child, fileId)) return true;
    }
  }

  return false;
}

function removeFolderFromFolder(root: PromptFolder, folderId: string): boolean {
  const index = root.children.findIndex(c => 'children' in c && c.id === folderId);
  if (index >= 0) {
    root.children.splice(index, 1);
    return true;
  }

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      if (removeFolderFromFolder(child, folderId)) return true;
    }
  }

  return false;
}

function updateInFolder(root: PromptFolder, fileId: string, updates: Partial<PromptFile>) {
  const file = root.children.find(c => !('children' in c) && c.id === fileId) as PromptFile;
  if (file) {
    Object.assign(file, updates);
    return;
  }

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      updateInFolder(child, fileId, updates);
    }
  }
}

function updateFolderInFolder(root: PromptFolder, folderId: string, updates: Partial<PromptFolder>) {
  const folder = root.children.find(c => 'children' in c && c.id === folderId) as PromptFolder;
  if (folder) {
    Object.assign(folder, updates);
    return;
  }

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      updateFolderInFolder(child, folderId, updates);
    }
  }
}

function getFolderPath(root: PromptFolder, folderId: string): string | null {
  if (root.id === folderId) return root.path;

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      const found = getFolderPath(child, folderId);
      if (found) return found;
    }
  }

  return null;
}

async function prepareUploadData(session: PromptSession): Promise<FormData> {
  const formData = new FormData();

  // Add prompt.txt
  const promptBlob = new Blob([session.promptText], { type: 'text/plain' });
  formData.append('prompt.txt', promptBlob, 'prompt.txt');

  // Add links.txt with notes
  const linksContent = generateLinksContent(session);
  const linksBlob = new Blob([linksContent], { type: 'text/plain' });
  formData.append('links.txt', linksBlob, 'links.txt');

  // Add files
  for (const file of session.files) {
    if (file.content) {
      formData.append(file.name, file.content, file.name);
    } else {
      // Placeholder for referenced files
      const placeholder = new Blob([`Reference: ${file.sourcePath || file.name}`], { type: 'text/plain' });
      formData.append(file.name, placeholder, file.name);
    }
  }

  return formData;
}

function generateLinksContent(session: PromptSession): string {
  let content = `Session: ${session.name}\n`;
  content += `Created: ${session.createdAt.toISOString()}\n`;
  content += `Files: ${session.files.length}\n\n`;
  
  content += `Attached Notes:\n`;
  for (const note of session.notes.filter(n => n.attachedToLink)) {
    content += `\n--- ${note.title} ---\n`;
    content += `${note.content}\n`;
  }

  content += `\nFile List:\n`;
  for (const file of session.files) {
    content += `- ${file.name} (${file.size} bytes) [${file.source}]\n`;
  }

  return content;
}

async function uploadToDrive(
  data: FormData, 
  sessionName: string,
  onProgress: (progress: number) => void
): Promise<{ folderPath: string; shareLink: string; rawLink?: string }> {
  // Implementation using Google Drive API
  // Create folder: Pro-MNT/SessionName/
  // Upload all files
  // Set permissions and get share link
  
  onProgress(50);
  
  // Mock implementation
  return {
    folderPath: `Pro-MNT/${sessionName}`,
    shareLink: `https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/mock-folder-id`,
  };
}

async function uploadToGitHub(
  data: FormData,
  sessionName: string,
  onProgress: (progress: number) => void
): Promise<{ folderPath: string; shareLink: string; rawLink: string }> {
  // Implementation using GitHub API
  // Create repo or use existing
  // Upload files to Pro-MNT/SessionName/
  
  onProgress(50);
  
  // Mock implementation
  const path = `Pro-MNT/${sessionName}`;
  return {
    folderPath: path,
    shareLink: `https://github.com/user/repo/tree/main/${path}`,
    rawLink: `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/user/repo/main/${path}/prompt.txt`,
  };
}
```

```typescript
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
```
