4. `src/components/PromptManager/PromptFileManager.tsx` (File Manager Panel)

```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';
import { usePromptStore, usePromptFolderStructure, usePromptSessionFiles } from '@/stores/promptStore';
import { Folder, File, Plus, Trash2, Edit2, Archive, MoreVertical, ChevronRight, ChevronDown } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { PromptFile, PromptFolder } from '@/types/prompt';

export function PromptFileManager() {
  const folderStructure = usePromptFolderStructure();
  const files = usePromptSessionFiles();
  const createFolder = usePromptStore((s) => s.createFolder);
  const renameFolder = usePromptStore((s) => s.renameFolder);
  const deleteFolder = usePromptStore((s) => s.deleteFolder);
  const addFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.addFile);
  const renameFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.renameFile);
  const deleteFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.deleteFile);
  const compressFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.compressFile);

  const [expandedFolders, setExpandedFolders] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set(['root']));
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [renamingId, setRenamingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [newName, setNewName] = useState('');

  const toggleFolder = (folderId: string) => {
    const newExpanded = new Set(expandedFolders);
    if (newExpanded.has(folderId)) {
      newExpanded.delete(folderId);
    } else {
      newExpanded.add(folderId);
    }
    setExpandedFolders(newExpanded);
  };

  const handleCreateFolder = () => {
    const name = prompt('Folder name:');
    if (name) {
      createFolder(name, '/');
    }
  };

  const handleUpload = () => {
    const input = document.createElement('input');
    input.type = 'file';
    input.multiple = true;
    input.onchange = (e) => {
      const files = (e.target as HTMLInputElement).files;
      if (files) {
        Array.from(files).forEach(file => {
          addFile({
            name: file.name,
            size: file.size,
            type: file.type,
            source: 'upload',
            folderPath: '/',
            isCompressed: false,
            content: file,
          });
        });
      }
    };
    input.click();
  };

  const startRename = (item: PromptFile | PromptFolder) => {
    setRenamingId(item.id);
    setNewName(item.name);
  };

  const confirmRename = () => {
    if (renamingId && newName) {
      const isFolder = 'children' in (files.find(f => f.id === renamingId) || {});
      if (isFolder) {
        renameFolder(renamingId, newName);
      } else {
        renameFile(renamingId, newName);
      }
    }
    setRenamingId(null);
    setNewName('');
  };

  const renderItem = (item: PromptFile | PromptFolder, depth = 0) => {
    const isFolder = 'children' in item;
    const isExpanded = expandedFolders.has(item.id);
    const isSelected = selectedItem === item.id;
    const isRenaming = renamingId === item.id;

    return (
      <div key={item.id}>
        <div
          className={cn(
            "flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 hover:bg-accent cursor-pointer group",
            isSelected && "bg-accent",
            depth > 0 && "border-l border-border ml-3"
          )}
          style={{ paddingLeft: `${12 + depth * 16}px` }}
          onClick={() => setSelectedItem(item.id)}
        >
          {isFolder && (
            <button
              onClick={(e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                toggleFolder(item.id);
              }}
              className="p-0.5 hover:bg-accent rounded"
            >
              {isExpanded ? (
                <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
              ) : (
                <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
              )}
            </button>
          )}
          
          {!isFolder && <span className="w-5" />}
          
          {isFolder ? (
            <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
          ) : (
            <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
          )}
          
          {isRenaming ? (
            <input
              type="text"
              value={newName}
              onChange={(e) => setNewName(e.target.value)}
              onBlur={confirmRename}
              onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && confirmRename()}
              className="flex-1 px-2 py-0.5 text-sm border rounded bg-background"
              autoFocus
            />
          ) : (
            <span className="flex-1 text-sm truncate">{item.name}</span>
          )}
          
          {!isFolder && (item as PromptFile).isCompressed && (
            <Archive className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
          )}
          
          {/* Actions */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100">
            <Button
              variant="ghost"
              size="icon"
              className="h-6 w-6"
              onClick={(e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                startRename(item);
              }}
            >
              <Edit2 className="w-3 h-3" />
            </Button>
            
            <Button
              variant="ghost"
              size="icon"
              className="h-6 w-6"
              onClick
Kimi: ={(e) => {
e.stopPropagation();
if (isFolder) {
deleteFolder(item.id);
} else {
deleteFile(item.id);
}
}}
>

        {isFolder && isExpanded && (
          <div>
            {(item as PromptFolder).children.map(child => 
              renderItem(child, depth + 1)
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );

};

return (

{/ Toolbar /}

Folder

Upload

      {/* File Tree */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {renderItem(folderStructure)}
      </div>

      {/* Status */}
      <div className="p-2 border-t border-border text-xs text-muted-foreground">
        {files.length} files • {formatBytes(files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size, 0))}
      </div>
    </div>

);
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
if (bytes === 0) return '0 B';
const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
let size = bytes;
let unitIndex = 0;
while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
size /= 1024;
unitIndex++;
}
return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

```

### 5. `src/components/PromptManager/PromptWritingArea.tsx` (Writing Area)
```typescript
import { usePromptStore, usePromptCurrentSession } from '@/stores/promptStore';
import { Textarea } from '@/components/ui/textarea';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { FileText, Clock, Hash } from 'lucide-react';

export function PromptWritingArea() {
  const currentSession = usePromptCurrentSession();
  const updatePromptText = usePromptStore((s) => s.updatePromptText);
  
  if (!currentSession) {
    return (
      <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground">
        <p>No active session</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const wordCount = currentSession.promptText.trim().split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean).length;
  const charCount = currentSession.promptText.length;

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
      {/* Stats Bar */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-4 px-4 py-2 border-b border-border bg-muted/50">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          <FileText className="w-3 h-3" />
          {wordCount} words
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          <Hash className="w-3 h-3" />
          {charCount} chars
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
          {new Date(currentSession.updatedAt).toLocaleTimeString()}
        </div>
        {currentSession.isCompleted && (
          <Badge variant="success" className="ml-auto">Completed</Badge>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Text Area */}
      <ScrollArea className="flex-1">
        <Textarea
          value={currentSession.promptText}
          onChange={(e) => updatePromptText(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Start writing your prompt here..."
          className="w-full h-full min-h-[500px] resize-none border-0 rounded-none focus-visible:ring-0 text-base leading-relaxed p-4 font-mono"
        />
      </ScrollArea>
    </div>
  );
}

6. `src/components/PromptManager/PromptSessionList.tsx` (Session List Panel)

```typescript
// src/components/PromptManager/PromptSessionList.tsx
import { usePromptStore, usePromptSessions, usePromptCurrentSession } from '@/stores/promptStore';
import { Clock, Copy, Trash2, Edit2, ExternalLink, FolderOpen } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';

export function PromptSessionList() {
  const sessions = usePromptSessions();
  const currentSession = usePromptCurrentSession();
  const loadSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.loadSession);
  const deleteSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.deleteSession);
  const duplicateSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.duplicateSession);
  const renameSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.renameSession);

  const handleRename = (id: string, currentName: string) => {
    const newName = prompt('New session name:', currentName);
    if (newName && newName.trim()) {
      renameSession(id, newName.trim());
    }
  };

  const handleOpenInDrive = (session: any) => {
    if (session.uploadResult?.shareLink) {
      window.open(session.uploadResult.shareLink, '_blank');
    } else {
      alert('Session not uploaded yet');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
      <div className="p-3 border-b border-border">
        <h3 className="font-medium text-sm">All Sessions</h3>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          {sessions.length} session{sessions.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''} saved
        </p>
      </div>

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-2 space-y-1">
        {sessions.length === 0 ? (
          <p className="text-center text-muted-foreground text-sm py-8">
            No sessions yet. Create one from the File Manager tab.
          </p>
        ) : (
          sessions.map((session) => {
            const isActive = currentSession?.id === session.id;
            return (
              <div
                key={session.id}
                className={cn(
                  "group flex items-center justify-between p-2 rounded-lg cursor-pointer transition-colors",
                  isActive ? "bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20" : "hover:bg-accent"
                )}
                onClick={() => loadSession(session.id)}
              >
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <FolderOpen className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
                    <span className="font-medium text-sm truncate">{session.name}</span>
                    {session.isCompleted && (
                      <span className="text-[10px] bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full">
                        Done
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-0.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                    <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                      <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
                      {formatDistanceToNow(session.updatedAt, { addSuffix: true })}
                    </span>
                    <span>{session.files.length} files</span>
                    <span>{session.notes.length} notes</span>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Actions */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-7 w-7"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      const newSession = duplicateSession(session.id);
                      loadSession(newSession.id);
                    }}
                    title="Duplicate"
                  >
                    <Copy className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                  </Button>
                  
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-7 w-7"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      handleRename(session.id, session.name);
                    }}
                    title="Rename"
                  >
                    <Edit2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                  </Button>
                  
                  {session.uploadResult && (
                    <Button
                      variant="ghost"
                      size="icon"
                      className="h-7 w-7"
                      onClick={(e) => {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        handleOpenInDrive(session);
                      }}
                      title="Open in Drive/GitHub"
                    >
                      <ExternalLink className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                    </Button>
                  )}
                  
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-7 w-7 text-destructive hover:text-destructive"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      if (confirm(`Delete session "${session.name}"?`)) {
                        deleteSession(session.id);
                      }
                    }}
                    title="Delete"
                  >
                    <Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            );
          })
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

We'll refactor the file system state to be per-panel, eliminating the global store and enabling parallel browsing.

## 1. Updated Panel Types (`src/types/panel.ts`)

Add file‑system specific fields to `PanelState`:

```typescript
// src/types/panel.ts (partial)
export interface PanelState {
  id: string;
  source: SourceType;
  // Storage‑specific state (was global)
  handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null;
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  path: string;
  history: { handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle; name: string }[];
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  viewMode: ViewMode;
  sortBy: SortBy;
  // ... other fields (accountId, width, isMinimized, isMaximized)

## 2. Refactored PanelStore (`src/stores/panelStore.ts`)

Integrate file system actions, each requiring `panelId`.

```typescript
// src/stores/panelStore.ts (excerpt)
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { PanelState, createDefaultPanel, MIN_PANEL_WIDTH, MAX_PANELS } from '@/types/panel';
import { SourceType } from './appStore';
import { ViewMode, SortBy, FileSystemEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';

interface PanelStore {
  panels: PanelState[];
  activePanelId: string | null;
  
  // Panel management
  addPanel: () => void;
  removePanel: (id: string) => void;
  setActivePanel: (id: string) => void;
  getPanel: (id: string) => PanelState | undefined;
  
  // File system actions (per panel)
  readDirectory: (panelId: string) => Promise<void>;
  navigateTo: (panelId: string, entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: (panelId: string) => Promise<void>;
  createFolder: (panelId: string, name: string) => Promise<void>;
  pickDirectory: (panelId: string) => Promise<void>;
  
  // UI actions
  setPanelViewMode: (panelId: string, mode: ViewMode) => void;
  setPanelSortBy: (panelId: string, sort: SortBy) => void;
  setPanelWidth: (panelId: string, width: number) => void;
  togglePanelMinimize: (panelId: string) => void;
  setPanelSource: (panelId: string, source: SourceType) => void;
}

export const usePanelStore = create<PanelStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    panels: [
      createDefaultPanel('panel-1', 0),
      createDefaultPanel('panel-2', 1),
    ],
    activePanelId: 'panel-1',

    // ... existing panel management methods ...

    // ---- FILE SYSTEM ACTIONS ----
    readDirectory: async (panelId) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel?.handle) return;
      
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.isLoading = true;
          p.error = null;
        }
      });
      
      try {
        const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.entries = entries;
            p.isLoading = false;
          }
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.error = (err as Error).message;
            p.isLoading = false;
          }
        });
      }
    },

    navigateTo: async (panelId, entry) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel?.handle || entry.kind !== 'directory') return;
      
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.history.push({ handle: p.handle, name: p.path.split('/').pop() || 'root' });
          p.handle = entry.handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle;
          p.path = `${p.path}/${entry.name}`.replace('//', '/');
          p.isLoading = true;
          p.error = null;
        }
      });
      
      await get().readDirectory(panelId);
    },

    navigateBack: async (panelId) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel || panel.history.length === 0) return;
      
      const previous = panel.history.pop()!;
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.handle = previous.handle;
          p.path = panel.history.length === 0 ? '/' : `/${previous.name}`;
          p.isLoading = true;
          p.error = null;
        }
      });
      
      await get().readDirectory(panelId);
    },

    createFolder: async (panelId, name) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel?.handle) return;
      
      try {
        await fileSystemBackend.createDirectory(panel.handle, name);
        await get().readDirectory(panelId);
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) p.error = (err as Error).message;
        });
      }
    },

    pickDirectory: async (panelId) => {
      const handle = await fileSystemBackend.pickDirectory();
      if (!handle) return;
      
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.handle = handle;
          p.path = `/${handle.name}`;
          p.history = [];
          p.entries = [];
        }
      });
      await get().readDirectory(panelId);
    },

    // ---- UI actions (already present, keep as is) ----
    setPanelViewMode: (panelId, mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) p.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },
    setPanelSortBy: (panelId, sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) p.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },
    // ... other setters ...
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const usePanel = (panelId: string) => usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(panelId));
export const usePanelEntries = (panelId: string) => usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(panelId)?.entries ?? []);
export const usePanelIsLoading = (panelId: string) => usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(panelId)?.isLoading ?? false);
export const usePanelPath = (panelId: string) => usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(panelId)?.path ?? '/');
export const usePanelCanGoBack = (panelId: string) => {
  const panel = usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(panelId));
  return (panel?.history.length ?? 0) > 0;
};
```

## 3. Updated FileManager Component (`src/components/FileManager/index.tsx`)

Now accepts `panelId` and uses panel‑scoped store methods.

```typescript
// src/components/FileManager/index.tsx
import { useState } from 'react';
import { usePanelStore, usePanelEntries, usePanelIsLoading, usePanelPath, usePanelCanGoBack, usePanel } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { Toolbar } from './Toolbar';
import { FileGrid } from './FileGrid';
import { FileList } from './FileList';
import { CreateFolderDialog } from './CreateFolderDialog';
import { MountPointsView } from './MountPointsView';

interface FileManagerProps {
  panelId: string;
}

export function FileManager({ panelId }: FileManagerProps) {
  const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  
  const panel = usePanel(panelId);
  const entries = usePanelEntries(panelId);
  const isLoading = usePanelIsLoading(panelId);
  const currentPath = usePanelPath(panelId);
  const canGoBack = usePanelCanGoBack(panelId);
  
  const { readDirectory, navigateTo, navigateBack, createFolder, pickDirectory, setPanelViewMode, setPanelSortBy } = usePanelStore();
  
  const handleNavigateTo = (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => {
    navigateTo(panelId, entry);
  };
  
  const handleNavigateBack = () => {
    navigateBack(panelId);
  };
  
  const handleRefresh = () => {
    readDirectory(panelId);
  };
  
  const handleCreateFolder = async (name: string) => {
    await createFolder(panelId, name);
  };
  
  // Sort entries (client side)
  const getSortedEntries = () => {
    const sorted = [...entries];
    switch (panel?.sortBy) {
      case 'name-asc': return sorted.sort((a,b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
      case 'name-desc': return sorted.sort((a,b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
      case 'date': return sorted.sort((a,b) => b.lastModified.getTime() - a.lastModified.getTime());
      case 'size': return sorted.sort((a,b) => b.size - a.size);
      default: return sorted;
    }
  };
  
  // If no directory selected, show mount points
  if (!panel?.handle) {
    return <MountPointsView onSelectMount={() => pickDirectory(panelId)} />;
  }
  
  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <Toolbar
        viewMode={panel.viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={(mode) => setPanelViewMode(panelId, mode)}
        sortBy={panel.sortBy}
        onSortChange={(sort) => setPanelSortBy(panelId, sort)}
        onCreateFolder={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}
        onNavigateBack={handleNavigateBack}
        onRefresh={handleRefresh}
        canGoBack={canGoBack}
        isLoading={isLoading}
        currentPath={currentPath}
      />
      
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {entries.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p className="text-sm">Empty folder</p>
            <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="mt-2" onClick={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}>
              Create folder
            </Button>
          </div>
        ) : panel.viewMode === 'grid' ? (
          <FileGrid entries={getSortedEntries()} onNavigate={handleNavigateTo} panelId={panelId} />
        ) : (
          <FileList entries={getSortedEntries()} onNavigate={handleNavigateTo} panelId={panelId} />
        )}
      </div>
      
      <CreateFolderDialog
        open={createDialogOpen}
        onOpenChange={setCreateDialogOpen}
        panelId={panelId}
        onCreate={handleCreateFolder}
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

## 6. Remove global `fileSystemStore.ts`

Delete `src/stores/fileSystemStore.ts` entirely – its state is now inside `panelStore`.

## 7. Update hooks and dependent components

- `useDragDrop` – no longer uses global fileSystemStore; relies on panelId for operations.
- `CreateFolderDialog` – now receives `panelId` and calls `createFolder(panelId, name)`.
- `MountPointsView` – receives `onSelectMount` callback that calls `pickDirectory(panelId)`.

## 8. Benefits of refactoring

- Each panel maintains its own `handle`, `entries`, `history`, `path`, `isLoading`, `error`.
- Panels can browse different folders simultaneously without conflict.
- Operations are explicitly scoped to a panel, improving predictability.
- Global `fileSystemStore` removed, reducing complexity.

This refactor makes the file system truly per‑panel and enables parallel browsing.

=======2=========

We'll implement a production‑grade multi‑panel container with draggable resizer bars. The system ensures total width constant, respects minimum panel width, and provides smooth UX.

## 1. Resizer Component

```tsx
// src/components/Panel/Resizer.tsx
import { useState, useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { MIN_PANEL_WIDTH } from '@/types/panel';

interface ResizerProps {
  leftPanelId: string;
  rightPanelId: string;
}

export function Resizer({ leftPanelId, rightPanelId }: ResizerProps) {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const startX = useRef(0);
  const startLeftWidth = useRef(0);
  const startRightWidth = useRef(0);
  
  const leftPanel = usePanelStore((state) => state.getPanel(leftPanelId));
  const rightPanel = usePanelStore((state) => state.getPanel(rightPanelId));
  const setPanelWidth = usePanelStore((state) => state.setPanelWidth);
  
  const handleMouseDown = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsDragging(true);
    startX.current = e.clientX;
    startLeftWidth.current = leftPanel?.width ?? MIN_PANEL_WIDTH;
    startRightWidth.current = rightPanel?.width ?? MIN_PANEL_WIDTH;
    
    document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
    document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
  }, [leftPanel, rightPanel]);
  
  const handleMouseMove = useCallback((e: MouseEvent) => {
    if (!isDragging) return;
    
    const delta = e.clientX - startX.current;
    let newLeftWidth = startLeftWidth.current + delta;
    let newRightWidth = startRightWidth.current - delta;
    
    // Enforce minimum width
    if (newLeftWidth < MIN_PANEL_WIDTH) {
      const deficit = MIN_PANEL_WIDTH - newLeftWidth;
      newLeftWidth = MIN_PANEL_WIDTH;
      newRightWidth = startRightWidth.current - (delta - deficit);
    }
    if (newRightWidth < MIN_PANEL_WIDTH) {
      const deficit = MIN_PANEL_WIDTH - newRightWidth;
      newRightWidth = MIN_PANEL_WIDTH;
      newLeftWidth = startLeftWidth.current + (delta + deficit);
    }
    
    // Apply new widths
    setPanelWidth(leftPanelId, newLeftWidth);
    setPanelWidth(rightPanelId, newRightWidth);
  }, [isDragging, leftPanelId, rightPanelId, setPanelWidth]);
  
  const handleMouseUp = useCallback(() => {
    setIsDragging(false);
    document.body.style.cursor = '';
    document.body.style.userSelect = '';
  }, []);
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      return () => {
        window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
        window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      };
    }
  }, [isDragging, handleMouseMove, handleMouseUp]);
  
  return (
    <div
      className="w-1 cursor-col-resize bg-border hover:bg-primary/50 transition-colors shrink-0"
      onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}
    />
  );
}
```

## 2. Updated PanelContainer with Resizers

```tsx
// src/components/PanelContainer.tsx
import { Plus } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { usePanelStore, usePanels, useActivePanelId, usePanelCount } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { ResizablePanel } from './Panel/ResizablePanel';
import { Resizer } from './Panel/Resizer';
import { MAX_PANELS } from '@/types/panel';

export function PanelContainer() {
  const panels = usePanels();
  const activePanelId = useActivePanelId();
  const panelCount = usePanelCount();
  const { addPanel, removePanel, setActivePanel } = usePanelStore();
  
  const canAddPanel = panelCount < MAX_PANELS;
  
  return (
    <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden bg-background">
      {/* Top bar with Add Panel button */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b border-border bg-card">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">
            Panels: {panelCount}/{MAX_PANELS}
          </span>
        </div>
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          onClick={addPanel}
          disabled={!canAddPanel}
          className="gap-2"
        >
          <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
          Add Panel
        </Button>
      </div>
      
      {/* Panels container with resizers */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-x-auto overflow-y-hidden">
        {panels.map((panel, index) => (
          <React.Fragment key={panel.id}>
            <ResizablePanel
              panel={panel}
              isActive={panel.id === activePanelId}
              onActivate={() => setActivePanel(panel.id)}
              onClose={() => removePanel(panel.id)}
            />
            {index < panels.length - 1 && (
              <Resizer leftPanelId={panel.id} rightPanelId={panels[index + 1].id} />
            )}
          </React.Fragment>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## 3. Update ResizablePanel (simplified, remove internal resize)

Since resizing is handled by the external Resizer, we can remove the old `useResizable` from `ResizablePanel`. Keep only the panel display logic:

```tsx
// src/components/Panel/ResizablePanel.tsx (simplified)
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { PanelHeader } from './PanelHeader';
import { PanelContent } from './PanelContent';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { MIN_PANEL_WIDTH } from '@/types/panel';

interface ResizablePanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  isActive: boolean;
  onActivate: () => void;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export function ResizablePanel({ panel, isActive, onActivate, onClose }: ResizablePanelProps) {
  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'flex flex-col h-full relative border-r border-border last:border-r-0',
        isActive && 'ring-1 ring-primary/20'
      )}
      style={{ 
        width: panel.isMinimized ? 60 : panel.width,
        minWidth: panel.isMinimized ? 60 : MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
        flexShrink: 0,
      }}
    >
      <PanelHeader
        panel={panel}
        isActive={isActive}
        onActivate={onActivate}
        onClose={onClose}
      />
      
      {!panel.isMinimized && (
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
          <PanelContent panel={panel} />
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

## 4. PanelStore width management (already present)

```typescript
setPanelWidth: (id, width) => {
  set((state) => {
    const panel = state.panels.find(p => p.id === id);
    if (panel) {
      panel.width = Math.max(MIN_PANEL_WIDTH, width);
    }
  });
}
```

## 5. Default panel width in `createDefaultPanel`

export const createDefaultPanel = (id: string, index: number): PanelState => ({
  id,
  source: index === 0 ? 'storage' : 'drive',

## 6. CSS for smooth resizing (optional)

Add to global CSS for smoother transitions when dragging:

```css
/* In index.css */
.panel-resizing {
  transition: none !important;
}
```

But we don't use transitions on width to avoid lag. The resizer directly updates widths.

## 7. Performance considerations

- The Resizer updates the store on every `mousemove`. This causes re‑renders of both affected panels, but React is efficient enough for up to 4 panels.
- If needed, we could throttle with `requestAnimationFrame`, but not necessary for this scale.

This implementation gives a robust, production‑ready resizable multi‑panel layout with independent state per panel.

=======3==========
We'll add a caching layer inside `PanelStore` to store directory contents per panel. This eliminates redundant file system reads and improves navigation performance.

## 1. Update Panel Types to include cache

```typescript
// src/types/panel.ts
export interface PanelState {
  id: string;
  source: SourceType;
  // ... existing fields ...
  // Cache: Map where key is path (string) and value is entries array
  cache: Map<string, FileSystemEntry[]>;
}
```

## 2. Update `createDefaultPanel` to initialize cache

```typescript
// src/types/panel.ts (inside createDefaultPanel)
export const createDefaultPanel = (id: string, index: number): PanelState => ({
  // ... existing fields ...

});
```

## 3. Modify PanelStore – add cache logic

We'll update the file system actions to use the cache and provide a way to invalidate it.

```typescript
// src/stores/panelStore.ts (excerpt)
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';

interface PanelStore {
  // ... existing methods ...
  
  // Cache invalidation
  invalidateCache: (panelId: string, path?: string) => void;
}

export const usePanelStore = create<PanelStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // ... existing state ...
    
    readDirectory: async (panelId) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel?.handle) return;
      
      const currentPath = panel.path;
      const cached = panel.cache.get(currentPath);
      
      if (cached) {
        // Use cached data
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.entries = cached;
            p.isLoading = false;
          }
        });
        return;
      }
      
      // Not cached – fetch
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.isLoading = true;
          p.error = null;
        }
      });
      
      try {
        const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
        // Store in cache
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.cache.set(currentPath, entries);
            p.entries = entries;
            p.isLoading = false;
          }
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.error = (err as Error).message;
            p.isLoading = false;
          }
        });
      }
    },
    
    navigateTo: async (panelId, entry) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel?.handle || entry.kind !== 'directory') return;
      
      // Save current path to history and update handle/path
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.history.push({ handle: p.handle, name: p.path.split('/').pop() || 'root' });
          p.handle = entry.handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle;
          p.path = `${p.path}/${entry.name}`.replace('//', '/');
        }
      });
      
      // Read new directory (will use cache if available)
      await get().readDirectory(panelId);
    },
    
    navigateBack: async (panelId) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel || panel.history.length === 0) return;
      
      const previous = panel.history.pop()!;
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.handle = previous.handle;
          p.path = panel.history.length === 0 ? '/' : `/${previous.name}`;
        }
      });
      
      await get().readDirectory(panelId);
    },
    
    refreshCurrent: async (panelId) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel) return;
      
      // Invalidate cache for current path
      get().invalidateCache(panelId, panel.path);
      // Then read again
      await get().readDirectory(panelId);
    },
    
    invalidateCache: (panelId, path) => {
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          if (path) {
            p.cache.delete(path);
          } else {
            p.cache.clear();
          }
        }
      });
    },
    
    // After creating a folder, invalidate parent directory cache
    createFolder: async (panelId, name) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel?.handle) return;
      
      try {
        await fileSystemBackend.createDirectory(panel.handle, name);
        // Invalidate cache for current directory
        get().invalidateCache(panelId, panel.path);
        await get().readDirectory(panelId);
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) p.error = (err as Error).message;
        });
      }
    },
    
    // ... other actions (pickDirectory, setPanelViewMode, etc.) remain unchanged
  }))
);
```

## 4. Update FileManager Toolbar – refresh button uses `refreshCurrent`

```tsx
// Inside FileManager component
const handleRefresh = () => {
  refreshCurrent(panelId);
};
```

## 5. Optional: Lazy loading for large directories

We can add pagination support to `fileSystemBackend` and modify `readDirectory` to accept `limit` and `offset`. For now, we fetch all entries; the cache will still help. If needed, we can implement a virtualized list later.

## 6. Benefits of caching

- **Faster navigation**: Going back and forth between visited folders is instantaneous.
- **Reduced API calls**: Avoids repeated reads from the underlying file system (especially important for remote sources like Drive/GitHub).
- **Manual refresh** clears cache for the current folder, allowing updates.
- **Panel‑scoped**: Each panel maintains its own cache, so no cross‑panel interference.

This caching layer significantly improves performance, especially when navigating deep directory structures.

=======4==========
We'll refactor the panel state to preserve each source's independent state, enabling fast switching without data loss.

## 1. Updated Panel Types (`src/types/panel.ts`)

Define source‑specific state interfaces and a combined `PanelState`:

```typescript
// src/types/panel.ts
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';
import { ViewMode, SortBy, FileSystemEntry } from './filesystem';
import { DriveFile, DriveViewMode, DriveSortBy } from './drive';
import { GitHubRepository, GitHubContent, GitHubViewMode, GitHubSortBy } from './github';
import { TerminalFileSystemEntry, TerminalViewMode, TerminalSortBy } from './terminal';

// Storage source state
export interface StorageSourceState {
  handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null;
  path: string;
  history: { handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle; name: string }[];
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  viewMode: ViewMode;
  sortBy: SortBy;
  cache: Map<string, FileSystemEntry[]>;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
}

// Drive source state
export interface DriveSourceState {
  accountId: string | null;
  currentFolderId: string;
  currentPath: string; // breadcrumb path
  pathHistory: string[];
  files: DriveFile[];
  viewMode: DriveViewMode;
  sortBy: DriveSortBy;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
}

// GitHub source state
export interface GitHubSourceState {
  username: string | null;
  token: string | null;
  currentRepository: string | null;
  currentPath: string;
  pathHistory: string[];
  repositories: GitHubRepository[];
  contents: GitHubContent[];
  viewMode: GitHubViewMode;
  sortBy: GitHubSortBy;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
}

// Terminal source state
export interface TerminalSourceState {
  isInitialized: boolean;
  currentPath: string;
  pathHistory: string[];
  entries: TerminalFileSystemEntry[];
  viewMode: TerminalViewMode;
  sortBy: TerminalSortBy;
  cache: Map<string, TerminalFileSystemEntry[]>;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
}

// Combined sources object
export interface PanelSources {
  storage: StorageSourceState;
  drive: DriveSourceState;
  github: GitHubSourceState;
  terminal: TerminalSourceState;
}

export interface PanelState {
  id: string;
  activeSource: SourceType;
  sources: PanelSources;
  // UI state (shared across sources)
  width: number;
  isMinimized: boolean;
  isMaximized: boolean;
}

export const createDefaultStorageState = (): StorageSourceState => ({
  handle: null,
  path: '/',
  history: [],
  entries: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  cache: new Map(),
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
});

export const createDefaultDriveState = (): DriveSourceState => ({
  accountId: null,
  currentFolderId: 'root',
  currentPath: '',
  pathHistory: [],
  files: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
});

export const createDefaultGitHubState = (): GitHubSourceState => ({
  username: null,
  token: null,
  currentRepository: null,
  currentPath: '',
  pathHistory: [],
  repositories: [],
  contents: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'updated',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
});

export const createDefaultTerminalState = (): TerminalSourceState => ({
  isInitialized: false,
  currentPath: '/',
  pathHistory: [],
  entries: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  cache: new Map(),
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
});

export const createDefaultPanel = (id: string, index: number): PanelState => ({
  id,
  activeSource: index === 0 ? 'storage' : 'drive',
  sources: {
    storage: createDefaultStorageState(),
    drive: createDefaultDriveState(),
    github: createDefaultGitHubState(),
    terminal: createDefaultTerminalState(),
  },
  width: 400,
  isMinimized: false,
  isMaximized: false,
});

export const MIN_PANEL_WIDTH = 200;
export const MAX_PANELS = 4;
```

## 2. Refactored PanelStore (`src/stores/panelStore.ts`)

Update store to manage source‑specific state and provide switching logic:

```typescript
// src/stores/panelStore.ts (excerpt)
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { PanelState, createDefaultPanel, MIN_PANEL_WIDTH, MAX_PANELS } from '@/types/panel';
import { SourceType } from './appStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';
import { githubApi } from '@/lib/githubApi';
import { webcontainerApi } from '@/lib/webcontainerApi';

interface PanelStore {
  panels: PanelState[];
  activePanelId: string | null;
  
  // Panel management
  addPanel: () => void;
  removePanel: (id: string) => void;
  setActivePanel: (id: string) => void;
  getPanel: (id: string) => PanelState | undefined;
  
  // Source switching
  setPanelSource: (panelId: string, source: SourceType) => void;
  
  // Storage actions (scoped to panel + source)
  readStorageDirectory: (panelId: string) => Promise<void>;
  navigateStorage: (panelId: string, entry: any) => Promise<void>;
  navigateStorageBack: (panelId: string) => Promise<void>;
  pickStorageDirectory: (panelId: string) => Promise<void>;
  createStorageFolder: (panelId: string, name: string) => Promise<void>;
  refreshStorage: (panelId: string) => Promise<void>;
  setStorageViewMode: (panelId: string, mode: ViewMode) => void;
  setStorageSortBy: (panelId: string, sort: SortBy) => void;
  
  // Drive actions (similar pattern)
  // GitHub actions
  // Terminal actions
  
  // UI actions
  setPanelWidth: (panelId: string, width: number) => void;
  togglePanelMinimize: (panelId: string) => void;
}

export const usePanelStore = create<PanelStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    panels: [
      createDefaultPanel('panel-1', 0),
      createDefaultPanel('panel-2', 1),
    ],
    activePanelId: 'panel-1',

    // Panel management
    addPanel: () => { /* ... */ },
    removePanel: (id) => { /* ... */ },
    setActivePanel: (id) => { /* ... */ },
    getPanel: (id) => get().panels.find(p => p.id === id),

    // Source switching – preserves state for each source
    setPanelSource: (panelId, source) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (panel) {
          panel.activeSource = source;
        }
      });
    },

    // ---- Storage actions ----
    readStorageDirectory: async (panelId) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel) return;
      
      const storageState = panel.sources.storage;
      if (!storageState.handle) return;
      
      const currentPath = storageState.path;
      const cached = storageState.cache.get(currentPath);
      
      if (cached) {
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.sources.storage.entries = cached;
            p.sources.storage.isLoading = false;
          }
        });
        return;
      }
      
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.sources.storage.isLoading = true;
          p.sources.storage.error = null;
        }
      });
      
      try {
        const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(storageState.handle);
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.sources.storage.cache.set(currentPath, entries);
            p.sources.storage.entries = entries;
            p.sources.storage.isLoading = false;
          }
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.sources.storage.error = (err as Error).message;
            p.sources.storage.isLoading = false;
          }
        });
      }
    },

    navigateStorage: async (panelId, entry) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel?.sources.storage.handle || entry.kind !== 'directory') return;
      
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.sources.storage.history.push({
            handle: p.sources.storage.handle,
            name: p.sources.storage.path.split('/').pop() || 'root',
          });
          p.sources.storage.handle = entry.handle;
          p.sources.storage.path = `${p.sources.storage.path}/${entry.name}`.replace('//', '/');
        }
      });
      await get().readStorageDirectory(panelId);
    },

    navigateStorageBack: async (panelId) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel || panel.sources.storage.history.length === 0) return;
      
      const previous = panel.sources.storage.history.pop()!;
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.sources.storage.handle = previous.handle;
          p.sources.storage.path = panel.sources.storage.history.length === 0 ? '/' : `/${previous.name}`;
        }
      });
      await get().readStorageDirectory(panelId);
    },

    pickStorageDirectory: async (panelId) => {
      const handle = await fileSystemBackend.pickDirectory();
      if (!handle) return;
      
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) {
          p.sources.storage.handle = handle;
          p.sources.storage.path = `/${handle.name}`;
          p.sources.storage.history = [];
          p.sources.storage.entries = [];
        }
      });
      await get().readStorageDirectory(panelId);
    },

    createStorageFolder: async (panelId, name) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (!panel?.sources.storage.handle) return;
      
      try {
        await fileSystemBackend.createDirectory(panel.sources.storage.handle, name);
        // Invalidate cache for current path
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.sources.storage.cache.delete(p.sources.storage.path);
          }
        });
        await get().readStorageDirectory(panelId);
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
          if (p) {
            p.sources.storage.error = (err as Error).message;
          }
        });
      }
    },

    refreshStorage: async (panelId) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
      if (panel) {
        panel.sources.storage.cache.delete(panel.sources.storage.path);
      }
      await get().readStorageDirectory(panelId);
    },

    setStorageViewMode: (panelId, mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) p.sources.storage.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setStorageSortBy: (panelId, sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (p) p.sources.storage.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    // ---- Drive, GitHub, Terminal actions would follow similar pattern ----
    // (omitted for brevity – same structure but using respective source state)

    // UI actions
    setPanelWidth: (panelId, width) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (panel) panel.width = Math.max(MIN_PANEL_WIDTH, width);
      });
    },

    togglePanelMinimize: (panelId) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
        if (panel) panel.isMinimized = !panel.isMinimized;
      });
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors for storage state (example)
export const useStorageState = (panelId: string) => usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(panelId)?.sources.storage);
```

## 4. Updated StoragePanel (uses panel‑scoped storage actions)

```tsx
// src/components/Panel/StoragePanel.tsx
import { usePanelStore, useStorageState } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { FileManager } from '@/components/FileManager';

interface StoragePanelProps {
  panelId: string;
}

export function StoragePanel({ panelId }: StoragePanelProps) {
  const storageState = useStorageState(panelId);
  const {
    readStorageDirectory,
    navigateStorage,
    navigateStorageBack,
    pickStorageDirectory,
    createStorageFolder,
    refreshStorage,
    setStorageViewMode,
    setStorageSortBy,
  } = usePanelStore();

  if (!storageState) return null;

  return (
    <FileManager
      panelId={panelId}
      state={storageState}
      onReadDirectory={() => readStorageDirectory(panelId)}
      onNavigate={(entry) => navigateStorage(panelId, entry)}
      onNavigateBack={() => navigateStorageBack(panelId)}
      onPickDirectory={() => pickStorageDirectory(panelId)}
      onCreateFolder={(name) => createStorageFolder(panelId, name)}
      onRefresh={() => refreshStorage(panelId)}
      onSetViewMode={(mode) => setStorageViewMode(panelId, mode)}
      onSetSortBy={(sort) => setStorageSortBy(panelId, sort)}
    />
  );
}
```

## 6. Benefits

- **State preservation**: Switching between sources restores exact state (path, history, view mode, sort, cache).
- **No data loss**: Each source has its own isolated state.
- **Fast switching**: No re‑initialization, just UI re‑renders.
- **Clear separation**: Each source's logic and data are encapsulated.

This refactor ensures that each panel maintains independent, persistent state for all four sources, enabling seamless switching without performance penalties.

=======5==========
We'll create a unified action engine that handles copy, move, and delete operations across all sources with validation and progress tracking.

## 1. Action Types (`src/types/actions.ts`)

```typescript
// src/types/actions.ts
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';

export type ActionType = 'copy' | 'move' | 'delete';

export interface ActionItem {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: 'file' | 'directory';
  size: number;
  sourceType: SourceType;
  sourcePath: string;
  sourcePanelId: string;
  sourceHandle?: any; // For Storage/Terminal
  sourceAccountId?: string; // For Drive/GitHub
  sourceToken?: string; // For Drive/GitHub
}

export interface ActionTarget {
  panelId: string;
  path: string;
  sourceType: SourceType;
  handle?: any; // For Storage/Terminal
  accountId?: string; // For Drive/GitHub
}

export interface ActionRequest {
  type: ActionType;
  source: {
    panelId: string;
    path: string;
    items: ActionItem[];
  };
  target?: ActionTarget; // Not needed for delete
  options?: {
    overwrite?: boolean;
    preserveTimestamps?: boolean;
    recursive?: boolean;
  };
}

export interface ActionProgress {
  totalItems: number;
  completedItems: number;
  currentItem: string;
  percent: number;
  status: 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed';
  error?: string;
}

export interface ActionResult {
  success: boolean;
  message: string;
  results: Array<{
    item: ActionItem;
    success: boolean;
    error?: string;
  }>;
}
```

## 2. Action Engine Service (`src/lib/actionEngine.ts`)

```typescript
// src/lib/actionEngine.ts
import { ActionRequest, ActionProgress, ActionResult, ActionItem } from '@/types/actions';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from './fileSystemBackend';
import { driveApi } from './googleDriveApi';
import { githubApi } from './githubApi';
import { webcontainerApi } from './webcontainerApi';

export type ProgressCallback = (progress: ActionProgress) => void;

class ActionEngine {
  private async validateAction(request: ActionRequest): Promise<{ valid: boolean; error?: string }> {
    // Source validation
    if (!request.source.items.length) {
      return { valid: false, error: 'No items selected' };
    }

    // Check source permissions (simplified)
    for (const item of request.source.items) {
      if (item.type === 'directory' && request.type === 'copy' && !request.options?.recursive) {
        return { valid: false, error: `Directory copy requires recursive option: ${item.name}` };
      }
    }

    // Target validation for copy/move
    if (request.type !== 'delete' && !request.target) {
      return { valid: false, error: 'Target destination required' };
    }

    // Size limits (example: 100MB per file for Drive API)
    if (request.type === 'copy' || request.type === 'move') {
      for (const item of request.source.items) {
        if (item.sourceType === 'drive' && item.size > 100 * 1024 * 1024) {
          return { valid: false, error: `Drive API limit: ${item.name} exceeds 100MB` };
        }
        if (item.sourceType === 'github' && item.size > 25 * 1024 * 1024) {
          return { valid: false, error: `GitHub API limit: ${item.name} exceeds 25MB` };
        }
      }
    }

    return { valid: true };
  }

  async execute(request: ActionRequest, onProgress?: ProgressCallback): Promise<ActionResult> {
    // Validate
    const validation = await this.validateAction(request);
    if (!validation.valid) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: validation.error!,
        results: [],
      };
    }

    const progress: ActionProgress = {
      totalItems: request.source.items.length,
      completedItems: 0,
      currentItem: '',
      percent: 0,
      status: 'running',
    };

    const results: ActionResult['results'] = [];

    for (let i = 0; i < request.source.items.length; i++) {
      const item = request.source.items[i];
      progress.currentItem = item.name;
      progress.percent = (i / progress.totalItems) * 100;
      onProgress?.(progress);

      try {
        if (request.type === 'delete') {
          await this.deleteItem(item);
          results.push({ item, success: true });
        } else if (request.type === 'copy') {
          await this.copyItem(item, request.target!);
          results.push({ item, success: true });
        } else if (request.type === 'move') {
          await this.moveItem(item, request.target!);
          results.push({ item, success: true });
        }
      } catch (error) {
        results.push({ item, success: false, error: (error as Error).message });
      }

      progress.completedItems = i + 1;
      onProgress?.(progress);
    }

    const allSuccess = results.every(r => r.success);
    return {
      success: allSuccess,
      message: allSuccess ? `${request.type} completed` : `Some ${request.type} operations failed`,
      results,
    };
  }

  private async deleteItem(item: ActionItem): Promise<void> {
    switch (item.sourceType) {
      case 'storage':
        if (!item.sourceHandle) throw new Error('No handle for storage item');
        await fileSystemBackend.delete(item.sourceHandle);
        break;
      case 'drive':
        // Drive API delete
        await driveApi.deleteFile(item.sourceAccountId!, item.id);
        break;
      case 'github':
        // GitHub API delete (requires commit)
        await githubApi.deleteFile(item.sourceAccountId!, item.sourcePath);
        break;
      case 'terminal':
        await webcontainerApi.delete(item.sourcePath);
        break;
      default:
        throw new Error(`Unsupported source type: ${item.sourceType}`);
    }
  }

  private async copyItem(item: ActionItem, target: ActionTarget): Promise<void> {
    // Read source content
    let content: Blob | string;
    switch (item.sourceType) {
      case 'storage':
        const file = await item.sourceHandle.getFile();
        content = file;
        break;
      case 'drive':
        content = await driveApi.downloadFile(item.sourceAccountId!, item.id);
        break;
      case 'github':
        content = await githubApi.getFileContent(item.sourceAccountId!, item.sourcePath);
        break;
      case 'terminal':
        content = await webcontainerApi.readFile(item.sourcePath);
        break;
      default:
        throw new Error(`Unsupported source type: ${item.sourceType}`);
    }

    // Write to target
    switch (target.sourceType) {
      case 'storage':
        if (!target.handle) throw new Error('No target handle');
        await fileSystemBackend.writeFile(target.handle, item.name, content);
        break;
      case 'drive':
        await driveApi.uploadFile(target.accountId!, target.path, item.name, content);
        break;
      case 'github':
        await githubApi.createFile(target.accountId!, `${target.path}/${item.name}`, content);
        break;
      case 'terminal':
        await webcontainerApi.writeFile(`${target.path}/${item.name}`, content);
        break;
      default:
        throw new Error(`Unsupported target type: ${target.sourceType}`);
    }
  }

  private async moveItem(item: ActionItem, target: ActionTarget): Promise<void> {
    // Copy then delete
    await this.copyItem(item, target);
    await this.deleteItem(item);
  }
}

export const actionEngine = new ActionEngine();
```

## 3. Backend Implementations (extend existing APIs)

Add missing methods to existing backends:

### File System Backend (`src/lib/fileSystemBackend.ts`)

```typescript
async delete(handle: FileSystemHandle): Promise<void> {
  if (handle.kind === 'file') {
    await (handle as FileSystemFileHandle).remove();
  } else {
    await (handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle).remove({ recursive: true });
  }
}

async writeFile(dirHandle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle, name: string, content: Blob): Promise<void> {
  const fileHandle = await dirHandle.getFileHandle(name, { create: true });
  const writable = await fileHandle.createWritable();
  await writable.write(content);
  await writable.close();
}
```

### Drive API (`src/lib/googleDriveApi.ts`)

```typescript
async deleteFile(accountId: string, fileId: string): Promise<void> {
  const account = getAccount(accountId);
  await fetch(`https://www.googleapis.com/drive/v3/files/${fileId}`, {
    method: 'DELETE',
    headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${account.accessToken}` },
  });
}

async downloadFile(accountId: string, fileId: string): Promise<Blob> {
  const account = getAccount(accountId);
  const response = await fetch(`https://www.googleapis.com/drive/v3/files/${fileId}?alt=media`, {
    headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${account.accessToken}` },
  });
  return await response.blob();
}

async uploadFile(accountId: string, folderId: string, name: string, content: Blob): Promise<void> {
  const metadata = {
    name,
    parents: [folderId],
  };
  const form = new FormData();
  form.append('metadata', new Blob([JSON.stringify(metadata)], { type: 'application/json' }));
  form.append('media', content);
  
  await fetch('https://www.googleapis.com/upload/drive/v3/files?uploadType=multipart', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${getAccount(accountId).accessToken}` },
    body: form,
  });
}
```

### GitHub API (`src/lib/githubApi.ts`)

```typescript
async deleteFile(accountId: string, path: string, message = 'Delete file via action engine'): Promise<void> {
  const { owner, repo, filePath } = this.parsePath(path);
  const { data: file } = await this.octokit!.repos.getContent({ owner, repo, path: filePath });
  await this.octokit!.repos.deleteFile({
    owner,
    repo,
    path: filePath,
    message,
    sha: (file as any).sha,
  });
}

async getFileContent(accountId: string, path: string): Promise<string> {
  const { owner, repo, filePath } = this.parsePath(path);
  const { data } = await this.octokit!.repos.getContent({ owner, repo, path: filePath });
  if (Array.isArray(data)) throw new Error('Path is a directory');
  return Buffer.from((data as any).content, 'base64').toString();
}

async createFile(accountId: string, path: string, content: Blob | string, message = 'Add file via action engine'): Promise<void> {
  const { owner, repo, filePath } = this.parsePath(path);
  const encoded = typeof content === 'string' ? Buffer.from(content).toString('base64') : await blobToBase64(content);
  await this.octokit!.repos.createOrUpdateFileContents({
    owner,
    repo,
    path: filePath,
    message,
    content: encoded,
  });
}

private parsePath(fullPath: string): { owner: string; repo: string; filePath: string } {
  // Expect format: "owner/repo/path/to/file"
  const parts = fullPath.split('/');
  const owner = parts[0];
  const repo = parts[1];
  const filePath = parts.slice(2).join('/');
  return { owner, repo, filePath };
}
```

### WebContainer Backend (`src/lib/webcontainerApi.ts`)

```typescript
async delete(path: string): Promise<void> {
  await this.instance!.fs.rm(path, { recursive: true, force: true });
}

async writeFile(path: string, content: Blob | string): Promise<void> {
  const data = typeof content === 'string' ? content : await content.text();
  await this.instance!.fs.writeFile(path, data);
}
```

## 4. React Hook for Actions (`src/hooks/useActionEngine.ts`)

```typescript
// src/hooks/useActionEngine.ts
import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { actionEngine } from '@/lib/actionEngine';
import { ActionRequest, ActionProgress } from '@/types/actions';

export function useActionEngine() {
  const [progress, setProgress] = useState<ActionProgress | null>(null);
  const [isExecuting, setIsExecuting] = useState(false);

  const execute = useCallback(async (request: ActionRequest) => {
    setIsExecuting(true);
    setProgress(null);
    
    try {
      const result = await actionEngine.execute(request, (p) => {
        setProgress(p);
      });
      return result;
    } finally {
      setIsExecuting(false);
    }
  }, []);

  return { execute, progress, isExecuting };
}
```

```tsx

  const result = await execute({
    type: 'copy',
    source: {
      panelId: sourcePanelId,
      path: sourcePath,
      items: selectedItems,
    },
    target: {
      panelId: targetPanelId,
      path: targetPath,
      sourceType: targetSourceType,
      handle: targetHandle,
    },
    options: { recursive: true, overwrite: false },
  });
  
  if (result.success) {
    toast.success('Copy completed');
  } else {
    toast.error(result.message);
  }
};

// Show progress
if (progress) {
  return <ProgressBar value={progress.percent} label={progress.currentItem} />;
}
```

=======6==========
We'll implement a complete background processing system with task queue, Web Workers, persistence, and UI integration.

## 1. Task Types (`src/types/task.ts`)

```typescript
// src/types/task.ts
export type TaskType = 'dfol' | 'compress' | 'copy' | 'move' | 'delete';
export type TaskStatus = 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'cancelled';

export interface Task {
  id: string;
  type: TaskType;
  status: TaskStatus;
  payload: any;
  progress: number;
  result?: any;
  error?: string;
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
  userId: string;
  sessionId: string;
}

export interface TaskQueueState {
  tasks: Task[];
  activeTaskId: string | null;
  isProcessing: boolean;
}
```

## 2. Task Queue Service (`src/services/taskQueue.ts`)

```typescript
// src/services/taskQueue.ts
import { openDB } from 'idb';
import { Task, TaskStatus } from '@/types/task';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';
import { useLogStore } from '@/stores/logStore';

const DB_NAME = 'task-queue-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

class TaskQueue {
  private db: any = null;
  private activeTask: Task | null = null;
  private isProcessing = false;
  private worker: Worker | null = null;

  async init() {
    this.db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
      upgrade(db) {
        db.createObjectStore('tasks', { keyPath: 'id' });
        db.createObjectStore('completed', { keyPath: 'id' });
      },
    });
    await this.loadPendingTasks();
  }

  async addTask(task: Omit<Task, 'id' | 'status' | 'progress' | 'createdAt' | 'updatedAt'>): Promise<Task> {
    const newTask: Task = {
      id: uuidv4(),
      ...task,
      status: 'pending',
      progress: 0,
      createdAt: new Date(),
      updatedAt: new Date(),
    };
    
    await this.db.add('tasks', newTask);
    this.notifyListeners();
    
    // Start processing if idle
    if (!this.isProcessing) {
      this.processQueue();
    }
    
    return newTask;
  }

  private async loadPendingTasks() {
    const tasks = await this.db.getAll('tasks');
    const pending = tasks.filter((t: Task) => t.status === 'pending' || t.status === 'running');
    if (pending.length > 0) {
      // Resume interrupted tasks
      for (const task of pending) {
        if (task.status === 'running') {
          task.status = 'pending';
          await this.db.put('tasks', task);
        }
      }
      this.processQueue();
    }
  }

  private async processQueue() {
    if (this.isProcessing) return;
    
    const tasks = await this.db.getAll('tasks');
    const pending = tasks.filter((t: Task) => t.status === 'pending');
    if (pending.length === 0) return;
    
    this.isProcessing = true;
    this.activeTask = pending[0];
    this.activeTask.status = 'running';
    this.activeTask.updatedAt = new Date();
    await this.db.put('tasks', this.activeTask);
    this.notifyListeners();
    
    try {
      await this.runTask(this.activeTask);
    } catch (error) {
      this.activeTask.status = 'failed';
      this.activeTask.error = (error as Error).message;
      await this.db.put('tasks', this.activeTask);
      this.notifyListeners();
      
      // Log error
      useLogStore.getState().logAction('task_failed', {
        taskId: this.activeTask.id,
        type: this.activeTask.type,
        error: (error as Error).message,
      });
    } finally {
      // Move to completed store
      await this.db.delete('tasks', this.activeTask.id);
      await this.db.add('completed', this.activeTask);
      
      this.activeTask = null;
      this.isProcessing = false;
      this.processQueue(); // Process next
    }
  }

  private async runTask(task: Task) {
    // Initialize worker based on task type
    let workerScript = '';
    switch (task.type) {
      case 'dfol': workerScript = '/workers/dfol.worker.js'; break;
      case 'compress': workerScript = '/workers/compression.worker.js'; break;
      case 'copy': workerScript = '/workers/copy.worker.js'; break;
      default: throw new Error(`Unsupported task type: ${task.type}`);
    }
    
    this.worker = new Worker(workerScript);
    
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.worker!.onmessage = async (e) => {
        const { type, progress, result, error } = e.data;
        
        if (type === 'progress') {
          task.progress = progress;
          task.updatedAt = new Date();
          await this.db.put('tasks', task);
          this.notifyListeners();
        } else if (type === 'complete') {
          task.status = 'completed';
          task.progress = 100;
          task.result = result;
          task.updatedAt = new Date();
          await this.db.put('tasks', task);
          this.worker!.terminate();
          resolve(result);
        } else if (type === 'error') {
          this.worker!.terminate();
          reject(new Error(error));
        }
      };
      
      this.worker!.postMessage(task.payload);
    });
  }

  async cancelTask(taskId: string) {
    const task = await this.db.get('tasks', taskId);
    if (task && task.status === 'running') {
      this.worker?.terminate();
      task.status = 'cancelled';
      await this.db.put('tasks', task);
      this.activeTask = null;
      this.isProcessing = false;
      this.processQueue();
    }
  }

  async getTasks(): Promise<Task[]> {
    return this.db.getAll('tasks');
  }

  async getCompletedTasks(limit = 50): Promise<Task[]> {
    const all = await this.db.getAll('completed');
    return all.slice(-limit).reverse();
  }

  private listeners: Array<() => void> = [];
  subscribe(listener: () => void) {
    this.listeners.push(listener);
    return () => {
      this.listeners = this.listeners.filter(l => l !== listener);
    };
  }
  private notifyListeners() {
    this.listeners.forEach(l => l());
  }
}

export const taskQueue = new TaskQueue();
```

## 3. Web Workers

### DFOL Worker (`public/workers/dfol.worker.js`)

```javascript
// public/workers/dfol.worker.js
self.onmessage = async (e) => {
  const { items, outputDir, profile } = e.data;
  
  try {
    for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
      const item = items[i];
      self.postMessage({ type: 'progress', progress: (i / items.length) * 100, currentItem: item.name });
      
      // Simulate DFOL operation (replace with actual logic)
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 500));
      
      // For real implementation, would copy folder structure, generate TXT/PDF, compress
    }
    
    self.postMessage({ type: 'complete', result: { outputDir, itemsProcessed: items.length } });
  } catch (error) {
    self.postMessage({ type: 'error', error: error.message });
  }
};
```

### Copy Worker (`public/workers/copy.worker.js`)

```javascript
// public/workers/copy.worker.js
self.onmessage = async (e) => {
  const { sourceItems, targetInfo } = e.data;
  
  try {
    for (let i = 0; i < sourceItems.length; i++) {
      const item = sourceItems[i];
      self.postMessage({ type: 'progress', progress: (i / sourceItems.length) * 100, currentItem: item.name });
      
      // Use backend APIs via postMessage to main thread for actual copy
      // Worker cannot directly access file system, so we delegate
      const result = await performCopy(item, targetInfo);
      if (!result.success) throw new Error(result.error);
    }
    
    self.postMessage({ type: 'complete', result: { copied: sourceItems.length } });
  } catch (error) {
    self.postMessage({ type: 'error', error: error.message });
  }
};

async function performCopy(item, targetInfo) {
  // Send copy request to main thread and wait for response
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const channel = new MessageChannel();
    channel.port1.onmessage = (e) => resolve(e.data);
    self.postMessage({ type: 'copyItem', item, targetInfo }, [channel.port2]);
  });
}
```

## 4. Task Queue Store (`src/stores/taskStore.ts`)

```typescript
// src/stores/taskStore.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { Task, TaskQueueState } from '@/types/task';
import { taskQueue } from '@/services/taskQueue';

interface TaskStore extends TaskQueueState {
  tasks: Task[];
  completedTasks: Task[];
  init: () => Promise<void>;
  addTask: (task: Omit<Task, 'id' | 'status' | 'progress' | 'createdAt' | 'updatedAt'>) => Promise<Task>;
  cancelTask: (taskId: string) => Promise<void>;
  refresh: () => Promise<void>;
}

export const useTaskStore = create<TaskStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    tasks: [],
    completedTasks: [],
    activeTaskId: null,
    isProcessing: false,

    init: async () => {
      await taskQueue.init();
      await get().refresh();
      
      taskQueue.subscribe(() => {
        get().refresh();
      });
    },

    addTask: async (task) => {
      return taskQueue.addTask(task);
    },

    cancelTask: async (taskId) => {
      await taskQueue.cancelTask(taskId);
      await get().refresh();
    },

    refresh: async () => {
      const tasks = await taskQueue.getTasks();
      const completed = await taskQueue.getCompletedTasks(20);
      set((state) => {
        state.tasks = tasks;
        state.completedTasks = completed;
        state.activeTaskId = tasks.find(t => t.status === 'running')?.id || null;
        state.isProcessing = tasks.some(t => t.status === 'pending' || t.status === 'running');
      });
    },
  }))
);
```

## 5. UI Component: Task Progress Panel

```tsx
// src/components/Task/TaskProgressPanel.tsx
import { useTaskStore } from '@/stores/taskStore';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { X, CheckCircle, AlertCircle, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';

export function TaskProgressPanel() {
  const { tasks, completedTasks, activeTaskId, cancelTask, isProcessing } = useTaskStore();
  
  const activeTask = tasks.find(t => t.id === activeTaskId);
  
  return (
    <div className="fixed bottom-4 right-4 w-96 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-xl z-50 flex flex-col max-h-96">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Loader2 className={cn("w-4 h-4", isProcessing && "animate-spin")} />
          <h3 className="font-semibold">Background Tasks</h3>
          {isProcessing && <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Processing...</span>}
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Active Task Progress */}
      {activeTask && (
        <div className="p-3 border-b border-border">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm mb-1">
            <span className="font-medium capitalize">{activeTask.type}</span>
            <span>{Math.round(activeTask.progress)}%</span>
          </div>
          <Progress value={activeTask.progress} className="h-2" />
          <button
            onClick={() => cancelTask(activeTask.id)}
            className="text-xs text-destructive hover:underline mt-2"
          >
            Cancel
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
      
      {/* Queue */}
      <ScrollArea className="flex-1 max-h-64">
        <div className="divide-y divide-border">
          {tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'pending').map(task => (
            <TaskItem key={task.id} task={task} />
          ))}
          {completedTasks.slice(0, 10).map(task => (
            <TaskItem key={task.id} task={task} />
          ))}
        </div>
      </ScrollArea>
    </div>
  );
}

function TaskItem({ task }: { task: Task }) {
  const getIcon = () => {
    if (task.status === 'completed') return <CheckCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-green-500" />;
    if (task.status === 'failed') return <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />;
    if (task.status === 'running') return <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin text-primary" />;
    return <div className="w-4 h-4 rounded-full border-2 border-muted-foreground" />;
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="p-3 flex items-start gap-3">
      {getIcon()}
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className="text-sm font-medium capitalize">{task.type}</span>
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            {formatDistanceToNow(task.createdAt, { addSuffix: true })}
          </span>
        </div>
        {task.error && <p className="text-xs text-destructive mt-1">{task.error}</p>}
        {task.status === 'running' && (
          <Progress value={task.progress} className="h-1 mt-2" />
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```
