## 8. Benefits

- **Offloads heavy tasks** to Web Workers – main thread stays responsive.
- **Persistent queue** – tasks survive page reload.
- **Progress tracking** – real‑time updates for users.
- **Cancellation support** – users can abort running tasks.
- **Integration ready** – DFOL, compression, copy operations can be easily converted to use the task queue.

This system provides a robust background processing foundation for all heavy operations.
=======7==========
We'll implement a comprehensive error handling system with per-panel error states, retry mechanisms, and persistent error logging.

## 1. Error Types (`src/types/error.ts`)

```typescript
// src/types/error.ts
export type ErrorSeverity = 'info' | 'warning' | 'error' | 'critical';
export type ErrorCategory = 'network' | 'permission' | 'quota' | 'api' | 'file_system' | 'auth' | 'unknown';

export interface AppError {
  id: string;
  message: string;
  code?: string;
  category: ErrorCategory;
  severity: ErrorSeverity;
  timestamp: Date;
  source?: {
    panelId?: string;
    sourceType?: string;
    action?: string;
  };
  originalError?: any;
  retryCount?: number;
  canRetry: boolean;
}

export interface PanelErrorState {
  hasError: boolean;
  error: AppError | null;
  isRetrying: boolean;
}
```

## 2. Error Handler Service (`src/services/errorHandler.ts`)

```typescript
// src/services/errorHandler.ts
import { openDB } from 'idb';
import { AppError, ErrorCategory, ErrorSeverity } from '@/types/error';
import { useLogStore } from '@/stores/logStore';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';

const DB_NAME = 'error-logs-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

class ErrorHandler {
  private db: any = null;
  private retryQueues: Map<string, Array<() => Promise<any>>> = new Map();
  private isProcessingRetry = false;

  async init() {
    this.db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
      upgrade(db) {
        db.createObjectStore('errors', { keyPath: 'id' });
      },
    });
  }

  async capture(error: Omit<AppError, 'id' | 'timestamp'>): Promise<AppError> {
    const appError: AppError = {
      ...error,
      id: uuidv4(),
      timestamp: new Date(),
    };

    // Save to IndexedDB
    await this.db.add('errors', appError);

    // Log to live log system
    useLogStore.getState().logAction('error_captured', {
      errorId: appError.id,
      message: appError.message,
      category: appError.category,
      severity: appError.severity,
      source: appError.source,
    }, 'system');

    // Trigger UI notification for critical errors
    if (appError.severity === 'critical') {
      // Could integrate with notification system
      console.error('[Critical Error]', appError.message);
    }

    return appError;
  }

  async getErrors(limit = 100): Promise<AppError[]> {
    const all = await this.db.getAll('errors');
    return all.slice(-limit).reverse();
  }

  async clearErrors() {
    await this.db.clear('errors');
  }

  // Retry logic with exponential backoff
  async retry<T>(
    fn: () => Promise<T>,
    context: { panelId?: string; action: string; maxRetries?: number; baseDelay?: number }
  ): Promise<T> {
    const maxRetries = context.maxRetries ?? 3;
    const baseDelay = context.baseDelay ?? 1000;
    let lastError: any;

    for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++) {
      try {
        return await fn();
      } catch (err) {
        lastError = err;
        
        // Determine if retryable
        const isRetryable = this.isRetryableError(err);
        if (!isRetryable || attempt === maxRetries) {
          await this.capture({
            message: (err as Error).message,
            category: this.categorizeError(err),
            severity: attempt === maxRetries ? 'error' : 'warning',
            source: { panelId: context.panelId, action: context.action },
            originalError: err,
            canRetry: isRetryable && attempt < maxRetries,
            retryCount: attempt - 1,
          });
          
          if (attempt === maxRetries) throw err;
        }

        // Exponential backoff
        const delay = baseDelay * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1);
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
      }
    }
    throw lastError;
  }

  private isRetryableError(error: any): boolean {
    // Network errors, timeouts, rate limits
    if (error.name === 'NetworkError' || error.name === 'TimeoutError') return true;
    if (error.status === 429 || error.status === 503 || error.status === 504) return true;
    if (error.message?.includes('network') || error.message?.includes('timeout')) return true;
    return false;
  }

  private categorizeError(error: any): ErrorCategory {
    if (error.name === 'NetworkError' || error.status === 0) return 'network';
    if (error.status === 403 || error.message?.includes('permission')) return 'permission';
    if (error.status === 507 || error.message?.includes('quota')) return 'quota';
    if (error.status === 401 || error.message?.includes('auth')) return 'auth';
    if (error.message?.includes('API')) return 'api';
    return 'unknown';
  }

  async wrapWithErrorHandling<T>(
    fn: () => Promise<T>,
    context: { panelId?: string; action: string; showInline?: boolean }
  ): Promise<T> {
    try {
      return await this.retry(fn, { panelId: context.panelId, action: context.action });
    } catch (error) {
      // Let the caller handle UI display
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

export const errorHandler = new ErrorHandler();
```

## 3. Error Store (`src/stores/errorStore.ts`)

```typescript
// src/stores/errorStore.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { PanelErrorState, AppError } from '@/types/error';

interface ErrorStore {
  panelErrors: Record<string, PanelErrorState>;
  globalErrors: AppError[];
  
  setPanelError: (panelId: string, error: AppError | null) => void;
  clearPanelError: (panelId: string) => void;
  setPanelRetrying: (panelId: string, isRetrying: boolean) => void;
  addGlobalError: (error: AppError) => void;
  clearGlobalErrors: () => void;
}

export const useErrorStore = create<ErrorStore>()(
  immer((set) => ({
    panelErrors: {},
    globalErrors: [],

    setPanelError: (panelId, error) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.panelErrors[panelId] = {
          hasError: !!error,
          error,
          isRetrying: false,
        };
      });
    },

    clearPanelError: (panelId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.panelErrors[panelId]) {
          state.panelErrors[panelId].hasError = false;
          state.panelErrors[panelId].error = null;
        }
      });
    },

    setPanelRetrying: (panelId, isRetrying) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.panelErrors[panelId]) {
          state.panelErrors[panelId].isRetrying = isRetrying;
        } else {
          state.panelErrors[panelId] = {
            hasError: false,
            error: null,
            isRetrying,
          };
        }
      });
    },

    addGlobalError: (error) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.globalErrors.unshift(error);
        if (state.globalErrors.length > 50) state.globalErrors.pop();
      });
    },

    clearGlobalErrors: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.globalErrors = [];
      });
    },
  }))
);
```

## 4. Inline Error Component

```tsx
// src/components/Error/InlineError.tsx
import { AlertCircle, RefreshCw, X } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { AppError } from '@/types/error';

interface InlineErrorProps {
  error: AppError;
  onRetry?: () => void;
  onDismiss?: () => void;
  className?: string;
}

export function InlineError({ error, onRetry, onDismiss, className }: InlineErrorProps) {
  const severityColors = {
    info: 'bg-blue-50 border-blue-200 text-blue-800',
    warning: 'bg-yellow-50 border-yellow-200 text-yellow-800',
    error: 'bg-red-50 border-red-200 text-red-800',
    critical: 'bg-red-100 border-red-300 text-red-900',
  };

  return (
    <div className={cn("flex items-start gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg border", severityColors[error.severity], className)}>
      <AlertCircle className="w-5 h-5 shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <p className="text-sm font-medium">{error.message}</p>
        {error.code && (
          <p className="text-xs opacity-75 mt-1">Code: {error.code}</p>
        )}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2">
          {error.canRetry && onRetry && (
            <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="h-7 text-xs gap-1">
              <RefreshCw className="w-3 h-3" />
              Retry
            </Button>
          )}
          {onDismiss && (
            <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-7 text-xs" onClick={onDismiss}>
              Dismiss
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      {onDismiss && (
        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-6 w-6 shrink-0" onClick={onDismiss}>
          <X className="w-3 h-3" />
        </Button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

## 5. Panel-Level Error Boundary

```tsx
// src/components/Error/PanelErrorBoundary.tsx
import { Component, ErrorInfo, ReactNode } from 'react';
import { useErrorStore } from '@/stores/errorStore';
import { errorHandler } from '@/services/errorHandler';
import { InlineError } from './InlineError';

interface Props {
  panelId: string;
  children: ReactNode;
}

interface State {
  hasError: boolean;
  error: any;
}

export class PanelErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
  constructor(props: Props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { hasError: false, error: null };
  }

  static getDerivedStateFromError(error: any) {
    return { hasError: true, error };
  }

  async componentDidCatch(error: any, errorInfo: ErrorInfo) {
    const appError = await errorHandler.capture({
      message: error.message || 'Unknown error',
      category: 'unknown',
      severity: 'error',
      source: { panelId: this.props.panelId, action: 'render' },
      originalError: error,
      canRetry: false,
    });
    
    useErrorStore.getState().setPanelError(this.props.panelId, appError);
  }

  handleRetry = () => {
    this.setState({ hasError: false, error: null });
    useErrorStore.getState().clearPanelError(this.props.panelId);
  };

  render() {
    if (this.state.hasError) {
      return (
        <div className="p-4">
          <InlineError
            error={{
              id: 'boundary-error',
              message: this.state.error?.message || 'Something went wrong in this panel',
              category: 'unknown',
              severity: 'error',
              timestamp: new Date(),
              canRetry: true,
            }}
            onRetry={this.handleRetry}
            onDismiss={this.handleRetry}
          />
        </div>
      );
    }
    return this.props.children;
  }
}
```

## 6. Integration with PanelStore and Actions

Modify existing panel actions to use error handling:

```typescript
// In panelStore.ts, wrap file system operations
import { errorHandler } from '@/services/errorHandler';
import { useErrorStore } from '@/stores/errorStore';

readDirectory: async (panelId) => {
  try {
    await errorHandler.wrapWithErrorHandling(
      async () => {
        // existing read logic
      },
      { panelId, action: 'readDirectory' }
    );
  } catch (error) {
    const appError = await errorHandler.capture({
      message: (error as Error).message,
      category: 'file_system',
      severity: 'error',
      source: { panelId, action: 'readDirectory' },
      originalError: error,
      canRetry: true,
    });
    useErrorStore.getState().setPanelError(panelId, appError);
  }
}
```

## 7. Global Error List Component (Admin)

```tsx
// src/components/Error/GlobalErrorList.tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { errorHandler } from '@/services/errorHandler';
import { AppError } from '@/types/error';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { AlertCircle, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';

export function GlobalErrorList() {
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState<AppError[]>([]);
  
  useEffect(() => {
    loadErrors();
  }, []);
  
  const loadErrors = async () => {
    const errs = await errorHandler.getErrors(100);
    setErrors(errs);
  };
  
  const handleClear = async () => {
    await errorHandler.clearErrors();
    loadErrors();
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border">
        <h3 className="font-semibold">Error Logs</h3>
        <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={handleClear}>
          <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
        </Button>
      </div>
      
      <ScrollArea className="flex-1">
        <div className="divide-y divide-border">
          {errors.map((error) => (
            <div key={error.id} className="p-3">
              <div className="flex items-start gap-2">
                <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <p className="text-sm">{error.message}</p>
                  <div className="flex gap-2 mt-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                    <span>{error.category}</span>
                    <span>•</span>
                    <span>{formatDistanceToNow(error.timestamp, { addSuffix: true })}</span>
                    {error.source?.panelId && <span>• Panel: {error.source.panelId}</span>}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </ScrollArea>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## 9. Initialize Error Handler in App

```tsx
// In App.tsx or main.tsx
useEffect(() => {
  errorHandler.init();
}, []);
```

This system provides:
- Centralized error capture and logging
- Per-panel inline error display
- Automatic retry for network errors with exponential backoff
- Persistent error storage in IndexedDB
- Integration with live logging
- Admin view for error logs

=======8==========
We'll implement a unified IndexedDB storage layer with encryption for sensitive data, versioned schema, and React hooks for easy access.

## 1. Database Schema and Initialization (`src/lib/db.ts`)

```typescript
// src/lib/db.ts
import { openDB, DBSchema, IDBPDatabase } from 'idb';
import CryptoJS from 'crypto-js';

// Encryption key – in production, derive from user session or environment
const ENCRYPTION_KEY = import.meta.env.VITE_STORAGE_ENCRYPTION_KEY || 'default-secure-key-32-chars!!';

export interface AppDBSchema extends DBSchema {
  // Google Drive accounts (sensitive: tokens)
  driveAccounts: {
    key: string; // email
    value: {
      email: string;
      name: string;
      picture?: string;
      encryptedToken: string; // AES encrypted access token
      expiresAt: number;
      createdAt: number;
    };
    indexes: { 'by-email': string };
  };
  // GitHub accounts (sensitive: PAT)
  githubAccounts: {
    key: string; // username
    value: {
      username: string;
      encryptedToken: string;
      avatarUrl?: string;
      permissions: string;
      addedAt: number;
    };
    indexes: { 'by-username': string };
  };
  // Panel state (optional restore)
  panelStates: {
    key: string; // panelId
    value: {
      panelId: string;
      state: any; // serialized panel state
      updatedAt: number;
    };
    indexes: { 'by-updated': number };
  };
  // Extension scan data
  extensions: {
    key: string; // extension name e.g. ".txt"
    value: {
      extension: string;
      count: number;
      totalSize: number;
      sources: string[]; // array of source types
      accounts: string[];
      lastScanned: number;
    };
    indexes: { 'by-count': number };
  };
  // Logs (system & user actions)
  logs: {
    key: string; // logId (timestamp + random)
    value: {
      id: string;
      timestamp: number;
      level: string;
      category: string;
      message: string;
      details?: any;
      userId?: string;
      sessionId?: string;
    };
    indexes: { 'by-timestamp': number; 'by-level': string; 'by-category': string };
  };
}

class AppDatabase {
  private db: IDBPDatabase<AppDBSchema> | null = null;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.db = await openDB<AppDBSchema>('app-storage', 1, {
      upgrade(db, oldVersion, newVersion, transaction) {
        // Drive accounts store
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('driveAccounts')) {
          const driveStore = db.createObjectStore('driveAccounts', { keyPath: 'email' });
          driveStore.createIndex('by-email', 'email');
        }
        // GitHub accounts store
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('githubAccounts')) {
          const githubStore = db.createObjectStore('githubAccounts', { keyPath: 'username' });
          githubStore.createIndex('by-username', 'username');
        }
        // Panel states store
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('panelStates')) {
          const panelStore = db.createObjectStore('panelStates', { keyPath: 'panelId' });
          panelStore.createIndex('by-updated', 'updatedAt');
        }
        // Extensions store
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('extensions')) {
          const extStore = db.createObjectStore('extensions', { keyPath: 'extension' });
          extStore.createIndex('by-count', 'count');
        }
        // Logs store
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('logs')) {
          const logStore = db.createObjectStore('logs', { keyPath: 'id' });
          logStore.createIndex('by-timestamp', 'timestamp');
          logStore.createIndex('by-level', 'level');
          logStore.createIndex('by-category', 'category');
        }
      },
    });
  }

  getDB(): IDBPDatabase<AppDBSchema> {
    if (!this.db) throw new Error('Database not initialized');
    return this.db;
  }

  // Encryption helpers
  encrypt(data: string): string {
    return CryptoJS.AES.encrypt(data, ENCRYPTION_KEY).toString();
  }

  decrypt(encrypted: string): string {
    const bytes = CryptoJS.AES.decrypt(encrypted, ENCRYPTION_KEY);
    return bytes.toString(CryptoJS.enc.Utf8);
  }
}

export const appDB = new AppDatabase();
```

## 2. Storage Service (`src/lib/storageService.ts`)

Provides typed methods for each store with encryption handling.

```typescript
// src/lib/storageService.ts
import { appDB } from './db';

// ----- Drive Accounts -----
export interface DriveAccountStorage {
  email: string;
  name: string;
  picture?: string;
  encryptedToken: string;
  expiresAt: number;
  createdAt: number;
}

export async function saveDriveAccount(account: Omit<DriveAccountStorage, 'encryptedToken'> & { accessToken: string }) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  const encryptedToken = appDB.encrypt(account.accessToken);
  await db.put('driveAccounts', {
    ...account,
    encryptedToken,
  });
}

export async function getDriveAccount(email: string): Promise<{ email: string; name: string; picture?: string; accessToken: string; expiresAt: number; createdAt: number } | null> {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  const record = await db.get('driveAccounts', email);
  if (!record) return null;
  const accessToken = appDB.decrypt(record.encryptedToken);
  return { ...record, accessToken };
}

export async function getAllDriveAccounts() {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  const records = await db.getAll('driveAccounts');
  return Promise.all(records.map(async (r) => ({
    ...r,
    accessToken: appDB.decrypt(r.encryptedToken),
  })));
}

export async function deleteDriveAccount(email: string) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  await db.delete('driveAccounts', email);
}

// ----- GitHub Accounts -----
export interface GitHubAccountStorage {
  username: string;
  encryptedToken: string;
  avatarUrl?: string;
  permissions: string;
  addedAt: number;
}

export async function saveGitHubAccount(account: Omit<GitHubAccountStorage, 'encryptedToken'> & { token: string }) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  const encryptedToken = appDB.encrypt(account.token);
  await db.put('githubAccounts', {
    ...account,
    encryptedToken,
  });
}

export async function getGitHubAccount(username: string): Promise<{ username: string; token: string; avatarUrl?: string; permissions: string; addedAt: number } | null> {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  const record = await db.get('githubAccounts', username);
  if (!record) return null;
  const token = appDB.decrypt(record.encryptedToken);
  return { ...record, token };
}

export async function getAllGitHubAccounts() {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  const records = await db.getAll('githubAccounts');
  return Promise.all(records.map(async (r) => ({
    ...r,
    token: appDB.decrypt(r.encryptedToken),
  })));
}

export async function deleteGitHubAccount(username: string) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  await db.delete('githubAccounts', username);
}

// ----- Panel State -----
export async function savePanelState(panelId: string, state: any) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  await db.put('panelStates', {
    panelId,
    state,
    updatedAt: Date.now(),
  });
}

export async function getPanelState(panelId: string) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  const record = await db.get('panelStates', panelId);
  return record?.state || null;
}

export async function getAllPanelStates() {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  return db.getAll('panelStates');
}

export async function deletePanelState(panelId: string) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  await db.delete('panelStates', panelId);
}

// ----- Extension Data -----
export interface ExtensionStatsStorage {
  extension: string;
  count: number;
  totalSize: number;
  sources: string[];
  accounts: string[];
  lastScanned: number;
}

export async function saveExtensionStats(stats: ExtensionStatsStorage) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  await db.put('extensions', stats);
}

export async function getExtensionStats(extension: string): Promise<ExtensionStatsStorage | undefined> {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  return db.get('extensions', extension);
}

export async function getAllExtensions() {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  return db.getAll('extensions');
}

export async function deleteExtensionStats(extension: string) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  await db.delete('extensions', extension);
}

// ----- Logs -----
export interface LogEntryStorage {
  id: string;
  timestamp: number;
  level: string;
  category: string;
  message: string;
  details?: any;
  userId?: string;
  sessionId?: string;
}

export async function addLog(log: LogEntryStorage) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  await db.add('logs', log);
}

export async function getLogs(limit = 100, level?: string, category?: string) {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  let tx = db.transaction('logs', 'readonly');
  let index = tx.store.index('by-timestamp');
  let logs = await index.getAll(null, limit);
  if (level) {
    logs = logs.filter(l => l.level === level);
  }
  if (category) {
    logs = logs.filter(l => l.category === category);
  }
  return logs;
}

export async function clearLogs() {
  const db = appDB.getDB();
  await db.clear('logs');
}
```

## 3. React Hooks for Storage (`src/hooks/useStorage.ts`)

```typescript
// src/hooks/useStorage.ts
import { useEffect, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import * as storageService from '@/lib/storageService';

// Drive Accounts
export function useDriveAccounts() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const accs = await storageService.getAllDriveAccounts();
    setAccounts(accs);
    setLoading(false);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  const save = useCallback(async (email: string, name: string, accessToken: string, expiresAt: number, picture?: string) => {
    await storageService.saveDriveAccount({ email, name, picture, accessToken, expiresAt, createdAt: Date.now() });
    await refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  const remove = useCallback(async (email: string) => {
    await storageService.deleteDriveAccount(email);
    await refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  return { accounts, loading, save, remove, refresh };
}

// GitHub Accounts
export function useGitHubAccounts() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const accs = await storageService.getAllGitHubAccounts();
    setAccounts(accs);
    setLoading(false);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  const save = useCallback(async (username: string, token: string, avatarUrl?: string, permissions = 'read') => {
    await storageService.saveGitHubAccount({ username, token, avatarUrl, permissions, addedAt: Date.now() });
    await refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  const remove = useCallback(async (username: string) => {
    await storageService.deleteGitHubAccount(username);
    await refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  return { accounts, loading, save, remove, refresh };
}

// Panel State
export function usePanelState(panelId: string) {
  const [state, setState] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const saved = await storageService.getPanelState(panelId);
    setState(saved);
    setLoading(false);
  }, [panelId]);

  const save = useCallback(async (newState: any) => {
    await storageService.savePanelState(panelId, newState);
    setState(newState);
  }, [panelId]);

  const clear = useCallback(async () => {
    await storageService.deletePanelState(panelId);
    setState(null);
  }, [panelId]);

  useEffect(() => {
    load();
  }, [load]);

  return { state, loading, save, clear, refresh: load };
}

// Extensions
export function useExtensions() {
  const [extensions, setExtensions] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const exts = await storageService.getAllExtensions();
    setExtensions(exts);
    setLoading(false);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  const save = useCallback(async (stats: storageService.ExtensionStatsStorage) => {
    await storageService.saveExtensionStats(stats);
    await refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  return { extensions, loading, save, refresh };
}

// Logs
export function useLogs(limit = 100, level?: string, category?: string) {
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const logEntries = await storageService.getLogs(limit, level, category);
    setLogs(logEntries);
    setLoading(false);
  }, [limit, level, category]);

  useEffect(() => {
    refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  const add = useCallback(async (log: Omit<storageService.LogEntryStorage, 'id' | 'timestamp'>) => {
    const newLog: storageService.LogEntryStorage = {
      ...log,
      id: `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`,
      timestamp: Date.now(),
    };
    await storageService.addLog(newLog);
    await refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  const clearAll = useCallback(async () => {
    await storageService.clearLogs();
    await refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  return { logs, loading, add, clearAll, refresh };
}
```

## 5. Migration from Existing Stores

Update `githubStorage.ts` to use the new service:

```typescript
// src/lib/githubStorage.ts (rewritten)
import { saveGitHubAccount, getGitHubAccount, deleteGitHubAccount, getAllGitHubAccounts } from './storageService';

export const githubStorage = {
  saveAccount: async (account: any) => {
    await saveGitHubAccount({
      username: account.id,
      token: account.token,
      avatarUrl: account.avatarUrl,
      permissions: account.permissions,
      addedAt: account.addedAt,
    });
  },
  getAllAccounts: async () => {
    const accounts = await getAllGitHubAccounts();
    return accounts.map(a => ({
      id: a.username,
      token: a.token,
      avatarUrl: a.avatarUrl,
      permissions: a.permissions,
      addedAt: a.addedAt,
    }));
  },
  deleteAccount: async (username: string) => {
    await deleteGitHubAccount(username);
  },
  // ... other methods
};
```

Similarly, update `googleDriveApi` to use `saveDriveAccount` and `getDriveAccount`.

## 6. Benefits

- **Unified storage** – all data in one IndexedDB with versioned schema.
- **Encryption** – tokens encrypted at rest.
- **Fast** – IndexedDB is asynchronous and fast for large data.
- **Type‑safe** – full TypeScript support.
- **React hooks** – easy integration in components.
- **Migration ready** – future schema upgrades handled by versioned upgrade.

This implementation provides a robust, scalable storage layer for the entire application.

We'll create a unified orchestrator that coordinates all subsystems: panels, actions, tasks, caching, and cross-source operations.

## 1. Unified Engine Class (`src/services/unifiedEngine.ts`)

```typescript
// src/services/unifiedEngine.ts
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { useTaskStore } from '@/stores/taskStore';
import { actionEngine } from './actionEngine';
import { taskQueue } from './taskQueue';
import { errorHandler } from './errorHandler';
import { ActionRequest, ActionResult, ActionProgress } from '@/types/actions';
import { Task } from '@/types/task';
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';

export interface CrossSourceCopyRequest {
  type: 'copy' | 'move';
  sourcePanelId: string;
  sourceItems: Array<{ id: string; path: string }>;
  targetPanelId: string;
  targetPath: string;
  options?: { overwrite?: boolean; recursive?: boolean };
}

export interface UnifiedEngineAPI {
  executeAction(request: ActionRequest, onProgress?: (progress: ActionProgress) => void): Promise<ActionResult>;
  queueTask(task: Omit<Task, 'id' | 'status' | 'progress' | 'createdAt' | 'updatedAt'>): Promise<Task>;
  refreshPanel(panelId: string): Promise<void>;
  getPanelState(panelId: string): any;
  syncAcrossSources(request: CrossSourceCopyRequest): Promise<ActionResult>;
  cancelTask(taskId: string): Promise<void>;
  getActiveTasks(): Promise<Task[]>;
}

class UnifiedEngine implements UnifiedEngineAPI {
  async executeAction(request: ActionRequest, onProgress?: (progress: ActionProgress) => void): Promise<ActionResult> {
    try {
      // Validate source and target panels exist
      const sourcePanel = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(request.source.panelId);
      if (!sourcePanel) throw new Error(`Source panel ${request.source.panelId} not found`);
      
      if (request.type !== 'delete') {
        const targetPanel = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(request.target!.panelId);
        if (!targetPanel) throw new Error(`Target panel ${request.target!.panelId} not found`);
      }
      
      // Route through actionEngine
      const result = await actionEngine.execute(request, onProgress);
      
      // Refresh affected panels after operation
      await this.refreshPanel(request.source.panelId);
      if (request.target) await this.refreshPanel(request.target.panelId);
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      await errorHandler.capture({
        message: (error as Error).message,
        category: 'api',
        severity: 'error',
        source: { action: 'executeAction', panelId: request.source.panelId },
        originalError: error,
        canRetry: false,
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }
  
  async queueTask(task: Omit<Task, 'id' | 'status' | 'progress' | 'createdAt' | 'updatedAt'>): Promise<Task> {
    return taskQueue.addTask(task);
  }
  
  async refreshPanel(panelId: string): Promise<void> {
    const panel = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(panelId);
    if (!panel) return;
    
    // Refresh based on active source
    switch (panel.activeSource) {
      case 'storage':
        await usePanelStore.getState().readStorageDirectory(panelId);
        break;
      case 'drive':
        // Refresh drive current folder
        // await usePanelStore.getState().refreshDrive(panelId);
        break;
      case 'github':
        // Refresh github current repo
        // await usePanelStore.getState().refreshGitHub(panelId);
        break;
      case 'terminal':
        // Refresh terminal current path
        // await usePanelStore.getState().refreshTerminal(panelId);
        break;
    }
  }
  
  getPanelState(panelId: string): any {
    return usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(panelId);
  }
  
  async syncAcrossSources(request: CrossSourceCopyRequest): Promise<ActionResult> {
    const sourcePanel = this.getPanelState(request.sourcePanelId);
    const targetPanel = this.getPanelState(request.targetPanelId);
    
    if (!sourcePanel || !targetPanel) {
      throw new Error('Invalid source or target panel');
    }
    
    // Build action items from source panel's current entries
    const sourceEntries = sourcePanel.sources[sourcePanel.activeSource]?.entries || [];
    const items = request.sourceItems.map(item => {
      const entry = sourceEntries.find(e => e.id === item.id || e.name === item.id);
      if (!entry) throw new Error(`Item ${item.id} not found in source panel`);
      
      return {
        id: entry.id || entry.name,
        name: entry.name,
        type: entry.kind === 'directory' ? 'directory' : 'file',
        size: entry.size || 0,
        sourceType: sourcePanel.activeSource,
        sourcePath: entry.path || entry.name,
        sourcePanelId: request.sourcePanelId,
        sourceHandle: entry.handle,
        sourceAccountId: sourcePanel.sources[sourcePanel.activeSource]?.accountId,
      };
    });
    
    const actionRequest: ActionRequest = {
      type: request.type,
      source: {
        panelId: request.sourcePanelId,
        path: sourcePanel.sources[sourcePanel.activeSource]?.path || '/',
        items,
      },
      target: {
        panelId: request.targetPanelId,
        path: request.targetPath,
        sourceType: targetPanel.activeSource,
        handle: targetPanel.sources[targetPanel.activeSource]?.handle,
        accountId: targetPanel.sources[targetPanel.activeSource]?.accountId,
      },
      options: request.options,
    };
    
    return this.executeAction(actionRequest);
  }
  
  async cancelTask(taskId: string): Promise<void> {
    await taskQueue.cancelTask(taskId);
  }
  
  async getActiveTasks(): Promise<Task[]> {
    return taskQueue.getTasks();
  }
}

export const unifiedEngine = new UnifiedEngine();
```

## 2. React Hook: `useUnifiedEngine`

```typescript
// src/hooks/useUnifiedEngine.ts
import { useCallback } from 'react';
import { unifiedEngine } from '@/services/unifiedEngine';
import { useTaskStore } from '@/stores/taskStore';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { ActionRequest, ActionProgress } from '@/types/actions';
import { Task } from '@/types/task';

export function useUnifiedEngine() {
  const refreshTasks = useTaskStore((s) => s.refresh);
  const refreshPanel = usePanelStore((s) => s.readStorageDirectory); // example
  
  const executeAction = useCallback(async (
    request: ActionRequest,
    onProgress?: (progress: ActionProgress) => void
  ) => {
    return unifiedEngine.executeAction(request, onProgress);
  }, []);
  
  const queueTask = useCallback(async (task: Omit<Task, 'id' | 'status' | 'progress' | 'createdAt' | 'updatedAt'>) => {
    const newTask = await unifiedEngine.queueTask(task);
    await refreshTasks();
    return newTask;
  }, [refreshTasks]);
  
  const refreshPanelState = useCallback(async (panelId: string) => {
    await unifiedEngine.refreshPanel(panelId);
  }, []);
  
  const syncAcrossSources = useCallback(async (request: any) => {
    return unifiedEngine.syncAcrossSources(request);
  }, []);
  
  const cancelTask = useCallback(async (taskId: string) => {
    await unifiedEngine.cancelTask(taskId);
    await refreshTasks();
  }, [refreshTasks]);
  
  const getPanelState = useCallback((panelId: string) => {
    return unifiedEngine.getPanelState(panelId);
  }, []);
  
  return {
    executeAction,
    queueTask,
    refreshPanel: refreshPanelState,
    syncAcrossSources,
    cancelTask,
    getPanelState,
    getActiveTasks: unifiedEngine.getActiveTasks.bind(unifiedEngine),
  };
}
```

## 6. Benefits

- **Cross‑source operations** – copy/move between different source types (Storage ↔ Drive, etc.) handled automatically.

- **Task queuing** unified.
- **Easy to test** and extend.

The unified engine becomes the backbone of the application, simplifying component logic and ensuring consistency.


=======2==========

We'll implement a smart panel synchronization system that refreshes only affected paths after actions, avoiding full reloads.

## 1. Panel Sync Service (`src/services/panelSync.ts`)

```typescript
// src/services/panelSync.ts
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { useFileSystemStore } from '@/stores/fileSystemStore'; // if still used, but we'll refactor to panel store
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';

export interface SyncEvent {
  type: 'copy' | 'move' | 'delete' | 'rename';
  sourcePanelId: string;
  sourcePath: string;
  targetPanelId?: string;
  targetPath?: string;
  affectedPaths: string[];
}

class PanelSync {
  private listeners: Array<(event: SyncEvent) => void> = [];

  subscribe(listener: (event: SyncEvent) => void) {
    this.listeners.push(listener);
    return () => {
      this.listeners = this.listeners.filter(l => l !== listener);
    };
  }

  async notify(event: SyncEvent) {
    // Notify all subscribers
    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(event));
    
    // Perform smart refresh
    await this.smartRefresh(event);
  }

  private async smartRefresh(event: SyncEvent) {
    // Refresh source panel at the affected source path
    await this.refreshPath(event.sourcePanelId, event.sourcePath);
    
    // Refresh target panel if present
    if (event.targetPanelId && event.targetPath) {
      await this.refreshPath(event.targetPanelId, event.targetPath);
    }
    
    // Also refresh parent directories of affected paths
    const uniquePaths = new Set<string>();
    for (const path of event.affectedPaths) {
      const parent = path.substring(0, path.lastIndexOf('/')) || '/';
      uniquePaths.add(parent);
    }
    
    for (const path of uniquePaths) {
      await this.refreshPath(event.sourcePanelId, path);
      if (event.targetPanelId) await this.refreshPath(event.targetPanelId, path);
    }
  }

  private async refreshPath(panelId: string, path: string) {
    const panel = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(panelId);
    if (!panel) return;
    
    const activeSource = panel.activeSource;
    
    // Only refresh if the panel's current active source matches the operation's source type
    // and if the path is relevant
    if (panel.sources[activeSource]?.path === path || path === '/') {
      // Refresh current directory if it matches the affected path
      await this.refreshPanelCurrentDirectory(panelId);
    } else {
      // Invalidate cache for that specific path
      this.invalidateCache(panelId, activeSource, path);
    }
  }

  private async refreshPanelCurrentDirectory(panelId: string) {
    const panel = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(panelId);
    if (!panel) return;
    
    switch (panel.activeSource) {
      case 'storage':
        await usePanelStore.getState().readStorageDirectory(panelId);
        break;
      case 'drive':
        // await usePanelStore.getState().refreshDrive(panelId);
        break;
      case 'github':
        // await usePanelStore.getState().refreshGitHub(panelId);
        break;
      case 'terminal':
        // await usePanelStore.getState().refreshTerminal(panelId);
        break;
    }
  }

  private invalidateCache(panelId: string, sourceType: SourceType, path: string) {
    const panel = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(panelId);
    if (!panel) return;
    
    if (sourceType === 'storage' && panel.sources.storage.cache) {
      panel.sources.storage.cache.delete(path);
    }
    // Similarly for other sources
  }
}

export const panelSync = new PanelSync();
```

## 2. Integrate with UnifiedEngine

Modify `UnifiedEngine` to trigger sync after actions:

```typescript
// In src/services/unifiedEngine.ts (add to executeAction method)
import { panelSync } from './panelSync';

async executeAction(request: ActionRequest, onProgress?: (progress: ActionProgress) => void): Promise<ActionResult> {
  try {
    const result = await actionEngine.execute(request, onProgress);
    
    // Build sync event
    const event: SyncEvent = {
      type: request.type,
      sourcePanelId: request.source.panelId,
      sourcePath: request.source.path,
      targetPanelId: request.target?.panelId,
      targetPath: request.target?.path,
      affectedPaths: request.source.items.map(item => item.sourcePath),
    };
    
    // Notify sync system
    await panelSync.notify(event);
    
    return result;
  } catch (error) {
    // error handling
  }
}
```

## 3. React Hook: `usePanelSync`

```typescript
// src/hooks/usePanelSync.ts
import { useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { panelSync, SyncEvent } from '@/services/panelSync';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';

export function usePanelSync(panelId: string) {
  const refreshPanel = useCallback(async () => {
    const panel = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(panelId);
    if (!panel) return;
    
    switch (panel.activeSource) {
      case 'storage':
        await usePanelStore.getState().readStorageDirectory(panelId);
        break;
      // ... other sources
    }
  }, [panelId]);
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const unsubscribe = panelSync.subscribe(async (event) => {
      // If this panel is either source or target, refresh
      if (event.sourcePanelId === panelId || event.targetPanelId === panelId) {
        // Smart refresh: check if current path is affected
        const currentPath = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(panelId)?.sources[usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(panelId)!.activeSource]?.path;
        if (currentPath && event.affectedPaths.some(p => currentPath.startsWith(p))) {
          await refreshPanel();
        } else {
          // Invalidate cache for parent directories
          // Already handled by panelSync service, but we can force re-fetch if needed
        }
      }
    });
    
    return unsubscribe;
  }, [panelId, refreshPanel]);
  
  return { refreshPanel };
}
```


## 6. Benefits

- **Selective refresh** – only affected paths are updated.
- **No unnecessary API calls** – reduces load.
- **Automatic** – panels stay in sync after any action.
- **Cache invalidation** – prevents stale data.
- **Cross‑panel consistency** – when copying between panels, both update correctly.

This system ensures that after any copy/move/delete operation, all relevant panels reflect the latest state without full page reloads.

=======3==========

We'll implement a global event bus to decouple modules, enabling loose coupling and easier testing.

## 1. Event Bus Implementation (`src/lib/eventBus.ts`)

```typescript
// src/lib/eventBus.ts
export type EventType =
  | 'ACTION_STARTED'
  | 'ACTION_COMPLETED'
  | 'ACTION_FAILED'
  | 'TASK_PROGRESS'
  | 'TASK_COMPLETED'
  | 'TASK_FAILED'
  | 'PANEL_UPDATED'
  | 'ERROR_OCCURRED';

export interface ActionEventData {
  actionId: string;
  type: 'copy' | 'move' | 'delete';
  sourcePanelId: string;
  targetPanelId?: string;
  items: any[];
  progress?: number;
  result?: any;
  error?: string;
}

export interface TaskEventData {
  taskId: string;
  type: string;
  progress: number;
  result?: any;
  error?: string;
}

export interface PanelEventData {
  panelId: string;
  sourceType: string;
  path?: string;
}

export interface ErrorEventData {
  errorId: string;
  message: string;
  category: string;
  severity: string;
  source?: any;
}

type EventCallback<T = any> = (data: T) => void;

class EventBus {
  private listeners: Map<EventType, Set<EventCallback>> = new Map();

  on<T>(event: EventType, callback: EventCallback<T>): () => void {
    if (!this.listeners.has(event)) {
      this.listeners.set(event, new Set());
    }
    this.listeners.get(event)!.add(callback);
    
    // Return unsubscribe function
    return () => {
      this.listeners.get(event)?.delete(callback);
    };
  }

  once<T>(event: EventType, callback: EventCallback<T>): void {
    const wrapper = (data: T) => {
      callback(data);
      this.off(event, wrapper);
    };
    this.on(event, wrapper);
  }

  off<T>(event: EventType, callback: EventCallback<T>): void {
    this.listeners.get(event)?.delete(callback);
  }

  emit<T>(event: EventType, data: T): void {
    const callbacks = this.listeners.get(event);
    if (callbacks) {
      callbacks.forEach(cb => {
        try {
          cb(data);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(`Error in event handler for ${event}:`, error);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // Debug: log all events if enabled
  enableDebugLogging() {
    const events: EventType[] = [
      'ACTION_STARTED', 'ACTION_COMPLETED', 'ACTION_FAILED',
      'TASK_PROGRESS', 'TASK_COMPLETED', 'TASK_FAILED',
      'PANEL_UPDATED', 'ERROR_OCCURRED'
    ];
    events.forEach(event => {
      this.on(event, (data) => {
        console.debug(`[EventBus] ${event}`, data);
      });
    });
  }
}

export const eventBus = new EventBus();
```

## 2. Integration with ActionEngine

Modify `actionEngine.ts` to emit events:

```typescript
// src/lib/actionEngine.ts (partial)
import { eventBus } from './eventBus';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';

class ActionEngine {
  async execute(request: ActionRequest, onProgress?: (progress: ActionProgress) => void): Promise<ActionResult> {
    const actionId = uuidv4();
    
    // Emit start event
    eventBus.emit('ACTION_STARTED', {
      actionId,
      type: request.type,
      sourcePanelId: request.source.panelId,
      targetPanelId: request.target?.panelId,
      items: request.source.items,
      progress: 0,
    });
    
    try {
      const result = await this._executeInternal(request, (progress) => {
        onProgress?.(progress);
        eventBus.emit('ACTION_PROGRESS', { actionId, progress });
      });
      
      // Emit completion event
      eventBus.emit('ACTION_COMPLETED', {
        actionId,
        type: request.type,
        sourcePanelId: request.source.panelId,
        targetPanelId: request.target?.panelId,
        items: request.source.items,
        result,
      });
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      eventBus.emit('ACTION_FAILED', {
        actionId,
        type: request.type,
        sourcePanelId: request.source.panelId,
        targetPanelId: request.target?.panelId,
        items: request.source.items,
        error: (error as Error).message,
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }
}
```

## 3. Integration with TaskQueue

Modify `taskQueue.ts` to emit events:

```typescript
// src/services/taskQueue.ts (partial)
import { eventBus } from '@/lib/eventBus';

class TaskQueue {
  private async runTask(task: Task) {
    eventBus.emit('TASK_STARTED', { taskId: task.id, type: task.type });
    
    this.worker!.onmessage = async (e) => {
      const { type, progress, result, error } = e.data;
      
      if (type === 'progress') {
        task.progress = progress;
        eventBus.emit('TASK_PROGRESS', { taskId: task.id, progress, type: task.type });
      } else if (type === 'complete') {
        eventBus.emit('TASK_COMPLETED', { taskId: task.id, result, type: task.type });
      } else if (type === 'error') {
        eventBus.emit('TASK_FAILED', { taskId: task.id, error, type: task.type });
      }
    };
  }
}
```

Emit `PANEL_UPDATED` after any panel state change:

```typescript
  path: panel.sources.storage.path,

```

## 5. Integration with UnifiedEngine

Listen to events and propagate or react:

```typescript

  eventBus.on('ACTION_COMPLETED', async (data) => {
    // Refresh affected panels automatically
    await this.refreshPanel(data.sourcePanelId);
    if (data.targetPanelId) await this.refreshPanel(data.targetPanelId);
  });
  
  eventBus.on('TASK_COMPLETED', (data) => {
    // Notify UI or log
    console.log(`Task ${data.taskId} completed`);
  });
  
  eventBus.on('ERROR_OCCURRED', (data) => {
    // Central error handling
    console.error('Global error:', data);
  });
}
```

## 6. React Hook: `useEventBus`

```typescript
// src/hooks/useEventBus.ts
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { eventBus, EventType } from '@/lib/eventBus';

export function useEventBus<T = any>(
  event: EventType,
  callback: (data: T) => void,
  deps: any[] = []
) {
  useEffect(() => {
    const unsubscribe = eventBus.on(event, callback);
    return unsubscribe;
  }, [event, callback, ...deps]);
}

// Example usage:
// useEventBus('ACTION_COMPLETED', (data) => {
//   console.log('Action completed:', data);
// });
```

## 7. Example: Listening for Errors in App

```tsx

    toast.error(error.message);
  });
  
  return null;
}
```

## 8. Benefits

- **Decoupling** – modules don't need to know about each other.
- **Extensibility** – new features can listen to existing events.
- **Debugging** – can log all events globally.
- **Performance** – events are lightweight.
- **Type safety** – fully typed with TypeScript.

This event bus completes the orchestration layer, enabling a fully decoupled, event-driven architecture.

=======4==========

We'll implement a system-wide recovery engine with automatic retries, fallback mechanisms, and non-blocking UI integration.

## 1. Recovery Types (`src/types/recovery.ts`)

```typescript
// src/types/recovery.ts
export interface RetryConfig {
  maxAttempts: number;
  baseDelay: number;
  backoffFactor: number;
  retryableErrors: string[]; // error names or status codes
}

export interface FallbackConfig {
  useCache: boolean;
  partialLoad: boolean;
  staleWhileRevalidate: boolean;
}

export interface RecoveryContext {
  source: string;
  panelId?: string;
  action: string;
  retryCount?: number;
}

export interface RecoveryResult<T> {
  success: boolean;
  data?: T;
  error?: string;
  fromCache: boolean;
  attempts: number;
}
```

## 2. Recovery Engine (`src/services/recoveryEngine.ts`)

```typescript
// src/services/recoveryEngine.ts
import { errorHandler } from './errorHandler';
import { eventBus } from '@/lib/eventBus';
import { RetryConfig, FallbackConfig, RecoveryContext, RecoveryResult } from '@/types/recovery';

const DEFAULT_RETRY_CONFIG: RetryConfig = {
  maxAttempts: 3,
  baseDelay: 1000,
  backoffFactor: 2,
  retryableErrors: ['NetworkError', 'TimeoutError', '429', '503', '504'],
};

const DEFAULT_FALLBACK_CONFIG: FallbackConfig = {
  useCache: true,
  partialLoad: true,
  staleWhileRevalidate: true,
};

class RecoveryEngine {
  private retryQueues: Map<string, Promise<any>> = new Map();

  async withRetry<T>(
    fn: () => Promise<T>,
    context: RecoveryContext,
    config: Partial<RetryConfig> = {}
  ): Promise<RecoveryResult<T>> {
    const retryConfig = { ...DEFAULT_RETRY_CONFIG, ...config };
    let lastError: any;
    let attempts = 0;

    for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= retryConfig.maxAttempts; attempt++) {
      attempts = attempt;
      try {
        const result = await fn();
        // Success
        if (attempt > 1) {
          eventBus.emit('RECOVERY_SUCCESS', { context, attempts });
        }
        return { success: true, data: result, fromCache: false, attempts };
      } catch (error) {
        lastError = error;
        const isRetryable = this.isRetryableError(error, retryConfig);
        
        if (isRetryable && attempt < retryConfig.maxAttempts) {
          const delay = retryConfig.baseDelay * Math.pow(retryConfig.backoffFactor, attempt - 1);
          eventBus.emit('RECOVERY_RETRY', { context, attempt, delay });
          await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
          continue;
        }
        break;
      }
    }

    // All retries failed
    await errorHandler.capture({
      message: (lastError as Error).message,
      category: 'api',
      severity: 'error',
      source: context,
      originalError: lastError,
      canRetry: true,
    });

    eventBus.emit('RECOVERY_FAILED', { context, error: lastError });

    return {
      success: false,
      error: (lastError as Error).message,
      fromCache: false,
      attempts,
    };
  }

  async withFallback<T>(
    primaryFn: () => Promise<T>,
    fallbackFn: () => Promise<T>,
    context: RecoveryContext,
    fallbackConfig: Partial<FallbackConfig> = {}
  ): Promise<RecoveryResult<T>> {
    const config = { ...DEFAULT_FALLBACK_CONFIG, ...fallbackConfig };
    
    try {
      const result = await primaryFn();
      return { success: true, data: result, fromCache: false, attempts: 1 };
    } catch (error) {
      eventBus.emit('FALLBACK_TRIGGERED', { context, error });
      
      try {
        const fallbackResult = await fallbackFn();
        return {
          success: true,
          data: fallbackResult,
          fromCache: true,
          attempts: 1,
        };
      } catch (fallbackError) {
        await errorHandler.capture({
          message: `Fallback failed: ${(fallbackError as Error).message}`,
          category: 'api',
          severity: 'warning',
          source: context,
          originalError: fallbackError,
          canRetry: false,
        });
        throw fallbackError;
      }
    }
  }

  async withStaleWhileRevalidate<T>(
    cacheFn: () => Promise<T>,
    freshFn: () => Promise<T>,
    context: RecoveryContext,
    ttl = 60000 // 1 minute default
  ): Promise<T> {
    // Try cache first
    let cachedData: T | null = null;
    let cacheValid = false;
    
    try {
      cachedData = await cacheFn();
      cacheValid = true;
    } catch (e) {
      // Cache miss or error
    }
    
    // If cache is valid and within TTL (simplified, would need timestamps)
    if (cacheValid) {
      // Revalidate in background
      freshFn()
        .then(freshData => {
          eventBus.emit('STALE_WHILE_REVALIDATE', { context, freshData });
        })
        .catch(err => {
          console.warn('Background revalidation failed:', err);
        });
      
      return cachedData!;
    }
    
    // No cache, fetch fresh
    return freshFn();
  }

  private isRetryableError(error: any, config: RetryConfig): boolean {
    const errorName = error.name || '';
    const status = error.status || error.statusCode;
    
    return config.retryableErrors.some(pattern => {
      if (pattern === String(status)) return true;
      if (errorName.includes(pattern)) return true;
      if (error.message?.includes(pattern)) return true;
      return false;
    });
  }
}

export const recoveryEngine = new RecoveryEngine();
```

## 3. Retry Wrapper Utility (`src/utils/retryWrapper.ts`)

```typescript
// src/utils/retryWrapper.ts
import { recoveryEngine } from '@/services/recoveryEngine';
import { RecoveryContext } from '@/types/recovery';

export function withRetry<T>(
  fn: () => Promise<T>,
  context: RecoveryContext,
  options?: { maxAttempts?: number; baseDelay?: number }
) {
  return recoveryEngine.withRetry(fn, context, options);
}

export function withFallback<T>(
  primary: () => Promise<T>,
  fallback: () => Promise<T>,
  context: RecoveryContext
) {
  return recoveryEngine.withFallback(primary, fallback, context);
}

// Decorator-style wrapper for class methods
export function retryable(maxAttempts = 3) {
  return function (target: any, propertyKey: string, descriptor: PropertyDescriptor) {
    const originalMethod = descriptor.value;
    descriptor.value = async function (...args: any[]) {
      const context: RecoveryContext = {
        source: target.constructor.name,
        action: propertyKey,
      };
      const result = await recoveryEngine.withRetry(
        () => originalMethod.apply(this, args),
        context,
        { maxAttempts }
      );
      if (!result.success) throw new Error(result.error);
      return result.data;
    };
    return descriptor;
  };
}
```

## 4. React Hook: `useRecovery`

```typescript
// src/hooks/useRecovery.ts
import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { recoveryEngine } from '@/services/recoveryEngine';
import { RecoveryContext } from '@/types/recovery';

export function useRecovery() {
  const [isRetrying, setIsRetrying] = useState(false);
  const [retryCount, setRetryCount] = useState(0);

  const executeWithRecovery = useCallback(async <T>(
    fn: () => Promise<T>,
    context: RecoveryContext,
    onRetry?: (attempt: number) => void
  ): Promise<T> => {
    setIsRetrying(true);
    try {
      const result = await recoveryEngine.withRetry(fn, context);
      if (!result.success) throw new Error(result.error);
      return result.data!;
    } finally {
      setIsRetrying(false);
    }
  }, []);

  return { executeWithRecovery, isRetrying, retryCount };
}
```

## 5. UI: Inline Retry Button Component

```tsx
// src/components/Recovery/RetryButton.tsx
import { RefreshCw, AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface RetryButtonProps {
  onRetry: () => Promise<void>;
  errorMessage?: string;
  className?: string;
}

export function RetryButton({ onRetry, errorMessage, className }: RetryButtonProps) {
  const [isRetrying, setIsRetrying] = useState(false);

  const handleRetry = async () => {
    setIsRetrying(true);
    try {
      await onRetry();
    } finally {
      setIsRetrying(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className={cn("flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg bg-destructive/10 border border-destructive/20", className)}>
      <AlertCircle className="w-5 h-5 text-destructive shrink-0" />

      </div>

        variant="outline"
        size="sm"
        onClick={handleRetry}
        disabled={isRetrying}
        className="gap-1"
      >
        <RefreshCw className={cn("w-4 h-4", isRetrying && "animate-spin")} />
        {isRetrying ? 'Retrying...' : 'Retry'}
      </Button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## 6. Integration with PanelStore (example for Storage)

```typescript
// In panelStore.ts readStorageDirectory
import { recoveryEngine } from '@/services/recoveryEngine';

readStorageDirectory: async (panelId) => {
  const panel = get().getPanel(panelId);
  if (!panel?.handle) return;

  const result = await recoveryEngine.withFallback(
    // Primary: fresh read
    () => fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle),
    // Fallback: cached data
    () => {
      const cached = panel.sources.storage.cache.get(panel.sources.storage.path);
      if (cached) return Promise.resolve(cached);
      throw new Error('No cache available');
    },
    { source: 'panelStore', action: 'readDirectory', panelId }
  );

  if (result.success) {
    // Update store with result.data (may be from cache)
    set((state) => {
      const p = state.panels.find(p => p.id === panelId);
      if (p) {
        p.sources.storage.entries = result.data;
        if (!result.fromCache) {
          p.sources.storage.cache.set(p.sources.storage.path, result.data);
        }
      }
    });
  } else {
    // Show error in panel
    useErrorStore.getState().setPanelError(panelId, {
      id: 'read-error',
      message: result.error!,
      category: 'file_system',
      severity: 'error',
      timestamp: new Date(),
      canRetry: true,
    });
  }
}
```

## 8. Benefits

- **Automatic retries** for transient failures (network, timeouts, rate limits).
- **Exponential backoff** prevents overwhelming APIs.
- **Fallback to cache** when primary source fails.
- **Stale-while-revalidate** pattern for background updates.
- **Non-blocking UI** – retry happens in background.
- **Inline retry buttons** for user-initiated recovery.
- **Full integration** with errorHandler and eventBus.

This recovery engine makes the application resilient to network issues and API failures, providing a seamless user experience.

=======5==========

We'll implement a resource manager to control memory usage, manage cache limits, prioritize tasks, and debounce rapid operations.

## 1. Resource Manager Types (`src/types/resource.ts`)

```typescript
// src/types/resource.ts
export interface CacheLimits {
  maxEntriesPerPanel: number;
  maxTotalCacheSize: number; // bytes
  maxAge: number; // milliseconds
}

export interface TaskPriority {
  UI: 1;
  BACKGROUND: 2;
  LOW: 3;
}

export interface DebounceConfig {
  delay: number; // milliseconds
  maxWait: number; // milliseconds
}

export interface ResourceStats {
  totalCacheEntries: number;
  totalCacheSize: number;
  activeTasks: number;
  pendingTasks: number;
  memoryUsage: number; // estimated MB
}
```

## 2. Resource Manager Service (`src/services/resourceManager.ts`)

```typescript
// src/services/resourceManager.ts
import { CacheLimits, ResourceStats, DebounceConfig } from '@/types/resource';
import { eventBus } from '@/lib/eventBus';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';

const DEFAULT_CACHE_LIMITS: CacheLimits = {
  maxEntriesPerPanel: 100,
  maxTotalCacheSize: 50 * 1024 * 1024, // 50MB
  maxAge: 30 * 60 * 1000, // 30 minutes
};

class ResourceManager {
  private cacheLimits: CacheLimits = DEFAULT_CACHE_LIMITS;
  private debounceTimers: Map<string, NodeJS.Timeout> = new Map();
  private debounceLastRun: Map<string, number> = new Map();
  private cleanupInterval: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null;

  constructor() {
    this.startCleanupInterval();
  }

  startCleanupInterval() {
    this.cleanupInterval = setInterval(() => {
      this.cleanupUnusedCache();
    }, 5 * 60 * 1000); // Every 5 minutes
  }

  stopCleanupInterval() {
    if (this.cleanupInterval) clearInterval(this.cleanupInterval);
  }

  async cleanupUnusedCache() {
    const panels = usePanelStore.getState().panels;
    let totalSize = 0;
    let totalEntries = 0;

    for (const panel of panels) {
      const storageCache = panel.sources.storage.cache;
      if (storageCache) {
        // Remove expired entries
        const now = Date.now();
        for (const [path, entries] of storageCache.entries()) {
          // Simple size estimation (entries array length * avg entry size)
          const entrySize = JSON.stringify(entries).length;
          if (now - this.getCacheTimestamp(panel.id, path) > this.cacheLimits.maxAge) {
            storageCache.delete(path);
            eventBus.emit('CACHE_CLEANED', { panelId: panel.id, path, reason: 'expired' });
          } else {
            totalSize += entrySize;
            totalEntries++;
          }
        }

        // Limit entries per panel
        if (storageCache.size > this.cacheLimits.maxEntriesPerPanel) {
          const entriesToDelete = storageCache.size - this.cacheLimits.maxEntriesPerPanel;
          const iterator = storageCache.keys();
          for (let i = 0; i < entriesToDelete; i++) {
            const path = iterator.next().value;
            if (path) {
              storageCache.delete(path);
              eventBus.emit('CACHE_CLEANED', { panelId: panel.id, path, reason: 'limit_reached' });
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // Global size limit
    if (totalSize > this.cacheLimits.maxTotalCacheSize) {
      // Aggressive cleanup: clear oldest entries across all panels
      await this.aggressiveCleanup(totalSize - this.cacheLimits.maxTotalCacheSize);
    }

    eventBus.emit('CACHE_STATS_UPDATED', { totalEntries, totalSize });
  }

  private async aggressiveCleanup(excessBytes: number) {
    const panels = usePanelStore.getState().panels;
    let cleaned = 0;
    
    for (const panel of panels) {
      const storageCache = panel.sources.storage.cache;
      if (!storageCache) continue;
      
      // Sort entries by age (oldest first)
      const entries = Array.from(storageCache.entries());
      entries.sort((a, b) => this.getCacheTimestamp(panel.id, a[0]) - this.getCacheTimestamp(panel.id, b[0]));
      
      for (const [path, entriesData] of entries) {
        const size = JSON.stringify(entriesData).length;
        storageCache.delete(path);
        cleaned += size;
        eventBus.emit('CACHE_CLEANED', { panelId: panel.id, path, reason: 'global_limit' });
        if (cleaned >= excessBytes) break;
      }
    }
  }

  private getCacheTimestamp(panelId: string, path: string): number {
    // Store timestamps in a separate map (simplified)
    // In production, store alongside cache entries
    return Date.now(); // Placeholder
  }

  // Debounce for rapid operations (e.g., navigation)
  debounce(key: string, fn: () => void, config?: Partial<DebounceConfig>): void {
    const debounceConfig = { delay: 300, maxWait: 1000, ...config };
    
    const now = Date.now();
    const lastRun = this.debounceLastRun.get(key) || 0;
    
    if (now - lastRun >= debounceConfig.maxWait) {
      // Execute immediately if maxWait exceeded
      fn();
      this.debounceLastRun.set(key, now);
      return;
    }
    
    if (this.debounceTimers.has(key)) {
      clearTimeout(this.debounceTimers.get(key)!);
    }
    
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      fn();
      this.debounceLastRun.set(key, Date.now());
      this.debounceTimers.delete(key);
    }, debounceConfig.delay);
    
    this.debounceTimers.set(key, timer);
  }

  // Cancel pending debounce for a key
  cancelDebounce(key: string): void {
    if (this.debounceTimers.has(key)) {
      clearTimeout(this.debounceTimers.get(key)!);
      this.debounceTimers.delete(key);
    }
  }

  // Priority-based task execution
  async executeWithPriority<T>(
    task: () => Promise<T>,
    priority: 'UI' | 'BACKGROUND' | 'LOW',
    context: string
  ): Promise<T> {
    const priorityLevel = { UI: 1, BACKGROUND: 2, LOW: 3 };
    const level = priorityLevel[priority];
    
    // For UI tasks, run immediately
    if (level === 1) {
      return task();
    }
    
    // For background tasks, defer with setTimeout
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      setTimeout(async () => {
        try {
          const result = await task();
          resolve(result);
        } catch (error) {
          reject(error);
        }
      }, 0);
    });
  }

  // Get current resource stats
  getStats(): ResourceStats {
    const panels = usePanelStore.getState().panels;
    let totalCacheEntries = 0;
    let totalCacheSize = 0;
    
    for (const panel of panels) {
      const cache = panel.sources.storage.cache;
      if (cache) {
        totalCacheEntries += cache.size;
        for (const entries of cache.values()) {
          totalCacheSize += JSON.stringify(entries).length;
        }
      }
    }
    
    return {
      totalCacheEntries,
      totalCacheSize,
      activeTasks: 0, // Would need task store integration
      pendingTasks: 0,
      memoryUsage: totalCacheSize / (1024 * 1024), // MB
    };
  }

  updateCacheLimits(limits: Partial<CacheLimits>) {
    this.cacheLimits = { ...this.cacheLimits, ...limits };
    this.cleanupUnusedCache(); // Immediate cleanup
  }
}

export const resourceManager = new ResourceManager();
```

```typescript
  const pending = tasks
    .filter(t => t.status === 'pending')
    .sort((a, b) => {
```

## 6. React Hook: `useResourceManager`

```typescript
// src/hooks/useResourceManager.ts
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { resourceManager } from '@/services/resourceManager';
import { ResourceStats } from '@/types/resource';

export function useResourceManager() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<ResourceStats>(resourceManager.getStats());

  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      setStats(resourceManager.getStats());
    }, 10000); // Update every 10 seconds

    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, []);

  const cleanup = () => resourceManager.cleanupUnusedCache();
  const updateLimits = (limits: any) => resourceManager.updateCacheLimits(limits);
  const debounce = (key: string, fn: () => void, delay?: number) =>
    resourceManager.debounce(key, fn, { delay });

  return { stats, cleanup, updateLimits, debounce };
}
```

## 8. Benefits

- **Prevents memory leaks** – auto-cleans expired cache.
- **Per‑panel limits** – no single panel dominates memory.
- **UI responsiveness** – UI tasks always prioritized.
- **Debounced navigation** – prevents rapid spamming of file system reads.
- **Configurable** – limits can be adjusted at runtime.
- **Monitoring** – stats available for debugging.

This resource manager ensures the application remains performant even with many panels and large file structures.

=======6==========

We'll implement a basic permission system with per‑action validation, token masking, and sandbox restrictions.

## 1. Permission Types (`src/types/permission.ts`)

```typescript
// src/types/permission.ts
export type ActionType = 'delete' | 'move' | 'copy' | 'rename' | 'format' | 'dfol';

export interface PermissionCheck {
  action: ActionType;
  required: boolean;
  confirmMessage?: string;
  validation?: (context: PermissionContext) => Promise<boolean> | boolean;
}

export interface PermissionContext {
  panelId: string;
  sourceType: string;
  path: string;
  targetPath?: string;
  items: any[];
  userRole: 'admin' | 'user';
}

export interface SandboxRule {
  pattern: RegExp;
  allowed: boolean;
  message?: string;
}

export const DEFAULT_SANDBOX_RULES: SandboxRule[] = [
  { pattern: /^\/system\//, allowed: false, message: 'System directory access denied' },
  { pattern: /^\/etc\/shadow/, allowed: false, message: 'Sensitive file access denied' },
  { pattern: /^\/proc\//, allowed: false, message: 'Process directory access denied' },
  { pattern: /^\/dev\//, allowed: false, message: 'Device access denied' },
];
```

## 2. Permission Engine (`src/services/permissionEngine.ts`)

```typescript
// src/services/permissionEngine.ts
import { ActionType, PermissionContext, SandboxRule, DEFAULT_SANDBOX_RULES } from '@/types/permission';
import { useAuthStore } from '@/stores/authStore';

class PermissionEngine {
  private sandboxRules: SandboxRule[] = [...DEFAULT_SANDBOX_RULES];

  // Per-action permission requirements
  private actionPermissions: Record<ActionType, PermissionCheck> = {
    delete: {
      action: 'delete',
      required: true,
      confirmMessage: 'Are you sure you want to delete these items? This action cannot be undone.',
      validation: async (ctx) => {
        // Additional validation: e.g., prevent deleting system files
        for (const item of ctx.items) {
          if (item.path?.startsWith('/system/')) return false;
        }
        return true;
      }
    },
    move: {
      action: 'move',
      required: true,
      confirmMessage: 'Moving items may affect linked resources. Continue?',
      validation: async (ctx) => {
        // Prevent moving system files out of system directory
        for (const item of ctx.items) {
          if (item.path?.startsWith('/system/') && !ctx.targetPath?.startsWith('/system/')) {
            return false;
          }
        }
        return true;
      }
    },
    copy: {
      action: 'copy',
      required: false,
    },
    rename: {
      action: 'rename',
      required: false,
    },
    format: {
      action: 'format',
      required: true,
      confirmMessage: 'WARNING: Formatting will erase all data. Continue?',
      validation: async (ctx) => {
        // Only admin can format
        const { currentUser } = useAuthStore.getState();
        return currentUser?.role === 'admin';
      }
    },
    dfol: {
      action: 'dfol',
      required: false,
    }
  };

  async checkPermission(action: ActionType, context: PermissionContext): Promise<{ allowed: boolean; message?: string; needConfirm?: boolean }> {
    const permission = this.actionPermissions[action];
    if (!permission) return { allowed: true };

    // Check sandbox restrictions
    const sandboxCheck = this.checkSandbox(context);
    if (!sandboxCheck.allowed) {
      return { allowed: false, message: sandboxCheck.message };
    }

    // Check user role if needed
    if (action === 'format') {
      const { currentUser } = useAuthStore.getState();
      if (currentUser?.role !== 'admin') {
        return { allowed: false, message: 'Admin permission required for format operation' };
      }
    }

    // Run validation if exists
    if (permission.validation) {
      const valid = await permission.validation(context);
      if (!valid) {
        return { allowed: false, message: 'Validation failed: operation not allowed in this context' };
      }
    }

    // Require confirmation if needed
    if (permission.required) {
      return { allowed: true, needConfirm: true, message: permission.confirmMessage };
    }

    return { allowed: true };
  }

  private checkSandbox(context: PermissionContext): { allowed: boolean; message?: string } {
    // Check source path
    for (const rule of this.sandboxRules) {
      if (rule.pattern.test(context.path)) {
        return { allowed: rule.allowed, message: rule.message };
      }
      if (context.targetPath && rule.pattern.test(context.targetPath)) {
        return { allowed: rule.allowed, message: rule.message };
      }
      for (const item of context.items) {
        if (item.path && rule.pattern.test(item.path)) {
          return { allowed: rule.allowed, message: rule.message };
        }
      }
    }
    return { allowed: true };
  }

  // Token masking – never expose raw token in logs or UI
  maskToken(token: string): string {
    if (!token) return '';
    if (token.length <= 8) return '****';
    return token.slice(0, 4) + '****' + token.slice(-4);
  }

  // Add custom sandbox rule at runtime
  addSandboxRule(rule: SandboxRule) {
    this.sandboxRules.push(rule);
  }

  removeSandboxRule(pattern: RegExp) {
    this.sandboxRules = this.sandboxRules.filter(r => r.pattern.source !== pattern.source);
  }
}

export const permissionEngine = new PermissionEngine();
```

## 3. Integration with UnifiedEngine

Modify `UnifiedEngine.executeAction` to check permissions before executing:

```typescript
// In src/services/unifiedEngine.ts
import { permissionEngine } from './permissionEngine';
import { useAuthStore } from '@/stores/authStore';

async executeAction(request: ActionRequest, onProgress?: (progress: ActionProgress) => void): Promise<ActionResult> {
  // Build permission context
  const { currentUser } = useAuthStore.getState();
  const context = {
    panelId: request.source.panelId,
    sourceType: request.source.items[0]?.sourceType || 'storage',
    path: request.source.path,
    targetPath: request.target?.path,
    items: request.source.items,
    userRole: currentUser?.role || 'user',
  };

  // Check permission
  const permission = await permissionEngine.checkPermission(request.type, context);
  if (!permission.allowed) {
    throw new Error(permission.message || 'Permission denied');
  }

  // Show confirmation dialog if needed
  if (permission.needConfirm) {
    const confirmed = await this.showConfirmation(permission.message);
    if (!confirmed) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Operation cancelled', results: [] };
    }
  }

  // Proceed with action
  // ... existing execution logic
}
```

## 4. Confirmation Dialog Helper

Add a simple confirmation method to UnifiedEngine:

```typescript
private async showConfirmation(message?: string): Promise<boolean> {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    // Use a global confirmation modal or window.confirm for simplicity
    // In production, use a proper modal component
    const result = window.confirm(message || 'Are you sure?');
    resolve(result);
  });
}
```

## 5. Token Masking in Logs

Whenever logging tokens, use the mask:

```typescript
// Example in GitHub or Drive API calls
import { permissionEngine } from '@/services/permissionEngine';

console.log('Using token:', permissionEngine.maskToken(token));
```

## 6. React Hook: `usePermission`

```typescript
// src/hooks/usePermission.ts
import { useCallback } from 'react';
import { permissionEngine } from '@/services/permissionEngine';
import { ActionType, PermissionContext } from '@/types/permission';

export function usePermission() {
  const check = useCallback(async (action: ActionType, context: PermissionContext) => {
    return permissionEngine.checkPermission(action, context);
  }, []);

  const maskToken = useCallback((token: string) => {
    return permissionEngine.maskToken(token);
  }, []);

  return { check, maskToken };
}
```

## 7. Example Usage in UI

```tsx
// In a component that triggers delete
const { check } = usePermission();
const { executeAction } = useUnifiedEngine();

const handleDelete = async () => {
  const context = {
    panelId: 'panel-1',
    sourceType: 'storage',
    path: '/docs',
    items: selectedItems,
    userRole: 'user',
  };
  
  const permission = await check('delete', context);
  if (!permission.allowed) {
    toast.error(permission.message);
    return;
  }
  
  if (permission.needConfirm && !window.confirm(permission.message)) {
    return;
  }
  
  await executeAction({ type: 'delete', source: { ... } });
};
```

## 8. Benefits

- **Per‑action permissions** – delete requires confirmation, move has validation.
- **Sandbox protection** – blocks access to system directories.
- **Token masking** – prevents accidental exposure in logs.
- **Extensible** – easily add new actions or rules.
- **Integration ready** – works with UnifiedEngine and existing action flow.

This permission engine adds a critical safety layer to the application.

=======7==========

We'll integrate the Prompt Manager with the main system, enabling drag‑and‑drop from panels, storing file references, and uploading via UnifiedEngine.

## 1. Update PromptFileManager to Accept Drag‑Drop

```tsx
// src/components/PromptManager/PromptFileManager.tsx (additions)
import { useDrop } from 'react-dnd';
import { usePromptStore } from '@/stores/promptStore';

export function PromptFileManager() {
  const addDragDropFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.addDragDropFile);
  const currentSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.currentSession);

  const [{ isOver }, drop] = useDrop(() => ({
    accept: ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'],
    drop: (item: any, monitor) => {
      // item contains dragged file/folder info from main panels
      addDragDropFile(item, item.panelId);
    },
    collect: (monitor) => ({
      isOver: !!monitor.isOver(),
    }),
  }), [currentSession]);

  return (
    <div ref={drop} className={cn("flex-1 overflow-auto", isOver && "bg-accent/20")}>
      {/* existing file tree */}
    </div>
  );
}
```
