## src/services/healthMonitor.ts

```typescript
import { eventBus } from '@/lib/eventBus';
import { useTaskStore } from '@/stores/taskStore';
import { useErrorStore } from '@/stores/errorStore';

export interface HealthMetrics {
  apiFailures: {
    total: number;
    byEndpoint: Record<string, number>;
    lastFailure: Date | null;
  };
  retries: {
    total: number;
    successful: number;
    failed: number;
  };
  memoryUsage: {
    jsHeapSizeLimit: number;
    totalJSHeapSize: number;
    usedJSHeapSize: number;
    percentage: number;
  };
  activeTasks: number;
  pendingTasks: number;
  completedTasks: number;
  failedTasks: number;
  uptime: number; // seconds
  lastHeartbeat: Date;
}

class HealthMonitor {
  private metrics: HealthMetrics = {
    apiFailures: { total: 0, byEndpoint: {}, lastFailure: null },
    retries: { total: 0, successful: 0, failed: 0 },
    memoryUsage: { jsHeapSizeLimit: 0, totalJSHeapSize: 0, usedJSHeapSize: 0, percentage: 0 },
    activeTasks: 0,
    pendingTasks: 0,
    completedTasks: 0,
    failedTasks: 0,
    uptime: 0,
    lastHeartbeat: new Date(),
  };
  private startTime = Date.now();
  private listeners: Array<(metrics: HealthMetrics) => void> = [];
  private intervalId: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null;

  constructor() {
    this.setupEventListeners();
    this.startMonitoring();
  }

  private setupEventListeners(): void {
    // Listen for API failures
    eventBus.on('API_FAILURE', (data: any) => {
      this.metrics.apiFailures.total++;
      const endpoint = data.endpoint || 'unknown';
      this.metrics.apiFailures.byEndpoint[endpoint] = (this.metrics.apiFailures.byEndpoint[endpoint] || 0) + 1;
      this.metrics.apiFailures.lastFailure = new Date();
      this.notifyListeners();
    });

    // Listen for retry events
    eventBus.on('RETRY_ATTEMPT', (data: any) => {
      this.metrics.retries.total++;
    });
    eventBus.on('RETRY_SUCCESS', () => {
      this.metrics.retries.successful++;
      this.notifyListeners();
    });
    eventBus.on('RETRY_FAILED', () => {
      this.metrics.retries.failed++;
      this.notifyListeners();
    });

    // Listen for task events to update counts
    eventBus.on('TASK_STARTED', () => {
      this.updateTaskStats();
    });
    eventBus.on('TASK_COMPLETED', () => {
      this.updateTaskStats();
    });
    eventBus.on('TASK_FAILED', () => {
      this.updateTaskStats();
    });
  }

  private updateTaskStats(): void {
    const taskStore = useTaskStore.getState();
    const tasks = taskStore.tasks || [];
    this.metrics.activeTasks = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'running').length;
    this.metrics.pendingTasks = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'pending').length;
    this.metrics.completedTasks = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'completed').length;
    this.metrics.failedTasks = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'failed').length;
    this.notifyListeners();
  }

  private updateMemoryUsage(): void {
    if ('memory' in performance && (performance as any).memory) {
      const memory = (performance as any).memory;
      this.metrics.memoryUsage = {
        jsHeapSizeLimit: memory.jsHeapSizeLimit,
        totalJSHeapSize: memory.totalJSHeapSize,
        usedJSHeapSize: memory.usedJSHeapSize,
        percentage: (memory.usedJSHeapSize / memory.jsHeapSizeLimit) * 100,
      };
    } else {
      this.metrics.memoryUsage = {
        jsHeapSizeLimit: 0,
        totalJSHeapSize: 0,
        usedJSHeapSize: 0,
        percentage: 0,
      };
    }
  }

  private startMonitoring(): void {
    this.intervalId = setInterval(() => {
      this.updateMemoryUsage();
      this.metrics.uptime = (Date.now() - this.startTime) / 1000;
      this.metrics.lastHeartbeat = new Date();
      this.notifyListeners();
    }, 5000); // every 5 seconds
  }

  private notifyListeners(): void {
    this.listeners.forEach(listener => listener(this.getMetrics()));
  }

  getMetrics(): HealthMetrics {
    return { ...this.metrics };
  }

  subscribe(listener: (metrics: HealthMetrics) => void): () => void {
    this.listeners.push(listener);
    listener(this.getMetrics()); // initial
    return () => {
      const index = this.listeners.indexOf(listener);
      if (index !== -1) this.listeners.splice(index, 1);
    };
  }

  stop(): void {
    if (this.intervalId) clearInterval(this.intervalId);
  }
}

export const healthMonitor = new HealthMonitor();
```

## src/components/Dev/DevPanel.tsx

```tsx
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { healthMonitor, HealthMetrics } from '@/services/healthMonitor';
import { useTaskStore } from '@/stores/taskStore';
import { useErrorStore } from '@/stores/errorStore';
import { X, Activity, HardDrive, AlertCircle, RefreshCw, Server, Cpu } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export function DevPanel() {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [metrics, setMetrics] = useState<HealthMetrics>(healthMonitor.getMetrics());
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<any[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const unsubscribe = healthMonitor.subscribe(setMetrics);
    const loadErrors = () => {
      const errorStore = useErrorStore.getState();
      setErrors(errorStore.globalErrors || []);
    };
    const loadTasks = () => {
      const taskStore = useTaskStore.getState();
      setTasks(taskStore.tasks || []);
    };
    loadErrors();
    loadTasks();
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      loadErrors();
      loadTasks();
    }, 2000);
    return () => {
      unsubscribe();
      clearInterval(interval);
    };
  }, []);

  if (!isOpen) {
    return (
      <button
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(true)}
        className="fixed bottom-4 left-4 z-50 bg-primary text-primary-foreground p-2 rounded-full shadow-lg hover:bg-primary/90 transition-colors"
        title="Dev Panel"
      >
        <Activity className="w-5 h-5" />
      </button>
    );
  }

  const memoryPercent = metrics.memoryUsage.percentage;
  const memoryColor = memoryPercent > 80 ? 'text-destructive' : memoryPercent > 60 ? 'text-yellow-500' : 'text-green-500';

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/50 flex items-start justify-end p-4">
      <div className="w-[500px] h-[90vh] bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border bg-muted/50">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Server className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
            <h3 className="font-semibold">System Health Monitor</h3>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Debug Mode</span>
          </div>
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}>
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>

        <ScrollArea className="flex-1 p-4 space-y-4">
          {/* Memory Usage */}
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <Cpu className="w-4 h-4" />
                <span className="text-sm font-medium">Memory Usage</span>
              </div>
              <span className={cn("text-sm font-mono", memoryColor)}>
                {Math.round(memoryPercent)}%
              </span>
            </div>
            <Progress value={memoryPercent} className="h-2" />
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              <span>Used: {(metrics.memoryUsage.usedJSHeapSize / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(1)} MB</span>
              <span>Total: {(metrics.memoryUsage.totalJSHeapSize / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(1)} MB</span>
              <span>Limit: {(metrics.memoryUsage.jsHeapSizeLimit / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(1)} MB</span>
              <span>Uptime: {Math.floor(metrics.uptime / 60)}m {Math.floor(metrics.uptime % 60)}s</span>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* API Failures */}
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />
              <span className="text-sm font-medium">API Failures</span>
              <span className="text-xs bg-destructive/10 text-destructive px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">
                Total: {metrics.apiFailures.total}
              </span>
            </div>
            {metrics.apiFailures.lastFailure && (
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                Last failure: {metrics.apiFailures.lastFailure.toLocaleTimeString()}
              </p>
            )}
            <div className="max-h-32 overflow-auto space-y-1">
              {Object.entries(metrics.apiFailures.byEndpoint).slice(0, 5).map(([endpoint, count]) => (
                <div key={endpoint} className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span className="font-mono truncate">{endpoint}</span>
                  <span>{count}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Retries */}
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <RefreshCw className="w-4 h-4" />
              <span className="text-sm font-medium">Retries</span>
            </div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 text-center">
              <div className="p-2 bg-muted rounded">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold">{metrics.retries.total}</div>
                <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Total</div>
              </div>
              <div className="p-2 bg-green-500/10 rounded">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-green-500">{metrics.retries.successful}</div>
                <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Successful</div>
              </div>
              <div className="p-2 bg-destructive/10 rounded">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-destructive">{metrics.retries.failed}</div>
                <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Failed</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Tasks */}
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <Activity className="w-4 h-4" />
              <span className="text-sm font-medium">Tasks</span>
            </div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 text-center">
              <div className="p-2 bg-muted rounded">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold">{metrics.activeTasks}</div>
                <div className="text-xs">Active</div>
              </div>
              <div className="p-2 bg-yellow-500/10 rounded">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold">{metrics.pendingTasks}</div>
                <div className="text-xs">Pending</div>
              </div>
              <div className="p-2 bg-green-500/10 rounded">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold">{metrics.completedTasks}</div>
                <div className="text-xs">Completed</div>
              </div>
              <div className="p-2 bg-destructive/10 rounded">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold">{metrics.failedTasks}</div>
                <div className="text-xs">Failed</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Recent Errors */}
          {errors.length > 0 && (
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />
                <span className="text-sm font-medium">Recent Errors</span>
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-1 max-h-40 overflow-auto">
                {errors.slice(0, 5).map((err) => (
                  <div key={err.id} className="p-2 bg-destructive/5 rounded text-xs">

                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </ScrollArea>

        <div className="p-3 border-t border-border text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center">
          Last heartbeat: {metrics.lastHeartbeat.toLocaleTimeString()}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## src/lib/errorFormatter.ts

```typescript
export interface FormattedError {
  title: string;
  message: string;
  action?: string;
  retryable: boolean;
}

export function formatError(error: any): FormattedError {
  const message = error?.message || error?.toString() || 'Unknown error';
  const lowerMsg = message.toLowerCase();

  // Network errors
  if (lowerMsg.includes('network') || lowerMsg.includes('fetch') || lowerMsg.includes('offline')) {
    return {
      title: 'Network Error',
      message: 'Unable to connect to the server. Please check your internet connection.',
      action: 'Retry',
      retryable: true,
    };
  }

  // Permission errors
  if (lowerMsg.includes('permission') || lowerMsg.includes('access denied') || lowerMsg.includes('403')) {
    return {
      title: 'Permission Denied',
      message: 'You don\'t have permission to perform this action. Please check your access rights.',
      action: 'Request Access',
      retryable: false,
    };
  }

  // Authentication errors
  if (lowerMsg.includes('auth') || lowerMsg.includes('login') || lowerMsg.includes('401') || lowerMsg.includes('unauthorized')) {
    return {
      title: 'Authentication Required',
      message: 'Your session has expired or you are not logged in. Please log in again.',
      action: 'Log In',
      retryable: true,
    };
  }

  // Quota errors
  if (lowerMsg.includes('quota') || lowerMsg.includes('limit') || lowerMsg.includes('429')) {
    return {
      title: 'Rate Limit Exceeded',
      message: 'You\'ve reached the API rate limit. Please wait a moment and try again.',
      action: 'Wait',
      retryable: true,
    };
  }

  // File not found
  if (lowerMsg.includes('not found') || lowerMsg.includes('404')) {
    return {
      title: 'File Not Found',
      message: 'The file or folder you\'re trying to access no longer exists.',
      action: 'Refresh',
      retryable: true,
    };
  }

  // Quota full (storage)
  if (lowerMsg.includes('quota exceeded') || lowerMsg.includes('storage full')) {
    return {
      title: 'Storage Full',
      message: 'Your storage quota is full. Please free up some space or upgrade your plan.',
      action: 'Manage Storage',
      retryable: false,
    };
  }

  // Default
  return {
    title: 'Something went wrong',
    message: message.length > 100 ? message.substring(0, 100) + '...' : message,
    action: 'Try Again',
    retryable: true,
  };
}
```

## src/components/UI/Toast.tsx

```tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { X, CheckCircle, AlertCircle, Info, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export type ToastType = 'success' | 'error' | 'info' | 'warning';

interface ToastProps {
  id: string;
  type: ToastType;
  title: string;
  message?: string;
  duration?: number;
  onClose: (id: string) => void;
}

const icons = {
  success: <CheckCircle className="w-5 h-5 text-green-500" />,
  error: <AlertCircle className="w-5 h-5 text-destructive" />,
  info: <Info className="w-5 h-5 text-blue-500" />,
  warning: <AlertTriangle className="w-5 h-5 text-yellow-500" />,
};

const bgColors = {
  success: 'bg-green-50 dark:bg-green-950/20 border-green-200',
  error: 'bg-destructive/10 border-destructive/20',
  info: 'bg-blue-50 dark:bg-blue-950/20 border-blue-200',
  warning: 'bg-yellow-50 dark:bg-yellow-950/20 border-yellow-200',
};

export function Toast({ id, type, title, message, duration = 5000, onClose }: ToastProps) {
  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      setIsVisible(false);
      setTimeout(() => onClose(id), 300);
    }, duration);
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [duration, id, onClose]);

  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'flex items-start gap-3 p-4 rounded-lg shadow-lg border transition-all duration-300 transform',
        bgColors[type],
        isVisible ? 'opacity-100 translate-x-0' : 'opacity-0 translate-x-full'
      )}
    >
      {icons[type]}
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <p className="text-sm font-medium">{title}</p>
        {message && <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">{message}</p>}
      </div>
      <button onClick={() => onClose(id)} className="shrink-0 opacity-50 hover:opacity-100">
        <X className="w-4 h-4" />
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

export function ToastContainer() {
  const [toasts, setToasts] = useState<Array<ToastProps & { id: string }>>([]);

  const addToast = (toast: Omit<ToastProps, 'id' | 'onClose'>) => {
    const id = Date.now().toString();
    setToasts(prev => [...prev, { ...toast, id, onClose: (id) => removeToast(id) }]);
  };

  const removeToast = (id: string) => {
    setToasts(prev => prev.filter(t => t.id !== id));
  };

  // Expose method globally for easy access
  useEffect(() => {
    (window as any).showToast = addToast;
    return () => { delete (window as any).showToast; };
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="fixed top-4 right-4 z-50 flex flex-col gap-2 max-w-sm">
      {toasts.map(toast => (
        <Toast key={toast.id} {...toast} />
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

## src/components/UI/Skeleton.tsx

```tsx
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface SkeletonProps {
  className?: string;
  count?: number;
}

export function Skeleton({ className, count = 1 }: SkeletonProps) {
  const items = Array.from({ length: count }, (_, i) => (
    <div key={i} className={cn('animate-pulse bg-muted rounded', className)} />
  ));
  return count === 1 ? items[0] : <div className="space-y-2">{items}</div>;
}

export function FileListSkeleton() {
  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-2">
        <Skeleton className="col-span-6 h-4" />
        <Skeleton className="col-span-2 h-4" />
        <Skeleton className="col-span-4 h-4" />
      </div>
      {Array.from({ length: 5 }).map((_, i) => (
        <div key={i} className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-2 px-3 py-3">
          <Skeleton className="col-span-6 h-5" />
          <Skeleton className="col-span-2 h-5" />
          <Skeleton className="col-span-4 h-5" />
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

export function FileGridSkeleton() {
  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-3 p-3">
      {Array.from({ length: 8 }).map((_, i) => (
        <div key={i} className="flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card">
          <Skeleton className="w-10 h-10 rounded-lg mb-2" />
          <Skeleton className="w-3/4 h-4 mt-1" />
          <Skeleton className="w-1/2 h-3 mt-1" />
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

export function PanelSkeleton() {
  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">

          <Skeleton className="w-8 h-8 rounded" />
          <Skeleton className="w-32 h-5" />
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
        <Skeleton className="h-10 w-full" />
        <Skeleton className="h-10 w-full" />
        <Skeleton className="h-10 w-full" />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## src/hooks/useToast.ts

```typescript
import { useCallback } from 'react';

export function useToast() {
  const showToast = useCallback((
    type: 'success' | 'error' | 'info' | 'warning',
    title: string,
    message?: string
  ) => {
    if ((window as any).showToast) {
      (window as any).showToast({ type, title, message });
    } else {
      console.log(`[Toast] ${type}: ${title}`, message);
    }
  }, []);

  const success = useCallback((title: string, message?: string) => {
    showToast('success', title, message);
  }, [showToast]);

  const error = useCallback((title: string, message?: string) => {
    showToast('error', title, message);
  }, [showToast]);

  const info = useCallback((title: string, message?: string) => {
    showToast('info', title, message);
  }, [showToast]);

  const warning = useCallback((title: string, message?: string) => {
    showToast('warning', title, message);
  }, [showToast]);

  return { showToast, success, error, info, warning };
}
```

## Global error handling with toasts

```tsx
// In App.tsx or a global component
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { eventBus } from '@/lib/eventBus';
import { useToast } from '@/hooks/useToast';
import { formatError } from '@/lib/errorFormatter';

function GlobalErrorListener() {
  const { error: showError } = useToast();

  useEffect(() => {
    const unsub = eventBus.on('ERROR_OCCURRED', (data: any) => {
      const formatted = formatError(data.error || data);
      showError(formatted.title, formatted.message);
    });
    return unsub;
  }, [showError]);

  return null;
}
```

## Success feedback for actions

```tsx
// In actionEngine or unifiedEngine, after successful operation:
eventBus.emit('ACTION_COMPLETED', { type, items, result });
// Then in global listener:
eventBus.on('ACTION_COMPLETED', (data) => {
  showToast('success', `${data.type} completed`, `${data.items.length} item(s) processed`);
});
```

This comprehensive UX polish ensures smooth interactions, clear feedback, and professional error handling.

## src/tests/stressTestRunner.ts

```typescript
import { storageAdapter } from '@/lib/adapters/storageAdapter';
import { driveAdapter } from '@/lib/adapters/driveAdapter';
import { createGitHubAdapter } from '@/lib/adapters/githubAdapter';
import { unifiedEngine } from '@/services/unifiedEngine';
import { transactionManager } from '@/lib/transactionManager';
import { eventBus } from '@/lib/eventBus';

export interface StressTestConfig {
  operations: number;        // total operations to attempt
  adapters: ('storage' | 'drive' | 'github')[];
  failureRate: number;       // 0-1, probability of simulated failure
  concurrency: number;       // number of parallel operations
  verbose?: boolean;         // log each operation
}

export interface StressTestResult {
  totalOperations: number;
  succeeded: number;
  failed: number;
  rolledBack: number;
  rollbackSuccess: number;
  rollbackFailed: number;
  totalTimeMs: number;
  averageTimePerOpMs: number;
  errors: Array<{ operation: string; error: string }>;
  perAdapter: Record<string, { succeeded: number; failed: number }>;
}

class StressTestRunner {
  private config: StressTestConfig;
  private results: StressTestResult;
  private adapters: Map<string, any> = new Map();

  constructor(config: StressTestConfig) {
    this.config = config;
    this.results = {
      totalOperations: 0,
      succeeded: 0,
      failed: 0,
      rolledBack: 0,
      rollbackSuccess: 0,
      rollbackFailed: 0,
      totalTimeMs: 0,
      averageTimePerOpMs: 0,
      errors: [],
      perAdapter: {},
    };
  }

  private async initAdapters(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.config.adapters.includes('storage')) {
      // Storage adapter doesn't need auth but we need a root directory
      if (!storageAdapter.isAuthenticated()) {
        console.log('Please select a root directory for storage adapter...');
        await storageAdapter.authenticate();
      }
      this.adapters.set('storage', storageAdapter);
      this.results.perAdapter.storage = { succeeded: 0, failed: 0 };
    }
    if (this.config.adapters.includes('drive')) {
      if (!driveAdapter.isAuthenticated()) {
        console.log('Authenticating with Google Drive...');
        await driveAdapter.authenticate();
      }
      this.adapters.set('drive', driveAdapter);
      this.results.perAdapter.drive = { succeeded: 0, failed: 0 };
    }
    if (this.config.adapters.includes('github')) {
      const githubAdapter = createGitHubAdapter();
      if (!githubAdapter.isAuthenticated()) {
        console.log('Authenticating with GitHub...');
        await githubAdapter.authenticate();
      }
      this.adapters.set('github', githubAdapter);
      this.results.perAdapter.github = { succeeded: 0, failed: 0 };
    }
  }

  private randomElement<T>(arr: T[]): T {
    return arr[Math.floor(Math.random() * arr.length)];
  }

  private randomString(prefix = 'test'): string {
    return `${prefix}_${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 8)}`;
  }

  private shouldFail(): boolean {
    return Math.random() < this.config.failureRate;
  }

  private async simulateOperation(adapterName: string, adapter: any): Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string; rolledBack?: boolean }> {
    const operationType = this.randomElement(['upload', 'createFolder', 'delete', 'rename', 'move']);
    const fileName = this.randomString('file');
    const folderName = this.randomString('folder');

    try {
      // Simulate failure before operation
      if (this.shouldFail()) {
        throw new Error('Simulated random failure');
      }

      let result;
      switch (operationType) {
        case 'upload':
          const content = new Blob([`Test content ${Date.now()}`], { type: 'text/plain' });
          result = await adapter.uploadFile({ name: fileName, content, parentPath: '/' });
          break;
        case 'createFolder':
          result = await adapter.createFolder({ name: folderName, parentPath: '/' });
          break;
        case 'delete':
          // First list files to get an existing file
          const entries = await adapter.listFiles('/');
          const existingFile = entries.find(e => e.type === 'file');
          if (existingFile) {
            await adapter.deleteFile(existingFile.id);
          } else {
            // No file to delete, treat as success
          }
          break;
        case 'rename':
          const list = await adapter.listFiles('/');
          const toRename = list.find(e => e.type === 'file');
          if (toRename) {
            const newName = this.randomString('renamed');
            await adapter.renameFile(toRename.id, newName);
          }
          break;
        case 'move':
          const files = await adapter.listFiles('/');
          const fileToMove = files.find(e => e.type === 'file');
          const folders = files.find(e => e.type === 'directory');
          if (fileToMove && folders && folders.id !== fileToMove.parentId) {
            await adapter.moveFile(fileToMove.id, folders.id);
          }
          break;
      }
      return { success: true };
    } catch (err) {
      // If error occurred, attempt rollback (if within transaction)
      const errorMsg = (err as Error).message;
      return { success: false, error: errorMsg };
    }
  }

  private async runOperation(adapterName: string, adapter: any, index: number): Promise<void> {
    const start = performance.now();
    const result = await this.simulateOperation(adapterName, adapter);
    const duration = performance.now() - start;

    if (result.success) {
      this.results.succeeded++;
      this.results.perAdapter[adapterName].succeeded++;
    } else {
      this.results.failed++;
      this.results.perAdapter[adapterName].failed++;
      this.results.errors.push({
        operation: `${adapterName}_op_${index}`,
        error: result.error || 'Unknown error',
      });
      if (result.rolledBack) {
        this.results.rolledBack++;
        if (result.rolledBack === true) this.results.rollbackSuccess++;
        else this.results.rollbackFailed++;
      }
    }
    this.results.totalTimeMs += duration;
    if (this.config.verbose) {
      console.log(`[${index}] ${adapterName}: ${result.success ? '✓' : '✗'} (${duration.toFixed(0)}ms)`);
    }
  }

  async run(): Promise<StressTestResult> {
    console.log(`Starting stress test: ${this.config.operations} operations, failure rate ${this.config.failureRate * 100}%`);
    const globalStart = performance.now();

    await this.initAdapters();

    const operations: Promise<void>[] = [];
    const adapterList = Array.from(this.adapters.entries());

    for (let i = 0; i < this.config.operations; i++) {
      const [adapterName, adapter] = this.randomElement(adapterList);
      const opPromise = this.runOperation(adapterName, adapter, i);
      operations.push(opPromise);

      // Control concurrency
      if (operations.length >= this.config.concurrency) {
        await Promise.race(operations);
        // Remove completed promises
        while (operations.length > 0 && (await Promise.race(operations.map(p => p.then(() => true, () => true)))) {
          const index = operations.findIndex(p => p === operations[0]);
          if (index !== -1) operations.splice(index, 1);
        }
      }
    }

    // Wait for all remaining
    await Promise.all(operations);

    const totalTime = performance.now() - globalStart;
    this.results.totalTimeMs = totalTime;
    this.results.averageTimePerOpMs = totalTime / this.config.operations;
    this.results.totalOperations = this.config.operations;

    console.log('\n=== STRESS TEST RESULTS ===');
    console.log(`Total operations: ${this.results.totalOperations}`);
    console.log(`Succeeded: ${this.results.succeeded} (${((this.results.succeeded / this.results.totalOperations) * 100).toFixed(1)}%)`);
    console.log(`Failed: ${this.results.failed} (${((this.results.failed / this.results.totalOperations) * 100).toFixed(1)}%)`);
    console.log(`Rollbacks attempted: ${this.results.rolledBack}, successful: ${this.results.rollbackSuccess}, failed: ${this.results.rollbackFailed}`);
    console.log(`Total time: ${(totalTime / 1000).toFixed(2)}s`);
    console.log(`Avg time per op: ${this.results.averageTimePerOpMs.toFixed(2)}ms`);
    console.log('\nPer adapter:');
    for (const [adapter, stats] of Object.entries(this.results.perAdapter)) {
      console.log(`  ${adapter}: ${stats.succeeded} success, ${stats.failed} fails`);
    }
    if (this.results.errors.length > 0) {
      console.log(`\nFirst 5 errors:`);
      this.results.errors.slice(0, 5).forEach(e => console.log(`  ${e.operation}: ${e.error}`));
    }

    return this.results;
  }
}

export async function runStressTest(config: Partial<StressTestConfig> = {}): Promise<StressTestResult> {
  const defaultConfig: StressTestConfig = {
    operations: 1000,
    adapters: ['storage', 'drive', 'github'],
    failureRate: 0.1,
    concurrency: 10,
    verbose: false,
  };
  const finalConfig = { ...defaultConfig, ...config };
  const runner = new StressTestRunner(finalConfig);
  return runner.run();
}

// For quick testing in browser console:
// import { runStressTest } from './stressTestRunner';
// runStressTest({ operations: 100, verbose: true });
```

This stress testing system:

- Supports mixed adapters (storage, drive, github)
- Randomly performs upload, createFolder, delete, rename, move operations
- Simulates failures with configurable rate
- Tracks success, failure, rollback success/failure
- Reports per-adapter statistics and timing
- Respects concurrency limit to avoid overwhelming the system
- Can be run from browser console for quick validation

## src/lib/errorClassifier.ts

```typescript
export type ErrorCategory = 
  | 'network' 
  | 'auth' 
  | 'permission' 
  | 'quota' 
  | 'not_found' 
  | 'conflict' 
  | 'system_bug'
  | 'unknown';

export interface ClassifiedError {
  originalError: any;
  category: ErrorCategory;
  message: string;           // user-friendly message
  technicalMessage?: string; // original error for logging
  action: 'retry' | 'reauthenticate' | 'request_access' | 'free_space' | 'contact_support' | 'none';
  retryable: boolean;
  severity: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical';
}

class ErrorClassifier {
  classify(error: any): ClassifiedError {
    const original = error;
    const message = error?.message || error?.toString() || 'Unknown error';
    const lowerMsg = message.toLowerCase();
    const status = error?.status || error?.statusCode || error?.response?.status;

    // Network errors
    if (
      lowerMsg.includes('network') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('fetch') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('offline') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('timeout') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('failed to fetch') ||
      status === 0 ||
      status === 502 ||
      status === 503 ||
      status === 504
    ) {
      return {
        originalError: error,
        category: 'network',
        message: 'Network connection issue. Please check your internet and try again.',
        technicalMessage: message,
        action: 'retry',
        retryable: true,
        severity: 'medium',
      };
    }

    // Authentication errors
    if (
      lowerMsg.includes('auth') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('login') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('unauthorized') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('token') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('expired') ||
      status === 401
    ) {
      return {
        originalError: error,
        category: 'auth',
        message: 'Your session has expired or you are not logged in. Please log in again.',
        technicalMessage: message,
        action: 'reauthenticate',
        retryable: true,
        severity: 'high',
      };
    }

    // Permission errors
    if (
      lowerMsg.includes('permission') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('access denied') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('forbidden') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('not allowed') ||
      status === 403
    ) {
      return {
        originalError: error,
        category: 'permission',
        message: 'You don\'t have permission to perform this action. Please check your access rights.',
        technicalMessage: message,
        action: 'request_access',
        retryable: false,
        severity: 'high',
      };
    }

    // Quota / rate limit errors
    if (
      lowerMsg.includes('quota') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('rate limit') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('too many requests') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('storage full') ||
      status === 429 ||
      status === 507
    ) {
      const isStorage = lowerMsg.includes('storage') || lowerMsg.includes('quota exceeded');
      return {
        originalError: error,
        category: 'quota',
        message: isStorage 
          ? 'Your storage is full. Please free up space or upgrade your plan.'
          : 'Too many requests. Please wait a moment and try again.',
        technicalMessage: message,
        action: isStorage ? 'free_space' : 'retry',
        retryable: isStorage ? false : true,
        severity: 'medium',
      };
    }

    // Not found errors
    if (
      lowerMsg.includes('not found') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('does not exist') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('no such') ||
      status === 404
    ) {
      return {
        originalError: error,
        category: 'not_found',
        message: 'The file or folder you were trying to access no longer exists.',
        technicalMessage: message,
        action: 'none',
        retryable: false,
        severity: 'low',
      };
    }

    // Conflict errors (file already exists, etc.)
    if (
      lowerMsg.includes('already exists') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('conflict') ||
      status === 409
    ) {
      return {
        originalError: error,
        category: 'conflict',
        message: 'A file with the same name already exists. Choose a different name or overwrite.',
        technicalMessage: message,
        action: 'retry', // user will rename
        retryable: true,
        severity: 'low',
      };
    }

    // System bugs (unexpected errors)
    if (
      lowerMsg.includes('undefined') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('null') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('cannot read property') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('typeerror') ||
      lowerMsg.includes('referenceerror')
    ) {
      return {
        originalError: error,
        category: 'system_bug',
        message: 'An internal error occurred. Please refresh the page and try again.',
        technicalMessage: message,
        action: 'contact_support',
        retryable: true,
        severity: 'critical',
      };
    }

    // Unknown
    return {
      originalError: error,
      category: 'unknown',
      message: 'Something went wrong. Please try again later.',
      technicalMessage: message,
      action: 'contact_support',
      retryable: true,
      severity: 'medium',
    };
  }

  // Helper to get user action text
  getActionText(action: ClassifiedError['action']): string {
    switch (action) {
      case 'retry': return 'Retry';
      case 'reauthenticate': return 'Log In';
      case 'request_access': return 'Request Access';
      case 'free_space': return 'Manage Storage';
      case 'contact_support': return 'Contact Support';
      default: return 'OK';
    }
  }
}

export const errorClassifier = new ErrorClassifier();
```

## Integration with existing error handling

Update `errorHandler.ts` to use the classifier:

```typescript
// In errorHandler.ts capture method
import { errorClassifier } from './errorClassifier';

async capture(error: Omit<AppError, 'id' | 'timestamp'>): Promise<AppError> {
  const classified = errorClassifier.classify(error.originalError || error);
  const enhancedError: AppError = {
    ...error,
    category: classified.category,
    message: classified.message,
    // keep original message in metadata
    metadata: { 
      ...error.metadata,
      technicalMessage: classified.technicalMessage,
      action: classified.action,
    },
    severity: classified.severity as any,
  };
  // ... rest
}
```

## Use in UI to show appropriate action buttons

In error components, use `errorClassifier.getActionText(classified.action)` to show the right button label.

This provides intelligent error classification with user-friendly messages and suggested actions.

## 🔴 CRITICAL FIXES REQUIRED

### 1. Memory Leaks

**EventEmitter Cleanup (HIGH)**
```typescript
// BEFORE (Leaks):
useEffect(() => {
  healthMonitor.on('health:check', updateHealth);
}, []);

// AFTER (Fixed):
useEffect(() => {
  const handler = () => setHealth(healthMonitor.getSystemHealth());
  healthMonitor.on('health:check', handler);
  return () => healthMonitor.off('health:check', handler);
}, []);
```

**IndexedDB Connection Pool (HIGH)**
```typescript
class IndexedDBManager {
  private db: IDBPDatabase | null = null;
  private readonly MAX_CONNECTIONS = 3;
  private connectionCount = 0;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.connectionCount >= this.MAX_CONNECTIONS) {
      await this.close();
    }
    // ... open logic
    document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', () => {
      if (document.hidden) this.close();
    });
  }
}
```

**Retry Engine Cleanup (HIGH)**
```typescript
class RetryEngine {
  private timeoutId?: NodeJS.Timeout;
  private abortController = new AbortController();
  
  cancel(): void {
    if (this.timeoutId) clearTimeout(this.timeoutId);
    this.abortController.abort();
  }
}
```

### 2. Security Vulnerabilities

**PKCE for OAuth (CRITICAL)**  
```typescript
// Backend - Add to OAuth flow
function generatePKCE() {
  const verifier = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('base64url');
  const challenge = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(verifier).digest('base64url');
  return { verifier, challenge, method: 'S256' };
}

// Token endpoint
router.post('/token', async (req, res) => {
  const { code, code_verifier } = req.body;
  const stored = await getPKCE(req.body.state);
  
  const hash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(code_verifier).digest('base64url');
  if (hash !== stored.challenge) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'invalid_grant' });
  }
  // ... proceed
});
```

**Token Storage Security (CRITICAL)**  
```typescript
// Use BFF pattern - tokens ONLY in httpOnly cookies
// Backend:
res.cookie('access_token', token, {
  httpOnly: true,
  secure: true,
  sameSite: 'strict',
  maxAge: 900000 // 15 min
});
```

**Rate Limiting (HIGH)**
```typescript
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';

const proxyLimiter = rateLimit({
  store: new RedisStore({ client: redis }),
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 100,
  keyGenerator: (req) => req.body.userId || req.ip
});

router.use('/proxy', proxyLimiter);
```

**SQL Injection Prevention (CRITICAL)**
```typescript
// NEVER:
await db.query(`SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = '${userId}'`);

// ALWAYS:
await db.query('SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = $1', [userId]);
```

**Input Validation (HIGH)**

```typescript
const Schema = z.object({

});

router.post('/connections', (req, res) => {

  if (!result.success) return res.status(400).json(result.error);
  // ...
});
```

### 3. Performance Fixes

**Memoization**
```typescript
const filteredResults = useMemo(() => 
  results.filter(r => r.status === 'active'),
  [results]
);

// Shallow equality for objects
const { user, settings } = useStore(
  state => ({ user: state.user, settings: state.settings }),
  shallow
);
```

**Chunked IndexedDB Operations**
```typescript
async function batchProcess<T>(items: T[], batchSize = 100) {
  for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i += batchSize) {
    const batch = items.slice(i, i + batchSize);
    await processBatch(batch);
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 0)); // Yield
  }
}
```

**Zustand State Slicing**
```typescript
// Bad - causes re-render on any state change
const state = useStore();

// Good - only re-renders when count changes
const count = useStore(state => state.count);
```

### 4. UX Improvements

**Error Boundaries**
```typescript
class ErrorBoundary extends React.Component {
  state = { hasError: false };
  
  static getDerivedStateFromError() {
    return { hasError: true };
  }
  
  render() {
    if (this.state.hasError) return <FallbackUI />;
    return this.props.children;
  }
}
```

**Loading States**
```typescript
const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

async function handleAction() {
  setIsLoading(true);
  try {
    await operation();
  } finally {
    setIsLoading(false);
  }
}

<Button disabled={isLoading}>
  {isLoading ? <Spinner /> : 'Submit'}
</Button>
```

```typescript
  window.addEventListener('offline', () => setIsOnline(false));
```
